Kase nu aawa Abrames caaqqidayssa qopana malane, nu morketa kusheppe izi nuna kessin nuni izas babboy baayndda oothanasinne, nu diza wode wurson ba sinthan nuna geeshshatethanne xillotethan essanassa.
<range>
<range>
Goda oge giigissanas ne izappe sinthara biza gish ta naazo neni woga Xoossa nabe geetetana.
Assay ba nagarappe maaretida gish deres attotetha erateth ne immana mala
nu Xoossa lo7o maaretethafe denddidayssan saloppe nuus away kezides.
Hessikka dhuman dizaytasne hayqqo kuwa garsan dizaytaskka po7isana malane nu tohotakka sarotetha oge kalethannassa.
Guutha naazikka diccides ayananka minnidees. Isra7eele asas qonccen beettanna gakkanaas bazo biittan deyides.
He wode biitta bollan diza asi wurikka taybeettidi xafistana mala orome kawo Awuggisxxossafe awajjay kezides:
Hessikka Qerenewoossa geetettizaysi Soore giza dere haariza wode hannida koyro dere taybo.
Hessa gish asi wuri xafistanaas ba dere biddes.
Yosefoykka asho dabbotethan Daawute bagafe gididda gish Galila awurajja garssan diza Naazirete katamappe Yuda awurajja Beettaleme geetettiza Daawute katamappe yidees.
Izi xafistana bishin izas giigistada yelana matida Maaramira biddes.
Izetikka heen dishin izis yelo wodey gakkides.
Izaka koyro attumma na yeliddaysafe guye imathi aqqizza keeththan aqqizza soy bayndda gish naaza carqqara xaaxadda miiza gaaxotan zin7adus.
Beettaleme achchan dorssa heemiza asati dorssa naagishe qammaara karen aqqizzayti deetees.
Goda kiitanchaykka istako yides, Goda boncho poo7oykka ista lanqqen yuuyi aadhdhannas po7ides. Istika keehi dagammida gish,
kiitanchay ista “babofite, wurso asas gidiza gita ufaysa miishshrachcho ekka yadis.
Hach kawo Daawute katama Beettalemen shemppo dhaley yellettidees. Izikka Goda kirstosa geetettees.
Cariqqara xaxeti zin7ida gaccino na demmanddista hessikka intes malaata gido gides.”
Izarakka hara daro salo kiitanchati beettidda. Xoossa galatishe,
bolla salon Xoossassi bonchoy gido sarotethaykka biitta bollan izi dosiza asas wursos gido gida.
Kiitanchati istafe shaakkettidi salo simmin dorsse heemizayti ba garsan issay issa “ane ha yite Goday nuus qonccisidaysanne haanddayssa Beistalame katama biiddi beyos” gida.
Istika elelli biiddi Maaramira, Yosefora mehe kath muziza gonggen zin7ida naara demmida.
Beyddaysafe guyyen Goda kiitanchay naaza gish istas yoottidayssa wursi zari yottida.
Heemizayti yoottidayssa siyida asay wuri keehi malalettides.
Gido attin Maarama yoza wurssa ba wozinan wotha dentha qoppashe gam7adus.
Heemizaytika handdays wurikka kiitanchay istas yoottida mala gididi beettidda gish siyidaysassine beyddayssas wursos Xoossa galatishenne bonchishshe simmida.
naazi yelettin osppuntha gallassan qaxaretiza wodey gakin aayeya iza qanthatanappe kase kiitanchay gida mala Yesussa geetettidi suummidees.
Muse woga mala isti geeyiza wodey wurini Yosefoyne Maarama guutha na Yesussa Godaa Xoossa sinthe shiishanas ekkidi Yerusaleme kezida. Hessika Goda wogan koyro yelettiza addey wuri Godas dumma gidana geetettidi Xafetidayssa polanaasinne,
<range>
qassekka Goda wogan nam77u wole kafotanne woykko nam77u wole kafo ciyista geetettiddayssa mala yarsho shiishanaassa.
He wode Yerusaleme kataman xilloonne Xoossa babbiza issi Simona geetettiza asi dees, izikka Isra7eele nayta attotetha naagiza asane xillo ayyaanany iza bolla shemppida asa.
Qassekka kirstossa beyontta dishe hayqqonta mala xillo ayyaanany izas qonccides.
Izika he wode xillo ayyaanany kaalethin maqqdase lasha gaath gelidees. Naaza aayeyiranne aawara Muse wogan bessizayssa polanaas guutha na Yesussa ekkidi gelida wode,
Simonay naaza ekki idimmidi Xoossa galatishe,
“Godo, ne caaqqida qaala mala ha7i tani ne ayylleya ne ashshizzayssa ta ayfera beyidda gish hi7a tana saron ekka, asa wurso sinthan ne giigisida attotetha ha7i ta ta ayfera beyadis.
<range>
<range>
Haysika wurso deres geemmettidayssa qoncisiza poo7o, ne dere Isra7eleska boncho” gides.
Aawaynne aaya iza gish haasa7etida yozan malaletida.
Simonaykka ista anjjidees, Maaramokka “daro asa wozina qofay qonccana mala haysi Isra7eelen diza darotas dhayosinne atethas, iza ixxizaytas qasse malaata gidana mala doorettides” gides.
Qassekka darota wozina qofay qonccana mala naaza michay qara mashsha mala ne wozina phaliqqana.
Qassekka Aasseere bagafe Fanu7eele na Haana geetettiza cimmida nabey daysu, izaka ba koyro azinara laappun layth kumeth deyadus.
Laythay izis osppun tammanne oydu layth gidana gakkanaas qammane gallas xoomashene woossashe maqqdaseppe shaakketonta am77etethan gam77adus.
He wodekka shiiqqada Xoossa galatadus. Yerusaleme wozetethi naagishe dizaytas wursos guutha naaza gish yootadus.
Yoseforane Maaramira Goda wogan azazettidayssa polidi Galila awurajjan diza ba so Naazirete katama simmida.
Guutha naazikka diccidi minni minni biddes, eratethankka kumides, Xoossa aaro keyatethaykka iza bolla dees.
Aawaynne aaya laythan laythan faaziga bonchannas Yerusaleme beettes.
Naazas laythay tammanne nam77u layth kumida wode kase dose gididayssa mala faaziga bonchanna kezida.
Faziga baaleza wursidi ba so simmishn guutha naazi, Yesussay Yerusalemen attides. Yelidaytikka izi attiddayssa eribeeyttenna.
Benara issife biza oge asara dees gishe issi gallassa oge bida. Gido attin izi istara baynddaysa eridi ba dabbota achchanne laggeta achchan dizakkonne giidi koyida.
Koyi koyidi beettontta ixiin Yerusaleme simmida.
Heezzu gallassafe guye maqqdasen tamarisizayta giddon uttidi siyishenne asata oychchishenne ista oychcha zarishe maqqdasen dishin demmida.
Siyidayti wuri Yesussa akekkaninne iza zarozan daro malaalettida.
Yosefoyne Maarama iza beyida wode malaaletida. Maaramaka ta nazo ays hayssa mala oothadi? ne aawaynne taninne nena koyishe keehi metottettidos gadus.
Izikka zaaridi tana ays koydettii? Tani ta aawa keeththan daanas bessizaysa eribeykketi gides.
Gido attin istas izi yoottidayssi gelibeynna.
Heeppe simmin istara issife Naazirete wodhidi istas azazettishe deyidees. Aaya Maaramaka he haanida miishsha wurssa ba wozinan naagashe gam7adus.
Yesussay cincatethan, geesaninne saban Xoossa sinthanne asa sinthan diccides.
Xiibaros geetettiza qeesarey kawottida tammanne ichachchantho laythan Phanxoossa Philaxosa gizays Yuda biitta haariza wode, Herdossay Galila biitta haariza wode, iza ishay piliphoossay, Ixuriyasanne Xirakkondose biitta haariza wode, Lisannyossay Sabilane biitta haariza wode,
Haanaynne Qayafay waana qeeseta gidida wode Xoossa qaalay baazo biittan diza Zakarassa na Yanisakko yides.
Yaanisay Yordanose shoore achchan diza dereta wurson “inte nagara atto gaanas nagarappe simmidi xamaqqetite” gidi yoottides.
Hessika qasse nabe Isayaasay bazon hizgidi wassiza asa koshinch “Godas oge giigissite baassidikka lo7ethite.
Shoobba biittay wuri kumana guutha zumayne gita zumay wuri ziq gaana geella ogey sitta moorettida ogey lo7o gidana.
Asa zerethi wuri ashshizza Xoossa woliqqa beyana giidi bazon wassiza asa qaala giireth” giidi ba maxaafan xaafida mala.
Yanisaykka iza kushen xamaqqistana yiza asas “inteno ha shoosha nayto yaana diza Xoossa hanqqofe haakkana mala ooni intena zoridee?
Inte naggara oothoppe simmidayssa erisiza ootho oothite <Abramey nu aaway nuus dees> gusi aggitte gides. Xoossi bees giikko ha shuchchatappe Abrames na oothi denthaanas dandda7izayssa erite”
Beyxxey mith qanxanas miththa xaphon dees. Lo7o ayfe ayfontta iita mithi wuri qanxettidi taman yegistana.
Asaykka “histtini ay oothooni” giidi oychchides.
Yanisaykka asas “nam77u mayoy diza issi mayoy bayndda asas imo qassekka qumay dizaykka shaakkidi immo” gides.
Qaraxa shiishizayttikka xamaqqistanaas yiidi “tamarisizayso nu ay oothino?” gida.
Izikka “inte azazettidayssafe bollara qaraxa shiishoppite” gides.
Wotadarattikka “nuni qasse ay oothino” giidi oychchida. izikka “oona miishshakka gidin dafi ekkofite qassekka oonane wordon mootopite inte damozay intes giddana” gides.
Asay Yanisa beyidi haysi kirstossa? giidi ba wozinan sidhides.
Yanisaykka wursos “tani intena haathan xamaqays gido attin ta iza caamma birshaanas besoontta tappe aadhdhizaddey yaana. izi intena Xillo Ayaananne taman xamaqqana.
Kath suragiza layiday iza kushen dees. Balezza kumetha geeshshanna gistteza qasse di7en qollana gafezakka to7onta taman xuugana” gides.
Yanissay asa hara dumma dumma zore qaalara minnithethi zorishe mishrachcho qaala yoottides.
Gido attin Galila biitta haariza Herdoosay ba isha machcho Herooddiyaado ekkida gishine hara daro iita oothida gish Yanisay iza hanqqida gish
kase mooro bolla hara gujjidi Herdossay Yaanisa woyne keeththan yegides.
Asay xamaqqettidappe guyyen Yesussaykka xamaqqetides, izi woosishin saloy doyettides.
Xillo Ayyaanaykka wole milattida iza bolla wodhides. “saloppe ta dosiza nay nena nenan tani ufa7istays” giza qaalay yides.
Yesussay Xoossa ootho oykkishn laythay izas heezu tamu laytha mala gidana. Asaykka izi Yosefo na, Eelle na,
Maati na, Lewe na, Milki na, Yuda na, Yosefo na,
Matattiyu na, Amoxxe na, Nahome na, Isilime na, Naage na,
Maate na, Matatiyo na, Semeye na, Yosefo na, Yuda na,
Yoonane na, Reese na, zerubbaabeele na, Selatiyale na, Nere na,
Milki na, hadi na, Yosa na, Qoosame na, Elimodamme na,
Yose na, Elazare na, Yorame na, Maaxate na, Eelle na,
Simoona na, Yuda na, Yosefo na, Yooname na, Eliyaqqeeme na,
Meliya na, Maaxate na, Naatane na, Daawute na,
Iseeye na, Iyobede na, Bo7eeze na, Selimoona na, Ne7asoone na,
Amnaddabe na, Aarame na, Aaronne na, Esrome na, Faareesse na, Yuda na,
Yaqoobe na, Yisaqqa na, Abrame na, tara na, Nakore na,
Seerohe na, Raggawe na, Faaleeqqe na, Aabere na, Saala na,
Qayneme na, Aarfakkisidde na, Seeme na, Nohe na, Lamehe na,
Matosala na, Henokke na, Yarede na, Malali7eele na, Qaynane na,
Henosse na Seete na Addamme na, Xoossa na, milatides.
Yesussay Xillo Ayyaanaan kumidi Yordanose shooreppe simmida mala Xillo Ayyaanaany iza kaalethidi bazzo biitta efides.
Heenkka xala7en oydu tamu gallassa paacetides. He paacetiza galassatan aykkokka monta gish wursethan gafides.
Xala7eykka Yesussa ne Xoossa na gidikko ane hayssa shuchchay kath gidana mala azaza gides.
Yesussaykka zaaridi asi kaththan xalla deenna geetettidi xafettides, giidi xala7es zaarides.
Hessafe kaallidi xala7ey Yesussa issi dhoqqa zuma bolla kessidi salo gufanthon diza kawotetha qiphphida ayfey xeelanas beesdine,
haysi ne beyizza biitta kawotetha duretethay wurikka taas imetides taka ta dosizaddes immanas dandda77iza gish, neeska immana gides.
Hesa gish ne kunddada taas goynnikko haysi wurikka nees gidana gides.
Yesussaykka zaaridi ne Godaa Xoossaassi kunddada iza xalla woosa geettetidi xaafettides gides.
Hessafekka Yesussa Yerusalemeni maqqdase xeera kessi essidi Xoossa maxaafan “nena naagana mala Xoossi ne gish ba kiitancha azazanna, ne toy shuuchchan qoxetonta mala kiitanchati ba kushera nena dhoqqu histi oykkana” geetettidi xaafettida gish ne Xoossa na gikikko ane hayssafe duge kundda gides.
<range>
<range>
Yesussaykka “ne Godaa Xoossa paacofa” geetettides giidi zaarides.
Xala7eykka ba paacanayisa wursidappe guyyen hara bees giiga wodey beettanashshe Yesussappe shaakkettides.
Yesussaykka Xillo Ayyaanaan wolqan Galila simmides. Iza lo7o nashoy Galila achchan diza deretan wurson siyettides.
Izikka mukkuraben tamaarisishin iza timirttey lo7in asay wurikka iza galatides.
Heeppe ba yellettida katama Naazirete yiidi kase sanbbata gallas mukurabe geliza mala mukurabe gelidi Xoossa maxaafa nabbabanaas dendi eqqides.
Nabe Isayasa maxaafay izas imetin maxaafa doyida mala
“Goda ayyaanaany ta bollan dees, manqotas mishrachcho qaala yootana mala tana tiyides, qachchetidaytas birsheteth, qooqqeti xeellana oge ta awajjana mala, metotettidayta aashsha na mala, dossettida Goda laytha awajja ta yootana mala tana kiittides” giza so demmida nabbabidinne,
<range>
maxaafa gordidi mukurabe naagizayssas zaari immidi uttides. Mukuraben dizayti wurikka iza tishsh oothi xeellida.
Izikka istas “haysi inte inte haythara siiyida maxaafa qaalay hach poletides” gides.
Asay wurikka iza gish lo7o xallala haasa7eetes. Qassekka iza duunappe keziza lo7o qaalappe denddidaysani malalettidi haysi Yosefo na gidennee? gida.
Izikka dhale Godo nerka nena patha. Qifirnahomen neni oothishin nu siyidaysa hayssan ne katamankka ootha giza leemuso inte ta bolla malaatanayisas sidhey baa giidi istas yoottides.
Qassekka ta intes tuma gays nabey ba yellettida deren bonchetti erenna gides.
Gidoattin ta intes tuma gays heezu laythinne baga gakanas saloy gordettin wolqama koshay biitta bolla hannida Elassa wode he laythatan daro azinay bayndda maccassati Isra7eele biittan deettes shin Elassay istafe isineykoka kiitetibeyna. Gidoattin Sidona giza biittan Serappta geetettiza kataman diza issi azinay bayndda maccaseyko kiitettides.
<range>
Nabe Elsa7e wode Isra7eele deren daro inchiracho harggizayti deetes shin Sooriya biitta asa gidida Ni7imaneppe attin he darotappe oonikka inchiracho harggefe paxibeyyna.
Mukuraben dizayti wurikka hessa siiyidi daro hanqqettida.
Be utidasooppe dendi eqqidi Yesussa katamappe kare kessidi duge zaari yedanaas ista katamaya oothettida dhoqqa zuma xeera ekki efida.
Gido attin izi ista giddon shaakki yegidi aadhdhi biddes.
Heeppekka Galila awurajjan diza Qifirnahome geetettiza katama wodhides. Heenkka sanbbata gallas daro asa tamarso oykides.
Izi Godatethara haasa7iza gish iza timirttan malalettida.
Mukuraben tuna ayyaanaany oykida addey dees. Izikka ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi
“Naazirete Yesussa ha7i ta waano? Nenara tana aazze gathidee? Ne yiday nuna dhaysanasee? Ne oonnakkoone ta erays ne Xoossa xillo gidikii?” giidi wassides.
Yesussaykka tuna ayyaanaan ha addezappe co7u gaada keza giidi seerides tuna ayyaanaaykka daro asa sinthan addezza boollafe yegidi issi qohokka gathonta yedidi kezides.
Asay wurikka malalettidi ba garsan issay issara aso haysi ay giza timirttee? Godatetharane wolqara iita ayyaanaan azazes istikka kezeetes giidi haasa7ettida.
Yesussa lo7o nashoyka wursoso gakides.
Hessafe guye Yesussay mukurabeppe kezidi Simoona keeth gelides. Simoona bolottiya wolqama micha harggey oykin sakistada dishin Yesussa izo patharki giidi woossida.
Izika iziko shiiqqidi hokidi micha harggeza seerides. Micha harggeyka yedin heeraka denda eqqada imathata mokadus.
Away wulana gishin dumma dumma harggey oykida asa wursi izako ekki yida. Izikka hargiza asata wurso bolla ba kushe wothidi pathides.
Tuna ayyaanaanti qassekka Yesussa “neni Xoossa na” gishenne waasishe daro asatappe kezida, gido attin izi ista seerides, tuna ayyaanaanti izi kirstosa gididayssa eriza gish isti isinoka haasa7ana mala koybeyna.
Gadey woonitishn Yesussay issi poqqetha so biddes. Daro asaykka iza koyishe izi diza so gakides. Izi istafe shaakettidi bontta mala digganas koyida.
Gido attin istas gede hara katama baada Xoossa kawotetha mishrachcho qaala yootanas taas besses, tani kiitettida gita qofay hessa gides.
Izika Yihuda mukurabistan qaala guji yoottides.
Yesussay Gensereexxe abba lanqqen eqqidi Xoossa qaala tamaarisishin siiyiza asay iza kuni7isides.
He wode nam77u wogoloti abba achchan dishin Yesussay be7ides. mole oykizayti wogolotappe wodhdhidi mole gitista meeceetes.
Yesussay wogolotappe Simoona wogolon gelidi biittafe gede abba gido shishanna mala oychidinne wogolo giddon uttidi asa tamaarsides.
Tamaarsidi wursidape guye Simoona abbay ciimmatizaso shiiqqa mole oykanas inte giteza abba gido yegite gides.
Simoonay Yesussas zaaridi Godo qamma kumeth daaburi aqqiddi issinokka oykibeyko, gidoattin ne qaalan giteza yegana gides.
Yegida wode daro mole oykida. Giteyka daakettides.
Hara wogolon dizayti yiidi ista maaddana mala kushera wuti xeygida. Istika yiidi nam77u wogolota mole kunthida. Wogolotika duge miteteth oykida.
Simoona geettetiza Phexiroossay hessa beyidi Yesussa gulbate bolla kundidi Godo ta nagarancha gidida gish ta achchafe kichcha gides.
Izi hessa giday izine izara dizayti oykida daro molezan malalettida gishassa.
Qassekka Simoona laggeti zabidoosa nayti Yaqobeyne Yanisayka wuri malalettida. Yesussaykka Simoona babofa hayssafe guye ne asa oykizadde gidana gides.
Istika wogolota biittako shiishshidi wursikka yegi7agidi Yesussa kaallida.
Yesussay katamatappe issineyin dishin inchirachcha harggey bolla wursi oykida issi asi he kataman dees. He urayka Yesussa beyidi iza sinthan kundidi “Godo ne koyko tana pathana danda7asa” giidi woossides.
Yesussay ba kushe yedi bochchidi “ta dossadis paxa” gides. inchirachchay heeraka dhaydes.
Yesussay izas “hayssa oonaskka yootoppa, gido attin baada nena qeese halaqas bessa istas marka gidana mala ne geeyidayssas Musey azazida yarshoza shiishsha” giidi azazides.
Gido attin iza gish asay haasa7iza worey kaseppe aakki aakki biddes. Keehi daro asay iza haasa7a siyanasinne bena sakiza harggefe paxanas izako shiiqidees.
Yesussay daro wode asi bayndda poqqethaso biidi woossides.
Yesussay tamaarsishin asay Galilappenne Yihudappe qassekka Yerusalemeppe yida Farsawetinne woga tamaarisizayti heen uttida. Izi pathana mala Goda wolqay izara dees.
He wode asay issi kumetha bollay silidi qaaxonta harggancha zaphara tooki ekki yiidi keethe gelthidi Yesussa sinthan wothanas paacida.
Asa darotethafe dendidaysani keethe gelthanas xoonetida gish pude keeththa kaara bolla kezidinne kaara lukidi harggancha zaphara tooki ehidi asa giddora Yesussa sinthan wothida.
Yesussay ista amano beyidi hayso ne ne nagarappe maaristadasa gides.
Muse woga xaafizaytine Farsaweti haysi Xoossa bolla xallatethan hayssatho haasa7izay izi oonee? Issi Xoossafe attin nagara maaranaas ooni danda7ize giidi qoppida.
Yesussay ista qofa erida gish “inte inte wozinan ays hessaththo qoppeti?” gides.
Neni nagarappe maaristadasa gusafenne dendada ba gusafe awayssi kawishee?
Gido attin ta hayssa giday asa naas biitta bolla asa nagarappe maaranaas Godatethi dizaysa inte erana mala. Qassekka he sila ura “nena gays! eqqa dendada ne zapha tookada baa” gides.
Izi heeraka ista sinthan dendi eqqides. Kase ba zin7ida zapha tookidi Xoossa galatishe beso bides.
He wode asi wuri malalettides. Xoossa galatishe hach malalisizaz be7ides giidi daro babida.

Farsawetinne ista Xaafeti qaraxa shiishshizaytarane nagaranchatara issife aazas meeti giidi Yesussa kaallizayta bolla zigirettida.
Yesussaykka istas hargganchatas attin paxa asas aakkime koshshenna gides.
Taka nagaranchata maaretethako zaranaas attin xillota xeyganas yabeykke gides.
Istika zaaridi Yanisa kaallizayti daro wode xoometesinne woosetes Farsawista kaallizaytikka izathokka oothetes. Nena kaallizayti gidikko wurso wode meettesinne uyettes gida.
Yesussaykka istas zaaridi mishray issife dishin diggissasi xeeysettidayta xoomisanaas bessizze? gides.
Gido attin mishray istafe shaakistana wodey yaana isti he wode xoomana.
Istas oorath mayoppe qanxi ekkidi gal77a mayo bolla wothi sikizaaddey deenna wothi sikkikko oorathazi gal77ara gaaggonta gish gal77aza daakkana gides.
Woyneppe othetida oorath cajje gal77a ogoron kunthidi wothiza asi oonikka baawa wothiza gidikko woyneppe oothettida ooratha cajjey gal77aza daakana. Woyne cajjezikka biittan gukkana gal7a ogoroy sinthafe go7ontaz gidana.
Hessa gish ooratha woyne ushy ooratha ogoron gujjistanas besses.
Histikko caalla woyne ush uyidaappe guye caalontazi uyana koyizay ooninne deenna gaasoyka caallay lo7o giza gish.
Issi sanbbata gallas Yesussay kaththa giddora aadhdhi bishin iza kaallizayti tiya xuphi ekkidi ba kushen shigechchi mishni,
Farsawistappe issi issi asati sanbbata gallas oothanas besoonttaysa ays oothetii? gida.
Yesussaykka istas Daawuttey izara diza asati gafida wode Daawutey oothidaysa nabbabibeyketii? giidi zaarides.
Izi Xoossa keeth gelidi qeeseti xalla maana mala azazettida dumma ukeetha bees miidi benara dizaytas immides.
Qassekka Yesussay asa nay sanbbata Goda giidi istas yoottides.
Yesussaykka hara sanbbata gallas mukurabe gelidi tamarisishin oshacha kushey silida issi assi heen dees.

Yesussaykka ista wozana qofa eridi kushey silida addeza wurso sinthan denda eqqa gides. addezzika dendi eqqides.
Yesussaykka ista ta intena issi miish ane oychchays sanbbata gallas oothanas bessizay lo7o ootho woykko iita oothoo? Shemppo asho woykko dhaysoo? giidi oychchides.
Qassekka Yesussay ba yuushon diza wursi yuushi xellidape guyyen addeza ne kushe piddisa gides. Addezzika Yesussay gida mala oothides. Iza kusheykka paxides.
Gido attin asati hanqettida, Yesussa bollankka ay oothanas koshizakonne ba giddon zorettida.
He gallassatappe issi gallas Yesussay woosanaas zuma bolla kezidi qamma kumeth Xoossa woosishe aqides.
Gadey wonitishin bena kaallizayta xeeygidi istafe tammanne nam77anta doorides. Istaka hawarista giidi sunthidees.
Istika Phexirosa giidi sunthida Simoonane iza isha Indirassa, Yaqobe, Yanisa, Pilphosa, Barttalemossa,

Yesussaykka bena kaallizaytas hiz gides Xoossa kawotethay intes gidida gish inteno manqqoto inte anjettidayta,
Inte guyyeppe kaallanna gish ha7i gafizayto inte anjettidayta, inte guyyeppe miicana gish inteno ha7i yekkizayto inte anjettidayta,
asay ta gish intena ixxishin, ba giddofe shaakkishin, borishin intena iita sunthara xeygishn inte anjettidayta,
Intes salon gita woytoy diza gish he wode ufaysan guppite, ays giiko ista aawati nabeta bolla hessaththo oothida.
Gido attin inteno dureto inte ha7i ufa77ettida gish intena ayye,
inteno ha7i kalidayto intena ayye inte guyyeppe yeekkana, inte guyyeppe michistanasinne yeekkana gish inteno ha7i miicizayto intes ayye inte guyyepe yekana,
asi wuri inte gish lo7o haasa7iza wode intena ayye ana, ays giiko ista aawati wordo nabetas hessa mala oothida.
Gido attin ta yootizaysa siyizayto tani intes yootizay inte morketa siiqite, intena ixxizaytas lo7o oothite,
intena qanggizayta anjite, intena qohizaytas woosite,
issi shagalan baqqikko, nam77antho shagala gujja bessa, oonine ne bollara mayidaysa qaari ekkikko gaathara mayidaysakka diggofa.
Nena woosiza wursos imma, ne miishsha ekkida assi zars immana mala oychchofa.
asi intes oothanna mala inte koyizaysatho intekka hara asas oothite.
Nagaranchattikka bena siiqizayta siiqiza gish inte intena siiqizayta xalla siiqikko intes ay dumma anjjoy dizee?
Inte intes lo7o oothizaytas xalla lo7o oothikko intes ay dumma anjjoy dizee? Ays giikko nagaranchattikka hessaththo oothiza.
Tal7e ekkidi zaarana danda7etes gizaytas xalla inte tal7ikko inte hara ay dumma anjjo demmanee? Ays giiko nagaranchatika isti tal7idaysa sire zaaridi ekkanas nagaranchatas tal7etesi.
Gido attin Xoossi bena galatontaytasinne iitatas keeha gidida mala inte morketa siiqite, lo7o oothite, guyyepe zaaridi ekkanas qoponta dishe tal7e immite, hessanika intes kushe zaaroy gita gidana, qassekka inte woga Xoossa na gidana.
Inte aaway keha gidida mala intekka kiyata gidite.
Inte harata bolla pirdoppite inte bollakka pirdetena, inte bolla firday darontta mala harata bolla firda darssoppite, asas atto gite inteskka atto geetetana.
Immite inteskka imettana, intes inte makkida miishshan simmidi makkistana gish naaqi baqqettiddi, yigettidi, kumidi woran gukanashe lo7o makkiza miishshan makettidi inte ki7on idiman imistana.
Qassekka Yesussay istas leemuso hiz gidi yoottides “qooqqey qooqe kaalethanas danda7izee? kaalethikkokka nam77ati issay issara oykettidi ollan gelettennee?
Tamaarey bena tamaarisizaddeppe aadhdhenna, gido attin lo7ethi tamaarida asi wuri ba astaamare mala gides.
Ne ayfe giddon diza tuussa xeellonta dashe ne isha ayfe giddon diza buura ays xellayii?
Ne ayfen diza tuussa beyontta ne isha tani ne ayfen diza buura ane kessays gaanas wosta danda7ayii? Neno milatisizayso koyrotada ne ayfen diza tuussa kessa, hessafe guye ne isha ayfen diza buura kessanas lo7etha xeellandasa.”
Lo77o mithi iita ayfe ayfenna, qassekka iita mithi lo7o ayfe ayfenna.
Mithi wurikka ba ayfe ayfen ereetes, agunthafe balase geettetiza miththa ayfey maaxettenna, laadeppe woyne ayfey qanxxettenna.
Lo77o asi ba wezina kumida lo7o miish kesses, iita asikka ba wezina kumida iita miishshafe iita kesses, asi wurikka ba wezina kumi palahidaysa ba duunan hassa7ees.
Tani gizaysa oothekista shin ays tana “Godo Godo” geetii?
Taako yiidine ta qaala siyyidi polizay wuri oonna milatizakkonne ta intena bessana, keethe keexanas ziq oothi bookkiddi shuchcha bollan ba keeth keexida asa milates. Haro haathi yiidi he keeththa suggides, gido attin minni keexetida gish qaathanas dandd7ibeynna.

Yesussay hessa wursikka dere sinthan yooti wursidaysafe guye Qifirnahome gizaso bi gelides.
Heen Qifirnahomen xeetu wotaddarata halaqqay dees he addezas izi siiqiza ashkkaaraay harggidi hayqqos shemppo bolla dees.
Izikka Yesussa gish siiyidi ba ashkaara pathana mala Yesussa wooserkketi giidi issi issi Ayhudde bagga asatappe cimata Yesussakko yeddides.
Kiitettidi bida asati Yesussako yiidi hayssa ashkaara addeza gish ne pathana besses giidi minnithi woosida.
Ays giiko haysi addezi nu asa daro dosees, nuusikka mukurabe keexisiday iza.
Yesussayksa izistara bides. Yesussay addeza keethako matiza wode addezi ba laggeta Yesussakko yedidi “Godo ne ta keeth gelanaas beessenna taka nena ta keethe gelthanas bessiza asi gidonta gish haa yashe daaburoppa” gides.

taaskka tana azaziza asi tappe bollara dees. Tappe garssara tani azaziza wotaddarati deetes. Issa haaya giiko yes issa he ba giiko bees ashkkaaraykka hessa ootha giiko azazettidayssa oothes.

Hessafe guye Yesussay Xoossa kawotetha mishrachcho sabbakishe dumma dumma katamata giddorane dere gaathara aadhdhidees. Aadhdhidi biza wode iza kaalliza tammanne nam77ati izara deetes.
Qassekka tuna ayaanaappenne iita harggefe paxida issi issi maccashati izara deetes. Istika laappun tuna ayaanaany izippe kezida Magidele giza dereppe yida Maaramo,

issi goshshanchay zerethi zeranas kezides, zerishinkka bagazi ogen wodhin asa toon yedhettides, salo kafotikka yiidi maxi mida,
issi zerethay shuuchcha gadeni wodhidi heerakka caarides gadezzikka mela gade gidida gish elle meli kichchides.
Qassekka hara zerethi aguntha giddon wodhides agunthaykka izara issife diccidi caarechchaykka dicconta mala cuullides.
Qassekka hara zerethay lo7o aradda gadeni wodhides caaridda wodekka xeetu kushe ayfides. Yesussay haasa7a wursidi qaala dhoqqu histidi “siyiza haythi diza asi siyo” gides.

izikka hizgiidi zarides Xoossa kawotetha xuura eroy intes imettides haratas gidikko leemusora yootays qassekka harati beyidi wozinan wothontamalanne siiyidi yuushi qopponta mala hannidees.
Zeretha leemusoykka hayssa, zeretha geettetidays Xoossa qaala,
oge lanqqen wodhidays qaala siyizayta giddo attin isti amanidi attontta mala xalla7ey yiidi qaala ista wozinappe eekkigidizayta.
Shuuchcha bolla wodhidaytikka qaala siiyidi ufaysara ekkizayta, istikka ha7is amanetes attin metoy ista bolla gakkiza wode xapho yedonta gish ellera amano kaddizayta.
Aguntha giddon wodhidayti qaala siiyizayta, heytikka aqqipey7iddi biitta bolla duussas qofaninne duretethan duusa lo7otethan culetidi lo7ethi ayfe imetena.
Aradda biittan wodhidays qaala suureninne lo7o wozinan siiyidi naaggizaytane danda7an minnidi ayfe ayfizzaytta.
Poo7o po7isidi baatha giddon woykko arssa garssan wothiza asi baawa, gido attin keethe geliza asas poo7ana mala qoncceson wothetees.

Yesussaykka zaaridi ta aayanne ta ishati Xoossa qaala siiyidi naagizayta gides.
Issi gallas Yesussay bena kaallizaytara wogolo giiddo gelidi abbafe he pinith pinnos gides.
Istika pinishin abba bolla gote carkkoy dendidi waayssiza wode Yesussay dhiskkides. Haathayka wogoloza giddo gelin asay daro metotettides.
Yesussa kaallizayti izakko shiiqqidi “Godo, Godo nu wurana hanos” giidi Yesussa dhiskofe denthida. Izikka beeggiddi carkozane abba danbbala seerin carkoyne abba danbbalay coo77u gides.
Izika bena kaallizayta inte amanoy awa bidde gides. Istika ba garssan babishshenne malaletishe carkonne haathenne azazizay, isttikka izas azazettizay izi oonee gida.
Izappe guye Galilape he pinithan diza Gergesenonne giza dere wogolora pinida.
Yesussay wogolozappe gadeni wodhida wode dayiddanthi iza bolla diza issi asi katamappe kezidi iza demmides, he uray daro wode mayo mayonta kallo keeththan aqontta duufo bees aqoso oothida asa.
Yesussa beydda wode wassishe Yesussa sinthan kunddides, qaala dhoqqu histidi “boncho Xoossa na Yesussa taasnne nees ay gaytotethi dizee? Ne tana waaysonta mala nena woosays” gides.
Tuna ayaanaay hessa gaanas danda7iday addezappe kezana mala Yesussay azazida gishassa. Tuna ayaanaanazikka woden woden denddiza gish addezzi sanithalataninne birattan toho qachi naaginkka qachettida sanithalata duuthethidi iza bolla diza dayiiddanthay iza duge bazo zaari efees.
Yesussay ne sunthi oonee giidi oychchides, izikka daro dayiiddanthati iza bolla gelidi diza gish ta sunthi “leegoone” gides.
Dayiiddanthatika wursethi baayndda cima oilan bena yegonta mala minnthidi woossida.
Henka zuma bolla daro gudunthi heemetes, dayiiddanthatakka gudduntha wudezan gelite giidi azazana mala woossida, Yesussaykka ero gides.
Dayiiddanthatika addezappe kezidi guddunthatan gelida, guddunthatikka aafozza dugunthara bichcharishshe biiddi abban gelidi abban mitettida.
Heemizayti handdaysa beydda wode beezhumi biiddi katama asasne dere asas yoottida.
Handdayssa beyana giidi asay ba dizasooppe Yesussakko yides, dayiiddanthay izappe kezida addezzika wozinay kanay simmini afala mayidi Yesussa toho garsan utidaysa beyidi babida.
Dayiiddanthan oyketida addezzi paxishin beyddayti izi waani paxidakkonne derezas yootida.
Gergesenonne matan diza asay keehi babbda gish Yesussa hayssafe kichch giidi woossida, izikka wogolozan gelidi simmi bides.
Dayiiddanthay izappe kezida addezzi Yesussara issife daanna mala woossides,
Gido attin ne so simadda Xoossi nees oothida gita miish yoota giidi moyzides. Addezzikka Yesussay izas oothida gita miish ba kataman diza asas wursos qonccen yootishe biddees. Ya7irosa naanne Yesussa mayo bochchidda maccassa
Assay wuri Yesussa yuusa naagishe gam77ida gish izi simmishni ufaysan mokki ekkida.
He wode Iya7irossa geetettiza mukurabe halaqqay yiidi Yesussa toho bolla kundidi Yesussa iza so baanna mala woossides.
Izi hessaththo oychchiday izas tammanne nam77u laytha kumida issi macca nay sakistada shemppo bolla diza gish. Izi he buussan dishin derey daridi ba garsan sugetidi iza keehi un7isides.
Tammanne nam77u laythi suuthi izippe gukishin diza issi maccashiya bees diza miishsha ubbaa dhale eriza asatas imma wursini izo pathanaas danda7ida uraykka isoykka baa.
Izakka guyyera shiiqqada Yesussa afala maccarata bochchadus, gukkiza
Yesussaykka “tana bochchidday oone?” gides. Wurika nuni bochchibeykko gi kadida wode phixrossay zaaridi Godo asi wuri yuuyi aadhdhidi nena suggerethidi un7ises gides.
Gido attin Yesussay asi tana bochchides, wolqay tappe kezidaysa ta erays gides.
Maccashiya eretonta qotistada baannaas danda7ontaysa erida wode kokorashe yaada Yesussa sinthan kunddadus. Izakka Yesussa waana bochchidakkonne qassekka ellera waana paxidakko wurso asa sinthan yootadus.
Izikka ta nayee ne amanoy nena pathides, saron ba gides.
Yesussay buro maccasheys haasa7a bolla dishin mukurabe halaqqa Iya7irosa keethafe issi asi Iya7irosas ne naya hayqqadus hessa gish hayssappe guye astamaareza mela daabursofa gides.
Yesussay hessa siiyidi Iya7irosa aykkoy ba baboofa amanna attin ne naya paxana gides.
Yesussay Iya7irosa keeth geliza wode Phexirosa, Yanisane Yaqobe qassekka nay aawappenne aayeyippe attin haray oonikka izara gelana mala koybeyna.
He wode asay wuri nayis wuwu gi wassi yekkishin Yesussay yeekofite iza zin77adus attin hayqqabeykku gides.
Asaykka naya hayqqidaysa eriza gish Yesussa bolla miicides.
Gido attin izi nay kushe oykkidi ta nayee denda gides.
Nayis shempoyka simmides. Heerakka denda eqqadus, Yesussaykka izis miza miish immana mala azazides.
Nka yelidaytika malaletida. Gido attin izi handdayssa oonaaskka yotonta mala azaziddes.
Yesussaykka tammanne nam77u hawarista issife xeeygidi dayiddanthata kessana malane harggefe pathana mala istas wolqanne Godatethi immides:
qassekka Xoossa kawotetha yootanasinne harggizayta pathanas ista kiittidees.
istaskka “oge bishe guufe woykko, qaraxite woykko, quma woykko miishshe woykko nam77u mayo aykkokka oykki baannas koshshenna.” gides.
intekka he katamayppe kezana gakanas koyro gelida oona keeththanka gidin heen gam7ite.
katama asay intena mokki ekkonta ixxikko he katamayppe kezidi intena mokkontaytas markka gidana mala inte tohon diza gudula pittidi kezite gides.
istikka Goday gida mala kezidi miishrachcho qaala yootishene hargganchata pathishe dere wurson guttappe gutta yuuyiida.
he wode issi issi asati Yanisay hayqqoppe denddides, baggati Elasay kezidi beettides, qasse bagati beni nabetappe issay hayqqoppe dendidees giidi haasa7etiza gish Yuda biitta haariza Herdoossay hessa siyidi hanza miishshan ba wozinan metotettides.

Herdoossaykka tani iza qoodhe qanxida xamaqiza Yanisay hayqqides, histin iza gish hayssa mala haasa7etishn ta siyizays izi oonee? giidi iza ba ayfera beyana koydees.
hawarettikka simmidi isti oothidaysa wursi Yesussassi yoottida. izikka ista xalla benara ekkidi Beettesaydda geetettiza poqqethan diza katama bides.
gido attin daro asay hessa eridi ista kaallides. izikka ista mokki ekkidi Xoossa kawotetha gish yoottides. qassekka harggefe pathanas bessizayta pathides.
gadey lem7ishin tamman nam77u hawareti izakko shiiqqidi “nuni dizay baazo biittan gidida gish asay biiddi bees aqana sonne miza miish koyana mala asa moyiza” gida.
gido attin izi istas zaaridi “mizaz inte istas immite” gides. istikka nuus ichachu ukeethafenne nam77u moleppe haray ba. ha asas gidiza kath koshikko shamanas besses gida.
Yesussaykka bena kaallizayta “asa ichachu tamu ichachu tamu histi shaakki shaakki utisite” gides. heenkka ichachu shi gidana attumma asay dees.
Yesussa kaallizaytika Yesussay azazida mala asa wursi utisida.
Yesussaykka ichachu ukeeththanne nam77u molista oykidi pude salo xeellidi Xoossa galatides. izikka ukeetha menithidi asa gathana mala bena kaallizaytas immides.
asay wurikka miidi kaallides. Yesussa kaallizaytika asappe atidda tammanne nam77u masobe kumeth maaddafe denthida.
issi gallas Yesussay berkka woossishin iza kaallizayti izara deetes. izikka ista “asay tana oona gizee?” giidi oychchides.
istikka izas “issi issi asay xamaqqiza Yanisa bagayti Elasa harati qasse beni nabetappe issay hayqoppe denddidees geetes” gida.
izikka ista “intech tana oona geetii?” giidi oychchides. Phexirosaykka “neni Xoossafe kiittetida kirstoosa” giidi zaaridees.
Yesussaykka ista hayssa oonaskka yootoppite giidi minnithi yoottidi
qassekka asa nay daro waayye ekkanas besses, dere cimatan qeese halaqqataninne Muse woga xaafizaytan ixistanane ista kushen hayqqanasinne hezantho gallassan hayqqpope dendana gides.
qassekka wursosi “ba shemppo ashshana giza asi wuri dhaysana, shin ba shempota gish giidi dhaysiza asi ashshana. hessa gish tana kaalana koyiza asi diikko bena kaddo, wurso gallas ba masqqale tookkidi tana kaalo” gides.

asi alame mule wodhisidi ba shemppo dhaysiko aaza go7ay dizee?
oonikka tananinne ta qaalan yeelatikko asa nay ba bonchora, aawa bonchoranne geeshsha kiitanchata bonchora yiza wode tani izan yeelatana.
ta intes tumu gays hayssan eqqida asappe hayqqanappe sinthan Xoossa kawotethi beyana bagga asati deetes.
Yesussay hessa gida osppun gallassa malappe guye woossanas zuma bolla kezides. bishe benara Phexirosa, Yanisanne Yaqobe ekki bides.
izi woosishin iza ayfesoy lametides. iza medhaykka wolqantha mala xoliqidi booxxidees.
nam77u asati Museynne Elasay izara haasa7ettida.
istikka bonchora qonccidi Yerusalemeni polistana diza Yesussa hayqqo gish haasa7ettida.
Phexirosane izara dizayta deexo dhiskkoy oykkides. istikka dhiskofe beeggidi Yesussa bonchonne nam77u asi izara eqqidayta beydda.
he nam77u asati Yesussappe shaakketi bishin Phexirosay Yesussa “Godo issi daasse nees, issi daasse Muses issi daasse Elasas oothidi haan dizaakko nuus lo7oshin” gides. gido attin Phexirosay ba gizaysa eronta gides.
izi hessa haasa7ishin shaaray yiidi ista genthides. shaara giddo gelidi babida.
shaara giddofekka “tani doorida nay hayssa iza siyite” giza qaalay setettides.
qaalay setettida wode Yesussay xalla beettides. Yesussa kaallizayttikka hanidda miishsha wursi ba wozinan oykkida attin oonaaskka yoottibeyitena.
wontetha gallas isti zuma bolla wodhin daro asay yiidi Yesussara gaagidees.
he wode asa giddofe issi uray qaala dhoqqu histidi “tamaarisizayso taas issi nay xalla diza gish iza ne xeellana mala ta nena woosays.
iza iita ayaanaay oykishin haasa7ay bayndda wasses, qakketishe duunara goppontto kesses, qoho gathidappe guye daro waayisdi agges.
nena kaallizayti nazappe kessana mala ista ta woosadisi, gido attin kessana dandda7ibeyitenna” gides.
Yesussaykka istas zaaridi “amanontta ha wode wobe asato tani intenara aydde gakkanaas daanee? intenakka aydde gakanas dandda7anee? naaza ane ha eha!” gides.
naazi yishin iita ayaanaay iza boollafe yegin qakkettides. Yesussaykka iita ayaanan seeridi naaza pathidi naaza aawas immides.
asaykka wuri Xoossa gitatethan malaletides. izi oothidaysan asay wuri malaletishn Yesussay bena kaallizayta
“asa nay asa kushen aadhdhidi imistana, intekka ha yoza baloppitte” gides.
gido attin izi gizaysi istas gelibeyna. ays giiko isti akekkontta mala yozi istafe geemettides, zaaridikka oychchonta mala babida.
iza kaallizayti ooni oonappe aadhizakkone ba garsan palametida.
Yesussaykka ista wozina qofa eridi guutha na ekki yiidi ba matan esidi
“ha guutha na ta sunthan ekkizaddey oonikka diikko tana ekkees, tana ekkizaddeyka tana kiitiddaysa ekkees. inte wursofe guutha uray izi wursofe aadhdhes” gides.
Yanisaykka “Godo issi uray ne sunthan dayiddanth kesishin beydos. gido attin izi nunara kaalonta gish digganas koydos” gides.
“intena ixonta asi wuri inte baga gidida gish diggopite” gides.
Yesussay salo biza wodey matida gish Yerusaleme baanas denddidees.
izikka sinthethidi ase kiittides. istikka koshiza miish giigissanappe kasetidi Samarya biittan diza issi guta bida.
gido attin derey izi Yerusaleme bizayssa erida gish mokki ekkibeyitenna.
iza kaallizaytappe Yaqobeyne Yanisay hanzaysa beyidi “Godo Elasay oothoysatho tamay saloppe wodhidi ista dhayso” giidi azazana mala koyay? gida.
gido attin Yesussay istakko yuuyiidi “intes ay mala ayaanaay dizakkon erekketii? asa nay yiday asa shemppo ashshanas attin dhaysanas gideenna” giidi ista seerides.
isti wurikka hara guta bida.
istikka birshin issi asi istakko shiiqidi “tani neni biza wursoso nena ta kaalana” gides.
Yesussaykka “worikenatas aqqizza olay, kafotas qasse aqqizza kafo keethi dees gido attin asa nas ba hu7e ayssiza soykka baawa” gides.
Yesussaykka hinkoysa “tana kaala” gides. he uraykka “Godo ta kasista baada ta aawa moogoo?” gides.
Yesussaykka “aggagga hayqidayti hayqidayta moogetto, neni gidikko baada Xoossa kawotethaa asas yoota” gides.
qassekka hara uray “Godo ta nena kaalana shin koyro so baada ta keeththa asa saro gaada yoo?” gides.
gido attin Yesussay “boora kaso oykkidi goyishe guye zaari xellizaddey oonikka Xoossa kawotethas beesena” gides.
Hessafe guye Goday hara laappun tammanne nam77u asa dooridi sunthidees. Istaka nam77u nam77u histtidi izi baanna sootane katamata wursika izeti kasettidi baanamala kiittides.
Maxa gakkida kaththay daro kaththa maxi shiishizayti guuthata hessagish kaththa Goday kaththa maxxidi shiishizayta kaththay dizaso yeddanamala woosite gides.
Hessa gish biite dorssati sudhume giddora biza mala ta intena yedays.
Korojo woykko qaraxite woykko caamma ekkofite, oge bolla oonakka saro gooppite.
Oona keethekka geliza gidikko koyrotidi “keeththa aso saro” giite.
He keeththan saro dosiza asi diikko inte sarotay hekeeththan shemppana, saro dosiza asi donta agikko inte sarotay intes simana.
Intes maana shiishida kath wursi miishshenne uyishe he inte gelida keeththan utite, oothiza uras ba woliqa wagga ekkanas izas besses. Ha keethafe he keeth yuuyoppite.
Inte ay katamakka gakkiza wode asay intena mokki ekkiko isti intes aathida quma miite.
He kataman diza hargganchata pathidi Xoossa kawotethi intekko matides giidi yoottite.
Gido attin inte biiddi issi katama gelishin he katama asay intena mokki ekkonta ixxikko he katama asay shiiqiza dubbusha kezidi
“nu to bolla diza inte katama gudula intes marka gidanamala nu toho boollafe pittos shin Xoossa kawotethay intekko matidaysa erite” giite.
Ta intes yootays firda gallas he katama firdappe Soddome katama firday shaykko gidana.
Kurazine nena ayye, Beette sayida nena ayye intenan oothetida malaatati Xirosaninne Sidonani oothetidakko istikka mayo mayidinne biiddinith gorppettidi he wode beni maaristanashin.
Gido attin firda wode intefe Xirosasinne Sidonaas shaykkana.
Hanne Qifirnahome pude salo dhoqqu dhoqqu gadii? Neni duge si7ole wodhana,
Inte gizaa siiyiza uray tana siiyes intena ekkonta uray tanakka eekkenna tana ekkontaykka tana kiitidayssa eekkenna.
Laappun tammanne nam77atikka ufa7etishe simmidi “Godo haray atoshin dayiddanthatikka ne sunthan nuus haaretida” giidi yootida.
Izika istas “xalla7ey wolqantha mala saloppe kundishin ta beyadis” gides.
Histikko shooshshanne masmasonne inte yedhana mala morkke woliqqa wurso bolla intes Godatethi immadis intena qohiza issi miishshkka deenna.
Inte sunthay salon Xafetida gish ufa7etite attin tuna ayaanaanti intes haaretida gish ufa7etofite
He wode Yesussay Xillo Ayaanaan ufa7etidi hizgides “salos biittas Goda gidida aabbo hayssa wursaka cincatappenne eratappe qotada guutha duudde naytas ne qonccisida gish tani nena galatays Ee aabbo haysi ne lo7o sheney hanidees.
Wuri ta aawa matappe taas imetides qassekka iza nay oonakkoone aawappe attin eriza uray baawa aaway oonakoone naazappe attin woykko naazi izas qonccisanas dosida urappe attin eriza uray baa”
Bena kaallizaytakko simmidi istas dumma “inte beyizzaysa beyiza ayfeti anjjettidayta.
Ta intes tuma gays daro nabetinne kawoti inte ha7i beyizzaysa beyanas koyidi beybeyttenna inte ha7i siiyizaysaka siiyanaas koyidi siybeyitenna.”
Issi gallas Muse woga tamaarisiza issi uray Yesussa paacanaas koyidi “tamaarisizayso tani medhina deyo laattanas ay oothoo?” gidi oychchides.
Yesussaykka zaaridi woga maxaafan ay geeteti Xafettidee? izape nees geliday aazee? giidi oychchides.
Uray zaaridi “ne Godaa Xoossa ne kumetha wozinappe, ne kumetha shemppofe, ne kumetha woliqqafene, ne kumetha qofappe siiqa, ne laggekka ne hu7e mala siiqa gees” giidi zaarides.
Yesussaykka lo7o zaaradasa nenikka hinnidan oothikko medhina deyo demmna gides.
Uray bena xilisanaas koyidi “histini ta laggey oonee?” giidi Yesussa oychchides
Yesussaykka zaaridi issi uray Yerusalemeppe Iyarko wodhishin panggati demmida iza mayo qaari ekkida, keehi qoxerethidi hayqqoppenne paxappe giddon yeggi aggi bida.
Issi qeesey he ogera bees duge wodhishe aamunthontta he qoxettida ura demmida pooqethara yegi aadhdhidees.
Qassekka issi Lewe baga asappe issi uray he ogera aadhdhishe qoxettida ura beyidi ha7ikka pooqidi aadhdhidees.
Issi Samaarya biitta asi he ogera aadhdhi bishe qoxettida ura bolla gakki wodhides, ura beyidinne keehi michchetides.
Urako shiiqidine maduntha dhaallana mala woyra zayitene woyneppe cajje maduntha bolla gusidi qachchides, ura ba hare togisidi imathi shemppizaso efidi lo7ethi xellides.
Wontetha gallas imathi shemppiza keeththa Godas nam77u dinnare immidinne nena hara miishsha kessisikko ta simashe nees immana neppe kessada lo7etha naaga gides.
Histiko ha heezu asatappe pangatan qoxetidi hayqqoppenne paxappe giddon yegettida uras keehi mata laggey nees awayssa milatizee?
Muse woga tamaarisizayskka michettidaysako! gides. Yesussaykka izas nekka baada izaysatho ootha gides.
Yesussayne iza kaallizayti oge bishin Yesussay issi guta gelides, Marta geetettiza issi maccashiya ba son Yesussa moka ekkadus.
Izis Maaramo geetettiza issi michchiya daysu. Maaramakka izappe qaala siyashe Goda toho garsan uttadus.
Shin martay ootho daroppe dendidaysani daaburada Yesussako shiiqqada “Godo ta michchiya ootho ubbaa ta bolla agadda utishin neni co7u gaz? Iza tana maaddana mala izis yoota attin” gadus.
Gido attin Goday hizgidi izis zaarides “Martanne Martanne neni daro yoho gish qofa darassa, dirbatasa tugatassa.
Koshizay gidikko issi miish xalla, Maaramaka lo7o exa dooradus, hessikka izippe ekettenna.”
Issi gallas Yesussay issi son woossides, woossa wursishin iza kaallizaytappe issay Godo xamaqiza Yanisay bena kaallizayta woossa tamaarsidaysatho nekka nuna woossa tamaarsa gides.
Izikka istas woosishe hizgidi woosite nu aawo ne sunthi anjjetto ne kawotethi haayo.
Hachsi gidiza quma nuus imma.
Nuna qohidayta nu maariza mala nuna maara paacenkka nuna gelthofa
Qassekka hiz gides “intefe issi uras laggey diikko giidi giddoth he laggezaso biiddi taas issi imathi ogeppe yin muzana kath bayndda gish heezzu buddennay diikko taas tal7arikii?” gides.
<range>
Laggezikka zaaridi tana waysoppa, kareyykka gordettides, tanikka naytara zin7akichadis ha7i denddada immanas danda7ikke gaandee?
Taka intes yootays laggetetha gish dendidi immonta agikkokka izi oychchon salethida gish denddidi koyizaysa wursi immides.
Hessa gish tani intes gizay woosite intes imistana, koyite inte demmna, kare qoxxite intes doyettana.
Ays giiko woosizay wuri ekkana, koyizayka demmna kare qoxxizadeska doyettana.
Intefe aawa gidi uttidi izi yelida nay mole oychchiko shooshu immizay daandee?
Woyko phuuphuule oychchiko masmaso immizay daandee?
Inte iitata gidishe inte naytas lo7o imota imo erikko salon diza inte aaway bena woosizaytaas Xillo Ayaanaan wosit darisi immennee?
Issi gallas Yesussay haasa7isonta mume dayiddanth kessides. dayiddanthazikka kezidappe guye duuna mume addezzi haasa7ides, beydda asatikka darsi malalettida.
Gido attin issi issi asati bi7eela zebula geetettiza dayiddanthata halaqan dayiddanthata kesses gida.
Issi issi asay iza paacanaas saloppe malaata bessa gidi oychchida.
Gido attin Yesussay ista qofa eridi hiz gides “ba garsan shaaketiza kawotethi wuri dhayanan, ba giddon sigay bayndda keethikka kundanna.
Inte tana bi7eel zubula dayiddanthata kesses giidi haasi7ista shin xalla7eykka ba giddon issay issafe shaaketikko iza kawotethi waani minnannee?
Histtikko tani dayiddanthata bi7eel zubula kessiko inte nayti oonani kesaneeshaa? Hessa gish inte nayti inte bolla firdizayta gidana.
Gido attin tani dayiddanthata kessizay Xoossa wolqan gakkides Xoossa kawotethay inteko matidaro erite.
Mino uray lo7ethi gixettidi ba keeth naagikko keeththan diza miishshi lo7oon naagetes.
Gido attin izappe hara mino uray yiidi xoonikko izi amanettidda ola massara wothi ekkidi izas diza haarozakka wursi haras gishanna.
Tanara gidontay tanara eqettes, tanarakka shiishshonta uray laalles,
Tuna ayaanaay asappe kezida wode shemppo koyishe haathi bayndda mela son wayetesi, shempo soy dhaykko tani kase kezidaso guye simana gees.
Izappe simmidi yishin kase izi aggi bida keethay pitettidinne giigi utidaysa demmes.
Hessafe simmidi biiddi izappe iitiza hara laappun dayiddanthata benara ekkidi yes, istikka gelidi heen dana, he uraskka koyroysafe guyyeys keehi iita gidana.”
Yesussay hessa haasa7iza wode asa giddofe issi maccash dizara ba qaala dhoqqu oothada nena tookkida qanthinne ne dhammida dhanthati anjjettidayta gadus.
Gido attin izi anjjettidayti Xoossa qaala siiyidi azazettizayta gides.
Daro derey Yesussako shiiqida wode Yesussay hizgides “haysi ha yellistay iita yellista, gita malaata beyana koyees. Gido attin Yoonassa malaatappe hara dumma malaatay imetenna.
Gaassoyka Yoonassay Nanawe asas malaata gidida mala asa nay tani ha yellistaas malaata gidana.
Duge baga dere macca kawoya Solomone erateth beyanas biitta gaxappe denddada yida gish pirda wode iza ha yellistara denddada pirdana heko Solomoneppe aadhdhizaddey han dees.
Yoonassay sabbakishin siiyidi Nanawe asay ba naggarappe maaretethan gelida gish ha yellistara issife dendidi pirdana.
Xomppe oythidi kareppe geliza asas poo7ana mala qoncceson wothetes attin geemason wothiza asi deenna.
Ne asatetha poo7oy ne ayfe ne ayfey paxa gidiko ne kumetha asatethay poo7o gidana ne ayfey sakettikko ne kumetha asatethay dhuma gidana.
Hessa gish nenan diza poo7oy dhumonta mala naageista.
Histikko ne asatethay poo7o gidikko dhumida asatethi deenna agikko ne kumetha asatethay xomppe lo7ethi po7iza mala lo7i beettanna.
Yesussay haasa7a wursida mala issi parsawey benara quma maanaas Yesussa xeygides.
Yesussay quma maana kushe mecetonta agiddayssa beyidi malalettida.
Goday izas hizgides ha7i inte parsaweti xu7asinne keres bollabbagga meeci geeshista inte garssa bagaz uuzetethaninne iitatethan kumides.
Inteno eeyato kare baga medhdhiday garssa baga medhibeynee?
Yohon gidiko giddon dizaysa muxaata immite he wode wurikka intes geesh gidana.
Inteno Farsaweto intes ayye anugappenne xalotappe qassekka dumma dumma kaththafe tamappe isino kessista. Gido attin tuma firdane Xoossa dosanaysa aggi aadhdheetta. Yohon gidiko inte aggi aadhdhannas beesena. Hankoysa aggonta inte oothanna bessizayttikka haayta.
Inteno Farsaweto intes ayye mukuraben uttana boncho oydde koyyista giya giddonka asay inte sinthan hokana mala doseista.
Asi eronta iza bollara biza qoteti diza duufo inte milatiza gish intena ayye.
Muse woga erizaytappe issay zaaridi tamarisizayso ne hessaththo haasa7iza wode nunaka cayaassa gides.
Yesussaykka zaaridi inteno Muse woga erizayto inteskka ayye asi tookanaas dandda7onta deexo toho asa toosista inte gidikko intes biradhdhe xeeranika bochchekkista.
Inte aawati wodhida nabeta duufo inte lo7ethiza gish intes ayye.
Histtikko inte inte aawata ootho minnithiza markata istinabista wodhida intekka ista duufo lo7etheista.
Hessa gish Xoossa erateth hizgadus nabetanne hawarista ta istas yeddana isttikka istafe issa issa wodhana haratakka gooddanna.
Hessa gish ha yellistay biittay medhetosooppe ha7i gakkanaas gukida nabeta wurso suutha gish oychistana.
Aabelle suuthafe oykkidi yarshiza sooppene Xoossa keeththa giddon gukida Zakarasa suutha gakkanaas koyetes Ee ta intes gizay ha yellistay hayssas oychchistana.
Inteno woga erizayto intena ayye eratetha qulfe wolqara wothi ekkidi inteskka gelibeykista gelanaytaka digeista.
Yesussay heeppe kezidappe guye Xafetinne Farsaweti eqettishe oychchan shemppo diggida.
Iza duunappe keziza qaalan iza qaxi oykkanas naagettida.
He wode daro derey ba giddon issay issara yedhistana gakanas shiiqi uttidashe Yesussay bena kaallizayta “Farsawista irshofe naagettite, hessikka lo7o qoodheppe qommo hano” gides.
Qoncconta kamettidi attizaynne erettonta qotan attannay baa.
Hessa gish inte geeman haasa7idazi wuri qoncce kezena, qassekka inte qol7an haythan sasukketi haasa7idazi wuri dere sinthan yootettana.
Ta laggeto ta intes gizay asho xalla wodhanappe attin hara aykkokka oothanas dandda7ontaytas babbofite.
Gido attin inte babbaanas bessizay oonakkoone ta intes bessana asho wodhidape guye ashonne shemponne issife gathi gaanname taman yegganas danda7izaysa babitte. Ee izas babbite gays.
Gaashe kafo ichachchati nam77u santes bayzettettees, gido attin istafe issiniyokka Xoossi dogenna.
Inte hu7e ithikey kumeth taybboon dees. hessa gish babbofite, daro gaashe kafotappe inte aadhdhista.
T intes yooays “ta gish asa sinthan markatiza asa wursos asa nay qassekka Xoossa kiitancha sinthan iza gish markkttana.
Gido attin asa sinthan tana kadida uray Xoossa kiitancha sinthan izi kaddistana.
Asa na bolla kawisha qaala haasa7iza uras naggaray wuri maaristana shin xillo ayanan cayiza uray maaretenna.
Asay intena oykkidi dere haarizaytakkonne Godatizaytako mukurabe oykki efikko ay zarino ay giino gidi hirgofite.
Ays giiko inte haasa7ana koshizaysa xillo ayaanaay he wode intena tamaarsana.”
Daro asa garsafe issi uray “tamaarisizayso ta ishay nu aawa lata miishshafe tana gakkizaysa taas immana mala izas yoota” gides.
Yesussaykka “hayso tana inte bolla pirdiza daanna oothiday oonee?” gides.
Qassekka istas “asas daro miish deyikkokka shemppoy he duretethan deyonta gish naagetite, yiiqqetethafe intena keehi naagite” gides.
Zarethidikka qasse istas leemuso hiz gidi yottidees “lo7ethi kath immiza gade Goda gidida issi dure asi dees.
He addezzika ba wozinan <ta kaththa shishshada wothizassoy bayndda gish ay oothoo?> gidi qoppides.
Addezzika <taas diza gootarata lalada hara aakkizaaz keexada kaththanne taas dizaz ubbaa izan shishshanna.
Ta shempiyokka ta shemppoye daro wodes gidiza kath shiishshida gish shemppa uttada ma, uya ufa7ista> gaana gides.
Gido attin <Xoossi haysso eeyazo ne shemppiyo hach omars neppe ekkana koyetes, hessa gish ne nees shiishshidays oonas gidanee?> gides.
Hessa gish Xoossa achchan dure gidonta bees miishshe shiishshiza asa wursethikka hessa mala.”
Hessafe guye Yesussay bena kaallizaytas “intes ta yootays inte duusas ay maanakkonne, woykko inte bollas ay mayanaakkonne daro qoppofite.
Ays giiko shemppoy kaththafe asatethi qasse mayoppe aadhdhees.
Quurota xellite zeretenna maaxetenna, kath shiishshiza gootaray istas baa shin Xoossi ista muzees. histtikko inte istafe keehi adhdheketii?
Gido attin intefe darsi qoppidi ba laytha bolla issi gallas gujjana dandda7izay oonee?
Histtikko guutha miish oothooy intes dandda7etontashshe ays hara miishshas keehi qoppetii?
Ciishshati waanidi diccizaakkonne ane xellite, waayyettenna, suqettenna gido attin ta intes yootays Solomoneykka giita asa shin istafe issineytho maybeynna.
Histtikko Xoossi hach beettiddi wonto taman wodhana maata hayssatho mayziza gidikko inteno amannoy paccidayto intena wosit aathi mayizanee?
Hessa gish ay minoo ay maynoo giidi inte wozinay darsi qoppofo.
Biitta bollan diza asi wuri hayssa koyees, gido attin hayssi wuri intes koshizayyssa inte salo aaway eres.

qaqnthan gixxidi giigetite, inte poo7oykka poo77o,

he ura Goday izi qopponta gallassan yaana giidi sidhonta saatten yana. yiidikka iza qanxerethidi iza exa amanonttaytara issife oothanna.

Gido attin eronta dishe shochas bessiza mooro oothida ashshkaray guuthara shocistana. Daro imetida asa wursofe daroy koyetes, daro haddara ekkida urappe daroy koyetes.
Tani yiday biitta bollan tama eethanassa. He tamay ha7i eexxi kezidakko tana daro ufaysanashin.
Gido attin tani xamaqistana xinqatay dees, he xinqatay polistanashe tani keeha metotettadis.
Intes tani biitta bolla saro ehanna yida milatizee? Gideenna, ta intes yootays tani yiday issa issafe shaakanassa.
Haysafe sinthan issi keeththan ba giddon shaakettida ichachu asati daana. Nam77ati heezata bolla heezati nam77ata bolla denddidi ba garssan shaakistanna.
Aaway ba attumma na bolla, attumma naykka ba aawa bolla, aaya ba macca nay bolla maca nayakka ba aayeyi bolla, bolota ba na machchey bolla, na machaka ba boloti bolla denddidi ba garsan shaakistana.
Qassekka derezas “inte awa arshey mokiza bagara shaaray kezishin beyidi elleraka iray yana gees geista inte gida malaka hanes.
Duge baggara pude carkishshin gallassay ho7o gidana geista, inte gida malaka hanes.
Inteno lo7o milatiza iitato saloysanne sa7a medha beyidi hananayisa ereista shin histini ha wodeza eroy intena waani xoonizee?
Histikko inte ays tuma firdeketii?
Ne morkera daana sinthan eqqana bishin buro oge bollan dashe izara giigana oge maqqa, ne histonta agikko nena gochchidi daana sinth efana, daannaykka nena aathiddi halaqas immana, halaqaykka nena woynen yeggana.
Ta nees yootays daannay firdida wursetha santime qanxa wursana gakanas heepe kezaka.”
He wode Philaxoossay ista suuthi ista yarshora gathi walakida Galila asata gish Yesussas yoottida asati heen iza ollan deetes.

Gideena ta intes yootays inte maaretonta ixxikko inte wurikka he asata mala dhayana.

Qassekka Xoossa kawotethi aazara leemusoo?
Issi maccash munuqa caallisanas daro dhiillera walakkida guutha irsho malaataysu gides.

issi uray izakko shiiqidi “Godo firdappe guutha asati xalla atannee?” giidi oychchides. Izikka zaaridi xuntha pengeyra gelanaas baxxettite, daroti gelanaas koyetes shin istas hanena.

Intena nam77antaka xeysidaddey yiidi ne utidasoza hayssaddes yeda gaana, nenika yelatashe ziqaso banddassa.
Gido attin xeysetida wode ziqaso xellada utta, nena xegidaddey yiidi ta lagge haaya dhoqason utta gaandes, nenika he wode nenara maaddan utida asa wurso sinthan bonchetana.
Ays giiko bena dhoqqu histizaddey wuri ziq gaana bena ziq histizaddey wuri dhoqqu gaana.
Yesussaykka xeygidaddeza hiz gides quma woykko ka7o muzanas xeysiko neysatho nena xeysidi muzonta mala ne laggeta woykko ne ishata, ne dabota, woykko durista woykko dure guttata xegopa
Gido attin asa xeysada muzana koyko manqota, kushey toy bayndda wobistane qooqeta xeysa neni anjetana.
Xeysetidayti kushe zaranaas danda7onta gish xillota dentha wode nees kushey zaretana.
Maaddan Yesussara issife utidaytape issay hayssa siyidi Xoossa kawotethan shiiqidi maaddafe miza uray anjetidadde gides.

Yesussaykka istas leemuso hiz gi yoottides
“Inte giddofe issi uras xeetu dorssi diikko he xeetu dorssatape issina dhaykko atidda uddufun tammanne uddufunata denbban yeggidi dhayidayssa demmna gakanas koyana bonttay oonee?
Demmida wode ufaysara hashen tookki ekkidi
beso simmes, ba laggetanne guta asata issi bolla xeeyggidi <dhayida ta dorssiyo demmadis tanara issife ufa7etite> gandes.
Ta intes yootays <hessathokka maaroteth koshonta uddufun tammanne uddufun xillotappe maaretethan geliza issi nagaranchan salon ufayssa gidana.” >
Woyko issi tamu bira santimey diza maccashiya he tamappe issiniyadhaykko xomppe oythada demmna gakanas keeththa gars pitada lo7etha koyonta maccash oonee?
Izakka demmida wode ba laggetanne ba gutata issife xeeyggada “tappe dhayida bira santimeyo demmida gish tanara issife ufa7etite” gandus.
Ta intes yootays “hessathokka maarotan geliza issi nagarancha uran Xoossa kiitanchata achchan ufays gidana”
Qassekka Yesussay asatas hizgides “issi uras nam77u nayti deetes.
Istappekka kaalo naazi ba aawa <aabo! nees diza miishshafe ta gish taas imma> gides. Aawaykka bees diza miishsha ba naytas gishides.”
Daro wode gam7onta dishe kaalo naazi ba miishsha wursi shiishshi ekkidi haho biitta biddes. Heenka bees diza miishsha go7ay bayndda coo mela dhaysides.
Izikka bees dizaysa wursi wursidappe guyyen he biittan iita koshay denddini daro waaydes.
Hessa gish he dereni diza asappe issaadekko shiiqidees. He uraykka ba guddunth heemana mala gudduntha heemizasso yeddides.
Naazikka guddunthati miza harqqo maanaas amottides, shin hessakka immizaddey baa.
Gido attin iza wozinay simmida wode “ta aawa ashkkaratappe aappunappe kath tirpize shin tani hayssan gafan hayqqana matadinaa?
Denddada ta aawa so baada <aabo! salon Xoossa: biittan nena ta qohadis.”>
Haysappe guye “ta nena geetistada xeeyggistanas taas beesena: ne ashkkaratappe issa mala tana taybba” gides.
Hessa gish dendidi ba aawakko biddes. gido attin buroo izi hahora yishin aaway beyidi michchettidinne izakko woxxi biiddi idimi oykkidi yerides.
Naazikka “aabo salon Xoossa, biittan nena ta qohadis, hayssafe guyyen ta ne na geetistada xeeyggistanas taas beesena” gides.
Gido attin aaway ashkkaratas eesottidi wursofe doorettida mayo ehidi mayzite iza biradhdhen yiichi, iza tohonkka caamma aathite.
Modhdho mirgo ehidi shukkite, miidi ufa7etos.
Haysi ta nay hayqqides shin paxides dhaydes shin beettides gides, hessafe guyyen ufa7eteth oykkida.
Haysi hanniza wode bayra naazi goshsha son dees, heepekka simmidi so matida wode diitha durus siyides.
Izika ashkkaratappe issa xeeyggidi “hessi aazzee?” gi oychchides.
Ashkaarazikka “ne ishay yides, izi saronne lo7ooni simmida gish ne aaway handadho mirgo shukides” gides.
Bayra ishazikka hanqqettidi so gelanaskka koybeynna. Aawaykka kare kezidi izi so gelana mala woosides.
Gido attin izikka zaaridi aawas “hekko tani hayssa gakanas nees aylle mala oothadis, azazoppe isinokka pacisabeyke, gido attin ne ta laggetara ufa7istana mala issi deyshsha laaqqakka imabeyka,
Gido attin haysi ne naazi nees dizaysa wursi laymatizaytara wursidi yishin handadho mirgo izas shukkadasa” gides
Awaykka “ta nazo ne wurso wode tanara daassa, taas gididay wurikka neessa.
Haysi ne ishay hayqqides shin paxides dhaydes shin beettides, hessa gish nuni ufa7istanas besses” gides.
Yesussay bena kaallizaytas hiz gides “issi dure adde daysas iza keeththa ayssiza issi assi dees, izi he dure addezza miishsha ogey bayndda lalizayssa worey ha dure addezza haythan wodhides.
Dure addezzi uraa xeeygidi <hayso ta siyizaysi aazzee? Haysafe doomada ne ta keethas ayssizadde gidanas dandda7ontagish ne alafetetha garsan diza miishsha oykkida mazgaba zaara>” gides.
Keetha ayssizaddezzi ba wozinara ta Goday tana ta alafetethafe goodana gees goya maanas taas wolqay baa, woossanas yeelatays, hessa gididagish ay ootho gides.
Tani alafetethafe kezikko asay tana mokki ekkana mala oothanna oge ta erays.
Hessa gish iza Goda acoy ista bolla diza asata issi issi ura xeeygides. Koyro yidaysa ne bolla Goda acoy aapunee? gides.
Issi xeetu xaaro kumetha zayitey ta bolla dees gides. Alafezi zaaridi kase ne faramida woraqqata hey ekka uttada elle ichachu tamu xaaro gaada xaafa gides.
Kaalidi hankkoysa nech ne bolla aappun dizee? gides. Ichachu tamu il7o gisttey dees gides. Alafezi zaaridi kase ne tal7ashe faramida waraqqata hey oyddu tamu il7o gaada xaafa gides.
Godazikka shocechiza alafezi oothida cincatetha gish nashides. Ha alame nayti bena milatizaytara diza gaagotethan poo7o naytappe aadhdhidi cincca.
Hessa gish tani intena gizay ha biitta miishshay wurida wode medhina keeththan inte ekettana mala ha7i intes diza miishshaara intes lagge medhdhite gays gides.
Guutha miishshan amanetizza uray daro miishshan amanettanna, guutha miishshan amanettonttaddey daro miishshan amanettenna.
Histikko inte ha biitta miishshan amanettenna ixxikko tuma miishsha hadara oykkite giidi ooni intes immanee?
Asa miishshan inte amanettontta ixxikko intes buzu7a gidana miish ooni immanee?
Nam77u Godas issi to issi bolla azazettana dandda7iza uray oonikka deenna woy issa dosidi issa ixxees woykko issakko shiiqidi hankkoysa leqqes. Xoossasine miishasinne haaristanas dandda7ekkista.
Miishsha darisi siiqiza Farsaweti hessa wursi siyidi Yesussa qidhida.
Yesussaykka istas inte intena asa achchan xilisista gido attin Xoossi inte wozina erees. Asa achchan bonchettidda uray Xoossa sinthan tuna giidi istas yoottides.
Muse wogayne nabeti Yanisay yaana gakanas haasa7ishe gam77ida. Hessa kaallidi qasse Xoossa kawotethas miishrachchoy sabbakketides, asi wurikka hee gelanaas wadhetes.
Gido attin Muse wogappe issi qeerina kundda atanaysafe saloynne biittaynne aadhanaysi kawisha gidana.
Be machcho anjji yedidi hara machcho ekkiza assi wurikka laymates ba addefe anjetta bidaro ekkidayskka laymatees.
Qassekka Yesussay istas lo7o mayo mayidi gallas gallas lo7o duussa ufayssan diza issi dure assi dees gides.
He addezza pengeni kumetha bollay madunth xalla gidida issi Alaazaaree geetettiza manqo adde dizaysi zin7idi dees.
Izikka he dure addezza keeththan asay kath miishni maaddafe hugen wodhiza duuxxeth maxi maanaas amotees. Kanatikka iza maduntha laacetees.
Ha manqo addezzikka hayqqin salo kiitanchati Abrame ki7o ekki bida dure addezzikka hayqqidi moogetides.
Si77olen wayetishe dhoqqu giidi haahon Abrame xellides, Alaazaareekka ba ki77n oykk dishin be7ides.
Dre addezzi aawa Abrame hayssan wayetiza taas michcharki Alaazaarey ba biradhdhe xeera irxx haathan bochchidi ta inxxrs irxisana mala yedarki giii wassides.
Gdo attin Abramey ta nazo neni biitta bolla dashe lo7o duus deyida mala Alaazaarey kase waye beydyss ne qopp gido attin ha7i izi ufa7etishn neni waaistassa gides.
Hessi wuri hanshin haan diza assi haappe hee intekko aadhdhontta mala qassekka intekkon dizay haa nukko aadhdhana koyiza uray haa aadhdhontta mala intesine nuus giddon gita aafoy giiggetides gides.
Dure addezzi qasse aabo hessi hessagidikko neni Alaazaare duge ta aawasso yedanamala nena woossays, taas ichachu ishati deetes, hayti hayssa waayeso yontamala biidi istas lo7ethi yootana mala Alaazaare yedarkki gides.
<range>
Abramey izas zaaridi Museynne nabeti heen ista achchan diza gish istafe siyeto gides.
Izika zaaridi aawa Abrame hessamala gidenna hayqqida asappe issi uray hayqoppe dendi biikko isti Xoossa maaretethan gelana gides.
Abrameykka zaaridi Museynne nabeti gizayssa siyonta ixxikko hayqqida asappe issi uray dendidakkokka isti amanettenna gides.
Yesussay bena kaallizayta hizgides “asa dhuphidi nagaran yeggiza miish yoontta aggenna, gido attin yaana dhuphezas gaaso gidizaddes ayye!
He uray ha guuthatappe issas dhuphe gidanappe woxa shuchi iza qoodhen qachetin abba gido izi yeggetizakko izas lo7o gidana.
Hessa gish inte hu7es naagetitte. Ne ishay nena qohikko hanqqista, izi ba mooro eridi simmikko maara.
Issi gallassan laappun to zaari zaari qohidi laappun toka zari zari maara giiko maara.
Hawaretikka Godo nuus amano gujja gida.
Godaykka gaashe ayfe lagge amanoy intes diikko hayssa etha dhoqqalista baada abban gela tokkista inte giikko izi intes azazettana” gides.
Qassekka Yesussay hizgides “inte giddofe issi asas goshshanchay woykko dorss heemiza ashkkaray diikko, izi goyidi simmiishni taas maana ka7o giigissa, ta maadda uyana gakanas gixistada taas ootha hessafe guye baggan maasa uyasa gees attin ha7i quma maana aadhdha gizee?
<range>
Histtikko he ashkkara Goday izi iza azazo polida gish iza galati erizee?
Hessa gish intenikka inte azazettidayssa wursi polida wode, nuni go7ay bayndda oothanchata nuus oothanas bessizaysa poli oothidos gite.”
Hessafe guye Yesussay Yerusaleme bishe Samaryarane Galila achchara aadhdhidees.
Issi mannidara gelida wode inchiracha hargiza tamu asati iza demmida. Istika haahon eqqidi
ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi “Yesussa! Godo! nuus michchistarkki” gida.
Izika ista beydda wode “biite intena qeesetas beesitte” gides. istikka buro bishe oge bolla paxida.
Istappe issay ba paxidayssa beyidi ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi Xoossa bonchishe simmides.
Izika Yesussa toho bolla kunddidi galattides, izikka Samariya biitta asa.
Yesussaykka addeza “paxidayti tamu assi detenne histini uddufunati awa bidoo?” giidi oychchides.
Haysa dumma dere asappe attin Xoossa galatizay baawa gusee?
Addezakka zaaridi denddada ba nena ne amanoy pathides gides.
Xoossa kawotethi aydde yaanakko Farsaweti Yesussa oychchida wode Yesussay “Xoossa kawotethi beettiza malaatatan yuukku” giidi zaaridees.
Asay Xoossa kawotethi haan daysu woykko heen daysu gaanas daandda7etenna, Xoossa ka7otethi inte giddon daysu.
Bena kaallizaytaskka “asa na gallassatappe issi gallasyo beyanas inte amotana wodey yaana, gido attin inte beyekkista” gides.
Asay intes haan daysu woykko heen daysu gaana shin inte ista kaallidi booppitte.
Gaasoykka wolqanthi wolqamidi salo gaxappe salo gaxa gakanas po7isiza mala asa nay yiza gallas iza mala hanana.
Gido attin haysi wuri hananappe koyro asa nay daro meto ekkanasne hayssa ha yelletethan kadhistanas besses.
Nohe wode handaysa mala asa na wodenka hessaththo hanana.
Nohey markabben gelana gallas gakanas asay miishnine uyishin ekishine gelishin dhaysiza haathi yiidi wursika dhaysides.
Looxe wodekka iza mala handees, asay meesinne uyes bayzesinne shammees tookizaz tokees keethekka keexxetes.
Shin Looxey Soddomeppe kezida gallas shuch mithi qoronta tamay diinney saloppe bukkidi wursi dhaysides.
Asa nay qonciza gallas hessaththo hanana.
He wode ba keeththa bolla diza uray oonikka keeththa giddon diza miish ekkana giidi wodhoppo, hessathokka goshsha son diza asi guye simmofo.
Looxe machcho qoppite.
Be deyo gam7isana koyizay wuri dhaysana ba shemppo aathi immiza uray gam7isana.
Ta intes gays he wode omars nam77u assi issi hiixxan zin7ana, isoy ekettana isoy attanna.
Nam77u maccashati issife gaaccishin isiniya ekettana hankora attanna.
Nam77u assi issife goshsha son daana issay ekettana issay attanna.
Istika zaaridi Godo isti awa ekettanee? gida. izikka anhay diza son ankotti shiiqqana gides.
Bena kaallizayti azalontta wurso wode woossanas bessizaysa erisanas Yesussay ha leemusoza istas yoottides.
“Issi kataman Xoossine babbontta asenne bonchontta issi daannay dees.
He katamankka issi am77i maccash daysu, izakka ta balggarara taas moottoy diza gish firdarikki gashe izakko simeristadus.
Daannazikka daro wode gakanas izis firdibeynna, gido attin guyyeppe ba wozinan Xoossi babbontta assekka bonchontta agikko,
hanna am77e maccashiya tana wayssiza gish ta izis pirdana, hessa histonta agikko wurso wode simeristada tana daabbursana.” gides.
Godaykka hizgides “makkal7ancha daannay gidayssa siyite,
Xoossi gallassinne omars izakko wassiza doorettidaytas fiiddenneyee? Tana ay metide giidi ba maado gam7issandee?
Ta intes gays istas elle firdana, gido attin asa nay yiza wode biitta bolla amano demandeeshsha?”
Bena xillo asa mala qoodidi ceqettizaytasnne harata leqo ayfen xeelizaytas leemusora hizgides.
Nam77u asati woossanas maqddase bida, issay Farsawe hinkkoysi qaraxa shiishizadde.
Farsawezikka eqqidi ba gish hizgi woossides, Xoosso! tani hara asa mala bonqqizadde, makkal7izadde, laymatizadde harapekka hayssa qaraxa shiishshizadde mala gidonta aggida gish ta nena galatays.
Samintan nam77a xoomays, taas dizaysafe tamappe issa immays.
Gido attin qaraxa shiishshizaddezi haahon eqqidi pude salo dhoqqu giidi xeellanas koybeynna, gido attin ba tira icishe “Xoosso! tana nagaranchaza maara gides.”
Ta intes yootays Xoossa sinthan Farsawezi xillotethi demibeyna shin haysi qaraxizaysi xilidi ba so simmides. Bena dhoqqusizay wuri ziq gaana, bena ziqsizay gidikko dhoqqu gaana.
Yesussay bochcherethanna mala asay guutha nayta izakko ehides. Iza kaallizaytikka hessa beydda wode hanqettida.
Gido attin Yesussay guutha nayta beekko xeeygidi hiz gides “guutha nayti taakko yanayisa diggoppite, Xoossa kawotethi haytanta malaatasa.
Ta intes tumu gays, Xoossa kawotethi guutha na mala ekkontay wuri izin gelenna.”
Ayhuddista halaqqatappe issay kiya astaamarezo medhina deyo lattanas ay ootho giidi oychchides.
Yesussaykka hizgidi zarides, “aazas tana kiya gazii? Issi Xoossafe attin hara kiyay deenna.
Laymatoppa, wodhoppa, kaysotoppa, wordo markkattofa, ne aawanne ne boncha giza azazoza eraasa.
Addezzikka hayta gidikko guutha natetethafe doomada naagadis gides.
Yesussaykka hessa siyida wode histtikko nees issi miish paces, nees dizaz wursa bayizadda manqotas imma, salo mazgaban demandasa, izape guye yaada tana kaalla gides.
Gido attin addezzi hessa siyida wode daro haaroy izas diza gish keehi michetides.
Yesussaykka addezza xeellidi daro miishi diza asati Xoossa kawotethi gelanays aymala meto” gides.
Durey Xoossa kawotethi gelanaysafe gaammelay narppe lukkora gelanaysi matana.
Hessa siyida asay histin oonii attanna dandda7izee? gides.
Yesussaykka asa achchan dandda7etontay Xoossa achchan dandda7etees gides.
Phexirosaykka hekko nuni nuus dizaz wursi aggiddi nena kaallidos gides.
Yesussaykka istas ta intes tumu gays Xoossa kawotethas giidi ba keeth, ba machcho, ba ishanta woykko bena yeliddayta woykko ba nayta aggida uray
Ha7i wode daro diikko kushe ekkontaynne yiza wode qasse medhina deyo ekkontay oonikka deenna gides.
Yesussaykka bena kaalliza tammanne nam77anta dumma efidi ha7i nuni Yerusaleme kezana goos, nabeti asa na gish xaafidaysi wuri polistana.
Dere asas aathi immana, istikka iza qidhi ka77ananne waysana, iza bolla cuttana
garafana hessafekka zaaridi wodhana. Izikka heezzantho gallas hayqqoppe dendana gides.
Iza kaallizayti gidikko hessa wursofe isinoka eribeyttenna. Iza guussaykka istafe gemettides. Izi aaza gish hasa7idaakkonne eribeyttenna.
Yesussay Yarko gizaso matida wode issi qooqe addey oge duunan uttidi woossishe dees.
Qooqe addezzikka daro asay ogera aadhdhizaysa siyidi hessi aazzee? gi oychchides.
Isttikka izas Naazirete Yesussay hayssara aadhdhes giidi yootida.
Izikka Dawite na Yesussa taas qadhetta gi wassides.
Yesussappe sintheti bizaytti c7o7uga giidi hanqqettida. gido attin izi Dawite no taas qadhetta giidi darisi waassidees.
Yesussaykka eqqidi addezza izakko ehanna mala azaziddes, izikka izakko shiiqida wode
ta nees ay oothanna mala koyay giidi oychchides. Qooqezikka Godo xeellanaas koyays gides.
Yesussaykka nena ne amanoy pathides xeella gides.
Addezzikka heerakka xeellidees. Xoossakka bonchishshe Yesussa kaallidees. Hessa beydda derey wuri Xoossa galattides.
Yesussay Iyarko giza sora aadhdhi bishin
Zakosa geetettiza issi assi he Yesussay biza oge bolla dees. Izikka dere qaraxa qanxisizaytas halaqqanne keehi dure asa.
Izikka Yesussa geetettizaysi awayssakkonne beyanas koyishin qaantha asa gidida gishinne daro derey Yesussa kaalliza gish Yesussa beyanas dandd7ibeynna.
Yesussay he ogera aadhdhishin sinthe qaxidi oge bolla diza issi etha miththa bolla kezides.
Yesussay etha gars gakidi dhoqqu histi xeellidi Zakosa hach ta ne keeththan pe7anaas besses elella wodha gides.
Izikka elle wodhidi ufaysan mokki ekkidees.
He wode heen izara diza asay hessa beyidi nagarancha asa keeththan imatistana gees giidi wurikka garsara zuzumettida.
Gido attin Zakosay eqqidi Godo tani taas diza miishshe wursofe baga shaakkada manqqotas immana tani oonappekka wordora bonqqa ekkidaazzi diikko oyddu kushe gujjada izades immanna gides.
Yesussaykka ha uraykka Abrame na gidida gish hach ha keethas paxatethi yides gides.
Haysas gaassoykka asa nay haa yidaysi dhayidayssa koyanasinne ashanassa.
Asay hayssa siyishin leemusora haasa7a oykkides gaassoykka izi Yerusaleme gakkanaas matida gishine asatas Xoossa kawotethi qonccanna hanza milattida gishassa.
Hessa gish issi kawo nay ba kawotetha shuumeteth ekki yanas haaho biitta biddes.
Be ashkarata giddofe tammata xeeygidi tamu minnane istas immidi, ta simadda yaana gakanas hayssa miishshan zal7ite gides.
He dere asati qasse iza ixxida gish haysi addezzi nu bolla kawotana mala koyokko giidi iza geedora aathi yedida.
Gido attin ha kawo naazi kawo gididi guye ba dere simmides. Kase bishe tamu minnane immida tamu ashkkarati izi immida biran zal7idi woysa tirfisidakkonne eranas ista xeeygidees.
Istafe koyroy shiiqidi Godo ne taas immida tamu minnaney hara tamu yelides gides.
Godazikka iza ne amanettida ashkkara, lo7o oothadassa, ne guutha miishshan amanettida gish tamu katamata ne haarana mala nees immadis gides.
Nam77anthozika izakko shiiqqidi Godo ne taas immida minnaneppe hara ichachu minnaney wodhides gides.
Iza Godazi izas zaaridi neni aysana mala tamu katamati nees imettida gides.
Qassekka hara oothanchay shiiqqidi Godo neni wothontasoppe ekkizadde zerontasoppe maxizaddenne menxxe iita asa gidida gish ta nees babbada curqan xaaxxa wothida ne minnaneyo hey ekka gides.
<range>
Iza Godazi zaaridi izas hayso iita oothanchazo ta ne qaalan nena zaara pirdays. Tani wothontasoppe ekkizaddenne zerontasoppe maxxiiza menxe iita asa gididaysa erasashin tani ta miishsha yelora ekkana mala he miishshan oothanna asatas aazas immabeyki gides.
<range>
Iza Godazikka heen eqqida asata iza kusheppe minnaneza ekkidine tamu minnaney dizaysas immite gides.
Istika zaaridi Godo izas tamu minnaney deesko gida.
Izikka zaaridi diza uras wursos haray gujjistana, bayndda uras kase dizaysi izappe eketti gidanna gido attin tani ista bolla kawotonta mala koyidayta hayta ta morketa taakko haa ehidi ta sinthan shukkite gides.
<range>
Hessa haasa7i simmidi Yesussay Yerusaleme kezanas istafe sintheti biddes.
Dabre zayite geetettiza zuma bolla diza Beettefaggenne Bittaanya geetettiza katamatakko matida wode bena kaallizaytappe nam77anta kiittishe heen inte sinthan diza qeeri katama biitte biiddi katama inte gelishin oonikka toggi eronta issi qachcheti diza hare gutte inte demmna iza birshidi haa taas ekki yite, intena oonikka aazas birsheti giidi oychchikko Godas koshes gite gides.
<range>
<range>
kiitetidaytikka biidi izi istas yoottida mala hare gutteza demmida.
Isti gutteza birshin gutteza Godati beyidi aazas birshetti giidi oychchida.
Istika Godas koshshees gida.
Hare gutteza Yesussako ehidi ba mayo wurissi gutteza bolla yegidi Yesussa hare gutteza togisida.
Asay wurikka ba afala Yesussay biza oge bolla miccidees.
Dabre zayite zuma bollara dugeth wothiza ogezakko matida wode qooday bayndda derey ba beydda malaata gish wurikka ufaysara ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi Goda sunthan yiza kawoy anjjettidaysa, saroy salon bonchoy saloppe bolla salon gido gides.
<range>
Deretappe issi issi Farsaweti Yesussa tamaarsizayso ha nena kaalliza asay gizaysa gonta mala hanqqa gides.
Izikka istas zaaridi hayti co7u gidakkonne shuuchchatikka waassana gides.
Yesussay Yerusaleme matishe katama beyidi izis yekides. nees saro gidizaz hach ne eridakko aazze dizayishin ha7i ne ayfeppe qotettida gish ne morkketi heera haara nena giddoothidi kun7isana wodey yaana gides.
<range>
<range>
Nenanne ne gibbe garsan nenara diza ne nayta wurssi biittara walakkana. Shuuchcha bolla shuuchchikka aggettenna. Hessi wurikka Xoossi nena koyishin neni eronta aggida gishassa.
Hessafe kaallidi Yesussay maqddase gelidi maqddase giddon zal7izayta kessides.
Qassekka ta keethay woossa keeththa gidanna geetettidi xaafettidees, inteni gidiko pangazi diza gonggollo histiddista gides.
Wontin wontin maqddasen izi tamaarishin Xaafetinne dere halaqqati iza wodhanaas koyida.
Gido attin derey wurikka izara oykettidi izi tamarsizaysa kaalliza gish oothanaazi istas kirq gides.
Issi gallas Yesussay dere asa maqddasen tamaarsishinne miishrachcho qaala sabbakishin qeese halaqqati Xaafetine dere cimati shiiqqettidi izakko yida.
Haysa ne oothizay oona shenenee? Nees shene immiday oonee? giidi iza oychchida.
Izikka istas hizgides taka intena issi oychcho oychchays, ane taas zaarite.
Yanisa xinqatay saloppeeye asappee?
Istika ba garsan hizgidi issay issara zorettida “nu Yanisa xinqatay salope giikko nuna histini aazas amanibbeykkettii? gaana.
Asappe giiko asay wuri Yanisay nabe gididaysa amanizza gish nuna shuuchchara caddana.
Hessa gish izi awappekkonne nu erokko giidi zaarida.”
Yesussaykka histtikko taka aaza wolqan oothizakonne intes yotikke gides.
Qassekka Yesussay asas leemusora hizgidi yoottidees. Issi uray woyne mith tokides, biitta goyizaytas kira immidinne hara dere biiddi heen gam7ides.
Kaxxiza bone wode kaththafe ekki yaana mala ba ashkkaratappe issi ura gadezza goyida asatakko yediin gada goyizayti kiita bida ashkkara qoxxidi mela kushe yedida.
Kaalethidi hara ashkkara yedin goshshanchati ha7ikka oykki qoxxidinne kawishidi mela yedida.
Ha7ikka kaalethidi heezantho ashkkara yedin goshshanchati izakka qoxxethi madunthidi gede kare olida.
Woyne miththa Goday ha7i ay oothoo? Oone erizayta keeha siiqiza ta naaza yedidakko iza bonchandettoshshaa? gides.
Gido attin biitta goyizayti naza beyddamala ba garsan haysi iza laatana naaza gidennee? Haa yite iza wodhidi biitta laattos giidi zorettida.
Woyne miththa tookkida sooppe gede kare kessidi naaza wodhida. Histtikko ha7i woyne miththa Goday ha asata wostanee?
Yiidine he goshshanchata dhaysana woyne miththa tookkizassoza haratas immana. Dereykka hessa izi gidayssa siyidi hayssa malay hanoppo gides.
Yesussaykka istakko xeellidi “histini shuuchchan keeth keexiza asati leqqi aggida shuuchchay keethas waana hu7e gidees geetetidi Xaafettida leemusozas birshethay aazzee?” gides.

hayssa addezzi asa wurssi makkali7ana mala denthethes giidi inte taakko ehin ta qorin iza oythiza issi iita miish demabeykke gides.

Asay zeridi kaqqa kaqqa giidi wassides.
