Daro dereynne ba tira ici ici yekkiza maccati
Yesussappe guyyera iza kaalida. Yesussay istakko simmi xeellidi inte Yerusaleme maccasay intesne inte naytas yekkite attin taas yekofite gides.
Sinthefe inte hekko makkarattine yelonta ulotine nay dhammonta dhanthati anjettidayta gaana wodey sinthara yees.
He wode zumato nu bolla wodite qeeri zumatikka nuna qottite gaana.
Histini qaye miththa bolla hayssatho oothidayti mela miththa bolla wostaneshaa?
Izara issife hayqqana mala hara nam77u iita oothida asata izara efida.
Qaraniyo geetettiza so gathidi kaqqida. Iita oothidaytappe issa oshacha baggara issa hadirissa baggara kaqqida.
Yesussaykka aabo hayti ba oothizaysa eridi ooothonta gish istas atto ga gides. Istika iza mayoza saama yegidi ba garssan gishetti ekkida.
Hessi hanshin asay wuri eqqidi xeellidees, daannatikka “izi hara asa ashshides shin Xoossafe dorettida kirstossay iza gidikko ane ha7i bena asho” giidi qidhida.
Wotadaratikka shiiqidi woyneppe aggettidda caalla usha ushidi qidhida.
Neni Ayhudde kawo gidikki ane ha7i nena ashsha gida.
Iza hu7e bolla baggara masqale koca bolla “haysi Ayhuddista kawo” giza qaala xaafi qaaphida.
Iita oothidi kaqqetida asatappe issay cashsha qaala Yesussa bolla qoqqofides. “ne kirstossa gidikii? ane nenaka nunakka ashsha” gides.
Iita oothidaytappe issay nees bessiza firda ekkashe Xoossassi babbikkii?
Nuni nu oothida iita oothos bessizaysa ekkos haysi addezzi gidikko issi iita oothibeyna.
Yesussa ne kawotethara ne yiza wode tana qoppa gides.
Yesussaykka zaaridi ta nees tumu gays hach ne tanara gannaten daana gides.
Hessa wode gadey seeta gallas shin biiddi udufun saate gakanas wurso biitta bolla dhummidees.
Awa arshe poo7oy digettides. Maqddase maggarajaykka daajkketidi nam77u kezides.
Yesussaykka keehi wassidi aabo ta shemppo ne kushen immays gida mala shemppo kezides.
Xeetu wotadarata halaqqay hessa beyidi “haysi addezzi tumappe xillo asakoshin” giidi Xoossa galatides.
Hessa beyanas heen shiiqidi derey wuri he hanidaysa beyidi tira ici icidi simmida.
Gido attin Yesussa kase lo7ethi erizayti wuri qassekka Galilappera iza kaalliza maccashati hessa xellishe haakki eqqida.
Ayhuddista duulata asappe issay izikka Yosefo geetettiza issi daro keehanne xillo asa.
Izikka kase asay Yesussa bolla duulatishn he duulatan deenna. Izikka issi Armattiyaasa geetettiza Ayhuddista katama asa shin Xoossa kawotethi yanayisa naagishe gam7ides.
Izikka Philaaxoossakko biiddi Yesussa anha immana mala Philaxosa woossidees.

Yesussayka izo “baadane ne azzinna xega ekkada ya” gides.
Maaccashayakka zaradaa “tas azinnay deena” hizgiin Yesussay hizgidees “ <ne tas azzinay deena> guussay tumukko.”
Gasooykka kase nes iichachuu azznati detes, qasse ha7i nenara dizzayyssi ne azzina giddenaa, hessa gish ne tummu gaddasa.”
Maccashaya izas hizgadus “Goodo neni nabe gdisayssa ta ha7i erraddis.”
Kasse nu awwatti haayssa zumaa bolla gooynidaa. Innte qasse “Assaye gooynnanass besizzasay Yerrussallamekko geista.”
Yesussaykka izzis hizgides “hanne maaccashshaye Xoossa aawas haayysa zuma boolla woykko Yerrussallamen inte gooynnota wodey yanaysa amaana”
Intene inte eroonta Xoossas goyynetta. Nu gidikko asas atootethi Ayyhudeppe giddida gishsha nuni nu erriza Xoossas goyynos.
Gido atin tuumu goynnizzayti Xoossa aawas Ayyananinne tumatethan goynizza woddey buuro yaanna. Haray atoshshn haiikka yiddes. Xoossa aawaykka kooyzay heesa malla gooyniizaytta.
“Xossi ba hu7es a7yanna. Iza goynizayti aynaninne tumatethan gooynanass beesees.”
Macashayakka “Xossay tiyidade Kirstosay yanaassa ta errayys, izi yiidi haniizzaz wurrsi nuus yoottana” gaddus.
Yesussayka izis “hii neenara hssaizzay ta izzakko.” giddes.
Hessi haniishshin izza kallizzayta ba biddassoppe simmida. Yesussay Maaccashshara hassa7izaysa maallalletida. Giddo atiin “hane a77y kooyazi? wykko haniira a7zzas hassazz?” giiddi o77nikka oychchana.
Hessafe guuyye Mccashshaya otooza hen agagada geede kattama bada, asas.
“Ta oththidaz wurrssi tass yottdadey ha yiddi beeyte, oone erazzy yanna Xossay tiyida Kirstosay izakkonne!” gadus.
Assayka kattamape kezzidi Yessusako bides.
He wode Yesussa kalizzyti Yesussa “Asstamarre qumma ma” gdii wossida.
Izi qaas “inte eronttay ta mizza qummay tas dees.” gidees.
Hssa gsha iza kalizayti “aykko miza kathth asii izas ehideshsh” giidi ba grrssan hasaeetda.
“Yesussayka istas zaridi ta quumay tana kiitda ta aawa shene o7thone iza ootho polo” gides.
Inte qaas “kaththa mxxay gkkans buro o7yddu agnna a7tddes gista gideketi? Qaas ta gidikko intena <doqu giidi kaththay maxaa gakiidaysa xeelitee.> gays.
Maxxizadey ba damussa ekaana, medhianas gidizza ayfe shishana, hessagish zerizzadeynne maxizadeey isfe ufe7istana.
Hesa gsha isadey zerana hara uray maxxana getettiza lemusooy tuuma.
Ta intena inte daburontayssa maxnamalla yedadis. Harati oothon daburida gido attin inte ista dabursan go7etidista.”
Mcashaya “ta oothidazi wurrsi tas izi yootides” gada asas marrkatida malla katamape daroo Samariya asay izan amanides.
Hesagisha Samarriya asay Yesussako yidine istakoon gmaa7nmalla wosiida. Izikka nma7u gallas hen gamides.
Iza Qalla siydi daroo asay Iza amaanides.
Macashayokka “ha7i nu iza amanizzay ne yootida qalla gish xalla gidonta nuuka nu baggra izape siyyda gishane tumaappe izi derre ashshizade gididaysa erida gishasa” gida.
Yesusay Samariyan nm77u gallasa gam7idappe guye Galillaa bidess.
Izi ba baggra “nabey ba derren boonchistan” gi yootides.
Gido atn izi Gallila bin Gallia asay Iza loo7ethi mooki ekkides. Gasoykka pazziga Ba7ale boonchana Yerusalame bidason hen dishshin izi oothidaysa wurrsi deyyda gishshasa.
Hessafe guye yesussay hathe Wayyne cajje oothida Gllilla derre garrsan dzza Qanna getittza ktama namantho bidees. He wode Qifrnahomen izas nay sakettida isi kawo shuumey dees.
Izika Yesussay Yihudda dereppe gede Galilla yidayysa siydi Yesussako bidees. Yesussay dugge Qifrnahoome wodhanmallane daroo saketdii haykqqana gizza naaza pathanamalla Yesussa woossidees.
Yesussaka izas “inte gita malatatanne malallsizaaz beyoonta aykokka amanekkta” gidees.
Shumezikka zaridi “Godoo ta naazi hayyqoonta elela woodharkki?” gides.
Yesussaka iza “neni ne soo ba nazi paxideess.” gidess. Adezikka Yesussay izas yootida Qalla amaniidi soo smmi bides.
Izi soo bishshn iza ahskkarati izara ogen gagidi “ne nazi paxideskoo.” gidi izas yootida.
Shumezika nazi ay saten paxxidakoone issta zari oychchides. isstikka izazs “qama gllasappe Lapuun Saten iza michchizayssi agides” gida.
Naza awaykka Yesussay “ne naazi paxidees” giday he issti izass yotizza woode gidaysa eriddess. Hessa gshsha he galassfe oykkdi izine iza so asay wuri Yesussa ammidda.
Hayssi malattay Yesussay Yihudappe Galila yiidi oothida nma77antho malata.
Hesafe kalidi Ayhudista Ba7lley dizza gish Yesussay Yerussallame bideess.
Yerusalamen doorsi gelizza pennge achchan iibrawista qalara Betesayda getettza issi pulltoofe shiqqida eloo hathey dees. Bollara kamay diza ichachu o7geti dettes.
Daro hargganchatti, ayyfe qooqeti, to woobetinne to silati ogge bolla zinniidi hathay qaxistana gakanas nagetees.
Isi isi woode Goda kiitanchay hathan woodhidi hatha qaththes. haththa qathafe kaldi koyrottdi hathan gelizza hargganchay bena sakiza ay hrggefekka paxes.
Hen gadaan heedzdzu tammane oosppun laythth kumeth sakketida isadeey dess.
Yessusay Adezza hen zin7idayssa beyddine izi daro laythth saketdayssa eridi “ne paxxana kooyaz?” gidess.
Hargganchazika zaridi “Godo haththay qaxxetiza woode tana hathan gelththiza assi dena, ta buroo bana gishshin harray tape kaseti hathan gelles.” gidess
Yesussayka Iza “dendda ne zin7ida algga tookada ba” gidess.
Adezzikka herakka paxxides. Be algga tooki ekidii bidess. Hessi hanidayy Ayhudista sambbata galassa.
Hesa gish Ayhudista hallaqat paxxida Adezza “hach Sambbattara ne algga tokkana mala Musse wogay azazena” gida.
Izikka Isttas “ne zini7ida algga tookkda ba gi yotides” gides.
Isttikka “nena algga tookkada ba giday oonne?” gi oychchida.
Deerey darida gishinne Yesussay hepee hakki bida gish iza oonni paththidakonne adezzi eribeyna.
Hesafe guye Yesussay Adeza Xoossa keeththan demmidi “hekoo ha7i ne paxadasa kaseysafe Adhizza iita miishi ne bolla gakontta mala nam77anththo nagara othofa” gides
Adezikka bidinne iza pathiday Yesussa gididaysa Ayhudista dannatas yotides.
Adezza sambbata gallas pathida gish Ayhudista dannat Yesussa oykkana yedi godida.
Yesussayka isstas “ta aaway wurso wode oothes, takka othana” gides
Hesa gason ayhudista dannat Yesussa wodhana malla kaseppe aththi denththethida, qase izi sammbatta morida gish xalla gidontta “Xoossi ta aawa” gida gishshinne bena Xoossara ginssida gishasa.
Yesussay isttsa hizgi zarrides “ta intes tummu gays aaway oothishin be7idaysa othoppe attin nazi ba shenen ayne otheena. Aaway othizaysa iza nay hessathoka oothes.
Gasoyka Aaway naaza doses ba othzaysakka wursi iza besees, inte malaletontta mala hayssafeka adhiza ootho buro bessana.
Aaway haqqidayta denththizaythone deyoo imizaysatho nazika hessathoo ba koydades deyoo immana.
Aaway oonna bollaka pirdeena gido attin pirda maata wuris ba nazas imiddes.
Izi hessaththo oththiday asay wuri aawa bonchana malane qaaseka nazaka bonchana malasa. Naza bonchonttay naza kitida aawakka boncheen.
Ta intes tumma gays ta qaalla siyzadeesine tana kitidaden amanizades medhina deyooy dees, izadeey hayqoope gede deyoon pinnidees atin iza bolla pirdetena.
Ta intes tummu gays kase hayqqida asat Xoossa na qaala siyza woodey yaana, he woodiyakka haano, siyzatii wuri deyoon deyaana.
Gasoykka aaway ba bagra deyooy diza mala nazikka ba baggara deyooy dana mala oothides
Izi asa na gidida gish pirdana mala Godatethth izas imiddes.
Haysan aykokka malaletoppite, Gasoykka buro kase hyqdii dufoon dizaayti wuri Iza qaala giireth siyizza woodey yana.
Lo7o oothdayt hayqqope denddid paxxna, Iita othidaayti gidikko hayqoope denddidi pirdistana.”
“Ta ta sheenen ayne oththanas danddaike, gido attin ta ta aawape siyda mala pirdays, tana kiitidaysa sheene oththaysi attin ta sheenen ta oththontta gish ta pirdan balay bawwa.
Tan ta gish tarkka markkatiko ta markkay tummu gidena.
Gido attin ta gish markkatizzadey haraay dees, izika ta gish markkatizzade, markkatethay tummu gididdaysa ta eraays.
Inteni Yanssako asse kitideistashin izika tummu markkatidees.
Ta hayssa gizay inte attana mala attin tas haara ass markkateth koshshida gish gideena.
Yanssay exidii pooizaa poo7 mala, intekka gutha wode iza poo7in uhaaththaaettana kooydista.
Tas gidikoo Yanssa markkatethape adhiza markkaay dees, ta markkayka ta aaway tas immida oothok, hesika ta oothiza othooy ta aaway tana kitidaysa tas markkates.
Tana kitida ta Aawayka ba huera tas markkatidees, inte gidiko iza qaala giireth mulekka siybeykkista, izas medhoka mulera beybeeykkista.
Izi kitidadden inte ammanontta gish iza qaalay inte achchan deyeena.
Intes geesha Maxxaafatape medhina deyoo demanas milatin maxaxafata piqqilista, maxxaafatikka ta gish markkatetes.
gido attin inte deyoo demaanas tako ha yana kooyekkista.
Ta asappe boncho kooykke.
ta intena errays, xoossa siqqoy intenan baynddaysa errays.
Tan ta aawa sunththan yadiis shin inte tana mooki ekiibeykeista hara uray qase ba sunththan yikoo inte iza mokii ekista.
Inte inte garssan isay isape boncho koyzzaytoo issi Xoossafe betizza boncho koyonttaytoo inte waanidi tana amaanana danddaeti,?
Ta aawa sinththan intena moottanay intes tana misatoopo intena moottanay inte iza uhaaththaaysi oothiza Musekko,
Museey ta gish xaafidaysa ammanidako inte tana ammanana.
Izi xaafidaysa inte ammanontta agikoo qase ta qaala inte woostti ammanane?”
Hesafe guye Yesussay xiibradoose geetettizaso gaalila abbafee he pinthth pinnidees.
Yesussay hargganchata paththida malata beydda gish daroo asay iza kaaliides.
Yesussay bena kaalizaytara pude zumma bolla kezii uttddes.
He woode Ayhudaata paziiga ba77eley matii utdees.
He woode daroo derey Izakoo yizayssa Yesussay dhoqu gi xeeliidi pilphphossa “hayssa deeras gidana quuma awapee shammana danddaiizoon?” gidess.
Yesussay Pilphphoossa hessathoo oychchiday iza paccanako, gido attin izi ba ooththanaysa erress.
pilphphossayka izas “issi issi urras issi bars gidza kath shamizakooka numm7u xeetu dinaren shaammida kathka hayssas gidena” gidees.
Yesussa kalizaytape isay siimoona Phxroossa isha Indryaassa,
“Ichchachu bangga ukethine namm7u mole oykkida issi nay hayssan dees, gidoo attin hana hayssa ha derezaas awa gakane?” gidees.
Yesussayka zardii “asa wuris utssite” gides, hen gadan daroo maatay diza gish asayka uttides, asa qoodayka ichchachu shi gidizaytako.
Hesafe guyee Yesussay uketha ekidi galata wossa wosidi uttdaa asas gishshides, molezaka hessathokaa gishshechides asay wurkka bes gidiza demiides.
Asay wurikka kaalli miin Yesussay bena kallizayta “maaddan attidaa kaththa isinooka ashoontta shishshite” gidees.
Isttika asay mishshin ichchachu ukethafe attida tammane namm7u leemate kumeth shishshida.
Asayka Yesussay ooththida malata beyydi “hayssaadey tummape ha allame yana nabezakko” gidess.
Asay qase wolqara Yesussa kawothana qopidaysa a erridi Yesussay qaseka isttafe haki bidi zumma bolla kezzdes.
Gadey qaammishshin Yesussa kalizayt duge abbakoo woodhida.
Wogolon geliddi qifiranaahone bana kezzda. istti kezshshn gadeey dhumiidees, Yesussay hessa gakanaskka isttakko yibeyyna.
wolqama carkkooy carkkiiza gish abbay keez qaaxides.
Iza kallzayt baga saate ogge mala wogoloza lagidape guyee Yesussay abba balara toora hamutti wogolozakoo mattishin demmidi baabbida.
Izika isttas “tankoo! baboopte!” gidees.
Isttika iza uhaaththaayysara gede wogoloza gi doo ekkana koyda, heraka wogolozika istt banaso gakides.
Abbafe he pinththan attida asay wonttetha gaalas abba bolla issi wogoloy xaala dizarro beyyda, Yesussa kalizayyt kase berkka bidayssane Yesussay isttara wogolon gelonttaaysa erridda.
Gido attin hankko wogolot xiibradoosepe denddidi Yesussay galata wosaa woosidi asa kaththa muzooso achchi yida.
Asayka Yesussay woykko iza kalizaytti hen baynddaysa beydii he wogolotan gelidi yesussa koshuu Qifranahomee bides.
Abbafe he pinththan iza demmidi “asttamare! ne aydee hayssa yadii” gidda.
Yesussayka isttas “ta intes tumma gayys inte tana koyzay kath mi kaallida gish attin malata be7ida gish gideena.
Dhayaana kaththas oosofite, gido attin hessafe athid xoossa aaway ammaanithza mattame iza bolla shoccida gish asa nay intes immiza medhina deyoos gidiza kaththas ooththite.”
isttika iza “histtin Xoossa ooso ooththanas nu azi ooththino?” gida.
Yesussayka “Xoossa oosoy Xoossi kiitida iza nazan ammano.” gidii isttas zaardes.
Isttika izas “nu beyddi nena ammanana mala ne nuna aaza malata beesane? qaseka azi ooththane? gides.
<Istti maana mala isttas qumma salope immides> geeteti xaafetida mala kase nu aawati baazoo bittan maan7e miida.”
Yesussay isttas. “ta intes tummu gays salope wodhida qumma intes imiiday musse giddena, tummu qumma salope intess immizaay ta aawakoo.
Gasooyka Xoossa qummay salope wodhidi allamees deyoo imiizaysako” gides.
Hesa gish asay “Godo hessa mala qumma nuss wuriso wode immarkkii” gides.
yesussayka isttas hizigidess “deyoo qummay tana, taakko yiza urray mulleka gafeetena, tana ammaaniizadeey aydeeka samotena.
kase ta intes gida mala inte tana beyddistashin ammanibeeykista.
Ta aaway tas immizaay wurkka taakko yana, takoo yizade ta gedee kaare goodike.
Gasoykka ta salope wodhiday tana kitidaysa sheene ooththanas attin ta sheene ooththanas gideena.
Tana kitidadeey sheene tas immidaytape issadeeka dhaysontta wurisetha gaalas ta denththana.
Ee ta sheeney naza beydii iza ammanizadeey wuri medhina deyoo demmanasiko, tanikka wuriseththa gaalas iza hayqqope denththana.”
Hesa gish Yesussay “salope wodhidda qummay tana” gidda gish ayhudat iza bolla zuzumeetida.
“hayisii Yoseefoo na Yesussa gideene? iza aawane iza aayoo nu errokoni? histtin hai izi <salope wodhadis> waani gizze?” gida.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgides “inte intee garrisaan gugummista.
Tana kittida ta aaway xeeygidape attin takoo yana danddaizadeey oonikka dena, berika takoo yana danddaizay oonikka dena, takoo yizadeka wurisetha gaalas ta iza hayqqope denithana.
Nabbista maaxxafatan asay wuri Xoossafe tammardade gidana geetet xaafeetidees, hessa gish aawape siyydi tammarda assi wuri takoo yana.
Hesa guus aawa beeyda assi dess guusu gidena. aawa beeyday Xoossa achchafe yidaysa xaala.
Ta intees tumma gays tanan ammanida asas medhina deyooy dees.
Tan deyoo qumma.
kasse inte aawat bazzo biittan man7e midda gido attin wurkka hayqqida.
Salope wodhida qummay hayssa, hayssa mizzadey mulleka hayqqena.
Salope wodhida deyoo qummay tana, hayssa ha qummape mizzadey wurkka medhinas dana, allames deyoo gidana mala ta immiza qummay ta ashshoko.”
Hesa wode Ayhuddat “haysi addeez nu iza ashsho mana mala woostt iimane?” gidi ba garssan palameetida.
Hessa gish Yesussay istta hizzigidees “ta intes tummu gays, asa na ashsho inte moontta aggikko iza suththika uyoontta aggikko intes deyooy deena.
Ta ashsho mizza urasine ta suththu uyzaa uraas wurisoos medhina deyooy dees, taka izzade wuriththetha gaalas hayqqope denththana.
Gasooyka ta ashshoy tummu qumma, ta suththayka tummu ushsha.
Ta ashsho mizzayne ta suththu uyzzay wuri tanan deeyana, takka izzaden deeyana.
Deyoo aaway tana kiitida malane takka izzan deyoon diza mala hessathoka ta ashsho mizzadey wuri tanan deyoon dana.
Hessa gish salope wodhida qummay hayssa, izika kase inte aawat midaaysa mala gidena, gasooykka he qumma midayt hayqqida, ha qumma mizayt gidikoo medhinas dana.”
Yesussay hayssa Qihaaththairanahomeen ayhudata woosa keeththan tammirisiza wode yotiddes.
Iza kaallizaytape darzzayt hessa siydii “haysi yoozi dexxoko hayssa oonni ekkane danddaize?” gida.
Yesussayka iza kaallizayt hessa yooza gish zuzumetidaysa ba wozinan erridi “<haysi intena dexxize?> gidees.
Assa nay Kirisitoossay ba dizzaso simm kezshshin beykoo inte ay gane?
Assas deyoo immizzay Xoossa ayanakoo, asa wolqay qaasse aynee go77ena, ta intes yootida qaalay deyoo immiza ayanakoo.
Gido attin inte garisan issi issi ammanoontta asat detes. Yesussay isttas hessa giday koyroope dommidi istta garisan ammanoonitayti oonanitakoone qaasse iza aththi immanadeeyka oonakoone erriza gishaskko.
Kallethidikka Yesussay aawa sheeney bayyndda takoo ha yana danddaizadeey dena gada ta intes yootiday hessassa.” gidees.
Hesafe denddidayssan iza kallizaytape daroot guyee simmida, he gaalasafe dommidi Yesussa kaalo aggida.
Hessa gish Yesussay bena kalliza tammane namm7ista “inteka bana kooyet?” gides.
Hessa wode Simoonna geetettiza phxxirossay “Godo ne medhina deyooy dishin nu oonakoo banee?
Ne geshsha Xoossa na gididdayysa erridi nun ammanidos” gidees.
Yesussayka istta “ta intena tammane namm7ista doorabeykina? histtin intefe isaay Xallaeko.” gidees.
Izi hessa giday Simoona na Asqqoroto Yuddaa gishasiko. ayysi gikko yudday tammane namm7istape iisa gididdakoka Yesussa athth immanay iza gididda gishshasiko.
Hesafe guye Yesussay galila garssan yuyettdees, gido attin Yuhudan yuyanas kooybeeyna, gasooykka Ayhudat iza wodhana kooyza gishshasiko.
He wode Ayhudata dase Ba77eley matti uttdes.
Hesa gish Yesussa ishshati izakoo shiqqidi hizzigida. “nena kallizayt ne ooththiza oosoza beyana mala ne heyssafe denddada Yuhuda dere ba.
Gasooykka qooccen erristana koyzadey ba ooso geeman oothena, neka heytantta wursa ooththashe nena allamen qoonccsana koshshes.”
Istt hessa gida gasooy iza ishshataka gidin izan ammanonttayta gidida gishshasiko.
Yesussayka isttas hizzigides. “ta wodey buroo gakiibeyna, inte wodey gidiko wuriso wode intes gigako.
Deerey intena ixxana danddaena, tana gidikoo ixxes, gasooyka ta allame oosoy iita gididdaysa izas markkattza gishshasiko.
Hai inte gede ba77elezaso bite, tass wodey gakontta gish hayssa ha Ba77elezaso bikke.”
Hesa gidii Yesussay Galilan attdess.
Gido attin iza ishshat Ba77elezaso bidappe guye Yesussay qonccera gidontta qotara ba77elezaso bidees.
Ayhudat iza “awan diize?” gishe Ba77elezason koydda.
Deereyka Iza gish garisara sasuqi hasaettdes. issi issi asat “izi loo7o asakoo” gishin bagay qase “loo7o gidena izi dere baleththes” gides.
Gido attin Ayhudata dannatas babiza gish oonnika iza gish qoonccen hasaibeyna.
Ba77elezii wurana baaga gakishin Yesussay xoossa keeth bidi tammariso oykkdees.
Ayhudat “haysii addezi tammarontta dishshe hayssa wursi woostti erride” gidi malaletidda.
Hessa gish Yesussay hizzgdes. “ta tammarithiza timmiritey tana kittda ta Aawape immetides attin tape gidenna.
Tana kittdaysa sheene ooththana koyzadeey dikko haysii ha timmiritey Xoossafe beetdaysa woykko ta tape hasaidaysa gidikkoka errana.
Bepe hasaizadeey ba boncho koyyes, kittidade boncho koyzadeey gidiko izi tummancha, wordooy iza bolla denna.
Mussey intes woga immidess gideene? gidikkoka inte garisan wog nagii poliidadey oonka deena, inte azass tana wodhana koyeti?”
Deereyka iza “ne bolla dayydanthth dees! ne wodhana kooyzay oonne?” gidees.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgi zarides “ta issi ooso ooththadiss inte wurikka hano ha oosoy malaleteista.
Musseey intes qaxxara woga immidees, he wogayyka immeetiday kase aawatape beetidees attin Mussepe gidena. histtin hekko intekka sambbatta gaalasiika asse qaxxarista.
Histtiko Musse wogay sharetontta mala assi smbbata gaalas qaxaretiysa gidiko histtin ta sambbata gaalas asas kummetha asateth paththiin azzas ta bolla hanqqetet?
Suurre pirda pirdite attin asa ayfeso xeelidi maadoo pirda pirdofite.”
Yerusalame asape issi issi asat hizzgda “istt woodhana koyza addezii hayssa gideene?”
heko izi qoonccen hasaees shin istt iza aykooka gibeytena, haysii xoossay kittidade giddidaysa dannat tummu eerizoshsha?
Histtin haysii addeezi awa asakone nu erroos, xoossay kitiddadey yishshin qaasse izi awapekone errizadey oonnika deena,
Hesa gish Yesussay xoossa keeththan tammarththishe ba qaala dhoqu histtdi “inte tana tummu errata, ta awape yidakone inte errata, gido attin tan ta sheenen yabeykke, tana kittdaysi izi tummancha, gidoshin inte qasse iza errekkista.
Ta gidikoo iza achchafe yida gishshine izi tana kittda gish ta iza errays” gidees.
Hesa woode iza oykanass koydaa, gido attin buroo wodey gakibeyna gish oonnika oykkbeyna.
Gido attin derezape darooy izan ammanides, asay hizgidees “xoossay kittiddadey yizza wode haysi addezi ooso malatape bollaara hara ootthhane?”
Assay Yesussa gish garssara sasuketi hasaishshin Parssawet siyda, hessa gish qeessista halaqatne parssawet yesussa oykkanas Xoossa keethth pengge naggizayta yediida.
He wode Yesussay “ta intenara guuththa wode dashshana, hessafe guye tana kittidaysako simma bana.
Inte tana koyana shin demekkista, inte ta dizzaso yanas danddaekeista.”
Hesa gish Ayhudata dannat ba garssan issay issara, “haysi addezii nu demmontta mala awa baneshsha? oonne errizzay Girikista giddo laleti diza Ayhuddatakoo bidi Girikista tammarisanesha?
Izi <inte tana koyana shin demekkista, ta dizasoo inte yanas danddaekista gishin hes ay gusee?>” gida.
Ba77eleeza wurithetha gita gaalas Yesussay dendidii eqqidne ba qaala dhoqu histtdii “hethth sammottda urray dikoo ha taakko yidi uuyoo.
Maxxafay gida mala tana ammanizadefe deyoo haththa pullitooy pullitana.” gidees.
Izi hessa gidaay izan ammanizayt buropee ekkana xiilo ayana gishshasiko, gasooyka yesussay boonchetza wodey buroo gakontta gish xiilo ayanay buroo qoonccoontta immetibeyna.
Hessa gish derezape issi issi asat he qaala siydii “yana giza nabey tummape hayssakoo” gida.
“Harati haysii xoossay kittiddadeko” gida. baggayyt qasse “xoossay kittiddadey Gliilape waan yane?
xoossay kittiddadey Dawitte zeereththape yeletanaysane dawitte katamma Bettelemepe yanaysii kase geshsha maxxafan xaafetibeyne?” gida.
Hessa gish iza gaason derey ba gidoon shaaketi wodhides.
Isttafe issi issi asat iza oykkana koyda, gido attin oonikka oykibbeyna.
Hessafe guye xoossa keeth naggizayt qeessata hallaqatakone Parisawettako simmid bida, izetika “aazas iza ekontta yidet?” gida.
Wootadaretika zaridi “ha addezi hasaizaysa mala ay assika hasai errena” gida.
parssaweti istta “intekka baletidet?” gida.
dannatape woykoo parssawistape iza ammanidayt dizosha?
Haysii mussee woga errontta derey tummape qanggetdaysa.
Haysafe kasse Yesussako bida Parssawistape isa gidida niqoodimoosay isttas
“Nu wogan issi mottetizadey ba mottos malththe immin siyonttane izi ay ooththidakone erretontta dishshin pirday pirdeet errize?” gides.
Isttika “neka galila asse? galilape nabey denddontaysa qoorerethada gakka erraa” gida.
hessafe guye isay isay beso bides.
Hesafe guye Yesussay debrrezaytte bidees.
Wontteththa gaalas malado wonttara xoossa keeth simmii yidess, dereyka wuri izakko yiin izi uttdii istta tammariso oykides.
Musse woga tammarisizaytine Parssawet issi laymatethan oyketda maccashsh dizaro eeki yidi dere sinththan eesida.
Yesussayka hizzgdes “Asttamare! heko hana maccashshaya laymatashe oykistadus.”
Hani mala maccashi shuchchan cadista hayqana mala mussey nu wogan nuna azazides, nech? hani gish ay gay?
Istt iza hessa giday iza bolla mottos gidiza gasoo demanasine iza paccana koyda gishshasa, gido attin Yesussay hokkdi biita bolla ba biradhera xaafoo oykdes.
Istt iza shir shir oychchin dhoqu gidi “inte giddofe nagaray bayndda urray koyro shuchchu izi bolla halo” gides.
hessafe qasseka hokidi biita bolla xaafides.
Isttika hessa siydii cmatape oykkdi wurkka isay isay bi kichchida, hessa gish Yesussay hen eqqida maccashshayra xaala attdes.
Hesafe Yesussay dhoqu gidi “hane maccashshaye nena mottizayt awan dizo? ne bolla pirdadey oonikka baye?” gides.
Izaka “Godo oonikka baawa.” gadus. Yesussayka “taka ne bolla pirdike, ba! Namm7enththo nagara oosofa.” gides.
qasse Yesussay “ta derey poo7o, tana kaallizadey wuri deyoo poo7o demmana, dhuman simerettena.” gidi isttas yootdes.
Parssawet “nenii ne gish markkatasa, ne markkaay tummu gideena” gida.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgi zaarides “ta ta gish ay markkatkoka ta awape ydakoone qasse ta awa banakoone ta erriza gish ta markkateth tummako, inte gidikko ta awape ydakoone qasse awa banakoone inte erreketta.
Inte ashsho qoofa mala pirdista, ta gidiiko oonna bollaka pirdike.
Ta pirdikkoka ta pirday tummu pirda, gasooyka ta tarkka pirdike, tana kittda ta aawayka tanara dess.
Namm7u asatta markkay tummu gididays inte wogan xaafetdes.
Hessa gish tan ta gish markkatays, tana kittda ta aawayka tasi markktes.”
Isttika “ne aaway awan dizee?” gidi iza oychchida, Yesussayka isttas “tana gidiin ta aawaka gidiin inte errekista, inte tana errizakoo ta aawaka errannakoshin” gidi isttas zardess.
Yesussay hessa isttas yootday Xoossa keethth gibben mishshe woththiza saxxine achchan tammarssishshe yootdes, shin izas oykeettza wodey gakontta gish oonnika iza oykiibeyna.
Yesussay qasseka “ta bana shin inte tana koyanane inte inte nagarara hayqana attin ta bizaso bana danddaekista” gides.
Ayhudatika ba garssan isay isara izi “<ta bizaso inte yana danddaekista> gizay berkka bena woodhanasesha?” geetetda.
Izi qasse istta hizzgdes “inte garssa asa, tan bolla asa, inte hayssa allamee asa, tani ha allamepe gidkke.
Inte ta oonnakone erridi ammanontta aggiko inte inte nagarara hayqqana gish ta inte! Inte nagarara hayqqana giday hessa gishshaskko.”
Isttika iza “ne oonne?” Gida, Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “hai gaakanas ta isttes iza gish yootzadey tanakko.
Ta inte bolla hasaizaysine pirdza yooy daroy dees, gido attin tana kittiddadey ammanetdade, taka izape siydaysa ha allamezas yootays.”
Izi isttas aawa gish yootzaysa akeki beytena.
Hesa gish yesussay “inte asa na dhoqu hisittd kaqqida wode he ta gidaddey tana gididaysa inte errana, aaway tana tammarssidaysa yootads attin tan ta sheene mala aykoka oosonttaysa inte akekana.
tana kittdayssi izi tanara dees, ay wodekka ta uhaaththaayzaz ooththiiza gish izi tana xaala yeegi aggibeyna” gidees.
Izi hessa yootda mala daroo asay izan ammanidees.
Yesussay bena ammanida ayhudata hizzgdes “inte tummu ta qaalan dikko inte tummupe tana kaallizayta gidana.
Tummay azakkone inte erranane tummayka intena geshshana.”
Isttika izas zaaridi “nuni Abbrame naytako, nu oonasiika aylleet erroko, histtiin ne nuna waanada inte wozistana gazi?” gida.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “ta intes tummu gays nagara ooththizadey wuri nagaras aylle.
Ay wodekka aylleey keeththan luxxe deeyena, yeloy gidkko aydeka keeththan deyes.
Histtko nazi intena wozikko inte wozettidayta gidana.
Inte Abbramee nayta gididdaysa ta errays, gido attin ta qaala inte erroo gi ekkoontta gish tana wodhanas koyista.
Tan ta aawa achchan be7idaysa ta intes yootays, inte qasse inte aawape siydaysa ooththista.”
Isttikka izas “nu aaway Abbrameeko” gidi zari yootin Yesussay isttas hizzgdes “inte Abbramee na giddiko Abbrameetho ooththana shin.
Ta Xoossafe siyda tumma intes yootin tana wodhanas qaachch denddidista, gido attin Abbrameey hessaththo ooththibeyna.
“Inte inte aawatho ooththista” isttika zaaridii “nu laymman yeeletida na gidoko, nu aaway issi Xoossa xaala” gidi izas zaarida.
Yesussay isttas hizzgdes “inte aaway Xoossa gididakoo taka Xoossafe keza yida gish inte tana dosanakko shin tana izi kittdes attin ta tarkka ta sheenen yabeykke.
Ta yootzaysa ays yuushi qoopeket? gasooyka inte ta qaala siyana koyontta gishshaskko.
Inteni inte aawa xalae nayta, inte aawa ammo polana koyista, izi kasseka shemppo wodhidadee, iza achchan tummay dena gish izi tumman eqiibeyna, izi ba huess wordanchane wordo aawa gidida gish izi wordo hasa7e beepe medhi ekkidi hasaees.
Ta qasse tummu hasaiza gish inte tana ammanekista.
Inte garssafe tana ne hano nagara ooththadasa gidi markkara laathanas moottana danddaizadey dizee? ta tummu hasaizade gidiko histtin aazas tana ammaneket?
Xoossafe gidida uuray Xoossi giza siyes, inte gidiko Xoossafe gidontta gish xoossa qaala siyekista.”
Ayhudatika zaaridi “nu nena ne Sammaryya asa, ne bolla daydanthth dees gooys tummu gideene?” gida.
Yesussay isttas hizzg zaarides. “tani ta aawa bonchays attin daydanththi ta bolla baawa, inte gidiko tana kawushshista.
Tan tas boncho koyke, ta bonchetena mala koyzadey qasse dees, izika pirda pirdanadeko.
Ta intes tummu gays, oonnika ta qaala naggikoo hayqqo muleka hayqqena.
Ayhudat iza hizzggda. “ne bolla daydanththii dizayysa hai nuni errdees, Abrrameyy hayqqdees, nabetika izatho hayqqda, ne qasse ooniko muleka hayqqoo beeyena ga yootassa.
Ne nu aawa Abrramepe adhaz? izi hayqqdees, nabettka hayqqda histtin ne nena oonna gaana koyadii?
Yesussayka isttas hizzgdees “ta tarkka tana bonchiko ta bonchoy hada, tana bonchizadey gidiko inte “izi nu Xoossa” gizzay ta aawako.
inte iza errontta aggikoka ta qasse errays, ta iza errike giikoo, taka inte mala wordancha gidays. ta qasse iza errayss, iza qaalaka naagays.
inte aawa Abrramey ta galas beeyanas ammotid beeydeesine uhaaththaaettidees.
Ayhudatii qasse “ness buroo ichchachu tammu layth kummontta ne abrrame beeyadi? gida.
Yesussayka “ta intes tummu gays, Abrramey yellettanape kase tani tanako.” gides.
ayhudat heraka iza caddanas wuri shuchchu denththida. gido attin Yesussay istta matape qotetidii xoossa keethafe kezi bides.
yesussay ogera adhii bishe ba aay uloope yelletethape ayfee qooqidade beeydes.
Iza kallizayt iza “tammarisizays haysi addezii qooqe gidi yellistana mala nagara oththiday oonne? iza yellidaytii oththidoye? izi oththide?” gidii Yesussa oychchida.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgdees “iza gidinkka iza yellidaytika nagara oththibeytena, izi hessaththo haniday Xoossa oththoy iza bolla qonccanasiko.
Gaalasara tana kittdade oththo oththanas tas besses, buroo oonnika othanas danddaontta qammay yaana?
Ha bitta bolla diza wode ha bittas poo7oy tana.”
Hessa gi simmidi bitta bolla cuchchu cuttdii ba cuchchan urqqa gigsidi addeza ayfeza he urqqa tydii addeza
“Baada selihomen asay xammaqetizason meccista” gides, selihome gusi kittetdaysa gusa, addezika bidi maccetdesine xeellishe simmi yides.
Iza dosatnne kase izi hen wosishshin be7ida asay “hayssadey kase uttid wosiza addeza gidene? gida.
Isttafe issi issi asati “ee izakko” gida, baggaytii “iza gidena” gida, izi qasse “ta izako” gidees.
Isttika “histtin ne ayfey wani xeelide? gidi oychchida.
Izika zaaridii “Yesussa geetetza assi bitta bolla urqqa urqqasddine ta ayfeza he urqqa tydiine tana baada seliihomen meccista gi yootin ta baada meccistada xeellanas dandda7eds” gidees.
Isttaka “histtin he uray hai awan dizee?” gida, izika “ta errke” gides.
Isttikka he kasse ayfe qooqe addeza parssawistako ehaaththada.
Yesussay urqqa urqqasiidii addeza ayfe paththida gaalasay ayhudata sambbata gaalasiko.
Hessa gish parssawetii addeza izii wostt xeeliidakone iza oychchida, addezika zaaridii “izi ta ayfen urqqa tydees, taka meccistadis, heko hai xeellides” gides.
parssawistape issi issi asati “hays addezi sambbata bonchonttade gidida gish izi Xoossafe gideena” gida, baaggay qasse “nagaranchay hayssa mala malata wani ooththana danddaize? gida, hessa gish istta gidon pallamay medhetides.
Hessa gish kase ayfe qooqe addezzako simmidi “ha ne ayfe paththida addeza gish ne ay gazz? Gida, addezii zaaridi “izi nabeko” gides.
Ayhudati addeza yellida ayeyrane aawara xeeygsi eehisana gakanas addezii kase qooqe gididdaysa ammanibeytena.
Isttka (yelidayta) “inte nusi qooqe nay yelletdes giza nazi hayse? histtin hai wanidi xeelana danddaide?” gida.
Yellidaytka hizzgi zaarida “izi nu na gididaysane qooqe gididi yelletdaysa errosu.
Hai qasse izi wani xeelana danddaidakone iza ayfe oonni pogidakone nu erroko, izi bena danddaidade gidida gish izi ba gish yootanas danddaees, iza oychchitee” gida.
Iza yellidayt hessaththo giday oonnika Yesussa izi Kristtossa giidi markkatday wuri ayhudata woosafe godistana mala Ayhudati kase seera oththida gish ayhudatas babidi gida.
Hesa gish iza yellidayt izi bena danddaidade gidida gish iza ochchte” gida.
Kase qooqe addeza qasseka xeeygd “hayso ne tummayo yootada xoossa boncha, haysi addezi nagarancha gididaysa nu errosu” gida.
Izika “izi nagarancha gididaysa ta errike, gido attin ta kase qooqe gididarone qasse hai ta xeelizaro hano xaala errays” gides.
Istt qasse iza “izi nes ay oththide? Ne ayfeza wostt pogide?” gidi oychchida
Izika “ta intes kase yootin wozinan woth siybeykista shin hai qasse aazas zarethi siyana koyetii? inteka iza kalliizayta gidana koyet?” gides.
Hesafe guye iza “nu musse kallizadentta, ne iza kallizade gida” gi caydda.
Kase Xoossi Mussera hasaetdaysa nu erros, haysi addezi awape yidakone nu erroko.”
Addezika isttas hizzgi zaarides “izi awapekone inte erronttays malalththes, gido attin ta ayfe xeelisdadey iza.
Xoossi bes babizadene iza sheene oththizades attin nagarancha ura siyonttaysa nu eerros.
Ayfe qooqidi yelletdade ayfey xeelides gizaysa allamey medhetdasope oonnika siyy errena.
Haysadey xoossafe gidonttako hayssa ooththanas danddaena.
Isttika iza “neni ne Mule asattethay nagaran munuqettin yelletdays ne nuna tammarssana wana xaladi?” gidi iza goodida.
Addeza goodidaysa Yesussay siydes, iza demmidine “ne asa nan ammanyy?” gides.
Addezika “godo ta izan ammanana mala izi oonne?” gidi oychchides.
Yesussayka “ne iza beyadasa hai nenara hasaizay izakoo” gides.
Addezika “Godoo iza ammanadis” gidi izas hooki goyniides.
Yesussayka “qooqeti xeelana malane xeelizayti qooqana mala pirdanas ta hayssa allamezan yadiis” gides.
Izara diza parssawistape issi issi asati hessa siydi “hesi ayy guuse? histtin nuka qooqe?” gida.
Yesussayka istta inte qooqeta gididdakoo intes nagara gidena shin inte hai nu xiiloosu giza gish inte nagaray diza mala dana” gides.
Ta intes tummu gays, doorssata yire penggerape attin hara baggara guupi geliizaay kaysoone bonqqizzade.
Penggera geliizadey izi doorssata hemmiizade.
Penggee nagzadey izas penggezza doyees, doorssatka iza qaala syeetes, ba doorssata sunththara sunththara xeeygi keesses.
Beyta wursi kessidape guyee istta sinthth adhidi kalethees, doorssatika iza qaala erriza gish iza kaletees.
Immatha urra iza qaala errontta gish izafe baqatetes, attin muleka iza kaletena.
yesussay hessa lemisoza isttas yootdes, shin istt qasse izi isttas yootdaysa aykoka erribeytena.
hessa gish yesussay qasseka isttas hizzgdes, “ta isttas tummu gays doorssat penggey tana.
Tape kasse ydayt wuri kaysoone bonqqzayta doorssat gidkoo istt giza siybetena
Pengeey tana ta, ta bagara gelizadey wuri attana, gelanane kezana hemmetizasoka demmana.
Kaysooy kaysootana wodhanasine dhaysanas xaala yees, ta gidiko intes deyooy dana malane intes kehi darana mala yadsi.
Ta loo7o hemmizzade, loo7o hemiizzdey ba shmppo ba doorssata gish aththi immees.
Mishshera qaxxaretdii himmizadey gidiko doorssat izas gidoontta gish sudhumey yizza woode doorssaatii yegidii bess baqaates, sudhumeyka doorssata daf daf meesene laales.
Baqattza mishshan qaxxarettdadee gidida gishine doorssatas michchetonttagishasa gshasa.
Loo7o hemmizadeey tana tani ta doorssata errays, isttika tana erretes.
Hesika aaway tana errizaysa mala tan ta shemppota doorssata gish aththa immana.
Hayssa ha doorssa yren geloonttayt tas hara doorssat deetes, ta isttaskka ha ehanaas tas beeses, isttika ta qaala siyanane issi mehe gidana, hemmiizayskka isadee gidana.
Ta zaarada denththanas ta shemppo ta aththa immiza gish ta aaway tana dooses.
Tani ta shemppo ta dossara aththa immadsi attin oonnika tape woothii ekkeena, ta aththa immanas gidiin woykoo zaara denththans gidiin sheeney tassa, hessa he azazoza ta ta aawape ekkadis.
Hessa he qaalape denddaysan ayhudata garssan qasseka shaketeth medhetdees.
Daroo asay “iza bolla daydanthth diza gishine gooshu gidida gish inte izi gizaysa ays syeeti? gida.
Baaggayti qasse “haysii daydanththi dizaddey hayssa mala gideena, daydanthth qooqda ayfe paththi errize? gida.
Yerusalamen xoossa keehta oratho ba77ele boncho woodey gakkides, woodeyka gaalas.
Yesussay Xoossa keethth giibe gidon seloomoney simmeretzaso geetetzasora adhishshin.
Ayhudati iza gidoo aththidi “ne aydee gakanas nu wozzna hirggan gammiisanee? ne Xoos kittidade gidikoo nus qoonccsa yoota gida.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgdees “ta intes yootadiskkoo shin inte qasse ammanibeykeista, ta aawa sunththan ta oththiza malatatii ta gish yootetes.
Inte qasse ta doorssata gidoontta gish tana ammanekista.
Ta doorssatii ta qaala siyetes, taka istta errays, isttikka tana kaalletes.
Ta isttas medhina deyoo immana, muleeka istti dhayetena, istt ta kushshepe woththii ekkanas danadey oonnika dena.
Tas istta immida ta aaway wurisofee adhes, ta aawa kushshepe istta oonnika bonqqanas danddaena.
“Tanine ta aaway nu issino.”
Ayhudati iza caadanas qasseka shuchchu denththida.
Yesussayka “aawape gidida daroo gita malatata ta intena bessads, histtin ha ta besidaytape awari gish tana shuchchara caadeti? gides.
Ayudatiika “nu nena shuchchara caadizay ne coo asi gida dashe nena nerkka xoossu kessada caashsha qaala ne hasaida gishshasape attin ne loo7o ooththidaysa gish gideena” gidii izas zaarida.
Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “inte wooga gidon <ta intena xoossata gadis> geeteti xaafetibeyne?
Xoossa qaalay isttas yida asata <xoossu gikoone maxaafay sharistanas danddaontta gidikoo.>
Histtin <ta Xoossa na> gida gish aaway ba shaaki dummasidaysane ha duge allame kittidaysa inte ne caayadasa gidi tana wordo aazas mooteti?
Ta aaway ooththizaysa ta oosontta aggkoo tanan ammanopite.
Ta izaththo ooththiza gidiko inte tana ammanontta aggikoka ta aaway tanan dizaysa taka izan dizaysa inte errana malane yuush qoopana mala izi ooththida malatan ammanite.”
Qasseka istti iza oykanas paacciida shin izi istta kushshepe keesi ekii bidees.
Hessafe guye Yesussay, Yanssaay kasse xammaqzasoo gede yoridanosepe he pinthth simmid hen gammides.
Daroo asay izako yides, istti qasse “Yanssay issi malataka ooththibeyna, gidoo attin hayssa addeza gish izi yootdaysi wurikka tummuko” gida.
Henkka daroo asay Yesussan ammanides.
Bittaniiya gizasoon Marammane diza manddaran Allazzare geetettizadey saketides.
Izi ishsha Allazzarey saketda Maramma kase Yesussa to bolla shiito gusada Yesussa to ba huee iththken quccdaroko.
Hayt michchet “Godo ne dosizaysi saketdes” gidi asse yesussako kittida.
Yesussay hessa siyd ha sakoy xoossa nay izan bonchetana malane Xoossi bonchetanasafe attin iza hayqqos gaththizaz dena” gides.
Yesussay martta izi michchyo marammone Allazare siqqees.
Gido attin Allazarey saketdaysa siyy woththdii hen ba dizason namm7u gaalas gammides.
Hessafe guye bena kaallizayta “anee Yuhuda bitta simm boosu” gides.
Isttika “asttammare! guththa wodepe kasse asay nena shuchchara caadana koyshshina, ne qasse hai hee simma banee? gida.
Yesussay isttas “issi gaalasan tammane namm7u sateey dees gidenee? Gaalasara hammutiza urray ha allameza poo7on simmeretontta gish dhubetena.
dhubeetzadey gidikoo qamara hammutizadee, gasooyka poo7oy bayndda gishasa.” gides.
Hessa isttas yootdape guye “nu lagge Allazarey ziniides, taka iza dhiskkofee denththana bayss” gides.
Iza kaallizati iza “godoo! izi dhiskkda gidiko denddana” gida.
Yesussay isttas hessa yootday iza hayqqo gishasa shin ia kallizaytas qasse dhiskko gish yootida milatides
hasa gish qoonccera isttas “Allazarey hayqqdes

Yesussay bi gakishshn Allazarey haqqi moogetin oydu galas gidides
Biitanyaay Yerussalamepe baga satee oge hakes.
Istta ishsha hayqqo gish Marammone martta minththethanas daroo ayhuda asay isttako shiqides.

Haika gidiko ne woosida wursi xoossi nes immanayssa ta errays.”

Marttay qasse “wurisethan denththa wode izi denddanaysa ta errays” gadus.
Yesussayka izis hizzgidess “dethine deyooy tanakoo, tana ammanizadey hayqqikoka paxa dana.
Tanan dizadeyne tana ammanizadey muleka hayqqena, hessa ne ammanay?”

hessa gadane simmada ba michchiyo Marammo dumma xeeyga kessada “Asttammarey nena koyes” gadus.

Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “heko asa nay bonchetza saatey gakkides.
Ta intes tummu gays gistte ayfey biitan wodhada hayqqontta coou ga uttko berkka atawus, iza hayqqza gidiko hara daroo ayfawusu.
Be shemhaaththao dosizadey dhaysess, hayssa biita bolla ba shemhaaththao ixxizadey gidiko medhina deyooy nages.
Tas ooththana koyzadey tana, tas ooththzadey ta dizason dana, tas ooththzade ta aaway iza bonchana.

aabo! ne ne sunththa boncha” hessafe kaalid “ta ta sunthth bonchadis, qasseka gujja bonchana” giza qaalay salope yides.

Tani dhoqqu gada kaqqetza woode asa wursa tako zaarana.”
Yesussay hessa yootday izi ay mala hayqqo hayqqanakoo errisanasiko.

Inte poo7o nayta gidana mala poo7oy dishin poo7on ammanite” Yesussay hessa gidape guye bidi istta ayfepe gemmides.
Yesussay isttas hessa mala malata istta sinththan ooththinkka ayhudat izan ammanbbeytena.
