Hessa gish ammananas danddaibeytena, gasooyka nabe isiyasay kase hizzgii xaafida gishshasiko.
“Isttii ba ayfen beeydi, ba wozinan yushshi qoopidi simmontta malane izi istta paththontta mala Xoossi istta ayfe qooqisides, istta wozinaka mumisides.”
Isiyasay hessa giday xoossay kittidade boncho beeyida gishshasa, hessa gish hessa Yesussay geesh yootdes.
Gidikoka ayhudista halaqatape daroo asay Yesussa ammanides, gido attin istta ayhudata woosa keethafe godontta mala parssawistas babiidi ba ammano qonccen markkatibeeytena.
Istti hessaththo haniday isttas Xoossafe immettza bonchofe aththidi asape immetza boncho dosida gishasa.
Yesussay ba qaala dhoqu histtdii hizzgides “tana ammanizadey tanan xalala gidontta tana kittdadenkka ammanes.
Tana beeydadey tana kittdadeeka beeyana.
Tana ammanizay wuri dhuman dontta mala ta poo7o gidada hayssa ha allameza yadis.
Ta qaala siydi oosonttade bolla pirdanay tana gidike, gasooyka ta yiday dere ashshanas attin dere bolla pirdanas gidena.
Tana koyonttadene ta qaala ekkonttade bolla pirdanadey dees, ta izas yootda qaalay wuriseththa gaalas iza bolla pirdana.
Gasooyka tani coo ta sheeneni yootabeyke, ta gizaysane ta yootza azazo tas immiday tana kittda ta aawako.
Iza azazoy medhina deyoo gididaysa ta errays, hessa gish ta yootzay wuri aaway tas yootdaysako.
He woodeyka ayhudata paziga ba77elepe kase Yesussay hayssa allameza yedidi aawako bana saatey gakkiidaysa erridees, hayssa allamezan diza ba baggata wuris sqqides, wurisethi gakkanaasika dosides.
Yesussayne iza kaallizayt isife kawo mishshin simmona nay Asqqoroto Yuday Yesussa aththi immana mala xalaey iza wozinan iita qoofa gelththides.
Yesussay aaway izas godateth wursi immidaysane izi xoossa achchafe kezidi yidaysa, qase simmidi xoossako banaysa erress.
Hessa gish maada bollafe denddine mayoo qaari woththdi pooxa ekkdi xeesan gixxides.
Too meecciza gonggen hathth gujjidi bena kaallizayta too meeche oykkdes, ba gixxida pooxanika meccida tooza quccides.
Yesussay Simmona geetetza phixirosako shiiqn Simmona geetetza phixirosay iza “goodo! ne ta too meccanee?” gides.
Yesussayka “tani ooththizaysa ne hai erraka guyepe qass ne erranddasa” gides.
Phixirossayka “ne ta too mulleka meeccaka” gides, Yesussay qasse “ta ne too meeccontta aggiko nesnne tas isifetethi dena” gides.
Simmona geetettza phixirossayka zaaridi “goodo hessa gidiko tas too xalala gidontta kushshera hueera wursa meecca” gides.
Yesussay qasse “ba asatethi meeccetdades kummetha bollay geshshi gidida gish izas too meechafe attin hara koshshena, inte gesha shin wuri gidekista” gides.
Yesussay “inte wurikka gesh gidekista” giday iza aththi immanadey oonnakone erriza gishshsiko.
Istta too meeccidape guye ba mayoo eeki maydii kase ba uttdasoo simmi uttdes, qasse isttas hizzgides “ta intes ay ooththidakone wozinan woththideti?
Inte tana asttammarene goda gista ta qass asttammarene goda gidida gish inte guusay tummuko.
Histtkoo ta intes godane asttammare gidashe inte too meeccza gidiko inteka inte garssan isay issa too meeccana beses.
Ta intes ooththdaysa mala inteka ooththana mala ta intes lemmuiso besadis.
Ta intes tummu gays ashshikaray godape adhena, kittetda urray kittidadepe adhena.
Inte hayssa erridi ooson peyshshiko inte anjjetidayta.
Ta hayssa gizay inte wurisota gish gidena, tani ta doridayta wursa errays, gido attin ta kaathi midadeey ta morkke gididi ta bolla denddides giza maxaafa qaalay poletenas koshshes.
Ta hayssa haira intes yootzay izi poletza woode ta oonnakone inte ammanana malako.
Ta intes tummu gays ta kittdadee ekkizzadey tana ekes, tana ekkizadey tana kittdade ekkes.
Yesussay hessa gi simmidi kezi qoofan gelidinee “ta intes tummu gays inte garssafe isadey tana aththi immana” gidi qonccen yootdes.
Iza kaallizayt hessa izi oonna gish gidakone errontta gish ba garssan isay isara xeeletdes.
Iza kaallizzayta garssafe Yesussay siqqiza isay Yesussa achchan uttides.
Simmona geetettza phixirossay Yanssa sommii besidi “izi oonna gish gizakone ane iza oychcha” gides.
Hessa gish izi ba qodhe gede Yesussa hayththako shishshidi “godo! izi oonne? gidi oychchdes.
Yesussayka zaaridi “izadey ta hai budena woxen dhim77eda barssizade” gides, hessa gi simmid budena woxen dhim77i ekkid asiqorotepe yida simmona na yuda barisides.
Yuday iza badhida mala herakka xalaeey izan gelides, Yesussayka Yuda “ne ooththanays qoopidaysa elela ooththa” gides.
Yesussay hessa aazas gidakoone maadan uttda asape gelidadey oonnika dena.
Yuday mishshe oykizade gidida gish Yesussa kaallizayttape baggat Yesussay yuda ba77elezas koshshizaysa shaama woykoo manqqootas muxata iima” gida milatdes.
Yudayka budena badhida mala herakka kezzidi bides, izi bishin gadeey qammako.
Yuday kezii bidape guye Yesussay hizzgdes “asa nay hai bonchetdes, iza gaason Xoossika bonchetdes.
Xoossi iza gaason bonchetza gidiko Xoossika iza bonchana, heraka gam77ontta bonchana.
Ta Naytoo, ta intenara daroo wode gam77ike inte tana koyana ta kase ayhudata halaqattasika “ta bizzaso inte yana danddaekeista gada yootda mala haika intesiika hessaththo yootays.
Inte inte garssan isay isara siqqistana mala ta intes oraththa azazo immays” ta intena siqqda mala inte inte garssan isay isara siqqetite.
Inte inte garssan siqqetkoo inte tana kaallizayta gididayssa asii wuri errana”
Hessafe guye Simmona geetettza phixirossay yesussa “Godo! ne awa bane?” gidii oychchdes, Yesussay qasse “ta bizasoo ne hai tana kaalana dandda7eka shin guyepe ne tana kaalana” gides.
Phixirossayka “Godo! ta nena hai kaalanas ays dandda7ikna? haray attoshshin tani ta shemhaaththaoka ne gish aththa immana” gides.
Yesussayka zaaridi ne ne shemhaaththao ta gish aththa immanee? ta nes tummu gays hachchi kuttooy wasanape kasistada ne tana hedzdzu to kadana” gidi zaaridees.
Kaalleththdka Yesussay hizzgdes “inte wozinay metotetoofo Xoossu ammanitee, tanaka ammanite.
Ta aawa achchan daroo dusasooy des, hessa gidonttakko <intes danaso gigisanasa ta bana gana shin.
Bada ta intes soo gigisidape guyee inte ta dizason dana mala ta simma yada intena ekkana.
Ta biza ogge inte errista.”
Tomassay “Godo! ne awa bizakoone nu errokoshin, oggezza nu wostt erranas danddaeizon?” gides.
Yesussayka izas hizzgi zaarides “oggeyne, tummay, deyooyka tanakoo, ta baggara gidikofe attin oonnika awako bana urray dena.
Inte tana errizako ta aawaka erranakooshin, hia hayssafe guyee inte iza errana iza beeyoka beydista.”
Pilphphosayka Godo! Ne nu aawa beesiiko nuss gidana” gides.
Yesussayka izas hizzgides “Pilphphosa! hayssa wode gakanas ta intenara deynkka ne tana erriki? tana be7ida urray aawaka be7ides, histtin neni wanada “nuna aawa besa gazi?
Tani ta awan, ta aawayka tanan dizaysa ammaniki? ta intes yootza qaala yootzay ta sheene mala gidena, gido attin oosoza wuris ooththizay tana diza aawako.
Tan aawan diza mala aawayka tanan dizaysa inte ammanite, akaye gikoo ta ooththiza oththota gishika tana ammanite.
Ta intes tummu gays, tana ammanizadey ta ooththiza ooso oththana, hessafeka aththana, gasooyka tani aawako bana.
Aaway naza gaason bonchetana mala inte ta sunththan woosidaysa ta intes wursa ooththana.
Inte ay mishsheka ta sunththan woosidaysa wursa ta oththana.
Inte tana doosiza gidiko ta azazoyo nagite.
Tani aawa woosana, izika intenara medhinasa dana mala hara intena menththeththanade intes immana.
Haysi minththeththiza ayanay dere asay iza beey errontt gish allamey ekkanas danddaontta tummu ayana gido attin inte iza errata, gasooyka izi intenara diza gishine izi inte gaththan diza gishasa.
Aayane aaway bayndda naytta mala ta intena xalala agiike, ta simmada ha inteko yana.
Guththa wodepe guye dere asay tana beeyena shin inte gidiko beeyanddista, tani deyoon diza gish inteka deyoon danddeista.
Tani ta aawan diza mala inteka tanan dizaysane taka intenan dizaysa inte he wode erranddista.
Ta azazoo ekkidi ooththiza urray tana dosees, tana dosiizadeka ta aaway dooses, taka iza dosana, tanaka izades qoonccisana.
Asqqoroto Yudda gidontta hankko Yuday “Godo! neni dere asas gidontta nuss wostta qonccisane” gides.
Yesussayka izas hizzgdes. “tana siqqizadey ta qaala nagana, ta aawayka iza dosana, nuni izako yana, yidika izadeera isipee deyana.
Tana dosonttadey ta qaala nagena, haysi inte siyza qaalay tana kittida ta aawa qaalape attin ta qaala gidena.
Tani hai intenara dashe hayssa intes yootdes.
Aaway ta sunththan yedana minththethiza xiilo ayanay qass haniza wuris intena tammarssana, ta intes yootoysaka wuris inte wozinan woththana mala maadana
Ta intes sarooteth aggada bays, ta sarootethika ta intes immana, ta intes immiza sarootethi derey immiza sarooteththa mala gidena, inte wozinay hirggofoone baboofo.
Ta bana, badaka intekoo simma yana gada ta intes kase yootidaysa siydista, inte tana doszzako ta ta aawako bizays intena uhaaththaaysanakoshin gasooyka aaway tape adhdhes.
Haysi haniza wode inte ammanana mala hasysa intes kasista yootadays.
Hayssa allameza hariza xalaeey yizza wodey gakkiida gish hai ta intenara daroo hasaiike, izi ta bolla aykooka ooththanas izas wolqay deena.
Gido attin tanii aawa dosizaysa derey errana mala aaway tana azazidaysa ta wursa polana anee hayssafe boos denddite.
Qasseka Yesussay hizzgdes “tummu woyne miththa anoy tana, akakilitteza ooththanchay ta aawa.
Ta bolla dishe ayfe immoontta hangge wuris ta aaway qanxxii diigana, ayfiza hangge gujji ayfaana mala qirxxi geshshana.
ta intes yootda qaala gaason inte hai geshshata.
Tanan diite, taka intenan dana, hanggey woyne ano bolla doontta aggiko berkka ayfe ayfana danddaonttaysa mala inteka tanan doontta dishshe ayfee ayfanas danddaekista.
Tane woyne miththa ano, inte qass hanggista, daroo ayfee ayfizadey tanan dizadene taka izan dizade, gasooyka ta bayndda inte aykoka ooththanas danddaekista.
Tanan baynddadeey qanxxetidi woora yegetida hangge mala kare yegetidi hen melana, heyta mala hanggista issi bolla shiqqid taman yegistanane exxana.
Inte tanan diiko ta qaalayka intenan diiko inte koydaysa oychchiko demmana.
Daroo ayfee inte ayfishin ta aaway bonchetes, hessa malan inte tana kaallizayta gididaysi hessan erristana.
Aaway tana dosiidaysatho taka intena dosadis, hessa gish inte ta siqqoon diite.
Tani ta aawa azazo polada iza siqqoon deyda mala inteka ta azazoo poliko ta siqqoon deyana.
Haysa ta intes yootzay ta uhaaththaaysii intenan gidana malane inte uhaaththaaysiika kumethth gidanasiko.
Ta intes immiza azazoy ta intena siqqida mala inteka inte garssan isay isara siqqistanasiko.
Asi ba lagees ba shemhaaththao aththii immope adhiiza siqqooy deena.
Ta Intena ta azazii wursi inte poliko inte ta laggeta.
Ashshikaray goday ooththizaysa erroontta gish simma hayssafe guyee ta intena ashshikarata giikee, gido attin tani ta aawape siydaysa wursa intes qonccisiida gish ta intena ta laggeta gadiis.
Ta intena doradiis attin inte tana doribeykista, inte bidi daroo ayfee ayfana mala inte ayfeey eeqi dana mala ta intena wothadis, hessa gish inte ta sunththan woosidaysa wursi aaway intes immana.
hessa gish inte intee garssan isay isara siqqistana mala ta intena azazays.
Kaalethidika Yesussay hizzgdes. “intena derey ixxiko intefee kase tana ixxidaysa errite.
Inte ammanoontta dere asa gidikoo dere asay ba bagga gididade doses, gido attin inte dere bagga gidontta gish ta intena derepe shakkada dorida gish derey intena ixxees.
Ashshikaray godape adhena gada ta kase intes yootoysa yushsh qoopite, istti tana godizayti intenaka goddana, istt ta qaala naggizako inte qaala naggana.
Istti tana kittidade errontta gish ta gaason inte bolla hessa wursi ooththana.
Ta yada isttas yootonttako isttas nagara gidenashin, hai qass istta nagaras haano giza gasooy bawa.
Tana ixxizadey ta aawaka ixxes.
Hara urray oosontta ooso ta istta garssan oosonttako isttas nagara gideenashin hai istt hessa wursi beeydape guyee tanaka ta aawaka ixxida.
Hessika handday kase <tana gasooy bayndda dishin ixxida> geetetdi istta wogan xaafetda qaalay polistanasiko.
“Gido attin aawape kezidi yanays taka ta aawa achchafe intes yedanays tumma ayanay minththethzays yidi izi ta gish markkatana.
Inte koyropeka tanara diza gish tas inteka markkatanddista.”
Qasseka yesussay hizzgdes “hekoo hayssa wursa ta intes inte ammanoy yarkketoope gada yootadiis.
Isttii intena ba keethape goodana, haray attoshshin intena wodhizadeey wuri xoossas ooththzade milatza wodey yana.
Istt hessaththo ooththizaay tanaka ta aawaka errontta gishshasa.
Ta hayssa intes hessa gakiza wode inte ta intes gidaysa qoopanasiko.” kaalleththidika yesussa hizzgdes “hayssa wursa ta intes yootontta aggiday ta intenara isife diza gishshasa.
Hai qasse tana kittdaysako bana gays gido attin intefe oonnika <awaa ne bane? gidi oychchanay bawa.
Gido attin hayssa wursa ta intes yootda gish inte wozinay muzetes.
Ta qasse tummu intes gays ta busii intes goo7e gidana, gasooyka ta bontta aggiko minththethiza ayanay intekoo yeena, ta bidappe guye iza intekoo yedana.
Izi yidi asa nagara gishine xiilotetha gish qasseka pirda gish errisana.
Asa nagara gish izi errisanay asay tana ammanoontta gishshasa
Xiiloteththa gish izi asa errisanay tani ta aawako buusa gishshine qasse namm7enththo inte tana beeyontta gishshasa.
Pirda gish izi errisanay hayssa dereza aysiza bolla pirdetda gishshasa.
Ta intes buuro yootana daroo yoy des gido attin hai intena dexxan.
Tumu ayanay yidi intena tumay dizaso kaalleththana, gasooyka izi siiydaysa yotana attin bepee gidontta gish izi sinththafe hanana yoota intes yootana.
Tas dizaysape ekkidi izi intes yootza gish tana bonchana.
Aawas gididay wurikka taysa <tas gididaysape ekkidi izi intes yootana> ta gidday hessasa.”
Yesussay gujjidi hizzgdes “guththa wodepe guye inte tana beeyekista, qasseka guththa wodepe guye inte tana beeyana.”
Iza kaallizaytape baggati ba garssan “haysii nus guththa wodeepe guye inte tana beeyekista qasseka guththa wodeepe guye inte tana beeyana, qasse ta aawako bana> gusii ayy guse? gida.
“Histtin haysi <guththa wodepe guye> gizaysi izi aze? izi yootzays nus erretena” gidi ba garssan zar zar oychchetida.
Istti iza oychchanaysa Yesussay erridi isttas hizzgdess “inte inte garssan isay isara oychchetzay ta intes “guththa wodepe guye inte nana byyekista qadeeka gutha woodepe guye inte tana beyanaa> gida gshshasee?
Ta intes tuma gays inte yekanashshb derey gidiko ufaana inte mmchistanashn inte mmchchy ufayydan ufaaysan lamistana.
Maccashii yeloo woodey gakiishn mixxasii hrigayysu shn naa yella yegidapee guyee bista boola nay yelletda gish uhaaththaasafe dendayssan kase ba wayedaysa zara qoopuku.
Hesatho inteeka hii mchchetista (yekista) qase ta intena beyana inte wozinaykka uhaaththaaeistana inte uhaaththaaysa zarii ekanadeey deena.
“Inte he woode tape aykooka wosedeista ta intes tumu gayys ta sunththa ta awa wosiiko intes wursikka iimana.
Hano gakanas inte ta sunththa aykooka wosi eerekista wosiite inte eekana inte uhaaththaaysaykka kumeeththa gidana.
“Hii gakanas ta intes lemussora yootadis shn hyssafe huye ta lemusoora yotonta wodde yana gidoo atiin awa gish intes wurssa qoonccsa yootana.
He wode inte ta nththan wosana taka <awa inte gish wosana> gikke.
Gasooyka away ba bagara intena dosiiza gishshasa away intena dosiizay inte tana dosiiza gishshasane ta Xoossa achchafe ydaysa intee amaniida gishshasa.
Tani awa achchfe kezzada hausa ha 7llamee yadissne qaseeka h 7llameza agada awako ta sima bana.”
Iza kaliizay hzgida “heko ne hii lemuson gidoonta nus qonccer yotadasaa.
Ne ubbaa eeriza malane oniika nena oycchcchanas koshontayssa hii nu eridassa hessa gishsha ne Xoossa achchafe kezidayysa nu amanoos.”
Yesussayistas hzgides “intee hii amaniidista”
Gdoo atiin inte intee bagara laleetda tana xala agana wodeyy gakiides he satiyka hii gakkadus gidoo atiin away tanara gidida gish ta tarka gidiike.
Ta hyysa intes yotizzay inte tanan deyyn intees sarotithii dana malla gada yotaays inte h 7llameen dishshn intes wayeyy dees gidoo atiin aykooy ba ta 7llamee xoondees.”
Yesussay hessa gidape guye pudee salo dhoqqu gi xeelid hizzgi wossides “aaboo hekoo hai saatey gakkides, ne nay nena bonchana mala neni ne naza boncha.
Ne bonchanayka ne izas immidaytas izi medhina deyoo immana mala ne izas asa wuriso bolla godateth immida gishshasa.
Medhdhina deyooyka ne xalala tumu xoossu ne kiittda Yesuss Kiristtoosa erro guusa.
Ne tas immida ooso tani wursada ha biita bolla nena bonchadis.
Ta aawa! allamey medhdhistanape kase tas nenara diza bonchon haika tana ne achchan bonchariki
Haysa dere asape ne tas deeran immida asatas ne oonnakone ta isttas nena qonccsadis, istt kaseka neyta shin ne tas immadasa, isttika ne qaala nagida.
Ne tas immidaysi wurikka nepe gididaysa hai istti errida.
Ne tas immida qaalataka isttas immadis, isttika ekkida, ta ne achchafe yidaysa tumape errida, ne tana kittdaysaka istt ammanida.
“Ta isttas wossays heytii ne tas immidayt istt neyta gidida gish ta isttas wossays, gidoshin hinkoo dere asas wossike.
Tas gididay wurikka neysa neysika wurikka taysa, taka isttan bonchetana.
Hayssafe guye Tani hayssa biita bolla diike, istt gidiko ha biita bolla deetes, hai ta nekoo bays, ta geshshazo! hayta ne tas immidayta istti nu mala ba garssan issino gidana mala ne tas immida ne sunththan istta naga.
Ta isttara isipe dashshe ne tas immida ne sunththan ta istta naggadis, ta naggadis, hessa gish kase xaafetda geshsha maxafa qaalay polistana mala izi kaseka dhayos diza nazape attin isttafe oonnika dhaybeyna.
Ta qasse hai neko bays, ta ha biita bolla dashshe hayssa yootizay ta uhaaththaaysi isttan polistana mala gada yootays.
Tani ne qaala isttas immadis, tani ha biita asa ginddoonttaysa mala isttika ha biita asi gidetena, hessa gish ha biita asay istta ixxides.
Ne istta iittape nagana mala ta nena wossays attin ne istta ha biitafe denththa efana mala nena wossike.
Tani biita asi gidonttaysa mala isttika ha biita asii gidetena.
Ne istta ne tuman nes shaaka, ne qaalayka tumu qaala.
Ne tana ha biita kittoysaththo taka istta biita bolla kittadis.
Istt tumape nes duma ass gidida mala tanika tana istta gish dummasays.
Istta qaala marikatetha tana ammananayta gishshara ta nena wossays attin ta nena istta gish xalala wossike.
Ta wossizay istti wurikka issino gidana malasiko, ta aawawu qasseka ne tanan diza mala nunan gidana malane ne tana kittidaysa ha derey ne ammanana mala wossays.
Nunii nu garssan issno gidida mala isttika ba garssan issino gidana mala ne tas ida boncho taka isttas immadis.
Ta wossizay sttan, neka tanan gidida mala isttika kumethth issino gidana malako, qasseka neni tana kittda mlane tana ne siqqida mala isttaka ne siqqidaysa dere asay erranasiko.
“ta aawawu! ne tana haysi biitayne saloy medhdhistanape kase dossida gish ne tas immidaa ta bonchoza istti beeyana mala hayta ne tas immidaytka ta dizasoon anara dana mala dossays.
Xiillo gidida ta aawawu! nena derey erribeyna, ta gidiko nena errays, haytka ne ana kittdaysa errida.
Ne tana siqqida siqqooy isttan gidana malane taka isttan gidana mala isttine nena errana mala ooththadis, qasseka istti errana malaka oohthana.”
Hessa wursi yootidape guye Yesussay bena kaallizaytara Qeedirone geetetza shooba pinidi akakiltte gidoo gelidees.
Yesussayne iza kaallizayti kasseka he gadeyin daroo wode isife shiqiza gish Yesussa aththi immida Y uday he gadeyo kasseka erress.
Hessa gish Yuday wotadarata, qeessista halaqatane Farssawistape kitteti yida ashshikarata wursi kaalleththi ekkidi he istti shiqizaso yidees. Izara yida asay paanoose, xoomipenee mashsha toora oykkidi yidees.
Yesussay ba bolla gakkanaysa wursi erridi yida asako bidi “Oonna koyeti? gides.
Istti qasse “Nazireete yesussa koyoos” gida, Izika isttas “Tani izakoo” gidees. Isttas aththi immida yuday isttara isife eqqides.
Yesussay “Ta izako” gida mala asati guye ganddigaridi biita bolla kunddida.
Yesussay ha7ika “Oonna koyeeti?” gidi oychchin istti zaaridi “Nazireete Yesussa koyoos” gida.
Izika zaaridi “Tani izako gadiiskkoo, histtkoo inte koyizay tana gidikoo hayti beto bochchofite” gides.
Hesi haniday “Ta aawawu ne tas immidaytape issadeka ta dhaysabeykee” gida qaalay poleistana malako.
Simmoona geetetza phixxirossay giththa mashsha oykkda gish mashsha shohope shodidi issi qeessista halaqa ashshikara dizaysa haythe mashshara padhi yegides. He ashshikaraza sunththi “malkosa” geetetes.
Yesussay qasse phixxirossa “Ne mashsha gede shohon zara gelththa. Nees ta aaway tas immida metoo ushsha ta uyoontta milatizee?” gidees.
Hessafe guye wootadarati, istta azazizaysinne Ayhudata ashshikarati Yesussa oykkidi qachchida.
Koyro he laythas qessistas halaqa gidida qayafaa bollo Haannakko ehaaththaida.
Qayafaay “Deere gish issadey hayqqiko lo7okko” gidi Ayhudata dulata kase zooridade.
Simmona geetettiza phixxirossayne Yesussa kaallizaytape issadey yesussa kaallida. He uray qessista halaqa achchan kehi erretidade. Hessa gish Yesussara isife qessista halaqaza gibbe gelides.
Phixxirossay gidikko penggefe kare baggara eqqdees. Qessista halaqa achchan kehi erretdi Yesussa kaallizaysi yidine penggen diza garadeya phixxirossa gibbe giddo gelththana mala yootdi Pixirosa ekki gelides.
Pengge naggiza garadeya Phixxirossa “Neka hessa addeza kaalliza asatape issa gidikki?” gadus. Izi qasse “Tani iza kaallizade gidike” gides.
Wodey meegiza wode gidida gish ooththanchatnne ashshikarati tama eththidi eqoon ho7etes. Pixxirossaykka isttara eqidii ho7es.
He wode qeessista halaqay Yesussa iza kaallizayta gishane izi tammarisida tmmirtte gish oychchides.
Yesussayka izas “Ta asa wursos qoonccen yootadas. Ayhudati shiqiza istta wossa keeththan gidinkka Xoossa keeththan tammarisadis; ta qootan haasa7idazii aykoyka deena.
Histtin ne tana oychchizay aazee? ta yootshshin siydayta oychcha; ta yootdiysa istti erretes” gides.
Yesussay hessa gida mala hen eqida ashshikaratape issay “Qeessista halaqas hayssaththo wosta zaaray” gishe Yesussa shagalan baqqa shayides.
Yesussayka zaaridi “Ta iitta hasa7ida gidiko anne ta gooysa ne markkata; ta yootday likee gidiko tana aazas baqqaz?” gides.
Hessafe guye Haanay qachchetida mala Yesussa Qeessista halaqa Qayafaakoo yedidees.
He wode Simmoona geetetza Phixxrossay eqqidii tama ho7ishin hankko asay iza haysoo, ne Yesussa kaallizaytape issa gidikii?” gida. Izika zaaridi “Ta iza kaallizade gidike” giidi kadides.
Kase Pixxrossay iza hayththe qanxxiidayssa dabooy qeessista halaqa ashshikaratape issay “wona ta nena akaakilitesoon isttara dishin beeyabeykkina? gidees.
Pixxrossay qassekka kadides, heraka kutooy wasides.
Hessafe guye Yesussa Qayahaaththaa keeththafe dere aysiza kawooza gibbe malladoo wonttara ekki bidda. Ayhuda asas pazziga ba77ele dorssa ashsho mizza wode gidida gish bena tunisontta mala giidi malladora dere aysizaysa gibbe gidoo gelibeytena.
Hessa gish Philaxoossay gede isttako kezidi “Hayssa addeza inte aazas mootetii?” gidii oychchidees.
Istti qasse “Haysi addeezi iita oosonttade gididako nu iza nes aththi immokoko shin” gida
Philaxossayka “Inte iza ekki bidi inte woga mala pirditee” gidees. Ayhudata aysizayti qasse zaaridi “Nu ass wodhana mala nuus fiqadey immetibeyna” gides
Hessika haniday Yesussay kase isttas izi waani hayqanakoone yoottida qaalay polistana gishshasko.
Philaxoosay qasseka guye gibbe gido gelidi Yesussa xeeygisidi “Ne Ayhudata kawoo?” gidii oychchidees.
Yesussaykka zaaridi “Ne hessa gizay nepeyee woykoo hara asatii ta gish nes yoottdoo?” gides.
Philaxoossayka “Ta Ayhuda asee? Nena tas aththi immidayti ne baggatanne qeessista halaqattako; ne ayy ooththadii?” gides.
Yesussaykka “Ta kawootethi hayssa ha biita bolla gideena, ta kawootethi hayssa ha biita bolla gididakoo Ayhudata dannata kushshen ta kunddoontta mala ta ashshikarati ta gish olistanakoshin. Ta kawootethi gidikoo ha biita bolla gideena” gides.
Philaxoossayka “Histtin ne kawoo?” gides, Yesussay qasse “Tani ne gidaysa mala ee kawoo, ta yeleetidayne ha biitta yiday tuma gish markkatanasko. Tumape gididay wuri ta qaala siyees” gides.
Philaxoossayka “Tumay azee?” gides. Hessafe guye Phiilaxossay namm7enththo Ayhudatako kezzidi “Ta iza bolla ayko bala beyabeyke.
Gido attin kasseka ta intes paziga ba77ele gaalas issi qachcho ass birshiza mala hayssa Ayhudata kawoo intes birshana mala koyeetii?” gides.
Istti gidiko “nus Barbbanne birsha attin hayssa gideena!” giidi wassida. Barbbanney ba hu7es pangga.
Hessafe guye Philaxoossay Yesussa eefidi gaarafisiidees.
Wotadaratikka aguunththa zawuude xaxiidi Yesussa hu7en woththida, zo77o kabakka mayzzida.
Izako shiqqi shiqqdi “Ayhuda kawoo saaro saaro!” gi gidi iza shagalan baqqida.
Philaxxossay qasseka kare kesiidi “Heko ta iza bolla aykoo morooka demoonttaysa inte errana mala ta iza intes haa kare kessana” gides.
Hessa gish Yesussay aguunththa zawuude hu7en woththi ekkidine zo77o kaba maydi kare keziides. Philaxxossayka isttas “Hekoo addezi haysichchi!” gides.
eQessista halaqatine istta ashshikarat Yesussa beeydi “Ne iza kaqqa! kaqqa!” gishe wasiida, Philaxxossay qasse “Ta ta baggara iza bolla issi moroka demmabeyke, koykoo inte ehaaththaidii kaqqite” gides.
Ayhuda asati qasse “Nuus wogay dees haysi addezi beena xoossa na giza gish nu woga mala izas hayqqoy besees” gida.
Philaxxossay hessa istti gizaysa siydi daroo babides.
Gede gibbe gelidi Yesussa “ne awape yadii?” gidi oychchidees. Yesussay qasse izas ayy malththeka immibeyna.
Hessa gish Philaxxossay “ne tas yootiki? ta nena kaqqanas woykko birsha yedanas godatethi tas dizayssa errikii?” gides.
Yesussayka izas zaaridi “sheeney ness Xoossafe immetoonttako nes ta bolla ay godatethika deenashin, gido attin tana nes aththi immidade bolla gita nagaray dees” gides.
Philaxxossay hessa Yesussa hassa7e siydapee guye iza birshi yedana koyides shin Ayudatas babida gish istti “ne hayssa addeza birshiko Rome kawoo qeessare bagga gidaka, gasooyka bena berkka kawooththizadey wuri Qeessares moorkke” gishe wurikka wasiida.
Philaxxossay hessa siyda mala Yesussa gede kare kesisidi “Loochcha shuchchu” geetettiza soon pirda wombbaran uttides. He pirda sooy ayhudata qaalara “Gabata” getetes.
He wode gadeey asii paziga ba77eles gigettiza gaalasa. Wodeyka gaalasafe usuupun saate mala gidides. He wode Philaxxosay Ayhudata “Hekoo inte kawoy hayssichii!” gides.
Gido attin istti qass “Gede digga, gede digga, kaqqa” gishe wasiida. Philaxxossayka “inte kawoo kaqqoo?” gides. Qeessista halaqati zaaridi “nus Qessarepe hara kawooy deena” gida.
Hessafe simmidi Philaxxosay Yesussa kaqqistana mala isttas aththi immides. Isttka Yesussa oykki ekkii ehaaththaida.
Hessafe guye Yesussay ba kaqqistana masqqaleza tookidii “Asa hu7ee guuge” geetettizaso kezides. He sooy Ayhudata qaalara “Golggoota” geetetes.
Iza heen kaqqiida. Yesussa gidoo gelththidi hara namm7u asata izatho hadirssarane oshshachchara kaqqidda.
Philaxxossay “Nazzirete Yesussay Ayhudata kawoo” giza qaala xaafidi iza masqqale bolla izas hu7esora qaphides.
Yesussay kaqqetidasooy katamas mata gidida gish daroo Ayhuda asay Philaxxossay xaafidaysa nababidees. Xaafeetidaysika Ayhudata qaalara, Latiine geetettiza qaalarane Girikee qaalarako.
Ayhudata qeessata Halaqati Philaxxossa “ne iza Ayhudata kawoo” gada xaafoopa, Gido attin “<haysi addezii bena ta Ayhudata kawoo gidees> gada xaafa” gida.
Philaxxossay qass “Ta xaafidaysa xaafadis” gides.
Wootadarati Yesussa kaqqidape guye iza mayooza ekkidi wotadarata issa issa gakana mala oydu kessi shakereththida. Garsara mayiza mayozaka hessaththo shakereththida. Ggido attin garsara mayza mayoz siketoontta pudepe duge gakkanaas coo yeda dees.
Hessa gish wotadarati ba garssan “Gishan oonna gakkanakoone errana mala iza bolla exxa yeggana attin dakooko” gida. Hessika hanidday kase “Ta mayoo istti gishshetii ekkida, ta bollara mayza mayoza bolla exxa yegiida” getetida geesha maxaafa qaalay poleistana malasa. Wotararatikka heesa oothida.
Yesussa masqqalle achchan iza aayiyane aayeeyi michchiya Qeliyyopha machcha Maramane Megidele geetettizasope yida Marama heen eqqida.
Yesussay ba ayiyone izi siqqza iza kaallizaysi ba achchan eqqidayta beeydi, ba aayiyo “Aayee ne naza hessa beeya” gides.
Hessafe kaalleththidi bena kaallizaysa “Ne ayo hinoo beeya” gides. Hinoo he saateype simmin he iza kaallizaysi Aayiyo besso ehaaththaidees.
Hessafe guye Yesussay ha7i wurikka poleettidaysa erridi geesha maxaafan xaafetdaysi poleistana mala “tana samees” gides.
Heen gadan caala phanqqida ushshii kumii uttida issi xaarro malay dees. Hessa gish heen gadan dizayti he caala ushsha zanzza milatza sppoonjje gizaysara hisophphe giza miththa xeeran qaphidi iza dunako shishshida.
Yesussay he caalla ushsha xunxxi xeellidi “poleetides!” gides. Be hu7e duge ziqisidi shempo kezides.
Hessafe guye Ayhudata danati kaqqetida asata meeqqethth wodirape menththidi istt iza masqqsale bollafe woththana mala Philaxxossa wossiida. Istti hessa ooththiday Ayhudati sambbatas gigetiza gaalas gidida gishshine he sambbatayka daroo giita ba77ale gidida gish sambbata gaalas ahay masqqale bolla gami77ontta malla koyida gishasa.
Hessa gish wotadarati bidii Yesussara kaqqetiida asata meqqethth wodiirape wodiirape menththida.
Istti Yesussako biin izi kasetidinee hayqqdaysa beeydi iza wodiira meqqethth menththibeyteena.
Gido attin wotadarata garssafe issadey toorara iza miileen cadiin heeraka suththine haththi gukkidees.
Hessa beeydadeyi inte izan ammanana mala markkattdes. Iza markkayka tuma. Izi yootzayka tumu gididaysa izi errees.
Hessika haniday “Iza meqqeththafe isinaka meeqquku” geetetida geesha maxaafa qaalay polistanassa.
Qasseka geesha maxafa harason “Istti ba caadide beeyana” gees.
Ayhudata dannata babidi qotan Yesussa kaalliza Armmatyasa getetizasoppe yida Yossefoy Yesussa aha ekkanas Philaxoossa wossin Philaxoossayka izas eeroo gides. Hessa gish Yossefoy bidi Yesussa aha ekkidees.
Kase Yesussakko qamara yida Niqoodimossayka kiilo bagga gidiza karbbeenne ireete geetettiza mishshara walakeetida shiito ekki yidees.
He namm7u asati Yesussa aha ekkidi Ayhudatii aha xaxiza mala shiito cacafidii le77e mayora xaxida.
Yesussay kaqqetidason issi akakilitesoy dees. He akakilitezason oonnika moggetonttay oraththa dufooy dess.
Ayhudata sambbatas gigeteza gaalas gidida gishshinne dufooykka matan diza gish Yesussa aha heen mogiida.
Wooga gaalas wontta malado buroo sosey zoishshin Magidale marama Yesussa dufooko badusu. Iza he gakkishin kase Yesussa dufoo izara goordida shuuchay dufooza duunape denddidi gendderidaysa beeyadusu.
Hessa gish iza Yesussa kaallizaytape Simmoona geetetiiza Pixirosakko Yesuyssay dosiza hankko iza kaallizaysako woxxa bada “Goda dufooppe keesi ekkidi awan woththidakone nu erroko” gadusu.
Heraka Pixxrossayne Yesussa kaalliza hinkko issay kezzidi gede duhaaththaoy dizasoo bida.
Namm7eyka ishaaththaee woxxida, gido attin Yesussa kaalliza hinkkoysi Pixxrossape pilatii woxxidi kaseti dufooy dizasoo gakkides.
Dufooza hookii xeelidi ahay xaxxetida mayoo xala dizayssa beeydes. Gido attin gede dufoo giido gellibeeyna.
Simmoona geetettiza Pixxrossayka iza kaalli gakkidi dufooza giido gellidees, ahay izan xaxxetida cariqqay hen dizayssa beeydes.
Yesussa hu77ey xaxxetida carqqay hankko xaththa carqqatara gidoontta duuma harasson xaxxeti dizayssa beeydees.
Koyroti gakkida Yesussa kaallizzaysika dufooza giido geli beeydi ammanides.
Gasooyka “Izi hayqqope denddana beeses” giza maaxxafe qaala istti buroo hasa7ibeeytena.
Hessafe guye namm7etika simmidi besso besso bida.
Magidale marama yeekashshe Yesussa dufoope kareera eqqada hokka dufooza giido xeelladus.
Yesussa Ahay dizasson boththa mayoo mayda namm7u kitanchatape issay hu7eson issay toson uttidayta beeyadus.
Isttika Maramo “Hane maccashshayee azaas yeekazii?” gida, izaka “Istti ta Goda ehaaththaidii awan woththidakoone ta errike gadus.
Iza hiino gada guye yuyshshin Yesussay eqqidayssa demaduus shin izi Yesussa gididayssa errabeykku.
Yesussay izo “Hanne maccashshayee! azass yeekazzi? Qasse oonna kooyazzi?” > gides, izika iziis akakkiltte nagizzadee millatiin “Godo! ne ekkida gidikoo ne woththidasso tass yootarkki, ta iza tass ekkana” gaduus.
Yesussay izo “Marame!” gides, izakka gede izakko simmada ayhudata qaalara “Rebuune!” gaduus, hessa birshechchi “asttamaree” guusa.
Yesussay qass “Ta buroo pude ta aawako kezzabeykke tana oykoofa, gido attin ne ha7i ta ishatakko bada “Ta ta aawakone inte aawako, ta xoossakone inte xoossako kezana gides gada isttas yoota” gides.
Hessa gish Magidale Marama Yesussa kaallizaytako bada iza Yesussa beeydaysane izi izis yootidaysa isttas yootadusu.
He gaalas wooga Omarss Yesussa kaallizayti Ayhudata dannatas babidii kare ba bolla goordidi keeththa giidon shiqoon dishshin karey dooyetoontta Yesussay iza kaallizayti shiqii diza keeththa gellidees. Istta gidoon eqqidii “Saaroy intes giidoo!” gides.
Hessa gi smmidi ba kushshistane ba miiye istta beesides. Iza kaallizaytika goda beeydii keezi uhaaththaa7etida.
Hessafe guye qasseka Yesussay istta “intes saaroy gido! ta aaway tana kittda mala taka intena kittays” gides.
Hessa gi simmidi istta bolla uuhaaththau gidi “inte Xiiloo Ayana ekkite.
Inte asa nagara atto gikko isttas atto geteettana, inte asa nagara attoo gontta ixxiko qass isttas attoo geteteena” gides.
Yesussay bena kaallizaytako yida wode tammane namm7istape issay Didimossa geteetiiza Toomassy isttara denna.
Hessa gish hankko Yseussa kaallizayti Toomassa “Nu Goda beeydooskko” gida. Toomassay qass “Miismmaren cadeetida iza kushshista ta ta ayfeera beeyoontta dahshene qasseka ta birdhdhe miismmarey gelidason gelitha xeelontta dashshene ta kushshe iza miiye maddunththan gelththa xeelontta dashshe ammanikke” gides.
Hessafe kaallin osppun gaalasafe guye iza kaallizayti qasseka keeththa gidoon dishshin Tommssayka isttara isife dishshin kareyka goordana dishshin Yesussay yiidi istta gidoon eqqidi “s saarotethth intes gido” gides.
Hessafe guye Toomassa “Ne biradhdhe ha ehada ta kushshista beeya. Ne kushshe ha ehada ta miiyeen gelitha ammana attin ammanonttade gidoopa” gides.
Toomassay “Ta Godoo! Ta Xoosso!” gides.
Yesussayka Toomassa “Neni tana beeyda gish ammanddassa, tana beeyoontta ammanizayti gidiko istti galateetidayta” gides.
Hayssa maaxfan xaafetontta daroo malatata bena kaallizayta sinththan Yesussay oththides.
Gido attin Yesussay ha yana kittetida Xoossa nay iza gididaysa inte errana malane ammanidi inte iza sunththan deyoo demana mala haysi xaafettdes.
Hessafe guye Yesussay Xibiradoose abba achchan bena kaallizaytas qasseka beetdes.
Simmoona geetettiza Pixxiroossay Didimoossa geetettiza Toomassay Gallila Qanna ass gidida Natinaelley Zabidossa naytika Yesussa kaallizaytape hara namm7ati wuri isife dishshin
Simmoona geetettiza Pixxiroossay isttas “Ta moole oykkana bays” gides, isttika izas “Nukka nenara bana” gida, izara kezzi bidi wogoolon gellida shin he gaalas omarssi issi mooleka oykkibeytena.
Gadey wonttishshin Yesussay abba achchan eqqides, iza kaallizaytii qass izi Yesussa gididayssa erribeyteena.
Yesussay istta “Naytoo mooley dizze?” gides, isttika “aykooka bawa” gida.
Izika “Giteza wogoolozape oshshacha baggara abban yeegite, inte demmana” gida gish giiteza abba giido yeegidane daroo mooley oykeetda gish giiteza molara gochchana danddaebeyitena.
Hessa wode Yesussay iza kaallizaytape Yesusa iza siqiza issay Pixxirossa “Hesi Godakko!” gides. Simmoona geetetza Phixxiroossay “hesi Godakko” giza qaala siyda mala kasse ooso diigofo gidi mayoo qaari woththidi kaloo diza gish herakka mayoo ekki mayidi abba giido guuppi gelidees.
Yesussa kaalliza hankkoyti qass biitafe xeetu mitire mala hakii diza gish mooley kumi dizza giiteza gochchi ekkidi wogoolora gakkida.
Istti wogoolozape wodhdhishin moley iza bolla diza bonqqo tamane ukethth beeyda.
Yesussay istta “Ha7i inte oykkida molezape ha ekki yiite” gides.
Hessa gish simmoona geetettiza Phixxiroossay wogooloza giido gellidi xeistane ichchachchu taammane hedzdzu woogga giita mooleti kumiida giiteza abbafe gede gade bolla gochchides. Hessa mala daroo molera diinika giitezi daketibeeyna.
Hessafe guye Yesussay istta “Ha yidi miite” gides. Izi Goda Yesussa gididaysa wursi errida gish iza kaallizaytape issadeykka “Ne oonne” gi oychchanas xallidadey bawa.
Yesussay yidi ukeththane moleza ekkidi isttas immides.
Yesussay hayqqope denddin iza kaallizayti iza beeyshshin haysi hedzdzanththo.
Istti mii gigishshin Yesussay simmoona Phixxiroossa “Yoona na Simmoona! hayiti tana dosizayssafe aththa tana dossayii?” gides. Izikka “Ee ta Godo! ta nena dosizayssa nekka errasa” gides.
Yesussay iza “Ta laqqata hemma” gides, namm7enththoka “Yoona na Simmoona! ne tana dossay?” gides, izika zaarid “Ee Godo! Ta nena dosizaysa neka errasa” gides, Yesussay qass “laqqata naga” gides,
Hedzdzanththo “Yoona na Simmoona Ne tana doossay?” gides. Izi hedzdzanththo “Ne tana dossay” gida gish Pixroossay michchetidine “Godo ne ubbaa errasa ta nena dosizayssakka errasa” gides, Yesussayka qasseka “Ta doorisata hemma” gides.
Ta nes tumu gays ne naatethan dashshe ne giththe nerkka gixxada ne koydasso baasashin ne ciimmiza wode gidiko ne ne kushshista pidiisin hara urray nena gixxisanane ne dosoonttaso nena ehaaththaana.
Izi Iza hessaththo giday Pixxroossay ay mala hayqqon xoossu bonchanakone izas erisanaskko. hessafe guye Phixxiroossa “Ne tana kaalla” gides.
Phixxiroossay yushshi xeelidi Yesussay dosizaysi iza kaallishin beeydes. He urray kase istt ka7o mishshin Yesussa hayththako shiqidi “Godo nena aththi immanadey izi oonne?” gii oychchides.
Pixxroossay iza beeydi “Godo hayssadeych wanandde?” gidi Yesussa oychchides.
Yesussaykka izas “Ta ha yana gakkanaashin ta iza paxxa woththiko nena azi gaththidee? ne tana kaalla” gides.
Hessa gaason ishshata garssan “izi hayqqo hayqqena” giza worey lalletides. Gido attin Yesussay “ta yana gakkanaas paxxa dana mala ta koyko nena azze gaththiday?” gidees attin “hayqqakka” giibeyna.
He yoota gish markkatidayne xaafiday ha Yesussa kaallizayssa. Iza markkatethika tumu gididayssa nuni erroos.
Yesussay oththida hara darooti deetes. Tas milatiza mala izi ooththida miishshata wursi issi bolla xaafizako xaafeetiza maxaafata haysii biitay tokkana dandda7ena.
Tofilosa, Yesussay oothanasine tammarissanas oykidayssa wursia ta nes koyro maxaafan xaafadis.
Hessika izi pude denththa gaalas gakkanaas ba doorida kitidaytas xiillo ayana baggara izi isttas immida azazoko.
Izi daro waye be7idappe guye istakko shiqidi hayqope denddanayssa haytannitas daroo markkara qonccisishe oydu tamu gaalas gakkanaas isttas gaalas galas beetishe Xoossa kawootetha gish yootides.
Isttara isife maadan uttidishe istta hizzgi azazides “Yerussalamepe kezoppite, gido attin ta intes yootishin inte siydayssa ta aaway immida uhaaththaayssa naagitte.
Yanissay haththan xaamaqqides shin inte qass guuththa wodeppe guye xiillo ayanan xammaqistana.
Isttika issibolla shiqetti uttidishe “Godo! isiraelista kawootethi zaarada hai essane?” gi oychchida.
Izika isttas “aaway ba sheenen woththida wode errooy intes immetibeeyna.
Gido attin xiillo Ayanay inte bolla wodhdhida wode inte wolliiqa ekkana, Yerussalamenika Yudanika Sammariyanika wursoson biita gaxxa gakkanaas inte tas markkata gidana” gides.
Hessa gi yootidape guye istti xeellishin pude salo denddides, salo sharayika istta ayfepe iza genththides.
Izi biishin istti iza tish histi pude salo xeelishin booththa mayo mayida namm7u asati qoponnita istta achchan eqqidi;
“inteno Galila asato! inte pude salo xeellishe hayssan aazas eqqidetii? Haysi inte maatappe pude salo dennidishin inte beeyza Yesussay salo keezishin inte beeyda mala hessaththoka izi simmi yaana” gida.
Hessafe guye Dabirezayite giza zumma bollafe wodhdhid Yerusalame simmida, he zummayka yerussalameppe issi killo mittire mala hakkes.
Gede kaatamayo gellida wode kase ba diza keeththa fooqe bolla keziida, heyttikka Phixxirossa, Yanissa, Yaqoobe, Inddarassa, Philliphossa, Toomassa, Barttelomossa, Matossa, Illifossa na Yaqoobe, ba bagga maddizade geetettiza Simmonane yaqoobe na Yuuda.
Heyti wurikka maccashatappe Yesussa aayoo marammira hessathokka iza ishshatara issi wozinnan issi bolla qanxxontta minni woossida.
He gaallasatan Phixxirossay xeistane namm7u tammu ammaniza asa giidon eqqiddi.
Hizzgides “ta ishshato! Yesussa oykkida asata kaalleth oyththida, yuda gish xiillo ayanay kassetidi dawute dunnan hasa7iida geesha maxaafa qaalay polistanas koshiza gishiko.
Izikka nuuppe issade mala taybeettidi hayssa ha oosozan gellanas exxa demmides.
Shin hayssadey ba iitta ooson demmida miishshan gade shammides. Hennikka ba liiphon gufanni kunnidin iza asatathay giidofe phalliqeti wodhdhides; iza maraccey biita bolla zazetides.
Hesikka yerussalamen diza asas wursios siyetides. Biitaykka istta qaalara “akeelidama” geetetides; Birishechayika suththa biita gusa.
Gujjidikka Phixxirossay “mazzimmure maaxaafan <iza biittay mela atto, iza biittan assi doopo qassekka iza dannatethi hara assi eekko> geeteti xaafetides.
Hessa gish Goda Yesusay nunara diza wode wurson nunara isife dizayta gidofe nu issade dorannas koshshes.
Hesikka Yanisa xiinqqateppe ha simmin Yesussay nuppe shakeetidi dendi bana gakkanaas nunara dizade gidannas beeses. Gasoykka ha asatappe issadey nunara Yesussa denththas markka gidana koshshes” gides.
Hessa gish Barissabasa woykko Yosixxossa geetettiza Yosehaaththaonne Matiyassa namm7ata shishshidi;
Hizzgi wossida “Godo! Ne asa wurso wozina errassa, hayta namm7ata giidofe ne oona doridakko issade nuna beessa.
Yuuday yeggi bidason ha ooththa ooththanadene haware gidanade ne doora” gida.
Hessafe exxa yeggin exxay Maatiyassas keezides. Izikka taammane issi hawaristara isife tayibeetides.
Phenxxaqonxxe geetettiza gaalas gakkanaas asay wurikka issi soon shiqii dishin,
Qohaaththaay bayinnida daroo miinno gotte caariko mala girethi asay diza keeththa kummides.
Tama lacco malay asas betidi shakeeti shakeeti issi issi urra bolla uttides.
Amanizayti wuri Xiillo Ayanan kummiidi Ayanay isttas hasa7anas immidayssa keena hara qaalara hasa7a oykkida.
He wode salo guhaaththaanththon diza derepe yida Xoossas babiiza ayhudati Yerusalamen deetes.
He gireththa siyidi derey shiqides. Issi issi asay ba qaalara hasa7izaysa siyidi malaletides.
Malaletidinne gizazi dhayin hizgida “hayti hasa7izayti wurikka Galila asi dettenee?
Histtin nuni nu yelletida nu dere qaalara isti hasa7ishin wossti siyizonii?
Nuni Pharite asay Meede asay Eelame asay Mesphphoxxomiyan Yudan Qaphedoqqiyan phanxxosan Isiyan,
Firgiyan, Phinhaaththailliyan Gibxen, Qaarena achchan diza Liibiyappenne Romeppe yida;
Nuni Ayhudatine gede Ayhudatethan gellida Qaarxesa asane Araabe asata gidishin Xoossa wolqama oosoza hayti nu qaalara hasa7ishin nu siyoos.
Wurikka kezi malaletidine gizazi dhayin ba giidon “Haysi azesha?” geetetida.
Bagga asay “Hayti daro woyne ush uyida” gidi istta qidhida.
Hessa wode Phixxirossay taammane issinistara eqqidine ne qaala dhoqqu histtidi deeras hizzgides “Inteno yuda asatto! Yerusalame dizayto inte wurikka hayssa issi mishsh erritenne ta gizaysa siyte.
Ha7i gadey wonttin buroo hedzdzu saate gidida gish inte qoppiza mala hayti asati maththotibeytena.
Gido attiin haysi kasse nabe yu7ellen hizzgi yootetida qaalay polistanasko,
“Xoossi hizzgees <wursetha gaalas ta ayana ashsho mayida wursio bolla ta guussana; inte macca naytine inte atumma nayti buroppe hananaysa beeyana, yelaga nayti ajjutta beeyana, Cimaati agumo agumeistana.
Hessa wode ta macca ashkarata bollanne ta atumma ashkarata bolla ta ayanappe ta guussana. Isttika buro hananaysa hassa7na.
Bolla salon malalisiza hanota ta beessana, garssa biittan malatata ta immana; suuththi, tammayinne tulaley hanana.
Gitanne boncho gidida Goda gaalasay yanappe kassetidi awa ayhaaththaey dhummana, agiinnaykka suuththu milatana.
Goda sunththu xeeyigizay wuri attana.
Isra7eele nayto hayssa qaala siyte; inte inte baggara errizayssa mala inte garssan malatanne assi siyi erroontta miishshata iza kushshen ooththidi Xoossi naziirete Yesussas markkatides.
Xoossi kase ba qachchidayssa izas beni erratetha mala hayssade inte kushshen aaththi immides. Intekka iita asata kushshen kaaqqeti hayqqana mala ooththidista.
Gido attin Xoossi iza bollafe hayqqo wolqa diggidi hayqqope denththides. Hayqqoykka iza oykki ashshanas dandda7ibeyna.
Dawiteykka iza gish hizzgides “Tanni Goda wurso wode ta sinththan beeyayis, izi ta oshachchan dees, mulekka hirigike.
Hessa gish ta wozinay uhaaththaa7etes, ta dunaykka galates, ta ashshoy uhaaththaayssan dees.
Ne ta shemmipiyo dufoon agaakka, ne na geshshaza wooqana mala agaagaaka.
Ne deyoo ogge ta errana mala ooththadasa, ne tanara diza gish ta uhaaththaayssay kumeth.”
Ta ishshato beni aawatappe Dawitey hayqqi moggetiddayssane iza dufooy hach gakkanaas nu achchan dizayssa babontta ta intes yootana dandda7ays.
Izi nabe gidida gish Xoossi iza zeerethafe issade iza kawootetha aliigga bolla wothanayssa kase caaqo qaalan yootidayssa errides.
Hessa kasetidi errida gishine iza ashshoy wooqqi duufon atoontta doretida kirstosa denththa gish hassa7ides.
He Yesussa Xoossi hayqqope denththidees. Nukka wuri hayssas markkata.
Hessa gish izi Xoossa ushshachchan dhoqqu dhoqqu giddape guye xiillo Ayana uhaaththaayssa ba aawappe ekkidi ha7i inte beeyzayssane siyzayssa duge guussides.
Dawitey pude salo kezibbeyna, izi ba dunnan hizzgides <Goday ta Godas; “ta ne morketa ne to garssan yeedhissana gakkanaas ta oshshachchan utta.” >
<range>
Hessa gish Xoossi inte kaqqida Yesussa Godane Kiristtossa hisitidayssa Isiraele asay wuri lo7ethi erro.
Deerey hessa siyda mala wozinay bochetides, Phixxirossane hanko yesussay kittidayta “nu ishshato histtin nu ay ooththino? gida.
Phixxirossayka hizzgides marotethan gellite; inte nagaray maristana mala intefe issi issi urray Yesuss Kiristtossa sunththan xammaqetite, izi immiza Xiillo Ayana inte ekkana.
Izi uhaaththaayssa qaalay intesine inte naytasa, qassekka Godaa Xoossay beeko xeeygiza hahon dizaytasara wursosiko.
Hara daroo qaalara isttas markkatishe “hayssa geella yeletethafe intena ashshite” gidi istta qofisides.
He gaalas qaala ekkidaytine xaammaqetidayti hedzdzu shiya mala asay kaseyta bolla gujjetides.
Isttika kittetidayta timmiritenn, isife qumma mussaninne wossan minnida.
Kittetidayta kushshen daroo malatati ooththetida gish asi wuri isttas babiides.
Ammanidayti wurikka isife deyida; bees dizazkka wursii issi bolla go7etida.
Bees diza mishshene mehe bayzi bayzi ba garssan koshshida mala gishechida.
Gaalas gaalas xoossa keeththan isife shiiqetes, ba keeththankka qumma isife uhaaththaayssanine suure wozinara meetes.
Istti Xoossa galatishe dere sinththan bonchetida, Godaykka istta bolla gaalas gaalas orathth ammanizata gujjidees.
Issi wode gallasappe udufun saate bolla Phixxirossayne Yanissay wossa saaten Xoossa keeth bana kezzida.
Issi yellet wodhdhosope dommidi toy sillidade Xoossa keeth gelliza asape muxxata wossana mala asay gaalas gaalas tokki ehaaththaidi wothin issi loo7o geetettiza Xoossa keeththa pengen wossizadey dees.
Izikka Phixxirossayne Yanissay Xoossa keethe gellishin beeyid isttafe muxxata wossides.
Phixxirossayne Yanissay iza tiishi histti xeellida. Phixxirossaykka iza “Ane haa nuna xeella” gides.
Addezikka isttafe aykko demmana gidi istta tiishi histti xeellides.
Gido attin Phixxirossay izas zaaridi “tas biraynne woorqqay denna gidikokka tas dizaz ta nes immays Nazireete Yesuss Kiristtossa sunththan dendadda ne toora hammuta” gides.
Izas oshacha kushshe oykkidi denththides, Herakka addeza tooyne too qirphpheey miniddes.
Guuppi denddi eqqidi Hammuththu oykkides. Heene haane hammutishene guuppishe Xoossaka galatishe isttara isife Xoossa keethth gibbe gellides.
Izi Xoossa galatishe heene ha simmeeretishin asay beeydi,
hayssadey haanife kase “loo7o” geetettiza Xoossa keeththa peengen uttidi muxxata wossizay iza gididayssa errides. Iza bolla hanidayssafe denddidayssan asay keezi malaletides.
Ha paxxida wossanchay Phixxirossakonne Yanisako shiphph gidi isttara oyketi dishin derey wuri malaletidi isttako “Sollommone simereetethaso” geetettizaso woththan yides.
Phixxirossay he asa beeyidi hizgides “Inteno Isra7eele dereto, hayssan aazas malaleteetii? Qassekka hayssa addeza nuni nu wolqan woykko nu nu xiillotetha paththidi hammutisida mala qodidi nuna aazas tish histi xeelletii?
Nu aawantta Abramentta, Yisaqantta, Yaqobentta Xoossi naza Yesussa bonchides, inte qass iza hayqqos aaththi immidista, Philaxossay izi birshana koynkka inte iza Philaxossa sinththan kadidista.
Geeshsha na xiilloza inte kadidi shemmppo wodhdhizaysi birshistana mala wossidista.
Deyo imizade inte wodhdhidista, gido attin Xoossi iza hayqqope denththides, hessas nuni markkata.
Haysi inte beeyizaysine inte errizayssi mini eqqiday Yesussa sunththan ammanida gishiko. Inte wurikka beeyza mala izi kumetha paxxa demiday Yesussa sunthaninne iza sunththan beettiza ammanoniko.
“Ha7ikka ta ishshato inte hessa ooththiday inte hallaqata mala errontta gididaysa ta errays.
Gidikokka kiristtossay wayye ekkanayssa Xoossi kasse nebista dunnan hasa7idayssa pollides.
Hessa gish inte nagaray qucceti dhayana mala marotethan gellite, inte biza oggepe simmite goda matappe inte oraxxana wodey intes yana.
Qassekka Xoossi kase intes doori wothida Yesussa Kiristtossa izi intes yeddana.
Xoossi kasse geshsha nabeta dunnan hasa7idaysa mala hannizaysa wursii oraxxisana wodey gakkanaas izi salon gamm7anas koshshes.
Musseykka <inte goda Xoossi inte giidofe ta mala nabe intes denththana, izi intes yootizaysa siyitte.
He nabeza siyontta ixxida shemmppoy wuri dere garssafe shaketi dhayo> gides.
Tumappe Samelappe ha simmin denddida nabeti wuri hayta wodeta gish hasa7ida.
Intekka nabeta naytakko. Qassekka Xoossi Abrames <ne zeerethan biitta asi wuri anjjistana> giidi izi caqqida caqqoza latannay intenakko.
Xoossi naza denththida wode intena issa issa inte iitatethafe zaaridi anjjana mala kassetidi inteko kittides.”
Phixxirossayne Yanissay asas hasa7an dishin qeessista hallaqatine Xoossa keethth nagizayta hallaqay qassekka saduqqaweti hasa7ay bayndda isttako yida.
Yiidine kittetidayti asa tammarsizaysasiine Yesussa baggara beettida hayqqidayta denththa gish sabakkizaysas keehi hanqqeetida.
Phixxirossane Yanissa oykkidi gadey qammishin wonttana gakkanaas qachcho keeththan ayssida.
Gido attin qaala siyda asappe dariza baggay ammanides. Ammanzza atuumma asa qooday gede ichchachchu shi gakkanaas dhoqqu gides.
Wonttetha gaalas istta halaqatine cimmat qasseka musse woga tammariszzayti yerussalamen shiiqida.
Istta qeessista halqqa Hannaynne qayahaaththaay, Yanissay, Iskkindirosaynne qeessista halaqaso asay wuri he gadan beettida.
Isttikka Phixxirossane Yanissa ba giidon aththi essiidi “hayssa inte ooththizay aza wolliqane? woykko oonna sunththane? gidi oychchida.
He wode Phixxirossay xiillo ayanan kummidi “inteno dere hallaqato! dere cimmato!
Inte hach ha too siila addezas ooththetida loo7o oosoy wani izi poxxidako inte nuna oychchiza gidiko,
inte kaqqin Xoossi hayqope denththida nazireete Yesuss kiristtossa sunththan izi paxxidaysane inte sinththan izi eqqidayssas intekka Isra7eele dere asay wuri hayssa errite.
Izikka inteni keeththa hiillati kadhi aggida shuchchay ginbbe keethas waanna hu7e gidides.
Atootethi hara oonnankka baawa, saloppe garssa baggara nu asa naytti atana mala nus immettiday hayssafe hara sunththi deena” gides.
Assaykka Phixxirossayne Yanissay hessaththo xali hasa7izayssa beeyddi isti tammarontta asi gididayssa erridi malaletidane istt kasse Yesussara dizadentta gididayssa akekida.
He paxxida addezi isttara eqqidishin beeyida gish isttas hara oothanas gaassoy dhayides.
Hessa gish istta duulatappe kessana mala azazida. Hessafe qassekka shiqeetidi ba garssan zooretida.
Be garssan hizgida “hayta asata wossitino? Yerusalamen diza asay wuri istta kushshen hannida giita malata errides. Hessa gish nu ha yooza asa ballethanas danda7okko.
Gido attin hayssi yoozi dere garsan keehi akkonita malane hayti asati namm7anththo hayssa ha sunththan hara onnaskka yootontta mala isttas loo7eththi yootana.”
Istta xeeygidinne mulleka Yesuussa sunththan hassa7ontta malane tammarsontta mala azaziida.
Phixxirossayne Yanissay qasse zaarid “nuni xoossafe bollara intes azazistanas beesizakonne ane inte Xoossa sinththan pirdite.
Nuni nu beeydayssane nu siydayssa hassa7anappe guye gookk” gida.
Qassekka istta bolla maanddidi yeedida, gasooykka hankko derey wuri hanida yooza gaason wurkka Xoossu galatiza gish istta qaxxayanas danddaibeyetena.
He giita malatan paxxida addezas layththi uyddu taammufe bollako.
Phixxirossaynne Yanissay qachchoppe birshetidi gede ba asattako simmidi qeessista halaqatine dere ciimati istta gidaysa wursikka yoottida.
Isttikka hessa siyida mala ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi isife Xoossakko hizzgi wassiida “Wooga Godo! neni salone sa7a abbane abba giidon dizayta wurssa medhdhadassa.
Ne ashshikkara nus aawa Dawite dunaara Xilo Ayanan “Hankko dere asay aazas hanqqeti denddide? Deerey aazas meella maqqetizee?
Biitta kawooti isife gagidi biitta harizayti issi bolla shiqeetida, Goda bollane dooreti tiyetidayssa bolla duullatida”> gides.
Tumappe Heridosayne Phanxxossa Philaxossay Isira7elatarane hara dere asaara hanno kaatamayin ne doora tiyida geeshsha naza Yesussa bolla yoo qachchanas shiqetida.
Haysnkka ne wolqaninne ne sheenen kasse ne qopidaysa isti polida.
Godo ha7ikka istta manddetha ne beeya, nuni ne aylleti ne qaala babontta kummetha xallatethara yootana mala dandda7isa.
Paththanas ne kushshe mica, ne na geshshaza sunththan gita malata ooththa.
Istti woosidappe guye istti dizasoy qaaxides. wurikka Xiillo Ayanan kummidi Xoossa qaala xallatethan yootida.
Ammanizayti wurikka issi wozinaninne issi qoofan gaagi deetes. Istas dizay wursi issi bolla dees attin bess dizaz “haysi tas buzu7a mishsha” gizadey deena.
Kittetidaytikka Goda Yesussa denththa giita wolqan markkateth oykkida, Wuriso bolla giita Xoossa kiyatethi dees.
Istta giidon meetottanchay issadeykka bawa. Gasooykka gade gidin keethe gidin bees diza wursii bayzzi bayzzi shishshida mishshe
kittetidayta kushshen woththidi issi issi urras izas koshshiza mala gisheetes.
Qophirose geetettizason diza Yossefo geetettizadey issi Lewe bagga assi dees. Izikka kittetidaytan “Barnnabassa” geeteti sumides. Hessas birshechay “minththetho naa” guussikko.
Izikka ba gade bayizida miishsha ehiidi kittetidayta kushshen wooththides.
Issi Hannaniya geetettiza asi Saphphira geetettiza ba machchira ba gade bayzides.
Machchiya Saphphiray loo7atha errishshin gadeza bayzzida miishshafe bagga shakki ashiidi bagga ehhidi kittetidayta kushshen immides.
Qasse Phixxirossay “haysso Hannaniya neni Xiillo Xyana bolla wordotanasine gade miishshafe ashshana mala xalla7ey ayys ne wozinan gellidee? Bayzanappe kasse gadez neeysa gidene? Ne bayzadeppe guye qasse miishshay ne kushshen deenee? Histtin ne hayssa mala wossita ne wozinnan qoppadii? Ne Xoossa bolla wordotadassa attin asa bolla gideena” gides.
<range>
Hessa siyida mala Hannaniyay kunidi hayqqides. Hessa siyida asay wuri daroo babbides.
Atumassay denddidi aha xaaxidine herakka ehaaththaidi mooggides.
Hedzdzu saatepe guye machchiya izi wanidakone errontta dashe yadus.
Phixxirossaykka “Anne tas yootta, inte gadeza bayzzida wagaay hano xalalaa?” gides, Izakka “Ee haano ha wagaayn bayzzidos” gadus.
Phixxirossaykka “inte Xoossa Ayana paccanas ayys issi dunna gidideti? heeko ne aziina moggida asati moggi simmidi karen pengge bolla deetes. Istti nenakka kessi eikki ehaaththaana” gides.
Iza siyda mala herakka iza too bolla kunddada hayqqadus. Atumassaykka soo geellida mala hayqqidaro beeyidi kessi ehaaththaidi izi azzina achchan moggides.
Kummetha wossa keeththa asayne hessa siydda asay wuri daroo babiides.
Kittetidaytikka dere garssan daroo malatanne mallalisiza mishsh ooththida. Amanizayti wuri “Solomonne pengge geetettiza assi simereetizason shiiqetees.
Istas babida gish oonnikka isttara wallakistanas koybeyna. Gido attin derey istta keehi bonches.
Daroo maccatinne addetti wodeppe woden Godan ammani ammani istta bolla gujjetida.
Hessa gaason Phixxirossay adhdhishin haray attin iza eeshshoy hargganchatappe bagga hargganchata bolla wodhdhana mala harggizayti zinniiza algga bollane zaphpha bolla karen zin7isetes.
Yerusalame yushon diza kaatamatappe harggizaytane tuna ayanay waysizayta ehin wuri paxxida.
Hessa wode qeessista hallaqayne izara diza Saduqaweti wuri qannate kumida.
kittetidayta oykkidi qachcho keeth gelthida.
Gido attin Goda kittanchay qaamara qachcho keeththa kaare doyydi istta kessidi,
“Biidi Xoossa keethth gibbe giidon eqqidi hayssa deyoo qaala wurso deres yoottite” gides.
Gadey wonitdda mala isttas yoottidayssa Xoossa keethth gibbe geellidi dereza tamarso oykkida, qeessista hallaqaynne izara dizaytti yidi Ayhudata duullatane Isra7ele dere cimmata kummeth issi bolla shishida. Kittetidayta qachcho keethafe ekki yanamala asse yedida.
Kitteeti bida asati bidi istta qachcho keeththan demmibeytena, Simmidine
“Qachcho keethay loeththi qulfeti dees, Naggizaytikka peengge bolla eqqidishin beeyidos, gido attoshin nu doyy gellishin qass keeththan oonikka bawa” gida.
Xoossa keeth naggizayta hallaqayne qeessista hallaqatikka hessa siyda mala hanozan daro malalettidane isttas hanoy wuri tikk gides.
Heerakka issi urray yiiddi “Hekko inte qachcho keeth gellithida asati Xoossa keeththa gibbe giidon eqqidi dere tammarison deettes” gidees.
Xoossa keeth naggizayta hallaqay ba oothanchatara bidi ista oykki ekki yidees. Oykki ehidaytti asay bena shuchchara cadontta mala babbidi wolqathontta loodara ehida.
Kittetidayta ehidi Ayhuda dulata sinththan essida. Qeessista hallaqaykka istta “Hayssa ha sunththan inte tammarsontta mala intes loo7ethi yootidoskkoshin inte inte timmiritan Yerussallame wursion deista. Qasse nunakka ha addeza suththas oychcheetizatyta histtanas gixxi denddidista” gides.
<range>
Phixxirossayne hankko kittetidaytika zaaridi hizzgida “Nuni asape aththidi Xoossas azazistanas beeses.
Inte iza miitha bolla kaqqi wodhdhida Yesussa nu aawantta Xoossi iza hayqqope denththides.
Izikka Isra7eele naytas nagarappe simmidi maristana mala Xoossi iza wursiofe bollanne ashshizade histtidi ba oshshachchan dhoqqu dhoqqu histtides.
Nuunkka hayssas markkata. Qassekka Xoossi bees azazetizaytas immida xiillo ayanayka markka.
Asati hessa siyddi iita hanqo hanqqetida, wodhdhanakka koyidda.
Gido attin dere achchan kehi bonchetida issi woga asttamare, izikka Gemalliyale geetettiza Faarssawista baggay dullata ass gidon denddi eqqidi kittetidayt guuththa wode Karen gamm7ana mala azazides.
Dulata asas hizzgides “Isra7eele asato inte hayta asata bolla ooththanayssa daroo akekkara ooththanas beesses.
Hessafe kase issi Tewodassa geetettizadey bena giita ass histti qoodi denddin oydu xeetu derey iza kaallides. Ggido attin izi asa kushshen hayqqides. Iza kaallizaytikka coo lallettin iza hanoy coo mela gidides.
Izappe guyekka derey tayybetiza wode Galila Yuday denddidi daro dere benara kaallethides. Bena kaallizaytakka demmides shin izikka dhayides. Iza kaallizaytikka wuri dhayda.
Hessa gish ta ha7i intena gizay hayta asata aggite, bochchopite. Istta qoofay woykko istta oosoy asappe gidiko dhayana.
Xoossafe gidiko qass inte istta teqqanas dandda7ekista. Oonne errizay inte Xoossara oyeetishe beistanakkonne.
Isttika iza zooreza ekkidi kittetidayta xeeygidi garafisida. Namm7anththo Yesussa sunththan hasa7onta mala azazidi yedida.
Kittetidaytikka iza sunththa gish kawushshateth ekkanas beesiza gish daroo uhaaththaa7etishe dulata asa achchafe kezzi bida.
Galas galas xoossa keeththaninne issa issa keeththan Yesussay izi Xoossi doridade gididayssa tammarsofenne sabbakope mullekka guye gibeytena.
Ammanizayta qooday dari dari biza wode girkke biittafe yida ayhuda asati yudan diza ayhuda asa bolla garssara zigiretida, gasooykka wursio wode miza kaathi gishishe ammiista wudan yegontta aggida gishasiko.
Hessa gish nu taammane namm7u kittetidayti ammaniza harata issi bolla shishshidi “Nuni kaathi gishshetho ooson gellidi Xoossa qaala tammariso agganas beesena” gida.
Hessa gish nu ishshato inte garssafe ciniccata, xiillo ayanan kummidaytane loo7o markkateeth dizayta lappun asi doorte, hayssa halafeteth nu isttas immana.
Nuni gidiko wossanine qaala yooton minnana.
Istti gida yoyi siyidayta uhaaththaayssides, Ammanonine xiillo ayanan kummidayt Isxxifanose, Philliphosa, Phirisqqorossa, Niqqarona, ximmona, Pharmmenane Yudatethan gellida anxxokiya dere asa gidida Niqqolossa doorda.
Heyta ehidi kittetidayta sinthth shishshida, istikka ba kushshe istta bolla wothidi isttas wossida.
Xoossa qaalay aakki aakki bides, ammannizayta qooday yerussalamen dari dari bides, qeessistape darooti ammanida.
He wode isxxifanosey Xoossa immotethanine wolqan kummid dereza garssan giitta malalisiza malatata ooththides.
Wozeetida Ayhudata woossa keeth geeteti xeeygetizasope yida asi gidida Qarenappene Iskkinddriyape; qassekka Kilqqiyappene Issiya awurajjatappe yida asatikka wuri Isxxifanosera marshetida.
Gido attin cinccatethan izi hasa7iza hasa7ane izan diza Ayana eqqistanas danda7ibeyteena.
Hessa gish “Isxxifanosey Musene Xoossu cayishin nu siydos” giza asata guyera gigisida.
Hessa wode dereza, dere cimmatane woga tammarisizayta denthethidanne Isxxifanose oyththidi dere duullatako shishshida.
Iza bolla “Hayssi addezi Haysa geesha sooza bollane woga bolla cashsha qaala hasa7a mullekka aggibeyna.
Gasooykka haysi addezi Nazirete Yesussay hayssa Xoossa keethth dhayssana gishinnine nu mussepe ekkida woga laammana gi hasa7ishin nu siyidos” gi wordora markkatiza asata shishshi markkasida.
Duullata uttida asay wuri Isxxifanose tiishi histti xeellishin iza ayfesoy isttas kittancha ayfeso millati beetides.
Qeessista halaqay Isxifanose “haysi ne bolla shiqqida yozi tuumee?” gi oychides.
Isxxifanoseykka hizigides “Ta ishaato, ta awwato ta giizaysa siyite nu awa Abramey Kaarane yanappe kasse buro Mesophoxomiyan dishin bonncho Goday izas qonccidi
<Ne dereppene ne dabbofe shakeistada ta neena bessizaso ba> gides.
Izikka Kaldawista biittafe kezidi Karane biittan uttides. Iza away hayqqidappe guye inte ha7i dizaso ha dere iza ehidees.
Haray atoshin issi toy eqiza gadey izas hayssafe immetibeyna. Gido attiin he wode izas issi naykka baynnida dishin izzine izappe guyen iza zerethi biittiyo laatana mala Xoossi izas ccaqqides.
Qassekka Xoossi izas hizigi yotides <ne zerethi alagga biittan bete ass gidana. Oyddu xeettu layth aylletetha qammibara garsan wayistana.
Gido attiin ista aylle mala harza dere ta qaxxayana. Hessafe guye isti he biittafe kezzidi haanno ha soyin tas goynana.>
Hesafe guye qaxxara woga ccaqo izas immides. Abrameykka Yisaqa yellidi iza osppuntha gallasa qaxxarides. Yisaqayka Yaqobe yellides. Yaqobeykka tamane namm77u qomota yellides.
He qommota awatti yosefo bolla qanattetidi iza aylletethas duge Gibixe bayzzida. Gido attiin Xoossi izara dees;
meto wursofe iza ashides. Gibxe kawo Faaronne sinthan bonncho qumma7isides. Faronney iza Gibxe biitaninne ba keeththa asa wurso bolla alafethethan shuumiides.
He wode Kanaaneninne Gibixen daro metto ehida gita koshay dennidides. Nu awataskka miza kaathi dhayides.
Yaqobey Giibixe deren kaathi dizayssa siyiddi nu aawata koyyro Gibxe yediides.
Istti nam77antho biza wode Yosefoy izi oonakkone bena ba ishatas qonccisides. Faroneykka Yosefo ishshata erides.
Hessafe guye Yosefoy kiitidi ba aawa Yaqobenne laappuun tamane ichachu gidiza ba dabota kuummeth ehiisides.
Yaqobey duge Gibxe woodhdh7ides. Izikka nu aawatikka wuri heen hayqqida.
Ista ahaykka Seekkeme gizaso ehaaththain Abramey Eemore nayytappe ba miishan shammida duhaaththaon moggettides.
Xoossi Abrames caaqqida qalay polletiza wodey maatishin Gibixen diza nu asa qodday dari dari bides.
Hesafe guye Gibixe bitan yoosefo eronta hara kawoy kawotides.
Izikka nu asa ba geene oothon metoothides. Buuro yelletida guutha naytti hayqqana malane yelliidayta kare kessi wora yeganamala wolliqathides.
He wode Musey yeletides. Izikka Xoossa achan dosetida malla loo7o na gidides. Be aawa keeththan hedzdzu aggina all7isson diccides.
Izi gede worra yeegettida wode kawwo Farone macca nayya deemada bees ekkadus. Be na mala oothada dichadus.
Museykka Gibxista eraatetha wurssi tammarides. Yoon erra, oothonikka miinno gididees.
“Muse laaythi ooydu tamu gida wode Musey ba ishata Isira7elle nayta beyanas ba wozinan qoppides.
Izikka isi Giibixe assi Muse baga asappe isi ura bolla qooho gaathishin beyiddi ba bagga adeza madidi he Gibxe adeza wodhidi he qoheetidayssa hallo keesides.
Muses Xoossi iza kushshen issta wozanayssa iza asay akekkiza millatides. Gido atiin issti hessa yuushi qoppibeyteena.
Wontetha gallas qasekka Isira7elle naytappe nam7ati ba garssan oyeetishin gakkidi oyetizayta iginthanas koyydi <haytto asato inte inte garssan ishantakko, inte wannidi issay issa qoheetii?> gides.
Be lageza bolla qoho gathidaysi Muse suggi yeggidi <Nena nu bolla nuna haarizadene nu bolla piridizade oothi shuumiday oonee? woykko qamma Gibxe adeza wodhoyssatho tannaka wodhana koyaazii?> gides.

Musey hessa siyidda mala Midiyame biitta beettidi hen bete ass gidi deyyides. Heenkka nam77u atuma na yeellides.
Hessafe oydu tammu laythafe guuye Siina zuma achchan diza bazza biittan qerii worra gidon exxiizza taamma laccon kiitannchay izas bettides.
Museykka iza beeydamala mallaleetides. Azakone shaki eranas izzi he izako shiqqishin Goda qalay “tanni ne awannta Xoossa abirame Yisaqane Yaqobe Xoossa gishin siydees. Museykka daro dagammides, xeellanaskka xalibeyna.

Godaykka izas hayssi ne eqqidasoy geeshaso gidiida gish ne toope ccamma shoda. Gibxen diza ta dereta waye ta tuumappe beyadis. Issti wasiza issta waye waso siiyada ista ashshanas woodhdhadis. Ne ha7ikka haya ta nena duge Giibixe zarada kiitana gides.

Histtin heyyti <nu bolla neena haarizadenne piridizade histti ooni shuumedee?> giidi asay kaase kadhdhida Musse Xoossi qeeri woora gidon izas beetida kiitancha bagara issta haarizadenne ashizade hisitidi istaako zarri yeedides.
Izikka ista kallethidi Gibxeppe keesides. Gibxen, zo7o abbanine bazo biittan oyydu taammu laythi daro mallalsiza miishatane gita malatata istas oothides.
Isrra7elle nayytas ta mala nabe Xoossi inte garsafe dennthana gidaysi hayssa Musekko.
Izikka Siina zuma bolla hassa7ida kitancharanne bazo biitan nu awatara dere dullata giidon dees. Deyyo qalakka ha nuus aathanas ekkides.
Nu awati gidiko izara eqqetida attiin izas azazistanas koyoonta gish ba wozinara guuye Giibbxe simmida.
Aarooneskka <Nu sinnthara biiza eeqqa nus gigisa nuna Giibbixefe kaallethi kessida Musey wanidako nu erroko> giida.
He wode mara miisile meedhdhidi eqqas yarsho shishida. Berkka medhida ba kuushe oothon uhaaththaa7ettidane guppiida.
Gido attiin Xoossi isttas zokko zarides. Isti sallo xollinntistas goynana mala aththi immides. Hesikka nabbista mxxaafan “inteno Isra7elle nayto inte baazo biittan oyddu tamu layth diza wode intefe yarshone muuna tas shishi ereetii?
Harappekka inte goynanaso othiida eeqqa Molookke dunkenane inte eqqa Refanne xollinnte misile dhoqu dhoqu hissti oykkidista. Hessa gisha ta intena inte dizasoppe dennthada Babiloonera aatha yeddana.” geetetidi xaahaaththaetides.
Xoossi Muse bessida lemmusoza malane azazzidayssa mala oothetida Xoossi asara gagiza dunkkaneya nu awatara baazzo biittan deyadus.
Nu aawati dunkeneyo ekkidayssappe guye Xoossi Iyaaso kallethin kaase ista gooddida dereta lattida wode dunnkaneyo ekki geellida. Dawite wode gakanas dunkaneyaa he biittan deyadus.
Dawiteykka Xoossa sinthan boncho demidi Yaqoobe Godas aqqoso gigisanas woossides.
Gido attiin Solmoney izas aqoso kexides.
Gido attiin woogga Goday asa kushey keexida keeththan deena. Hesikka nabey <salloy ta zuuppane biittaykka tas tos shemmposo, hiistiin inte tas ay mala keeth kexxeti woykko ta shemmppanasoy awaysse? Hayssa wursi ta kuushshey oothibeynnee? gees Goday> getetti xafetida mala.

Inteno wozana mumeto, haytha tuleto, intekka inte aawata amala wursio wode Xiillo Ayanara eqateista.
Nbistappe inte aawati gooddonnta naabey oonee? Xiillozi yanayssa kasseti yottida nabetakka wodhida intekka ha7i izza aathi immidistane wodhidista.
Kitanncha bagara intes immetida woga ekkidista attiin naggibeykista.” Isxxifanosey Shuchchan Cadeti Hayqidess.
Duulatan diza asay hessa siydamala daro hanqitidi, iza bolla ba achche gariccides.
Gidinkka Isxxifanosey Xiillo Ayanan kummidine puude salo tish histi xeellishin Xoossa bonchon Yesussay Xoossa oshachan eqqidayssa beydi “Heeko ta saaloy doyeetidayssane asa nay Xoossa ushachan eqqiidayssa beyays” gidees.
