Hessafe guye ta Yerusalame simmada Xoossa keeththan wossishin ajjutay tas beettides.
Godaykka tas qonccidi “ne ta gish immana markkateth istti ekkontta gish ne gammi7ontta dashe Yerussalamepe ellela keeza!” gides.
Takka izas hizzgadis “Godo ta Ayhudata wossa keethati dizaso ba baada nena ammanizayta wursia qachchada istta bukkidayssa ba baggara isttikka erretes.
Ne gish markkatiza Isxxifanose asay wodhdhiza wode takka he wohdhiza asata achchan eqqada istti wodhdhizayssa takka dosadissenne wodhdhizayta mayookka nagadis.
Godaykka <Hahoon diza Ayhude gironta asakko ta nena kittiza gish denddada ba> gides.”
Asay hinno gakkanaas Phawulossa hasa7a wozinappe loo7ethi siyishe aggidi ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi “hayssa mala asi nu biitafe dhayo, hayssa mala asi nu biitan shemppora danas bessena” gishshe wassides.
Asay wassishe ba mayoo qarri qarri wuxxishene biita puude salo dharccides.
Ola asa azazizaysi hessa beeyidi Phawulossa wotadarati dizaso gellithana mala azazides; Deereykka iza bolla aazas hessa mala wassizakko errana mala iza garafidi paxxisana mala azazides.
Gido attin dafon waxxi qachchidi iza garahaaththaana gigeetishin Phawulossay ba achchan eqqida issi xeetu wotadarata hallaqas “Rome as gidazade pirday bayinida garehaaththaanas intes fiiqadey dize?” gides.
Xeetu wotadarata hallaqay hessa siyida mala gede halaqata azazizayssakko biidi “ay ooththana gaaz? haysi addezi Rome asakko” gides.
Hessa gish halaqata azazizayssi Phawulossako shiiqidi “ane taas yoota, ne Rome ase?” gides; Izikka “Ee ta Rome asa” gides.
Azazizayssikka “ta Rome asa gidanas daroo mishshe qanxxada shaammadis” giin Phawulossay “tani gidiko Romen yeellistadis” gides.
Hessa gish iza marimaranas gigettida asati herakka iza achchafe hakkida; azazizayssikka izi Rome as sanththalatan qachchidayssa yuushsh qoppidi babbides.
Wonttetha gallas azazizayssi Ayudati Phawulossa motiza ayfe yooy azakone erranas koyides; qessista hallaqatine Ayhudata shengeo dulata asay wuri issadeykka attontta kumeth shiiqana mala azazides; Phawulossakka qashoppe birshidi shiiqida asa sinthth shishshi esides.
Phawulossay duulata asa tiishi histti xeellidi “ta ishato hach gakkanaas ta Xoossa sinththan loo7o qohaaththaara dayss” gides.
Qeessista hallaqa hananiyay qasse Phawulossa duunan shoccana mala iza achchan eqqidayta azazides.
Herakka Phawulossay Hananiya “Haysso paanara tiyetida keethazo; nenakka Xoossi shoccana; wogara pirdana uttada wogay baayindda tana shoccana mala azazazi?” gidees.
He wode hen diza asay Phawulossa “Xoossa qeessista hallaqa cayazii?” gidees.
Phawulossaykka isttas “ta ishato! izi qeessista hallaqa gididayssa errabeykke; Gasooykka <he dere hallaqa bolla iitta qaala gooppa> gizayssi xaafetides” gides.
Phawulossay hen diza asape baggay Saduqqawista, baggay Parisawista gididayssa erridine “Ta ishto! ta Parisawepe yeelistadsine; takka parisawe hekko hai ta pirdistana shiiqiday hayqqidayti denddanayssa ta uhaaththaays ooththiza gishshasa” giidi ba qaala dhoqu histtidi duulata asa sinththan yootides.
Phawulossay hessa yootida mala Parisawista gidoonine Saduqqawista gidoon oshshi denddin duulatay nam77u shaaketi wodhdhides.
Gasooykka Saduqqaweti hayqqidaytas denththi deena, kitanchaykka bawa, ayanaykka dena gizayta, parisaweti qasse heyiti wurkka dettes gi ammanizayita.
Hessa wode daroo shiroy asa garssan haniddes; Parisawista baggata gidida issi issi Musse woga tamaarizayiti denddidi “nu hayssa addeza bolla aykokka iita mishsh demmibeykko; ayanay woyikko kitanchay izas yootida gidana; nu ay errizoni?” giidi palammettida.
Pallamay minni minni bida gish asay Phawulossa tarsherethonta mala babbidi halaqata azazizayssi “duge wodhdhidi Phawulossa asa gidoofe ha kessi ekki yitdi gede ola asati dizaso ehaaththaite!” giidi olla asa halaqata azazides.
Wonttetha gaalas giiddi giiddoth Goday Phawulossa achchan eqqidi “aykkoy ba ne Yerusalamen tas markkatidayssatho Romenkka ne tas markkatanas beses” gides.
Gadety wonttin ayhuda asati shiqettidi “nu phawulossa wodhdhontta dishe kathth mokko, haththekka uyookko” gi caaqettida.
Hessa he maqqozan isfe gidida asa qooday oyddu taamafe bollara dees.
Isttikka qeessista hallaqatakonne dere ciimatakko biidi isttas hizzgida “nu Phawulossa wodhdhontta dishe kathth montta mala minththi caaqqidos.
Hessa gidida gish inte dere ciimatara zooretidi iza keehi marammariza misatidi istti intes Phawulossa ehana mala azazizayssa oychchite; Nukka izi ha hano gakkanape kasetidi iza wodhdhana gigetidos.”
Gido attin issi Phawulossas michchi nay hessa istta maqqoza siyida gish wotadarati dizaso bi geellidi yooza Phawulossas yootides.
Phawulossaykka xeistata hallaqatape issa bekko xeeyigidi “hayssi nazi olla asa azazizayssas yootiza yoy diza gish gede izakko ehaaththaa gides.
Xeistata hallaqay naaza wana azazizayossakko ekki geellidi “qachchetida Phawulossay tana bekko xeeygidi hayssi naazi nes yootiza yooy diza gish ta iza neekko shishshana mala tana wossides” gides.
Azazizayssikka naaza kushshe oykki ekkidi haraso pooqidi “Ne tas yootanaysi azze?> giidi iza dumma oychchides.
Nazikka “ayhuda asati Phawulossa yooza loeththi maramarizade milatissidi wontto ne iza isttas shishshana mala oychchanas qachchi woththida.
Gido attin ne isttas erro gooppa; Gasooykka <nu iza wodhdhontta dishe kathth mokko haththeka uyokko> giidi caaqqettidayti oyddu taamafe bolla gidiza asi iza wodhdhanas ogge bolla zugges; Ha7i istti nagizay ne malithe xalala” gidees.
Azazizayssikka “ne hayssa tas yootidayssa hara oonnakka errissofa” giidi naaza mooyzzides.
Hessafe guye olanchata azazizayssi xeetu hallaqatape nam77ata xeeyigidi “qammape hedzdzu saate gidishin Qisariya gizaso bana mala nam77u xeetu olla asata, lappun taamu toga asstanne, nam77u xeetu toora asa gigissite.
Phawulossaskka paara gigissidi dere hariza filkkissekko loo7o gakkana mala oththite gides.
Dabbidabe hizgi xaafides;
“Deere harzza boncho Filkkisas, Qalawudossa Lusyyossappe; saarotethi nees gido.
Hayssa addeza Ayhuda asati oykki wodhdhana gishin izi Rome assi gididayssa ta gakka errida gish olla asatara gakkada ashshadis.
Istti iza aazas motizakonne ta errana koyada dere duulatakko shishshadis.
Istti iza bolla shishshida mootoy ba woga gish gididayssa erradis; Gido attin iza hayqqoss woykko qachcchos gaththiza miishshi denna.
Hayssa addeza wodhdhanas asay maqetidayssa ta siyada herakka siyida mala neekko yeedadis; mootizaytika hen ne sinththan ba mooto shishshana mala isttas yoottadis.”
Hessa gish olla asati ba azazetida mala Phawulossa qammara ehaaththaidi Anttiphaxxirosse getetizaso gaththida.
Wonttetha gallas toga asay Phawulossara baana mala oththidi istti qass guye soo simmida.
Toga asay gede Qisariya gakkidi dabbidabeza dere harizayssas immidi Phawulossa iza sinthth shishshida.
Deere harizayssi dabbidabeza nababidine Phawulossa “ne awa dereppe yadi?” gi oychchides; Izi Kilqqiya dere asi gididayssa erridi;
“Nena mootizayti yishin ta ne yoza siyana” gides; Herodossa gibbe *(Foot note) gaththan izi nagistana mala azazides.
Ichchachchu gaallassape guye qeessista hallqa hananiyay issi issi ciimatarane xerixxulossa geetettiza xabaqara qisariya bides; Isttikka dere ayssiza Filkkiseko shiiqidi Phawulossa mootida.
Phawulossay xeeygetti shiiqin Xerixxulossay iza hizzgi mootides “boncho Filkkise! nu ne baggara daroo sarooteth demmidos; ne loo7o aysonkka nu deres loo7etethth beettides.
Hessa ne loo7o oosoza nu awankka gidin aydekka gidin dhoqqu gida bonchorane galatara ekkoos.
Ta ha7i nena gam7isontanne nena daburissontta qanththara nees yootizayssa keyateththan ne nu giza siyana mala wossos.
Hayssi addezi nus iita hariige gididees; alamen diza Ayhudata wursio bolla meto medhdhes, nazirawe geettetiza wordo asata wanna kaallethizadey izakko.
Izi xoossa keeth tuunissana gishin nu iza oykkidos; nu woga mala nu iza bolla firdana qohaaththaidos.
Gido attin olla asa halaqata azazizayssi Lusiyossay gakkidi nu kushshepe iza wollqqara woththi ekkides.
Iza mootiza asaykka neekko yana mala azazides. Hayssi nu iza bolla shishshida mootozi wuri tummu gididayssa ne ne baggara iza oyychcha erranas dandda7asa.”
Hinkko Ayhuda asatikka “ee hayssi yoozi wurkka tummukko” giidi ammanettida.
Deere ayssiza filkkisey Phawulossay hasa7ana mala ba kushera malatti beesides; Phawulossaykka hizzgides “Ne daroo wodessoppe hayssa dereza ayssizade gididayssa ta erriza gish ta bolla shiiqida mootozas ta nes uhaaththaayssan malthe shishshayss.
Ta xoossas gooynnanas Yerusalame biin hachchi tammane namm7u gaallassape daroonttayssa ne ne baggara errana dandda7asa.
Xoossa keeththan gidin Ayhudata wossa keeththan woykko kaatama garssan ta oonnarakka palammettishin woykko dere gidoon meto medhdhishin tanna demmibeytenna.
Ha7i ta bolla istti shishshida mootozas ay markkaka shishshanas dandd7ettena.
Gido attin ta nes qonccisana koyzay istti wordo giza Goda ogera nu aawantta Xoossas gooynayssine Musse wogane nabeta maxxahaaththaan xahaaththaetidayssaka wursia ammanayss.
Isttikka uhaaththaayssi ooththiza mala takka nagaranchatine xiilloti hayqqope denddanayssa Xoossan ammanetays.
Hessa gish Xoossa sinththanine asa sinththan sidhdhey bayndda hanoy tas daana mala wursio wode minnays.
Ta Yerussalamepe kezin tas daroo layth gididappe guye ta dere asas maado mishshene Xoossas immetiza mishshe ekka yadis.
Tana istti xoossa keeththan demmiday ta hessa gaththishinkko; He wode ta geeyza woga pollishin tanara daroo asine deenna, oshshine shiroykka deenna.
Gido attin Isyyape yida issi issi Ayhuda asati dettes; isttaskka tana mootos gaaththizaz diza gidikko ne sinththan tana mooteto.
Hessafe guye ta duulata sinthth shiiqikko ta ooththida qohooy diikko he asati yooteto.
Tana hayssas gaaththida gasooy ta istta gidoon eqqada <hayqqidaytas denththi dees ga yootida gish hachchi pirdas inte sinthth shiiqadis> ta gaada qaala dhoqu histta yootadis attin hara ta oththida miishshi deena.”
Filkisey Goda oge loo7ethi erriza gish “ola asata halaqata azazizayssa Lusyyossay yiza wode ta inte yooza gish qachcho gidiza yoo immana” giidi istta yeeddides.
Phawulossa naggiza xeetu olla asa hallaqay “iza daroo wayisontta loo7etha nagga; iza laggeeti izas koshshiza miishshi ekki yiikko diggofa” gides.
Guuththa wodepe kaallidi Ayhuda ass gidida ba machchiyo Dirusilara yides; phawulossaka xeeyigidi Yesuss Kiristossan ammano gish izi yootishin siyides.
Phawulossay xiillotetha gishine asi berkka bena haaro gishene burope yaana pirda gish yootin Filikisey babbidi “Ha7i ne ba; hara wode tas gigishin ta nena xeeyga ekkana” gides.
Filikisey Phawulossape gubbo ekkanas uhaaththaayssi ooththi naggida gish daroo wode gakkanaas xeeyigi xeeyigi hasa7isides.
Namm7u laythafe guye Phorqiyosa Fisxxosay Filikise ollan shuumetides; Filikisey Ayhudista uhaaththaayssanas koyidi Phawulossa qachchosoon aggagides.
Fisxxossay ba ayssiza dere Qissariya gellidi hedzdzu gallas aqqetidi heppe Yerusalame bides.
Hen diza qeessata hallaqatine issi issi Ayhudista garssafe gita gita asati Phawulossa bolla ba mooto shishshida; “Phawulossa ha Yerusalame ehidi nus loo7o ooso oththarkki” giidi wossida; istti hessa giday Phawulossa naagidi oge bolla wodhdhanas kooyda gishaskko.
<range>
Gido attin Fisxxossay “Phawulossay Qissariyan qachcho keeththan naggetes; takka ha7i elle simmada he izakko baana.
Inte garssafe dannateth dizaytti tanara Qissariya beeto; Phawulossay oththida qohoy diza gidikko hen mooteto” gides.
Fisxxossay osppun woykko tammu gaallassafe daroontta wode isttara gamm7idi guye Qissariya bides; He gakkida mala wonttetha gallas pirda wombbora bolla uttidi Phawulossa izakko shishshana mala azazides.
Phawulossay iza sinthth shiiqin Yerussalamepe yida Ayhudati Phawulossa giddothidi markkay bayndda daroo deexxo mooto iza bolla shishshida.
Phawulossaykka “Tani Ayhuda woga bolla gidin Xoossa keeththa bolla woykko Rome kawoo Qessare bollaka gaaththida qoohoy deena” giidi istta mootoza shaariza mallththe isttas immides.
Gido attin Fisxxossay Ayhudata uhaaththaayssanas koyidi Phawulossa “Ne Yerusalame baada hayssa yooza hen ta sinththan pirdistana koyazii?” gides.
Phawulossay qasse hizzgidi izas zaarides “Hekko ta pirdistanas tas bessiza Qessare pirda wombbara sinththan eqqadis; nekka loo7etha erriza mala ta Ayhudata bolla ooththida aykko qoohoy deena.
Ta qoohida gidikko woykko tana hayqqos gaaththiza qooho ta ooththida gidikko ta hayqoppe attana giike; Gido attin istti shishshiza mootoy mela hada gidiko oonikka tana isttas aththi immanas dandda7ena; Takka ta yooy Qeessare sinthth shiiqana mala yigibaayne gadis.”
Hessa wode Fisxxossay bena zoorizayitara hasa7etidi “ne Qeessareko yigibaayne giza gidiko Qeessareko baanddassa” gides.
Guuththa gaallassatape guye kawoo Agirphphayne Barniqey Fisxxossa “Hashshu loo7on yadassa” gi mokkanas gede Qissariya bida.
Istti hen daroo galas uttida gish Fisxxossay Phawulossa yooza kawoo Agirphphas hizzgi yootides “Filkisey qaachcho kethan yegi agiida issadey haan dees.
Ta Yerusalamen bida wode qeessista hallaqatinne Ayhudata ciimmati ha addeza yoo taako ehidi ta iza bolla pirdana mala oychchida.
Ta qasse mootetidadey mootizayta sinththan eqqidi bena mootiza yoozas beessiza malththe immontta dishin mootetidade aththi immooy Rome kawootethas woga gidena” gaada zaaradis.
Hessa gish iza mootizayti shiiqetidi yida mala herakka wonttetha gallas pirda wombboran uttada Phawulossa ta sinthth shishshana mala azazadis.
Iza mootizayti iza achchan eqqida wode istti iza bolla shishshida mootoy ta baggara izi iitta oothontta agena gaada qopida mala gidibeyna.
Gido attin istti izara mootetizay ba ammano gishshine Phawulossay issi hayqqidade <Paxa dees> giza Yesussa gish gidides.
Takka hessa mala yoo qora xeellanas tana metida gish Phawulossa <Ne Yerusalame baada heyssa yooza hen pirdistana koyyaz?> gadis.
Hizzgin izi qasse yoozi Rome kawoo sinththan beyistana mala koyidi <ta yooy Qeessare sinthth shiiqana mala oychchayss> gida gish iza yoo Qeessarekko ta yeeddana gakkanaas izi qachcho keeththan gamm77ana mala azazadis.”
Agirphphay Fisxxossa “Takka izi giza siyana koyayss” gides; Fisxxossaykka “Wontto siyanddassa” gides.
Hessa gish wonttetha gallas Agirphphayne Barniqey kawooti mayiza mayo maydine daro bonchora ola asa halaqatarane he kaataman diza giita asatan azhabbeti yiidi pirda keeth gellida. Hessafe guye Fisxxossay Phawulossa xeeyigisides.
Fisxosay hizzgides “Kawoo Agirphpha! qass nunara diza asato; Ayhuda asati wuri <hayssi addezi hayssafe guye paxxa daana beessena> giidi wassishe Yerussalamenkka haanikka iza bolla pirdistana mala istti tana oychchizay hayssa inte beeyiza addeza gishshaskko.
Ta ta boggara iza hayqqos gaaththiza issi balakka iza bolla demmabeyikke. Izi ta yooy Rome kawoo sinthth shiiqi beeyeto gida gish ta iza he yeeddanas qachchadis.
Gido attin iza gish ta ta godas xaahaaththaana giza errettida yoy deena; Hessa gish iza issi issi pacce oychchota oychchiko tas xaahaaththaanaysi daanakkone gaada inteko; harapekka kawoo Agirphpha neekko shishshadis.
Gasooykka qachcho assi puude bollattiza dhoqqa dannakko bishin izi mootetiza yo qonccisontta aggoy asa eyya kessizayssi tas bettides.”
Agirphphay Phawulossa “ne ne gish hasa7anas dandda7assa> gides. Phawulossaykka ba kushe denthidi malththe hizgi immides.
“Kawoo Agirphpha! tana Ayhudati moootiza yoo wursisos hach ta ne sinththan tana maadana malththe immiza gish tana daroo ufayses.
Gasoyka ne Ayhudata wogane istta palama wursia looetha errasa; Hessa gish ne ta giza wursia dandda7ada siyana mala ta nena wosays.
“Tani guuththa nateththa wodeppe oykkada waana deydakko Ayhuda asati erretes. Koyrope ha7i gakkanaas ta ta dere asa gidoonine Yerusalamen ta deyda duussu asay erres.
Qassekka istti markkatana koykko nu ammano gish ta keha minththa woga naggiza Parsawe bagga gidada gamm7idade gididayssa istti koyrope denththidi erretes.
Ha7i qasse pirdas tana hayssan essiday Xoossi kasse nu aawatas immida caaqqo qaala uhaaththaayssa gishaskko.
Ha uhaaththaayssako gakkanaas nu zarkketi taammane namm7ati Xoossa gaallasine qamma goyinnishe naggida. Kawo nees too! takka Ayhudati tana mootizay ha yoza gishaskko.
Xoossi hayqqidayta denththanayssi wannidi Ayhuda gidida inte achchan ammanetibeyne?
Takka ta baggara Nazirete Yesussa sunththa eqqistanas beses gada qoppadis shin;
Tani Yerusalamen ooththidaykka hessakoshin; Qeessista hallaqqatape ta ekkida godateththara ammanizaytape daroota qasho keeththan yegiissadis; istta wodhdhishin wodhdhizaytara isfe days.
Daro wode Ayhudata wossa keethati dizason awankka istti qaaxxayistana malanne ba ammano kadana mala ooththadis; Istta bolla daro hanqqistadakka Isra7eleppe karen diza hara kaatamatakka baada ammanizayta goodadis.
“Hayssa ha yoozas Qeessista hallaqatappe kummetha godateththine azazo ekkada dammasqqo gizaso ta bishin;
Kawoo nes too! Buroo ta ogen dishin gadey seeta gallas gidishin awa arshe poo7oppe adhdhiza poo7o beyadis; He poo7oy tanane tanara biza asata yuuy adhdhidi salope po7ides.
Nu wurkka biita bolla kundidishin Ayhudata qaalara <Sawulle! Sawulle! tana aazas goddazi? Neni qara maashsha bolla eqqiikko nerkka nena qohasa> giza qaala siyadis.
Takka <Godo! ne oonne?> Gadis; Godaykka <Ta ne Goda Yesussako!
Ha7i denddada ne toon eqqa; ta nes qoncciday ne tana ha7i beyidaysanine sinththafe ta nena beessanayssan ne tas markkatizade gidana mala ta nena shuumana koyadis.
Isra7ele asa kushepene ta nena isttakko kittiza Ayhuda gidoontta dere asata kusheppekka ashshana.
Ne istta ayfe doyana malane dhumape poo7on kessana mala qassekka xalla7es harettizasope Xoossakko ne zaarana mala ooththana; isttikka tana ammanida gish ba nagarappe marettana qasse dorettidayta giddon istti laata gade demana> gidees.
“Hessa gish kawoo Agirphpha! Salope tas immetida ajjutas ta azazettadis.
Gido attin ta kassistada Dammasqqon diza asa kaaliethada Yerussalamenine Yuhuda deren wursion dizayta qassekka Ayhuda gidoontta deretikka nagare ogeppe Xoossakko simmidi maretna mala erisadis. Istti nagarappe simmidayssa beessizayssa ooththana mala ta isttas yootadis.
Hessa gaason Ayhudati ta Xoossa keeththan dishin tana oykkidi wodhdhana koyda.
Hachch gakkanaaskka tas Xoossafe maadoy pacci errena. Hesa gish guuththaskka gitaskka markkatashe hayssan eqqadis. Nabetinne Mussey kassetidi hayssa malay hanana gidayssa yootope attin ta hara aykkokka yootabeykke.
Isttikka yootidaysi <Xoossi kittidadey meto beeyana, hayqqope denddon koyro gididi, asi attana poo7o Isra7ele deresinne Isra7ele nayta gidontta deretas qonccana> gizayssakko.”
Phawulossay hessa yootishin Fisxxossay “Phawulossa! ha7i ne gooyyontta aggakka; ne daro taamaridayssi nena goshshides” gi wassides.
Phawulossay gidikko izas hizzgi zaarides “boncho Fisxxossa! ta nes tuma erada yootayss attin goyabeyke.
Ta iza sinththan qonccera yootida kawooy hayssa yooza erres; hayssikka qootara ooththetonttayssa gidida gish kawooy erranayssa ta ammanetayss.
Kawoo Agirphpha! nabeta ammanasa gidikki? ne ammanizayssa ta errayss.”
Agirphphaykka Phawulossa “Hekko ne tana hanno guuththa wode garssan ammanthana koyasa” gides.
Phawulossakka izas zaaridi “guuththa woden gidinkka woykko daro woden ne xalla gidontta dishin hach ta yootidayssa siday wuri hanno ta qachcheteththia atta wurikka ta mala gidana mala ta Xoossa wossayss” gides.
Hessafe guye kawooy, dere ayssizaysi, Barnqanne isttara uttida asaykka wuri denddides.
Istti hepe kezi bishe ba garssan hays addezi hayqqos woykko qachchos gaththiza mishshe aykokka ooththibeyna” gida.
Agirphphaykka Fisxxossa “hayssi addezi yooza Qessares shiiqo gonttako aykko woththoy bayndda mela yedistanako shin” gides.
Nuni Xaallane dere markkaben baana mala geeteti qachchetida gish Phawulossane hara qachcho asatakka kawoo Awugisxxossa ola wotadarata gidoofe gidida Yulliyossa geetettiza xeetu halaqas aththi immida.
Issiya abba achan diza dereta biza markkaben gillidi bidos. Tesellonqqen diza issi Maqidonyya asi Arisxxirokossa geetettizadey nunara dees.
Wonttetha gallas sidona gizaso gakkidos; Yulliyossay Phawulossas loo7o gidida gish Phawulossay ba laggetakko biidi asay izas koshshiza maado ooththana mala piqade immides.
Heepe danddi nu bishin sinththa baggara carkkoy nu bolla carkkiza gish abba gidoon diza Qophphorosse deren gemmetidi gede sinththe bidos.
Killqqiya gizassone Phinhaaththailiya giza dere achchan diza abba pinddi Luqqiya giza deren diza Muura giza kaatama gakkidos.
Heen xeistata hallaqay Xallane dere biza iskkinddiriya dere markkabe demmidi nuna izan gellithides.
Daroo gallas loddu gi gi biidi daroo wayettidi Qandose geetettiza kaatama achchi gakkidos; Carkkoykka nu sinthth boontta mala diggin Sallimoon achchara adhdhidi Qarxxese geetettiza abba gidoon diza haruro deren gemettidi bidos.
Daroo wayettidi dira dira oykki nu adhdhidape guye Lasyya giza kaatama achchan diza “Loo7o” geetettiza markabe getetizaso gakkidos.
Nu biza oge bolla daroo dabuuran xooma wodey adhdhida gish ha7i abba bolla baanas daroo meeto gidida gish Phawulossay benara diza asay naggettana mala hizzgides.
“Aso! hayssafe nu kaallidi baana buussay daroo meetora dizayssi tas beettes; Markkabezan diza caanaza bollanne markkabeza bolla xalala gidoontta asa shemppo bollaka gita qohooy gakkana.”
Xeistata halaqay qass Phawulossa zoreppe bollara markkabeza lagiza wanazinne marakabeza goday gizayssa siyides.
He markkabey eqqizasoy ballggoy adhdhana gakkanaas markkabes loo7o shempposo gidoontta gish dariza bagga asay “hammutha sinthth gujjanas dandda7ettiko away wullizasope duge baggarane puude baggara diza Pinqqe gizaso Qarxeese markkabe shempposo nu gakkidi ballggo heen aaththos” giidi ba qoofa shishshida.
Duge baggara guuththa carkkooy carkkishin beeyidi istti qoppida mala hanana millattin baana kezida; Markkabey eqqizasope baana denddidi qarxxeese achchara dira dira oykkidi adhdhi bida.
Gido attin guuththa wodepe guye “Away mokkizasope puude bagara yiza gote carkko” geetettiza iita wolliqama carkkoy abba gidoon diza dereype denddidi isttakko abba gidoo yides.
Markkabeya carkkoy sugin carkkara eqqeettana dandda7ontta ixxin nu coou giidi carkkoy ehaaththaizaso bidos.
Qeeda geetettiza abba gidoon diza dere dizarin geemettidi nu bishin daroo wayettidi markkabeza qeeri wogoloyo oykkidi essanas dandda7idos.
Markkabeza laaggizayti qeeri wogoloyo markkabezako goochchi keessidi markkabeza woodorora xaxxida. Markkabezikka Surtese geetettiza abba accey dari dizason kunddontta mala babbidi iza bolla diza shaara woththidi carkkon laageti bida.
Gote carkkoy miinni bida gish wonttetha gallas markkkabezan caanettida miishshata issa issa abba gidoo yeggeth oykkida.
Hedzdzanththo gallas markkabezas koshshiza miishshatakka ba kushera kessi kessi yeggida.
Daroo wode gakkanaas awa arsheka xoolintteka beyontta aggida gishinne carkkoyka kasseppe miinni miinni biza gish hayssafe guye nu attana dandda7okko giza qohaaththaan ufays qanxidos.
Asay kathth moontta daro gallas uttides. Hessa gish phawulossay asa gidoon eqqidi hizgides “ha asato! Inte ta giza siyidi Qarxxeseppe denddonttako ha qohoyne ha dhayoy inte bolla gakkenakoshin.
Ha7ikka markkabezi xalla qohettana attin intefe issade shempoykka dhayenna. Hessa gish aykkoy bawa; babbofite gaada intena zorayssl.
Qamma omars ta izas gidida ta goynniza Xoossi kittida kitanchay ta achchan eqqidi
<Phawulosa! Babbopa ne Qeessare sinththan eqqana beeses; hekko nenara isfe bizayta wurssi Xoossi ne gish hayqqope ashshana> giidi tas yootides.
Hessa gish inteno asato aykkoy bawa; Xoossi tas hayssa yootidayssa polanayssa ta ammanayss.
Gidikokka hayssa gote carkkozi gede issi abba gidoon diza dere achchi ehaaththaidi nuna yeggana.”
Taammanne oyddanththo qaamma Mediterane abba gidoon carkkoy nuna wayssishin bishe gidi giddothi markkabeza lagaizaytas abbafe biita bolla gakkida millatides.
Hessa gish abba ciimmmateth erranas abban yeggi xeelliza wodoro istti yeggi xeellishin; abba ciimmatethi oyddu taamu mitire keena gidi beettides; gammishe haikka yeggin hedzdzu taamu mitire keena ciimma gididayssa demmida.
Nu diza markkabey abba gaxxan diza zaalla shuchchara gaccetontta mala babbidi markkabezappe guye baggara markkabey qaxxontta mala nagiza dhishshike duge abba gidoo yeggida. Hessafe guye isttas qamay wonttana mala woossa oykida.
Markabeza lagizayti markkabezape kezidi baqqatana koyda gish markkabezappe sinththa baggara markkabe naggiza dhishshke yegiza millatidi markkabeza bolla diza qeeri wogoloyo duge aabba gidoo yeggida.
Hessa wode phawulossay xeetu olla asa hallaqane olla asa wotadarata “hayti markkabezan diza asati markkabeza bolla shemppidi uttontta aggiko intekka attana dandda7ekkista” gides.
Hessa gish olla asati wogoloyo oykkida wodoroza qanxxi yeggin iza abba bolla tookistana mala yeedi aggida.
Gadey wonttana gishin wurikka kathth maana mala phawulossay istta hizzgi wossides “inte aazi hananesha giidi hirgan kathth moontta aaggin hachchi taammane oyddanththo gaallaskko.
Hessa gish inte kathth maana mala ta intena wossayss. Inte miikko miinnana; muleka aykko qohoykka inte bolla gakkena.”
Izi hessa gidape guye kathth ekkidi xoossu galatidi asa wursso sinththan kaath muussu oykkides.
Hessa wode wurikkka minetidi kaththi mida.
Markkabeza gidoon diza asay wuri nam77u xeistane laapun taammanne usupuna.
Wurikka mi kaallidape guye markkaben caanetida gistteza duge abba gidoo yeggidi markkabeza deexo kawushshida.
Gadey wonttin ba dizaso erribeytena. Gido attin accEy dizaso abba kirqqunththu demmida. Isttas dandda7etizako markkabeza he sugi shishshana qoppida.
Markkabeza oykkiza dhishike qanxidi aabba gidoo yeggida. He wode markkabe laggiza wodorota birshida. Ha baggara diza shaara carkko bagga dhoqu histtidi kezana abba gaxa bida.
Gido attin markkabeza droo accey koreti uttidayssara iccetidi duge gufaniddes.; Siidhe bolla duge dhishshiketidi qaxxonttayssa giddies. Qass abba dambbalay daroope denddidayssan guye baggara meqqereteth oykkides.
Qachcho asappe isadeykka abban wodhdhidi kessi ekkontta mala olla asati wodhana qoppida.
Xeistata hallaqay qass Phawulossa ashshanas koyda gish istta qohaaththaa ekkana koybeyna. Gido attin haththe waadhi errizayti markkabezape duge abban guppi guppi woodhdhidi gede biita bolla kezana mala azazides.
Hinkko attidayti qass sanqqata bollane markkabepe meeqqi wodhdhida sanqqa bolla abba pinnanamala azazides; hessaththo handdi wurikka saaron abba gidoofe biita bolla gakkida.
Nu biittay dizaso saarotethan gakkidape guye nu gakkida abba gidoon diza derey malta geetettizaro gididaro erridos.
He dereyin diza asay daroo malaliza keyateth nus ooththides. He wode iray bukkida gishine meego gidida gish tama eththidi nuna mokki ekkida.
Phawulossay ahaaththaira miithth shishshidi taaman gujin taama seelappe denddidayssan shoshshi kezidi iza kushe bolla xaaxxetides.
Malta asay shoshshi Phawulossa kushe bolla xaaxxetidayssa beeyidi “hayssi addezi shemppo wodhdhidade; gasooykka abba bullahepekka izi attidi yikokka pirdiza Xoossafe kessi ekkidi paxxa daana dandda7ebeyna” giidi ba garssan hasa7ettida.
Phawulossay qass shoshsha duge taman qooqofi yeegidi aykokka hanibeyna.
Asaykka “Aydepe ayde iza asatethay kixxanesha, woykko qoopontta kundidi hayqqana” giidi naggides; Gido attin istti daroo wode naggishin iza bolla aykkoyne hanonttayssa beeyidi ba qoofa lammidi “hayssi addezi Xoossa” gides.
He nu dizaso matan abba gidoon diza dereyo ayssiza Puppulyyosa geetettizadees gadey des; he addezi nuna mookki ekkidi besoon hedzdzu gallas gakkanaas loo7ethi imatides.
Heeni Puppulyyosa aawa michchayinne guso harrigey sakkin zinniidi des; Phawulossay izakko gellidi izas wossidesinne iza bolla kushe woththidi paththides.
Hessi hessaththo hanidape guye he dereyin diza hara harriganchati yiidi paxxida.
Asaykka nus daroo mishshe ehidi nuna bonchizayssa nuna bessida; nu markkaben baana denddin nus koshshizayssa markkaben wursi caandda.
Nu maltan hedzdzu aggina gammidape guye ballggoy adhdhana gakkanaas abba gidoon diza dereyin gammiidi Iskindiryappe yiza markkaben gellidi baana denddidos; He markkabeza bolla Diyossiqqorossa geetettiza nam77u mentte eqqata mislley dees.
Gede Sirakkose geetettiza kaatama gakkidi heen hedzdzu gallas gammidos.
Heepe abba bollara biidi Regiyome geetettiza kaatama gakkidos; Heen issi gallas aqidi duge baggara yiza carkkoy carkkida gish nam77anththo gallas Putiyolusa geetettizaso bidos.
Heen ammanizayta demmidi isttara nu lappun gallas gakkanaas uttana mala nuna wossida. Heeppe qasse Rome bidos.
Romen diza ammaniza asay nu gish siyidi Ahaaththaiyossa geetettiza giyane “hedzdzu aqoso” geetettizaso gakkanaas nuna mookkana yida; phawulossaykka ista beeydi Xoossu galatidesinne minetides.
Nuni Rome gelida wode Phawulossa naganas issi wotadaray izas immettin Phawulossay berkka daana mala izas fiiqadey immettides.
Hedzdzu gaallassafe guye Phawulossay Romen diza Ayhudatape gita asata beekko xeeyigisides; isttikka izakko shiiqin hizzgides “Ta ishato! tani isiraele dere bollane nu aawata woga bolla ooththida issi qohooykka deena; Gido attin yerussalamen tana qachchidi Rome asatas aththi immida.
Rome asati tana qori oychchidappe guye tana hayqos gaththiza mishshe demmontta aggida gish birshi yeedana koyida.
Shin Ayhude asay ta issi wothoy bayindda yeedetontta mala eqqettin ta yooy Qeessare sinthth shiiqidi beetto gaanas tas gidde giddies. Gido attin tani ta dereta mootiza gasoy tas deena.
Ta qass ha7i intena xeeygisiday intena beeyanasine haanno intes yootanaskko. Hayssa sanssalatan ta qachchetiday isiraele naytas immettida uhaaththaayssa gasoonkko.
Isttikka izas hizzgi zaarida “Ne gish Yuhuda derepe xaahaaththaettida debidabey nuna gakkibeyina. Ha yida asatape oonikka ne gish iita hasa7iday baawa.
Hayssa ne kaalliza ammanoza gish awankka asay iitta hasa7izaysa nu erros. Hessa gish ne qoohaaththaay azakkone nu siyana koyos” gida.
Bare izas immidi hara gallas kushe kumidi izi diza keeth yida. Izikka maladoppe omarss gakkanaas Xoossa kawootetha gish markkatethan ba qohaaththaa isttas qonccisides. Musse wogappene nabeta maaxxahaaththaatape xaqqasi xaqqasi Yesussa gish isttas gellththi yootides.
Isttafe issi issi asati izi yootida qaala ammanida; Bagayti qass ammanibeytena.
Isttikka ba garssan issay issara qohaaththaan gaggontta shakketida; Phawulossay wurssethan yootishe hizzgides “xiillo ayanay nabe isyyasa baggara kasse inte aawatas yootidayssi tumakko.
Izi yootida qaalay hizzges <Hayssa deerakko baada inte sissi siyana shin yushshi qoppekista, ayfera beeyana shin wozinan woththekista gaada yoota.
Gasooykka he asata wozinay mumides, istta hayththeykka tuullides; istta ayfey qoqides. Hessaththo hanonttakko istti ba ayfera beeydi ba heyththera siyidi ba wozinan yushshi qoppidi taakko ha simmanane takka istta paththanashin.>
Histtikko Xoosi asi ashshiza kittay ayhuda gidoontta deretaskka kitteetdayssa inte errit; Isttikka erro giidi ekkettes.”
Phawulossay hessa yootidappe guye Ayhuda asati ba garssan daroo pallametishe kezi bida.
Phawulossay kiratida keeththan nam77u laythth kumethth de7ides; Beekko yiza asa wursii mokki ekkides.
Xoossa kawooteth sabbakkon Goda Yesuss Kiristtossa gish oonikka iza diggontta xalatethara asa taamarisides.
Yesus Kiristoosa ayllene haware gidanasi xeygettida mishiracho qaala yootanaas kiitettida taape Phawulossape kiitettida kiita.
He mishshiracho qaala gishshi kase nabeta baggara geesha maxaafatan ufaysi immetides.
Mishshiracho qaalaykka ba naza gishshi izi asho baggara Dawite zereththafe gididayssa yootiza gishshikko.
Hessaththoka nu Goda Yesusi kirstoosay ba Geeshatetha ayanan hayqope denddidaysi izi Xoossa na gididayssi gita wolqan qonccides.
Kirirstoosa sunththa gishshi ammanontta derey ammanana malane azazistana mala iza baggara nuni hawaratethas gathiza kiyateth ekkidos.
Inteka Yesus Kirisitoosayta gidana mala xeygetidaytara deista.
Xoossan dosetidaytanne geeshata gidanaas xeygetida Orome biittan diza intes wurisos nu Aawa Xoossafene nu Goda Yesus kirstoosape kiyatethine sarotethi intes gido.
Inte ammanoy alame kumethan siyettida gishshine inte gishshi ta Godaa Xoossa, Yesus Kiristoosa baggara galatays.
Ta inte gishshi wuriso wode ay mala qopizakone Xoossa na mishshiracho sabakoni ta izas oothiza ta Xoossi taasi marika.
Tani ta woosan wuriso wode intena qopoysa. Ha7i qasse wurisethan Xoossa shene gidiko ta inteko baana mala Xoossi taas oge doyana mala woossays.
Inte minnana mala maadiza ayana imotethi ta intes shakanassine intena ayfera beyanas laamotays.
Heskka intenine tan issay issa amnanon ministanaskko.
Ta ishato harason ammanontayta matan taas hanida mala inte matanika taas ooso ayfey beettana mala daro wode qopadisi shin haanno gakanaas ta digistada dizaysa inte erana mala koyays.
Tamaridaytas gidin tamarontayskka, eratasine eeyatas wurisos ta bolla tamarssana accoy dees.
Intes Oromen dizaysatasika ta mishshiracho qaala yootanas ta amotizay hessaskko.
Aammanizayti wuri attana mala Xoossa woliqa gidida gishshi ta mishshiracho qaalan yeelattike; Hesika koyro ayhudatas kallidi hanko dere asaskko.
“Xilloy Xoossa ammanon deyees” geetetidi kase xaafetida mala Xoossa xiilloteth mishshiracho qaalan qonccina; He xiillotethay koyrope wurisetha gakanaas ammanon hanana.
Tuma, ba iittatethaninne makali7an tucii oykizayta iittatetha bollan istta makall7atetha wuriso bolla Xoossa hanqoy sallope qoncana.
Istti eranas bessizazi Xooss wursi isttas qoncisida gishshi Istti Xoossu eranaas qoncceko.
Alamey medhettosope haa simmini asa ayfen beetti erontta Xoossa hanotethi hesika izas diza medhina woliqayne Xoossatethay izi medhida medhetethan qonicen bettees. Hessa gishshi asay shiishana gaasoy deena.
Istti Xoossu erikoka iza, iza Xoossatetha mala bonchibeytenane galatibeyttena. Gido attin istta qofay mela go7ay baynidazi gididesine yuushi qopontta mala istta wozinay dhumides.
Istti bena era gizayta gidikkoka eeyata gidida.
Medhina Xoossa boncho hayqqiza asanine kafotan, mehistanine biitta bolla goochettiza medhetethatan milatissidi laammida.
Hessa gishshi Xoossi istta ba garssan issay issara berkka ba asatethan tuna ootho oothana mala geeshshatethi bayndda laymmatethas aathi immides.
Istti Xoossa tumateth wordon laammida; medhdhida Xoossa olla medhdhetethas goynnidanne isttas oothida. Medhdhida Xoossi izi medhdhinas galatettidayssa; amin77i.
Hessa geedon Xoossi istta yelachiza amotethas aathi immides. Istti macasati benara zin7anas besontaytara zin7ana mala bena aathi immida.
Hessaththoka attuma asay bees bessiza macasatara zin7anaas bessishin addey addera zin7anaas amon xuugetidi macasatara zin7iza mala addery addera zin7idi pala miishshi oothida. Heytanti berka ba oothida iitta oothozas bessiza qixaate ba bolla ehida.
Qasseka istti ba qofara Xoossu eroy nuna maaddena gida gishshi istti oothanaas besonttayssa oothana mala Xoossi istta go7ontta qofas aathi immides.
Wuriso baggara makali7ane iittateth, yiiqene iitta oothon xalala kumida; qanatetethan, shemmipo wodhon, ooshshan, balethoninne genen kumidayta qasseka zigirizayta gidida.
Asa sunthu moorizayta, Xoossu ixxizayta, ase cayzata, otoronchatanne ceeqettizayta gidida, wuriso wode iitta oothanas oge koyzayta, bena yelidaytas azazetontayta,
Yuushshi qopontayata, gida qaala zaari lallizayata, asas michchetontayta menxxe iittata.
Hessa oothizayti wurikka hayqqanaas besses giza Xoossa woga istti erishe heytantta bees ootho xalala gidontta hessathoka oothizaytakka minithetheetes.
Hessa gishshi neno hara bolla piridizayso neni ta hanni geedon oothadisi gaada gaasoy neesi deena. Ne hara ura bolla piiridizayssan nerika nees kunane ekkaasa. Gaasoykka hara ura bolla ne piridizaysa neka zaarada iza oothiza gishaskko.
Hayta malata oothiza asata bolla Xoossa piriday liike gididayssa nu erossi
Hesa gishshi ne asa bolla piridashe he ne piiridizasa zaara oothizade gidiko ne Xoossa piiridafe kessa eka attana nees millatizee?
woykko Xoossa kiiyatethi nena marotethako kallithizaysa shaaka erontta dashe iza gita kiiyatethane iza danida7a duretetha ne liiqazii?
Gido attin neni ne wozina mumetethanine marotethi koyontta ne wozina geedon tuma Xoossa piiriday qoniciza wode Xoossa hanqo gallasa ne daro hanqqo shiishshasa.
Xoossi isi isi uras iza ootho mala immana.
Lo7o ootho aggontta oothidi boncho sabane medhina dusi koyzaytas miidhina deyo immana.
Gido attin berika bena dosizaytasine tuma agagidi iitta kallizayta bolla piiridayne hanqoy gakana.
Itita oothiza ay asa bolla koyro Ayhude asa bolla kaallid hanko hara dere asa bolla wayeyne metoy gakana.
Gidikkoka lo7o oothizades oonasika Ayhuda asas gidin hankko dere asas sabay, sarotethinne bonchoy gidana.
Xoossi oonaka shaakk maaddena.
Kase wogay eqontta wode nagara oothida asay wurikka wogay bayinida dhayana. Wogay eqi simmini nagara oothidayti wogan oyketidi piiridistana.
Aysi gikko Xoossa achan xiillo geetettizayti eqida wogaas azazetizaytape attin woga sisi siyzayta gidetena.
Wogay baynida dere asati wogay yootizaysa coo mela hanotethafe eridi oothishin isttas wogay baynida agikokka isttas medhetetha wogay diza gishshi istti ba oothanayssa ereetes.
Istta wozinay isttas marikatiza gishine istta qofay istta mootiza gishshi qasseka istta maaddiza gishshi wogay yootizay istta wozinan xaafetidayssa ereetes.
Hesikka ta mishshiracho qaalan tamarssiza mala Xoossi asa wizinan qotetidayssa Kirisitoosa baggara piiridiza gallasan qoniccana.
Ne nena Ayhuda asi gikko wogan ammanetasane neesi Xoossara diza issipetethan ceeqetaasa.
Woga kaalliza gishshi Xoossa shene erada kumethi gidizazi shaakka erida gidiko
Ne qoqista kallethizade dhuman dizaytas poo7o gididaysa ne amanetidade gidiko
Wogape ne demida eratethaninne tumatethan hankko eronitayta zorizade, guutha nayitta tamarisizade gidikko
Histiko neni harata tamariso agada ne hu7es aazas tamarikii? Ne hara ura kaysottopa ga sabakashe neesi kaysotazii?
Ne hara asay laymatontta mala yootashe nees laymaytazii? Nees Eeqa ixxasashin Xoossa keeththa miisha bonqqazii?
Neesi wogan ceeqetasa shin woga ne baggara oothontta aggada Xoossa kawushizii?
Hesikka “Inte geedon Xoossa sunthi hanko dere asa achan cayetesi” geetetti xaafetida mala hanides.
Ne woga naaga pollizade gidiko qaxaras goo7ay dees. Ne wogaa oothonttade gidiko qasse ne qaxaray coo melakko.
Qaxaretontta dishe wogaa gizaysa polliko qaxaretidadera gina qodetenee?
Nees xaafeti wogayne qaxaray nees diikko diza woga ne nagonttade gidikko hanko qaxaretontta wogas azazetiday ne bolla piridana.
Issade coo mela sunthas asa ayfen ta Ayhuda asi gidana gikko izi Ayhuda asi gidena. Tumape qaxeretethi coo karera asho ayfeni bettiza qaxxara gidena.
Gidikkokka issi uray Ayuda asa gidanaas danda7izay izas gaatha baggara Ayude asa gidishinkko. Qaxarayka qaxara gidizay xaafetida wogaa xalala gidontta ayanan wozinape gidida qaxxara gidikokka hessa mala assi galata asape gidontta Xoossafe demmees.
Histinko Ayude asa gidethasi aaza go7ay dizee? Qaxaray ay go7izee?
Awaraka gidin go7ay daro. Harape koyro Xoossa qaalay hadara Ayudatasi immetides.
Isttafe issi issi uras ammanoy baynida aggiko Xoossa ammanotethi diigizee?
Mulekka diggena! Asi wurikka woridancha “Neni ne qaalape denidayssan tumanicha; Piridanika xonizade gidaasa” hessaththo geeteti xaafettida mala Xoossi qasse tumanicha.
Nu makali7a oothoy Xoossa xiillotethi qonccen besiizayssa gidikko hisitini nu ay ganee? Coo asa woga mala palamistanas Xoossi ba hanqqo nu bolla ehizaysi nuusu bessena ganeyee? Hesaka ta giizay asatho qofankko.
Tumape hessaththo hanena. Hesatho haniza gidiko Xoossi alame bolla wostti piiridanidee?
Ta woridotethi Xoossa tumatethi qonccisizayssan iza bonicho gede gujiizassa gidikko hisitin ha7i gakanas wostti ta bolla nagarancha mala piiridetize?” giidi pallamistana assi daana danda7ees.
Hessa gussi “Lo7oy yaana mala ane iitta oothosu” geetesi gidi issi issi asati nu bolla woresizayssa malakko. Hayta asata bolla gakkiza piiriday tumu piiridako.
Histinni nu aazi ginoo? Nuni isttafe adhizonii? Mulekka adhoko. Ayhudata gidikkoka hanikko dere asa gidikokka wurikka nagarape garisa baggara diza gish ta wursikka kassistada isttas yootadis.
“Xiilloy oonikka deena issi uraykka deena.
Yuushi qopiizadey bawa; Xoossu koyzay issadeyka bawa.
Wurikka balletidane issi bolla go7onttayta gidida. Loo7o oothizay oonikka bawa; issadeykka deena”
Istta duunay doya diza duufo mala istta duunay wuriso wode hasa7ees. Istta meterishay shoosha marzzera dees.”
“Istta duunan qanigethin cammo miish kumides.”
“Istta tooy suuthu gussanasi eesotees.
Istta ogen dhayosoyne mulera dipp gi dhayoy dees.
Istti Sarotetha oge eri eretena
Istta ayfesonni Xoossas baboy bawa” geeteti xaafettida malakko.
Hessa gishshi duunay wurikka goridistana mala derey kumetha Xoossas mallithe immana mala wogay gizay wurikka wogape garsara dizaytas gididaysa nu eroosu.
Hessa gishshi wogay nagaray aazakone erisees attiin wogaa nagon oonikka iza achani xiillo geetistanas danida7ena.
Ha7i qasse wogaa kasse nabeti izas marikatidaysi wogape karera gidida Xoossa xiilloteth qonicides.
Hessi Xoossa xiillotethi Yesus Kirisitoosa amanon dummatethi bayndda bettiza xiillotethikko.
Gaasoykka asi wurikka nagara oothides. Xoossa bonichoykka asa naas paciides.
Asay Yesus Kirisitoosay, asa na gishshi oothida kiyatethafe denididayssan coo mela xiillides.
Iza suuthan gidida ammanon naagarape maristana yarsho histtid Xoossi Yesusa shishides. Izi hessa oothiday kassetidi polletida nagara qaxayonta danida7a adhida ba xiillotethi bessaanaskko.
Izi hessa ha wodezan oothiday ba xiillotetha heskka ba baggara xiillo gidi Yesus Kirisitoosan ammanizade xiilisizaysa bessanaskko.
Histinni nuni izan ceeqettiza miishshi aazi dizee? aykko miishshankka ceeqetokko. Nu ceeqistana gaasoy aazee? woga naagiza gishshee? gidenna ammanonkko.
Ay asikka ammanon attin woga naagon atonttaysa nu geeshshi yoottos.
Xoossi Ayhudata Xoossu xalalaa? Haniko dere asaskka Xoossu gidenee? Ee hanko dere asaskka izi Xoossa.
Qaxaretidayssa ammanon qasse qaxaretonitaysakka he ammanonikka xiillisizayka izi isi Xoossa xalalakko.
Histin hessi hessa gidikko ammano geedon woga go7ay bayndazi oothinoo? Muleka hessaththo hanena. woga nu minthana attin.
Hessa gish kasse nu Abiramey hayssafe ay go7a demide ginoo?
Abiramey ba oothon xiilidako izi ceeqistanayssi deesiko shin; izi Xoossa siinithan ceeqetenas danida7ena.
Geeshsha Maxaafay “Abiramey Xoossu ammanidesine iza ammanoy izas xiillotethan qoodetides” gees.
Issi uray ootho oothiko izi ekiza miishay izas coo kiyatethi immetizayssa gidontta izades ootho waga gides.
Gido attin ootho oothontta nagarancha ura xiillo kessiza Xoossan ammanizaades iza ammanoy izas xiillotethen taybetteyes.
Dawiteykka xiillotethi izas qoodettizay loo7o oothon gidontta asa gishshi hiziges,
Isttas istta bolla oothoy atto geetetidaytine istta nagaray maretidayt anijjetidayta.
Iza nagara Goday muleka qoodontadey izi anijjtidade”
Ha anijjozi qaxarretidaytas xalalayee? woykko qaxaretontaytasaraa? kase koyro nu Aawa Abirame ammanoy izas xiillotethan paydetides gidos.
Histin wani izas hessaththo paydetide? Izi qaxaretidape guye? woykko qaxaristanape kassee? Izas xiillotethan paydetiday izi qaxaristanape sinithana.
Izi kasse qaxaristanape kasse demmida xiillotethay qaxarisi malata gidida heskka xiillotethas matame ekides. Hessa gish qaxaretontta ammanizaytas xiillotethi paydistana mala wurisotasi izi Aawa.
Izi qaxaretidaytaskka Aawa qaxaretidaytas xalala gidontta nu Aawa Abiramey kasse qaxaristanape sinithe izas diza ammano geedo kallizaytas wurisossa.
Izi alame latizade gidana mala Abirimeynne iza zereththati ufaysa qaala ekiday waga baggara gidontta ammanon gidida xiillotethankko.
Woga nagizayti lattizayta gidiko ammanos go7ay deenna; ufaysikka coo mela gidana shin.
Wogay hanqqo kalethes. wogay baynidason wogappe adhethi deenna.
Hessa gishshi ufaysi ammanon yides. Hessikka iza ufaysay iza kiiyatethan gidanadanine Abirame zerethasi wurisosi ammanetizayssa gidana mala hanides. Hesikka wogan izayta gididaytas xalala gidontta ammanon Abirame nayta gididaytas wurisotaskko. Izikka nuus wurisoskka Aawako.
Hesikka “Ta nena daro dere Aawa oothidis” geeteti xaafetida mala hanides. Izikka hayqidaytas deyo immizaden baynidayssa qasse diza mala oothizaden ammanida Xoossa sinithan izi nuusu Aawakko.
Kasse izas “Ne zerethi hessaththo hanana” geetetida mala ayko ufaysikka baynida dishin Abiramey Xoossi hanana gidaysa ammanidi daro dere Aawa gidides.
Abiramesi yelettini xeetu layith gidi kichin Abiramey ba asatethay hayqetha mala gididaysanne sarasi yello wodey aadhi bidaysa erisheka ammanon lepibeyna.
Gede gujjid ammanon minidi Xoossas boncho immides attin Xoossi gida qaala sidhibeyna.
Xoossi izas immida ufaysay polistanaysa kumetha wozinape ammanides.
Hessa gishshi izasi xiillotethan qodetides.
“Izas xiillotethan paydetides” giza qaala xaafettiday izas xalala gidena.
Gido attin Xoossi nu xiillotetha iza baggara paydiza nu Goda Yesusa hayqope denithidaysan ammaniza nusarakko.
Izi nu nagara gishshi hayqanasi aadhi immetides. Izi nuna xiillota hisitina hayqope denidides.
Histiko nuni xiillida gishshi nu Goda Yesus Kirisitoosa baggara nuusu Xoossara sarotethi dees.
Hayssa ha ammanozan miinid diza kiyatethan nuni geliday iza baggara gidida gishshi ufayssan Xoossa boncho gishetti ekizayta gidida gishshi nu ufa7etosu.
Hayssan xalala gidontta nuna gakiza waayenkka ufa7eetoos. Gaasoyka waayey danda7an gathizaysa nu erosu.
Danida7ay paaccen minoteth immes; paaccen minoteth ufaysi immees.
He ufaysay nuna qasse nuna yellachena. Xoossi nuusu immida xiillo ayanan ba siqqo nu wozinan gusiida gishshi he ufayssay nuna yellan gathena.
Nu daburanchata gidi dishin Xoossa wodey gakida mala Kirisitoosay nu nagara gishshi hayqides.
Xiillo asa gishshi hayqana asi bistanays daro metees. Loo7o asa gishshi hayqanas xalana asi oonee erizay bettana dandda7ees.
Gido attin nu buro nagaranicha gidi uttidishin Kiristoosay nu gishshi hayqides. Hesikka Xoossi nuna siqiza ba siiqo heysan besses.
Nuni iza suuthan geyidayta gidikko harappeka iza baggara Xoossa hanqqofe attana.
Nu Xoossas morketa gidi dishe iza naaza hayqon izara giigidayta gidikko nu izara giigdappe guye iza shemppo baggara nuni keehi attana.
Hessa xalala gidenna; qassekka nuni ha7i izara giiga demmida nu Goda Yesusi kiristoosa baggara Xoossankka ufays oothos.
Hessa gishshi nagaray issade geedon duge ha alameza yida mala hayqoykka nagara geedon yides. Hayqoykka hessa baggara asa wurisoko yides. hessas gaasoy asi wurikka iza baggara nagara oothida gishshikko.
Wogay immettanape kase nagaray biitta bolla deesishin wogay baynddason nagaray nagara gidena.
Shin Addameppe ha simmin Muse wode gakkanaas diza woden Addame mala woga menththid nagara oothontayta bollaka hayqoy kawotides. Addamey buro yaana kiristoosas lemisokko.
Gidikokka iza kiyatetha immotay asa qoho mala gidena. Issadey mooridayssan daro asay hayqqikokka Xoossa kiyatethanine issi asi Yesusi kiristoosa kiyatethan yida immotay darotas keehi dari immetides.
Qasseka Xoossa immotay issade baggara yida nagarappe beettida ayife mala gidenna. Gaasoykka iza piriday issade nagara kaallid pirida ekki yides. Iza immotay qase daro qoho geedon xiilloteth ehides. Hayqoy hayssade baggara kawotidayssa gidikko daro tiripa gidida Xoossa kiyatethinne xiillotetha immota ekkidayti issade baggara hessika Yesusi kiristoosa baggara xoonidi deyon daana.

Hisitko issade qoho geedon piriday asa wuriso bolla gakkida mala hessathokka issade xiillotetha oothon asi wurisos deyo immiza xiillotethi beettides.
Issadey azazetontta ixxida gishshi daro asay nagarancha gidida mala issade azazetethan qase daroti xiillana.
Wogay yiin mooroy darides. Gido attin nagaray daroyssafe bollara Xoossa kiyatethi keehi darides.
Hesska handay nagaray hayqo bolla kawotidayssa mala Yesus kiristoosa baggara qasse medhina deyoy bettana mala iza kiyatethan kawotanaskko.
Histin nu ay giinoo? Xoossa kiyatethi darana mala nagara gujji othinoo?
Mulekka gidenna. Nuni nagaras hayqidosu. Histin hayssafe guye nu waani nagaran daanee?
Nuni Yesusi Kiristoosara issino gidana mala xamaqetidayti iza hayqon nu issife gidanas xamaqetidayssa hayssa inte ereketii?
Hessa gishshi Kiristoosay ba Aawa bonchon hayqoppe denddida mala nunikka hessaththo ooratha deyon daanas xinqqaten hayqqidi izara moogetidosd.
Nuni hessa mala hayqon izara isife gidikko qasse denithanka izara isife gidosu.
Hayssafe guye nu nagarasi aylle gidontta mala nagara asatethay kiichana mala kase nu ceea asatethay izara isife kaqetidayssa nu erosu.
Gaasoykka hayqida asi nagarape shemipidis.
Nuni Kiristoosara hayqidayti gidikko nu izara isife danaysa ammanosu.
Kiristoosay hayqope denidida gishshi nam7antho izi hayqonitaysanne iza bolla hayqossa wolqay bayndayssa nu erosu.
Izi hayqida wode isito wursi nagara gishshi hayqides. Gida attin Xoossas paaxa dusu dees.
Hessaththoka inte nagaras hayqidi Xoossas Yesus Kiristoosa baggara paxxa dizaysa erite.
Hessa gishshi iitta oothana koyza iitta asho qofa koydi hayqida inte asatetha bolla nagaray kawotana mala oothofite.
Inte asatetha iitta ootho oothiza mishi oothi nagaras harisopite. Hessa mala oothanape hayqope gede deyon pinida asata mala intena Xoossa harisite. Inte asatetha xiillotetha miishsha mala Xoossas harisite.
Inte Xoossa kiiyatetha garisan deista attiin woga garisan dontta gishshi intena nagaray haarena.
Histin aazi oothinoo? wogaa garisan gidontta nuni Xoossa kiyatetha garisan diza gishshi nagara oothonoo? mule oothanaas bessena.
Inte intena aylle mala shiishshiza wode inte azazetizades aylle gididayssa ereista. Hessaththoka gede hayqokko efiza nagaras woykko xiilotethako gathiza azazetethas inte aylle gididayssa ereketii?
Inte kasse nagaras ayllista gidikko intes imettida timiritezas inte wozanappe azazetida gishshi Xoossi galateto.
Inte nagarape wozetidi xiillotethas aylle gididista.
Hayssa ta asa qaalan intes qonccen yootizay inte Yeletethan daburanicha gidida gishshikko. Inte kase wode inte asatetha aylletethasine kassepe adhi iittana mala oothi immista shin ha7i qasse gede geeshatethako efiza xiillotethes aylle hisiti haarisite.
Inte kasse nagarasi aylletidi diza wode inte xiillotethafe mella atidista shin.
Ha7i qasse inte yelatiza miishshatape he wode ay go7a demmidetii? Hessa he hanoza go7ay hayqoko.
Ha7i qasse inte nagarape wozetidi Xoossa ayllista gididista. Hessikka Intena gede geeshatethako kallethes. wurisethaykka medhina deyoko.
Nagara waagay hayqokko. Xoossa immotay gidiko Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara medhiina deyoko.
Ta ishato tani wogaa eriza asatas yootays. Wogaa shemipora paxxa diza asa xalala harizayssa inte ereketii?
Issi macashi azina geliko ba azinara wogan iza qachetizay azinay paxxa diza wode gakanaskko. Azinay hayqiko iza machcho gidiza wogape anjjistaysu.
Gido attin azinay paxxa dishin iza hara azina gelliko laymatasusu geetistaysu. Azinay hayqiko qase hara ura iza gelliko kase azina wogape anjjistadus attin layma getetuku.
Hessa gishshi ta ishato inteka Yesus Kiristoosa asho baggara wogas hayqidista. Inte hayqope denidida kiristoosa bagga gidin nuni Xoossas ayfe ayfanaskko.
Nagarancha medhetetha shenen nu diza wode hayqo ayfe nu ayfana mala wogay denththethida nagara amoy nu bolla oothides.
Ha7i gidiko kasse nuna waaxi qachida hayqida gishshi wogape wozetidosu. Hesikka kase cega wogan xaafetidayssan gidontta dishe ooratha ayana ogen nuni oothanaskko.
Histin nu ay ginoo? Be hu7es wogay naragaa? muleka gidena. wogaa bagara gidonttako nagaray azakone nu erokoko shin. wogay “amotofa” gonttako amoy azakone tumupe ta erikke.
Nagaray qasse wogape kezida azazoy bessida ogen go7ettidi ta gidon dumma dumma iitta amo denithethides. wogay yanappe kasse nagaray hayqithiko.
wogay baynida kase tani paxxa dayisse shin wogay yiini qase nagaray paxxa gidides. ta gidikko hayqadis.
He asi ashana qofetida azazoyka hayqo ekii yidaysa eradis.
Nagaray woga baggara bettida gaason go7ettidi tana balethidesine azazon wodhides.
Hessa gishshi wogay ba baggara geeshshikko. azazoyka geesh, xiilone loo7okko.
Gido attin loo7osu hanidaysi taas hayqos gididee? Mulekka gidena. Gido attin nagaray ba nagaratethan eretana mala loo7o gidida hano bagara ta bolla hayqo ehides. Hesikka nagaray azazo baggara kassepe aathi nagara darisides.
Wogay ayana yo gididaysa nu erosu. Ta qasse nagaras aylle mala bayzetida asikko.
Tani ta oothizayssa erike. Ta oothana koyzayssa ootha erike shin ta ixxiza miishsh oothays.
Ta oothana koyontta miish oothiza gidikko wogay loo7o gididaysa ta marikatays.
Hessa oothizay tana gidontta ta gaathan diza nagaray oothees.
Tanan hesikka nagarancha gidida ta madhetetha gidon ayko loo7o miishshi baynidayssa ta erays. Loo7o oothanasi taas amotethi dees shin polla ootha erikke.
Ta oothizay oothana gaada koyza loo7o ootho giden. Gido attin ta oothana koyontta iitta ootho oothays.
Tani oothanas koyonttayssa oothiza gidiko hessa oothizay tana gidontta ta gidon diza nagarakko.
Hessa gishshi haysi wogay oothon dizaysi taas gellides. Hessikka tani loo7o oothana koyaysishin tani iitta oothays.
Tani ta gaathara Xoossa wogan ufa7istays.
Gido attin ta asatetha gidon oothiza nagara wogay tana qachi oykidi ta qofa wogara oletiza hara wogay ta asatetha gidon oothishin beyays.
Ta aymala laafa asee! Hayssa hayqosi imettida asatethafe tana ashanay oonee?
Nu Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara galatay Xoossas gido. Histinkko tani ta baggara ta qofan Xoossa wogasi aylle gidashe tani Ta medhetetha wogan nagara wogas aylleko.
Hessa gishshi Yesus Kiristoosa ammanizayta bolla piriday deena.
Gaasoykka deyo ayana wogay Yesus Kiristoosa baggara nagarape istta geeshida gishikko.
Nagarancha ashoppe dendidayssan wogay polanaas danida7ontaysa Xoossi ba naaza nagarancha asa lemusson nagaras yarishistana mala yedidi pollides. Hsitidi nagara iza ashon piridides.
Hessikka nuni ashon gidontta ayanan simeretiza nupe wogay koyza xiillotetha pollanaskko.
Asho shene mala daana koyza asata wozinay ashoy koyza mishan shemipees. Ayana shene mala dizayti qasse ba wizinaa, ayanay koyza miishsh bolla wothetes.
Ashos xalala qofay hayqo gidishin ayana yoosi qofay gidiko deyone sarotethikko.
Nagaras haretiza wozinay Xoossara ooshshakko. Gaasoykka izi Xoossa wogasi haretennane haristanas danida7ena.
Asho shene mala diza asatikka Xoossu ufaysanasi danida7etena.
Inte qasse Xoossa ayanay intenan diza gidiko ashon gidontta ayanan deista. Kiristoosa ayanay iza bolla deennadey he uray Kiristoosas gidena.
Kiristoosay inte gidon dikko qasse inte asatethay naagara geedon hayqethi gidikokka inte ayanay qase xiillotetha gaason deyon dees.
Yesusa hayqope dinthida iza ayanay inte bolla diza gidiko Kiristoosa hayqope denthidaysa inte gidon diza iza ayanay hayqanas diza inte asatethas deyo immana.
Hessa gishshi ta ishato! hesikka wolliqara hanana shin nu asho shene mala daanas ashosi gidokko.
Asho shene mala deyzayssa gidiko inte hayqanane asho ootho iittaza inte ayanan wodhi gidiko inte deyon daana.
Xoossa ayanan kallizadenti heytantti istti Xoossa naytakko.
Inte ekida ayanay zaaridi intena ayletethan hariiza ayana gidontta “nu Aawa abbo” gi xeygisiza naatetha ayana ekidista.
Nuni Xoossa nayta gididaysa he ayanay ba baggara nu ayanara issife nuusu marikatees.
Nuni iza nayti gidikko nu iza latizaytako. Nu iza bonchoza latizayta gidana mala adafeka izara iza metoza gishetezayta gidikko nu Xoossu latizadeko; Kirisitossara issife latizayitakko.
Ha7i nu ekiza waayey buro nuusu sinithan giigi uttida bonchozara gathi xellishin aykokka gidena gays.
Medhetethay wurikka Xoossa nayti qonccanaysa lamotethan naagon dees.
Medhetethi wurikka mela hada gidana mala piridettides. Hesikka ba doron gidontta sinithafes haristana mala izi ba shene mala harisida gishaskko.
Hesikka medhetethi wurikka dhayssa aylletethafe wozitidi Xoossa naytasi gidida gede bonichitida shene mala dizaso gakanaskko.
Ha7i gakanas medhetethi wurikka mixxa mala waayen shenotishe dizaysa nu erosu.
Iza xalala gidontta koyro ayana ayfe demmida nunikka nu asatethay attana nu iza na gidanaysaka lamotishene wozinara mixxatishe dosu.
Hayssa ha ufaysan xalala attidosu. Ufaysi qasse ayfen betiza miishsh gidiko burope naagiza miishsh gidena; Ha7i ba ayfen beyza miishshi buropes nagiizadey oonee?
Gido attin nuni buro nu ayfen beyontta miish ufaysan naagiza gidikko salistay baynida naagosu.
Hesathokka qasse nu daburishin ayanay nuna maades. Wossa nu wositi wossanakone nu erontta gishshi ayanay nuni qaalan qonccisanas danida7etontta qaalara nusu wosses.
Nu wozina paacci eriza ayanay izi ayana qofa eres. Gaasoykka ayanay Xoossa shene mala ammaniza asasi nuusu wosses.
Xoossi bena dosizaytasine iza shene mala xeeygetidaytasi wurisos oothiza miishshi wursikka lo7os oothizaysa nu erosu.
Xoossi kasseepe ba erizazayta istti iza naaza milatana mala kasseka doori wothides. hesikka daro ba ishata gidofe izi bayra gidanasa.
Kasse koyrope ba dooridayta istta xeeygides. Qassekka xeygidata xiilisides. Be xiilisidaytaka bonchides.
Histinni hessa nu ay ginoo? Xoossi nunara gidikko nunara eqistana danida7izay oonee?
Be yellos michetontta nu gishshi oothi immiday izako. Hesitin wuriso miishsh nuusu izara kiyatetha aazas immenee?
Xoossi dooridayta motiza oonee? Xillisizay Xoossa.
Hisittini piridizay oonee? Hayqidi hayqope denididi Xoossa oshachan uttida Yesus Kiristoosay nu gishshi ganates.
Nuna Kiristoosa siqope shakanay oonee? Metoye, waaye, woykko godetethee, woykko gafa, woykko kallotethee woykko qopontta gakiiza metoyee, mashaa?
Hesikka kasse “Ne gishshi nu shuketiza dorisa mala qoodettidosu. gallasi kumethi ne gish nuni hayqora baxistana” geeteti xaafetidayssa malako?
Nuna aazika shakena. Haysa wurison nuna siqidaysan xoonizaytapekka nu aadhosu.
Hessa gishshi hayqo gidin deyo gidin kiitanchata gidin woykko ha7i diza miishsh gidin buro yaana miishsha gidin woykko ay wolliqama gidin
Dhoqqa gidin woykko ziqa gidin woykko ay medheteth gidin Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara nuusi diza Xoossa siqope nuna shaakana danda7iza miishshi bayndayssa ta shaaka eradis.
Ta Yesusa sunthan tumu gays; woridotikke; ta wozinaykka xiillo ayana baggara taas marikatees.
Taas wozinape kiichontta iitta qofay michay ta wozinan dees.
Ta baggara asa gishshi ta qanigetidane Kiristoosape shakistada wora wodhidako dosays.
Isttikka Isiraa7eele naytako. Istti Xoossa na gidana mala Xoossa bonchoyne caaqo qaalay ne wogayne Xoossa keeththa woga ufaysi isttasi imetides.
Kase Aawatikka istta bagga Kiristoosa asho baggara istta zeretha zariken qoodetes. Izikka wurisofe bolla gidida medhinas galatetida Xoossa; amin7i.
Gido attin hessa guussi Xoossa qaalay attides guussu gidena. Isiraa7eelepe yelettiday wuri Isiraa7eele gidenna.
Abiramepe yelettidayti izape yelletida gishshi wurikka iza yellista gidetena shin “Ne zerethi Yisaqa bagara xeygistana” geetetida mala hanides.
Hessa guussikka Xoossa na geetetidayti istti ashon yellidayta gidetena shin Abirame nayta geetettizayti burope yellistanaytakko.
“Yiza Layth hani wode ta ha simmana; Sarayka nees attuma na yellana” geetetidi izas ufaysa qaalay imettides.
Hessa xalalaka gidena. Iribiqa nayti issade nakko. Izikka nu Aawa Yisaqakko.
Meniteti yelletidi buro iitta woykko kiya oothontta dishin Xoossa qofay miinana mala
Oothon gidontta xeeygidayssafe gidida gishshi “Bayray kaallozas haaristana” geetetidi Iribiqas yootides.
Hessikka “Ta Yaqobe dosadis; Eessa ixxadis” geeteti kasse xaafetida mala hanides.
Histin nu ha7i ay ginoo? Xoossi besontta ogera maadi erizee? Muleka maadi erena.
Xooss Muses “Ta marana koydade marana; Ta Michistana koyza urasikka michistana” gees.
Hessa gish hesikka assi koyda mala gidontta woykko asa daburan gidontta Xoossa maarida mala hanees.
Geesha maxaafey Farone “Ta woliqay ne bolla bistana malane ta sunthi biitta wurisoson yootistana mala ta nena hayssasi denithadis” gees.
Hessa gish Xooss marana koyzade maares. Iza wozina muumisana koyzade wozana muumises.
Intefe isadey “Histin hanoy heyssa mala gidiko nuna hano gakanasi aazas waayisizee? Gaasoykka iza shene digana danida7izay oonee?” gaada oychchontta agaka.
Shin Xoossas mallithe zaara immizay ne oonee? “Oothetida miishshi, zaaridi oothidayssa ne tana aazas hayssatho oothadii?” gi erizee?
Uriqqa medhizadey he uriqafe bagga bonichos bagga qasse coo hiriyso oothosi medhanas iza shene gidenee?
Xoossikka ba hanqqo besanasine ba wolliqa erisanasi koydi iza hanqqo qoniccisizayta dhayanasi giigetidayta dhayssontta agagikkochii!
Koyro bonichos gigisida iza marotetha besizaytas iza bonicho duretethay eretana mala izi oothanaskko.
Xeygidadey Ayhudata baggafe xalala gidontta hanko dereza baggafe gidida nunakka ashontta xeygides.
Hose7e maxaafan “Ta dere gidontayta tani ta dereta” ga xeygana; “dosetonttayta iistta ta dosetidayta” gada xeygana.
Qasseka “Inte ta dere dekista geeteti yootteidason henka <Isiti deyo Xoossa nayta> geteti xeygistana.”
Isayasaykka Isra7eele nayta gish hizigi yootides “Isra7eele nayta qoday abba acce mala darikokka guuthati xalala attana.
Goday ba pirida biitta bolla elle piridana.
Hessikka kase Isiyasay “Woga Goday nusu zerethi ashonitako nu sodoma katama malane gamira katama mala nukka dhayanashin” geetetidi kasse Isayasa dunani yootidaysa mala hanides.
Histin nu ay giinoo? Amanon bettida xiilloteth demanas hanko dere asay daburontta demides.
Gido attin xiillotetha wogaa kaalliza Isiraa7eele nayti demibeytena.
Hessi aazas hessaththo hanidee? Istti ammanon gidonta oothon demana kallida gishshikko. Isttikka dhuphe shuchan dhuphetida.
Hessikka “Hekko asa dhuphiza shuchu Istta kunidisiza zala xiyone bolla ta wothana, Iazn ammanizadey yelletena” geetetidi kasse geeshsha maxaafan xaafetidayssa mala hanides.
Ta ishato Isra7eele nayta gishshi ta amaone ta Xoossu wossizay istti dhayonta attanaskko.
Istti Xoossa yoosi michetizayta gididaysa ta istta gishshi marikatana danida7ays; Istta michetethi gidiiko eratethan gidena.
Xooss asi xiillisiza oge erontta aggidi ba xiillotethas oge kaallida attin Xoossa xiillotetha oge kaallibeyttena.
Amaniza asa wursi xillisanas Kiristoosay woga wuris polides.
Musey Woga baggara bettiza xiilotetha gish erisishe “Hayta wogata polli oothizadey ha wogatan daana” gizayssakko.
Ammanon bettiza xillotethi qase hiziges “Ne wozinara pud sallo oonee baanayii? gopa” hesstho gussi Kiristoosa sallope duge ha wothana gussukko.
“Woykko <Duge cimman oonee wodhanayii? goppa” hesikka Kiristoosa hayqope buro denithana guussukko.
Gido attin qaalay ay gize “Qaalay ne achan dees; ne dunanine ne wozinan dees. Nuni ammano gishshi sabakiiza qaalay hayssakko.
Neni ne dunara “Yesusay Goda” gaada marikatiko Xoossi iza hayqope denithidayssa ne wozinan ne ammanikko attana.
Neni xiillanay wozinan ammanikoko shin ne atanay ne dunara marikatikoko.
Geesha maxaafay giza mala “Izan ammanizay wurikka yellatena.”
Ayhudata gidonine hiniko dere asa gidon dumatethi dena. Issi Goday wurisosikka Godakko. Iza wossizayta gujj anjes.
“Goda sunithu xeygizayti wurikka atana” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetides.
Histin iza ammanonttayti iza wozigi xeyganee? Qasse iza gishshi siyontta dishe wossiti ammananee? Sabakey baynida dishin wossiti siyanee?
Kitetonita wositi sabakanideto? Hesikka “mishiracho qaala ekkii yizayta yuus ay mala loo7o” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetida mala hanides.
Gido attin siydayti wurikka Mishiracho qaala ekibeyttena; Isayasay “Godo nu yootidaysa ooni ammanidee?” gida mala hanides.
Hessa gishshi ammanoy bettizay yootiza qaala siyethankko. yootetiza qaalaykka Kiristoosa gishshi yootiza qaalapekko.
Gido attin asay siybeyneshaa? aada ta oychays; tumape asay siydes; Geesha maxaafan xaafettida mala “Ista qaalay biitta wurisonine alame gaxxa gakanasi siyetides.”
Ta qasseka oychays; Isra7eele nayti qaalaa eribeyteneshaa? Koyiro Musey isttas “Ta dere gidonttaytan ta istta mindasana; yuushi qopontta deretan ta istta yilochana” gides.
Isayasaykka xalatethan “Tana koyonttaytas ta bettadis; tana oychonttaytas tana qonicisadis” gides.
Isiraa7eele gishshi qase “Taas azazetontta derekone taas eeno gontta dereko kumetha gallas ta kushe miccadis” gees.
Histin Xoossi dereta yegi agidee? Gaada ta oychays; Muleka agibeyna; takka ta baggara Biniyame zarike, Abirame zereth gidida Isiraa7eele asakko.
Xoossi koyrope ba erida dereza yegibeyna. Elasay Isiraa7eele nayta bolla motoy Xoossakko wozigi shishshidakone geesha maxaafay iza gishshi ay gizakone inte eriketii?
“Godo! istti ne nabeta wodhida. nees yarishizasoka lallida. Qasse tani tarka atadis. Tanaka wodhana geetes.
Xoossi isttas hizgi zaarides “Ba7alle geeteiza Eeqas goynonttayta laapun shihi asi taas ashshadis.”
Hessa malaka ha7i ha wodezanika Xoossa kiyatethan Isiraa7eele asape dooreti attida guuthati deetes.
Histtin hessi Xoossa kiyatethan gidiko asa oothon gidena. Asa oothon gididaakko Xoossa kiyateth, kiyateh gidena.
Histin ay gaanee? Isiraa7eele nayti loo7ethi koydayssa demmibeyttena. Xoossan dooretidayti gidiko demmida. Haniko attidayta wozinay muumides.
Kase “Istta ayfey xeelontta mala, istta hayitheyka siyontta mala Xoossi hanno ha gallasiyo gakanaas isttas doccisiza ayana immides” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetida malakko.
Dawiteykka “Istta maaday istta oykiza narixa gido; Istta dhuphizazine qixate gido.
Istta ayfey xeellofo goozzeto; Istta zokkoy medhinas kuuno” gides.

Gido attin qasse istta hanko dere asas anjjo gidides. Istta kunidethika qasse hanko deretas anjjo gidiko istti simmi attidakko ay mala gita anjjo gidandeeshin!
Hankko Dere asazo, ta intes yootays, ta hanko dere asas kiittetidade gidida gishshi ta oothoza ta minnada polana.
Hessikka ta bagga asati minidatana mala denithethada isttafe guutha asata ashshanaas ufaysan oothays.
Xoossi istta aggida hanko dere asay Xoossara giigikko Xoossi Isiraa7eele nayta zaaridi ekkiza wode intes aazi hanazi milattizee? Hessa guusi “hayqqope dendides” guusa malakko.
Koyro bukasoy loo7o gidikko hanko izappe oothetizaas wurikka loo7okko. Hessaththoka issi miththa xaphphoy loo7o gidikko hanmkko iza bolla diza hanigetikka loo7o gideetes.
Keththa dan77on diza miththa hangista malati inte meqqi wodhdhin hankko woran diza miththata milatiza hankko dere asati inte olla gididi inte haaronne inte anjjo shaaki ekkizadentta gidikko;
Heyta he meqqi wodhdhida hangista bolla othoretofa. inte istta bolla otoretiko qasse hanno wozinan wothite. He miththaa tookiday nena gidaka. miththay nena tookides attin.
Histinko “He hanigeti meqqi wodhdhiday nuni istta olla gelana malakko” gontta agekista.
Tumu gidista shin istti meqiday ammano paceppe denididayssankko. Inteka ammanon eqidista. Babbite attin otoretofite.
Xoossi koyrope diza hanigistas michetonttade gidiko inteskka michetena.
Hessa gishshi Xoossa kiyatethine iza menxxe iittatetha ane xeella. Iza menxxe iittethay kunididayta bollakko. Iza kiyatethay qasse inte iza qadhetetha garisan diza wode gakanaas xalalakko. Hessi baynida aggiko intekka qanixistana.
Istti ammanontta minni eqidasope simmiko kase beso simmi gelana. Xoossika istta zarisi gelithana danida7ees.
Inte bazo miththafe qanixettida kase inte medhetethafe gidontta loo7o miththan inte gelana danida7iko koyrope ba medhetetha hanigista gididayti heyti kase iza bolla diza miththan simmi geloy isttas waani hanenee?
Ta ishato, inte ciincca asi gididayssa intes milatontta mala hayssa gido xuura yooza inte erontta attana mala ta koyke. Hesikka hiniko dere asape xeygetidayti wuri ammanana gakanaas Isiraa7eele nayta wozinay muumides.
Hessa gishshi Isiraa7eele nayti wurikka attana. “Ashshizadey Xiyonepe yaana; Yaqobepeka iittateth digana.
Tni istta nagara wursa dhayssidape guye ta isttara caaqon geliza qaalay hessako. geetetidi kase geesha maxaafan xaafettida mala handes.
Intes hanko deretas Mishiracho qaalay gakana mala Isiraa7eele nayti Xoossan ixettida asi gidida. Gidikokka kase dooro mala gidiko ba Aawata baggara istti dosettidaytakko.
Xoossi dooridappene ba kiyateth immmidape guye ba oothida miishan simmidi handattena.
Inteka kase azazetonttaytako. Istti azazetontta ixxin ha7i intena maaridayssatho
Xoossi Intena maarida geedon isttika maaristana mala ha7i azazetonttayta gidida.
Xoossi wursika maaranas asi wuriska azazetontta mala goridides.
Xoossa cinccatethine iza erateth ay mala ciimma! Iza priday ay malakone paacetena. Izi adhida geedoyka eretena.
“Goda wozina eriday oonee? Izas zore immiday oonee?”
Xoossi zaari immana mala izas tal77e immiday oonee?
Wurikka izape, izain, izasko. Izas bonichoy medhinape medhinas gido. Amini7i.
Hesa gishshi ta ishato inte asatetha geeshine Xoossu ufaysiza paxa yarsho oothidi inte shiishshana mala ta intena Xoossa qadhetan woossays. Hesikka wozinamma asa mala inte Xoossas oothiza oothokko.
Loo7o ufaysizazine kumeth gididazi Xoossa sheney azakone inte paaci erana mala inte qofan oraxidi lamettite attin hayssa alame asa milatopite.
Intes Xoossi immida ammano mala interika intena paaci xeellite attin ha7i dizaysafe bolara intena dhoqisi xeellontta mala tani taas imettida Xoossa kiyatethan intena issa issa zorays.

Hessaththoka nuni darota gidi uttidi Kiristoosan issi ashoko. Nuni issay issas ashokko.
Nuusi immetida imota mala dumma dumma imotethi dees. Isades burope hananazi yooto gidiko izades immetida ammano mala yooto.
Oothi maadizadey oothi maado. Tamarisizadeyka tamariso.
Zorizade gidiko zoro. Baynidaytas immizadey gujji immo. Aysizadey minni aysso. maarizadeyka ufaysan maaro.
Inte siqotethi qoodhepe qomo gidopo. Iitta gididayssa wursikka ixxite. Loo7o gididayssara issife oykettite.
Inte inte garisan issay issara ishata mala loo7ethi siqetite. Issay issa beppe aathi bonichizayta gidite.
Godas oothana ayanan xugetizayta gidite attin hessa he minotethafe guye gooppite.
Ufayssan ufa7etizayta gidite; meto danida7ite; woossan minnite.
Ammanishe waayetizaytas intes dizayssafe shaaki immite. Imath mokite.
Intena qanigizayta anjjite attin qanigofite.
Ufa7etizaytara ufa7etite; muzotizaytara muzotite.
Inte inte garisan dosetethan diite. Maniqotara isopetethan daanas koyte attin otoropitene ceeqetopite.
Oonasikka iitta gishshi iitta zaaropite. Asi wuriso achan loo7o miishshi oothanas minnite.
Intes danida7etiko inte inte baggara asi wurisora saron diite.
Ta siiqoto, inte halo Xoossi kesso attin interika halo kesopite “Halo kesanay tanakko” gees Goday geeteti geeshsha maxaafan xaafetides.
Halo kessanape “Neni ne morikey gafiko muza; izi saamotiko usha; ne hessaththo oothiko tama boniqo iza bolla korasa” geetetidi geeshsha maxaafan xaafetides.
Iitta loo7o oothon xoono attin iittan xonettofa.
Ay asikka bena aysiza daanatas haaristana bessis. Xoossafe imetontta dishin daanatethi deena. Ha7i diza daanati Xoossafe daanatidaytakko.
Hessa gishshi daana bolla makali7idey Xoossa woga bolla makali7ees. He makali7izaytika ba bolla pirida eheetes.
Dere aysizati iitta oothizayta babiseetes attin loo7o oothizayta babisetena. Ne dere aysizades babbontta agana koyazii? Histinko loo7o ootha; izikka nena galatana.
Izi nees loo7o oothanas Xoossa oothanichako. Gido attin ne iitta oothida gidiko izas babba. Gaasoyka izi masha coo mela gixxiibeyna; Izi iitta oothizade qaxayanas Xoossa oothanichako.
Hessa gishshi iza qixxetes babo xalala gidontta ne qofapankka daanatizades azazistanas besses.
Inte giira immizay hessaskko. Aysizayti hessa he oothoza bolla Xoossi istta wothides.
Isttafe issas issas bessizayssa immite. Giira immana besizaytas giira immite; qaraxa qanxxanaas bessizaytas qaraxa qanxxite; Babanas bessizaytas babbite; bonichanas bessizata bonichite.
Inte garisan issay issara siiqetethafe attin oona bollaka accoy doopo. Ase siiqiza uray izi wogaa pollides.

Inte garisan ammanon buro minnonttade shiishi ekkite attin iza qofa bolla piridofite.
Issi issi asi bettidayssa wursi maanas ammanoy dees. Qase ammanon minonta uray akakilate xalala mees.
Bettidayssa wursi mizadey wursi monttade kadhopa. Monitadey qasse mizade bolla piridofo. Xoossi wursaka ekides.
Haniko oothizade bolla piridizadey ne oonee? Izadey kunidiko woykko eqikoka iza Godas. Goday iza esanas danidaeza gishshi izi eqandes.
Issadey gallasatape issi gallas hara gallasafe aathidi bessi dumma gallasi gi qopees. Hara uray qasse gallasati wurikka issi gina gi qopees. Issi issi uray ootho.
Issi gallas hara galasafe dummasi qopizadey izi hessa oothizay Goda bonchos gidiko mizadeyka Goda bonchos giidi meesi. Miidi Xoossu galates. Monttadeykka Goda bonchos giidi muusu aggesine Xoossas galata immees.
Nupe oonikka bessi dizadeyne beppe bessi hayqizadey deena.
Nu diikoka Godas dosi. Hayqikoka Godas hanqosu. Hessa gishshi diikoka woykko hayqiko nu Godaskko.
Hessa gishshi hayqidaytasine paxxa dizatas Goda gidanasi Kirisitoosay hayqidi Hayqoppe paxxi denidides.
Histin ne aazas ne isha bolla piridazii? Aazasi ne isha leqazii? Nu wurikka Xoossa pirida womibara sinith shiqos doosu.
“Ta paxxa days. Gulibatey wurikka taasi gulibatana. Inxarisi wuri Xoossas marikatana” geeteti kase geesha maxaafan xaafetides.
Hesa gishshi nuni issi issi uray Xoossas Xoossa sinthi shiiqidi nu ootho gishshi izas zaaro immana.
Hessa gish nuni nu garisan isay isa bolla piridanape ane naagetos. Hesa aggidi nu ishas dhuphe gidizayssa woykko iza oykiza narxxa wothontta mala ane nu naagetos.
Tani Goda Yessusan amanida miza kaththan tunay baynidaysa eradis. Gido attin isadey isi miish tuna gi qopiko he mishay izadesi tunako.
Neni ne isha miza kaththa geedon dhuphe gidiko siiqoni simeristabeyka. Kirisitoosay iza gish haniqida ne isha ne miza kaththa gaason wodhopa.
Inte loo7o giidi popiza mishi iitta getistana mala oothofite.
Xoossa kawotethi xiilo ayanani bettida xilloteth sarotethine ufaysafe attin Muusa yoone usha yoo gidena.
Haysatho Krisitosas oothizadey Xoossu ufaysesinne asa achanika galatetes.
Hessa gish sarotethi betiza ogene nuni nu garisani loo7onas besiza oge ane koyosu.
Nuni Miza kaththa gish giidi Xoossa ootho ane laaloko. kathi wurikka geeshkko. Gido attiin hara urasi dhuphe gidiza kaath muusi qass balla oothoko.
Ne ishasi dhuphe gidizazi gidiko ashoka manapene woyne ush uyanape woykko ay mishika ne oothontta aggiko lo7oko.
Hessa gish haytantta milatiza mishatasi neesi diza ammanoy ne gidonine Xoossa gidon deyo. Haysi likeko giidi ammanon ekida mishan berika ba bolla piridonttadey izadey anijjetidadeko.
Gido attin wozinara sidhishe miiko izi ammanon moontta gish iza bolla piridetides. Ammanoni oothonttazi wurikka nagara.
Nuni amanoni minidayti hanko amanoni minotayi meto tokanasi besisi attiin nu Xoossa ufaetizayta gidanaso nusu besena.
Nuni wurikka nu lageista gusasine ista ufaysizazi othanasi beses.

Ta ishato inte loo7ethan kumidayta erateth wurisoni kumidaytane harata zorinas eray dizayta gididaysa ta adafe shaka eradis.
Ta Xoossafe ekida imotetha gina qaseka intena qofisanasi isi isi yota bolla xalatethan intesi xafadis.
Xoossa wonigilan qasetetha oothoy hanko deretasi Yessusi Krisitossa oothanicha gidanasa. Hesikka hiniko derey xillo ayanan Xoossasi dumatidi Xoossi ekiza yarsho gidanasa.
Hesa gish tani Xoossas oothiza gish Yessusa Krisitossan ceeqetays.
Ta yotidaysanine ta oothidaysani hanko dere asay Xoossi azaistana mala Kirisitosa azazistana mala Kirisitossay tana gididi oothidazape attin hara hasa7ana xalike.
Hesikka haniday xillo ayana woliqani malatata bera hanides. Hesa malanika Yerusalame iliwaqore yehsi gakanasi ta Kirisitossa wonigila polla sabaladisi.
Hara uray kasse oothidasoni ta gelonitamala gada kasse Krisitossa sunitha xeygeti eronitason wonigila sabakanaysi tasi ommo.
Harapeka “Iza gish istasi yotitonitati iza beyana.
Hesa gidoni ta intiko bonitamala daro wode digistadis. Oerome beyanasi Phawulossa gegetethi
Hi7 qasi tasi hani oothoy baynida gish daro laythape ha sinini intena beyanasi ta daro lamotaadis.

Intes daro daaburidaro maaramo saro giite.
Tnara issife qachchetida Anddiraqoonene Yuliyane saro giite. Heytanti hawarista garisan lo7o sunththara dizaytane kiristoosa taape kase ammanidaytako.
Tani Goda baggara daro siiqiza Philyaxone saro giite.
Kiristoosa ootho tanara issife oothiza Irobanene ta siiqiza Senxxkeka saro giite.
Kiristoosan iza ammanoy paacetidi galatetida Aphilises ta saroka gathite. Arisxabalo so asasikka ta sarota gathite.
Ta dabbo Herodiyona saro giite. Godan diza Niriqqaso so asa saro giite.
Godan gididi minotethan oothiza macashata Tirifimonone Xirofimono saro giite. Godas oothon daro daaburidaaris tani izo siiqiza Xarsidis ta saroka gathite.
Godan doorettida Rufonoosone taas Aayo gididaris iza Aayeys ta saroka yootite.
Asqqerinene Afilesonpha, Herimene, Phaxirobane, Herimanene isttara diza ishata wurisotas ta saroka gathite.
Filegones, Yuliyas, Neriyasone iza micheyis hessathoka Alixones isttara diza ammanizaytaskka ta saroka gathite.
Issay issa yeer yeer ekkidi sarothetite. Kiristoosan ammaniza woossa keeththa asay wurikka intena saro gees.
Ta ishato asa garisan shaaketeth medhizaytape inte tamarida timirtta ekkontta ixxon intes dhuphe gidiza asatape inte naagetite.
Heytantta mala asati Yesus kiristoosas oothizayta gidontta ba qanththa kaththa gishshi oothizaytakko. Shugo qaalara haasa7anine wozina kiya asata balethetes.
Inte mishshiracho qaalas azazetizayta gididayssa asi wuri siyides. Hessika tana daro ufayssides. Gidikkoka inte lo7o hanos cinccata qasse iitta oothos eeyata gidana mala ta koyays.
Sarotetha Goday xala7e eeson inte too garisa aathi dinccerethana. Goda Yesus kiristoosa kiyatethi intenara gido.
Tanara issife oothiza Xintoosay qasseka ta dabbo Luqiyesay, Iyaasoneyne Susiphixirosay intena saro saro geetes.
