Daro ootha daburadis, Daro wode dhisikabeykke, Gafanine haatha saamon waayetadis, Daro wode miza kathi taasi dhaydes, meegoyne kaloteth tana gakkides.
Tani hara miishi qopontta, gallas gallas tana qopisizay woossa keethata wuriso gishshi qopiza qofakko.
Issi uray daaburishin tani izara daaburontta ayde aggadinaa? Issi uray nagaran kundishin ta qasse iza hanqetontta ayde aadha erazinaa?
Ceeqistanas koshshizazi gidiko ta ceeqistanay ta daburancha gididayssa tana bessiza miishan ceeqistayss.
Medhinas galatetida Goda Yesus Kiristoosa Aawa Xoossi ta wordotonttayssa erees.
Tani Demasiqo kataman dishin kawo Arisixosiyossape garisara dere ayssizayss tana oykkanas koyid he katama pengeta zabetan naagissides.
Gidikoka asay tana keechen yeggidi he katama ginbbe masikotera duge wothi yeddin kessa ekka attadis. Si7il yaasifeligal.
Ceeqetethan ayne go7ay bayinda agikoka ceeqistanas koshshiko Goday taas qonccis immidayssanine izi bessida ajjutan ta ceeqistana.
Kiristoosas gidida issade ta erays. He uray tammane oyddu laythafe kase hedzdzanttho salo ekketi bides. (Izi ekkettiday ba ashozara gidin woykko ashora gidontta aggin erikke shin Xoossi qasse eres.)
Gididkoka izi ba ashozara biin woykko mela biin ta erike. Xooss qasse erees.
Izadeyka pude ganate ekketidi asa qaalan qonccisanasine asi gaanas danda7onttazi izi siyides.
Tani hessa mala asan ceeqistayss. Ta hu7es gidiko ta daburisafe hara ta izan ceeqistana miishi deena.
Histin tani tuma hasa7iza gishshi ceeqistanas koyikoka ta eeya gidike. Gido attin oonikka ta bolla ba beyzazapene tape siyizayssafe bollara qopontta mala gaada ceeqistanape naagistayss.
Hayta taas qonccida gita hanotta geedon tani otoretontta mala ta asatetha aguntha mala caddiza sakoy taas imettides. Hessika xala7epe kiitetid tana cachan waayisid ta ceeqetontta mala digges.
Hayss tana waayissizayss taape kichana mala ta Goda hedzdzu too woossadis.
Gido attin Goday qasse “Ta wolqay kumetha gidi qonccanay ne daburisan gidida gishshi ta kiyatethi nees gidana” gides. Hessa gishshi Kiristoosa wolqay ta bolla gidana mala ay wodepeka bollara tana daaburisishin he wode ufayssan ceeqistanas dosayss.
Tani wollqa demmizay daburiza wode gidida gishshi ta Kiristoosa gishshi daaburishin, cayetishin, metotishin, goodetishin, muzotishin tana ufaysses.
Tani eeya asa mala hasa7adis! Tani hessaththo hasa7ana mala oothiday intenakko. Inte tana galatanas besseskko shin ta oonakkone eretonttade gidikkoka hanko gita geetetida hawaristape tani aazanka guuxxike.
Tani tumu haware gididayssa erissiza hanoti ta intenara dashe danda7an polida oothotakko. heyttika malatata, gita ooratha miishistane malalithiza oothotakko.
Tani intes tooho gidontta aggoripe attin hanko hara woossa keethatape intena aazan paccisadinaa? Hessika mooro gidiko inte tana maarite.
Tani he inteko baanas giigettishin hayssi hedzdzanthoko. Tani intes tooho gidanas koyke. Tani intena koyayss attin inte miishe koyke. Aawati naytas miishe shiishetes attin nayti Aawatas miishe shiishi erettena.
Tani inte gishshi tanaka taas dizazi ubbaa intes aatha immidako tana daro ufaysses. Histin tani intena hayssa mala daro siiqishin inte qass tana waani guuthara siiqetii?
Ay gidikkoka ta intes tooho gidabeykke shin intes ta intena coo genen baletha oyikidazi milatees.
Ta inteko kiitta yeddida asatape issade baggaraka intefe go7ettadinaa?
Titosay inteko baana mala ta iza woossadis. Hessa nu ishazaka izara gatha yedadis. Histin Titosay intefe ayko go7ettidee? Tanine izi intes oothiday issi wozinan gidenee? Kase nu hanoy issi mala gidenee?
Inte wurikka ha7i gakkanaas qopizay nu inte sinthan nuna ashanas haniza miisha mala xeelletii? Nuni Kiristoosan gididi intes yootizayss Xoossa sintthankko. Ta siiqoto! nu hayssa wursi yootizay intena go7anas giidiko,
Tani hee biza wode oone erizay inte ta koyida mala hanontta aggiko taka inte koyiza mala gidontta dashe gagistanesha gaada hirigayss. Hessaththoka inte giddon ooshshi, qanatetethi, hanqoy, zupeteth, asa suntthu iisoy, zigirisi, otoretethine kachchi duusu aggena gaada hirigayss.
Tani qasseka he inteko bishin oone erizay ta Goday tana inte sinthan kawushande gaada hirigayss. Hayssafe kase nagara oothidi he oothida tunatethan, laymmanine coo mela yeda duussas maarotethan gelontta asata gaason ta muuzotethan wodhandina gaada hirigayss.
Histiko tani inteko bishin hayssi taas hedzdzantthokk. Aydeka gidin yooy minnizay nam77u marikan woykko hedzdzu marikankko.
Intena beyanas ta nam77anttho boyssan ta intenara dashe inte naagistana mala ta intes mintha yootadisikoshin; Ha7ika qasse hahon daada hayssafe kase nagara oothidaytasine hankoytas minitha yootayss. Ha7i ta inteko hee simma biikko isttafe oonaskka michettike.
Hessika qasse bessizay tanan gidid intes yootizay Kiristoosa gididayssa inte shaaki eranas koyzaysssakko. Inte achan diza kiristoosay wolqama attin laafa gidena.
Izi masiqale bolla kaqettidi daburisan hayqikoka ha7i qass Xossa wolqan paxa dees. Nuka izara laafata gidikkoka inte gishshi giidi Xoossa wolqan minni doosu.
Inten ammanon minni dizakone eranas ane interka intena paaci xeellite. Yesus Kiristoosay intenan dizayssa shaaki eribeyketii? Hessatho hanontta aggiko inte paacen kundidista guusuko.
Nuni paacen kundonttayssa inte shaaki erana gaada ufayss oothayss.
Inte iitta miishi oothontta mala nuni Xoossu woossosu. Nuni woossizayka nu aykoka danda7izayta gidontta aggikoka inte wurso wode lo7o ootho oothanape attin nu goobateth intena bessanas gidena.
Nuni tumatethas oothos attin tumape karera aykoka oothina danda7okko.
Nuni daburanchata gidin inte qass minota gidishin nuna ufaysses. Nu woossay inte wothoy bayndayta gidana malakko.
Tani hayssa intes yeddiza kiitaza intefe haaka dashe xaafiday hessa gishikko. Hessa malan ta inteko biza wode taas Goday immida Aawatethan ta intena waaysike. Goday taas Aawateth immiday intena minissanaskko attin laalanas gidena.
Ane ha7i ta ishato! saro diite; inte duusa lo7ethite; ta intena zoroyssa kaallite; asay issay issara sigettite. Saron diite; siiqone saro Goday intenara gidana.
Siiqo yeereteth yeeretidi issay issara saroketite.
Ammaniza asay wurikka intena saro gees.
Assi xeygidaden asi Kiitidade gidonta Yesuss Kiristossa hayqope denthida iza aawa Xoossafe kiititda Phawulossape.
Tanagara diza ishata wurisofe Gelatiyan diza wossa keethatas.
Nu aawa Xoossafe Goda Yesuss Kiristossa Xoossa kiyatethine saroy intes gido.
Nu aawa Xoossa shenemala hayssa ita 7alamezape nuna ashanas nena aththi imidaysas.
Xoossas medhiipe medhiina gakanas izas bonchoy gido.
Inte intena Kiristossa kiiyatethan xeygidaysa agagidi hara duma shako mishiracho qaalakko siimidaysi tana daro garanthes (malalises)
Tumape qasse isinipe hara mishiracho qaalay dena. Coo intena balethanasne Kiristossa mishiracho qaala miirqanas koyza is asati detes.
Gido attiin nuna gidin woykko sallo kiitanchata gidinka nu intes sabkiida mishiracho qaalape hara duma mishiracho qaala sabakiko he uray medhiinaso qangetidade giido.
Nu kase gidamalaka ta haikka zaridaka kasse inte eko mishiracho qaalape hara duma mishiracho qaala sabakiko izadey medhinas qangetidade gido gays.
Haii ta asi tana eroshi hashuganamala koyazina ye Xoosi hashu gaana mala koyazina? Woykko asa ufaysana koyazina? Ta ase ufaysana koyzako Kiristossa oothancha gidikke.
Ta ishato ta intes sabakiida mishirachoy asa ootho gidontaysa inte eranamala koyays.
Ta asape ekabeykene asape tamara beyke. Yesuss Kiristossa tas qonccisides attiin.
Tani kasse Ayhudata amano wana diidakone Xoossa wossa keethe ta aymala godidakone qasse mule dhaysanas ta aymala dafetidakone inte siydista.
Kase ta diza woden diza daro Ayhude asata darotape amanon adhays. Kasse nu awata waga naganas daro minays shin.
Gido attiin kasse koyro tana ta ayy ullon bes shakiida ba kiiyatethan ana xeygida Xoossi.
Amanonta dereza gidon iza gish ta sabakanamala ba naza tanan qoncisana dosida gish ta asho mayda asara oonaraka zoristabeyke.
Tape kasse Haware gididaytako Yerusalame ba beyke shin amanida mala heraka arabe biita badis hepekka Damasqo simadis.
Hepeka heezdzdu laythae guye Phixirossara gaganas Yerusalame kezadis. Izara gagada tamane ichachu galas gakanas gam7adiis.
Gidikokka Goda Gakanas gam7adis.
Haysa ta intes xafizaysan wogado hasa7ontaysa Xoossa sinthan yotays.
Hessafe guye gede Soriyane Kilqiya getetiza dere badis.
Kirstossa amaniza yodan diza wossa keethata asay tana bey eretena.
Gido attiin “Beni nuna amano gish godi dhaysana koyza adezi haii he amano zari sabakes” Giza wore xala siiyda.
Isti ta giidon Xoosu galatida.
Tamane oydu laythafe guye qassekka Yerusalame keezadis. He wode Barnabasara days Titossaka tanara ekka badis.
Tas qoncida giish he badis. Amanonta dereza gidon ta sabakiiza mishiracho qaalaka istas yotadis. Shin ta kasse mella woxxiidakone gane qassekka sinthafe coo mela woxonta mala hirgada wanatizaytas duma erisadis.
Haray atosin tanara diza Titosay izi girike asa shin wolliqara iza qaxxara qaxaretibeyna.
Haysi ha yozi dendiday isi isi wordo amanizayti nuni Yesussa Kiristossan demida goqatetha yuuy yuuy pacci beyanasne nuna ayletethan gelithanas lodara nuko salli gellida gishasa.
Hayta ha asatasi nuni isitoka hafeti beyko. Hesikka inte wongile tumatethan eqi danamala gidiko.
Wana milatiza asati tas aykokka milatetena Xoossi asa ayfeso beydi mado ootherena. Heyti he asati ta kiitiza yotas tas ooykoka gujji beytena.
Gido attiin Phexirosay Ayhudatas mishiracho qaala sabakanas hadara ekiidaysa mala taka qaxaretontaytas mishiracho qaala sabakanas hardara ekidaysa istti erida.
Phixirosa Ayhudistas Haware gidi oothana mala oothida Xoossi taka amanonta deretas Haware gida oothana mala taas imides.
Wana tusamala gidida Phesxirosane Yansaykka tas imetida Xoossa imo akekidi tasne ista qasse Ayhudatas qasla yotanas qaala gagidos.
Isti nus hadara giday manqotas qofa nu agontamala gida. Tasikka hessa oothaysi amo.
Phixirossa anxokiya yda wode erettida bale oothida gish ta iza qonccen izi gizaysa ixxadis (izara eqitadis)
Isi isi asati Yaqobe achafe yanape kase Phixirossay amanonta deretara isipe kaththa miizaysa asati ydape guye qaxaretida asatas babidi amanonta dere asape shaketida guye guye ooykides.
Barnabasayka istathoka qoshepe qomon hanon ekistana gakanas hara Ayhudatika iza hanon izara ispetida.
Ista oothoy mishiracho qaala tuma gidontaysa ta erada kumetha asa achan Phixirosa “Ne Ayhuda asa shin amanonta dereta wogan attiin Ayhudista wogan daka histin amanonta dereti Ayhudata dereta wogga kalanamala aazas woliqathize?
“Nuni nu yeletethan Ayhudatape attiin nagarancha amanonta dereta gidoko.
Asi Yesuss Kirstossa amanon xiilana attiin Muse woga nagon xiilontaysa nu erosu. Hessa gish wogga nagon gidonta Kirstossa amanon nu xiilanamala nukka qasse Yesuss Kistossa amanidosu. Muse wogga nagon oonikka xellena.
Nu Ayhudati wurikka Christosa baggara Xoossara giganas koyos. Nukka hankko asa mala nagaranchata gididaysa eros. Histin Kirstossay nagaray akii banamala koyize? Muleka koyena.
Tani lalida woga zara ta kushera keexxiza gidiko taka wogga moridade gididaysa amanistays.
Tani Xoossas danamala Muse wogga bagara he wogas hayqasdis.
Tani Kiristossara kaqitadis hayssafe guye dizay tana gidike shin Kiristossa ta gidon des. Haikka ta ashon diza dusay tana dosidi bena ta gish oothi imida Xoossa na bolla diza amanon days.
Tani Xoossa kiyateth kawushike. Xiilotethi Muse wogga nagon betiza misha gidiko Kirstossay mella hed hayqides gusaka?”
Inteno yushi qoponta Gelatiya asatoy! intes baletontamala iza kaqetetha ta inte sinthan milale mala gigisa besdisko shin intena oone biitiday?
Inte Xillo ayana ekiday Muse wogga nagone ye sabaketida qaala amanone? Ta hano isiniyo ta intefe erana koyays.
Inte hessamala qopi eronta asse? Ayanan oykidaysa zaridi ashon geyanas wayeteti?
Tumu inte hano gakanas daburida daburisay co mella?
Xoossi intes ayana imidayne inte achan malata oothiday inte Muse wogga nagida gisheye Woyko inte siiyda qalan amanida giishe?
Ane inte Abirame gish qoppiite “Izi Xoosu amanin amamoy izas xiillotethan qodetides.”
Hesa gish amanizayti Abirame nayta gididaysa yushi qopiite (Wozinan wothiite)
Dere asay amanon atanaysa eridi Xoosu kasse maxxafan “Derey wuri ne bagara anjjistana” Giidi mishiracho qaala Abiirames erisides.
Hesa gish amanizayti wurii amaniza Abiramera isipw anjjetidayta.
Muse wogga nagon amanetizayti wurikka qantha garisan detes. Muse wogga maxxafatan xafetidaysa wursi Othontadey zi qangetidade” geteti xafetides.
“Xiillo uray amanon deyos” giiza gish onikka Xoossa sinthan Muse woggan atontaysi gesha.
Muse woggan amanon xaphiibeyna. Gido attin “Muse wogata Musesi nagizadey he izi nagidaysan deyon dana getetides.
“Miitha bolla kaqetizadey he uray qangetidade” geteti xafetida gish Kiristossay nu gish qangetidade gididi nuna Muse wogga qangethafe wozinas.
Abirime imetida anjjoy Yesuss Kiristosa bagara deres gakanamala nuna wozides. Hesikka nuni amanon Xoossi immana gida iza ayana ufaysa ekanamala hanides.
Ta ishato ane ta intes asi ba dusan hanizamisha Museso imays. Haray atoshin asi isito bazida qaala isito bazidappe guye oonikka sharanas woykko hara iza bolla gujjana danda7ontaysamala haysikka hessa malakko.
Xoossi Abirames yotida qaala Abiramesne iza zerethas. Maxxafay daro asas yotizamala “Iza zerethatas” Gena gido attiin isi asas yotetizamala “Ne zerethas” ges. Hesikka Kiristossa.
Ta gizaykka hayssako ooydu xistane heezdzdutamu laythafe guye imetida Muse wogay kasetidi Xoosi minthida caqqoza lalidi buro hanana ufaysa qaala sharena.
Biita latoy Muse wogan hanizako ufayasa qaala gelanas koshena gish Xoossi ba kiiyatethan qalan Abirames imetides.
Hiistin Muse woggan azzas imetide? Muse wogay gudetiday asay woga yedhi athiza gish he ufaysay besiza zerethay yana gakanas Muse wogay ydayka kiitanchata bagara naga giiza isade bagara ydes.
Gidikkoka ganazi isa baga xala xelizade gidena. Xoossi gidiko izi isa xala.
Histin Muse wogay inthafe Xoosi wothina qaala digizaze? Cirasheka digena. Muse woga imetiday asi izan deyo demanas gididako tumuka xiilotethi bistanakoshin.
Qasse maxxafay haysi 7alamey wurikka nagaran qachetidaysa awajjes. Hesikka asi wurikka Yesuss Kiristossa amanon betiza ufaysay amanizaytas wurisos imistanasa.
Haysi amanoy yanape kasse nuni Muse wogan qachetidi gordana dosu.
Hessa gish nu amanon xiilana mala Muse wogay nuna Kiristosakko gathanas nagizade mala gidi nagides.
Ha7i qasse he amanoy yida gihs hayssafe guye nuni Muse wogga garisan dokko.
Inte wurikka Yesuss Kiristossa amanon Xoossa nayta.
Inte Kirstossara gidana xamaqetidayti wurikka Kiristossa maydista.
Inte wurikka Yesusi Kiristossan isino attiin Ayhudene Girike aylene Goqqane maccane ade giza dumatethi dena. Inte wurikka Yesusi Kiristosan isi asho.
Inte Kirstossayta gidiko inte Abirame zerethata kasse imetida ufaysa qaala mala inte latanayta.
Ta gizay aawape yelettida nay aawa latay izas gidikokka izi bidi latana gakanas aylefe duma gidena.
Iza aaway izi diccidi giita gidana gakanas dichizade kushe gasan deyos.
Nuka buro natethan diza wode hayssa 7alameza timirte mala ayletethan hareti deydos. Wogga garisara yeleti ba naza yeddides.
Gido attiin kasse ba qopii wothida wodey gakin Xoossi maccashayfe yelettidaysa Muse woggape garisara yeleti ba naza yeddides.
Hesika nuni iza naa gidanamalane Muse wogga garisan dizayta wozana mala hanides.
Inte iza na gidida gish Xoossa “Nu aawa obo” gidi xaygiza ba naza ayana nu wozina gido yeddides.
Hesa gish hayssafe guye ne nape attiin ayle gidaka. Nuni na gidida gish Xoossi nena bena latizade histides.
Inte Xoosu eranape kasse Xoosu gidonta eqatas aylista.
Ha7i qasse Xoosu eridista hessafeka Xoossan eretidista. Histin qasseka guye simidi ede goy7ay baynda co daburisiza timrteka wanidi simizeti. Simidi qaseka ayletetha qamibaran waxistana koyeti?
Duma galasata aginata wodetane laythata bonchideti?
Ta inte bolla daburidays co mela gidande gada babaysi
Ta ishato ta intena milatidamala inteka tana milatanamala ta intena wasays. Inte tana aykoka qohibeykista.
Inte erizamala ta intes koyro mishiracho qaala sabakiday sako gasona.
Ta sakoy intes metto gidinka tana saletibeykista woykko tana harisebeykista gido attiin inte tana Xoossa kiitancha malane hessafeka bollara Yesuss Kiristos mala moki ekidista.
Histin hai he inte ufaysay awa gakiide? intes hanizaz gididako inte inte ayfe tas kees imanas inte guye gontaysa ta intes marikatays.
Tani tuma kesa yotida gish inte morike gidadinasha?
Heyti asati intena beko ekanas daburetes attiin loo7os daburetena. Isti koyzay intena nupe shakidi ba asa kesanas.
Loo7os mindatethi loo7oko hesika hananas besizay wuriso wode gidikofe attiin ta intenara diza wode xala gidena.
Ta intena siqqiza ta nayto Kiristossay inte wozinan xafetin ta beyana gakanas inte gish ta miixatays.
Ta inte gish qofan metotistadis. Ta dandaizako hai inte gidon bistada hanqo qalara intes yotizako aymala dosazina shin!
Omteno Muse wogga garisan aqana koyhayto ane tas yotite Muse woga ay gizakone siybeyketi?
Abirames isay aydeype asay qase godaiyfe yelettida nam7u nayti dizaysi kase xafetides.
Ayleyfe yelettida nazi asho wogga mala yeletides hanko goqaype (Godateyfe) Yeletidaysa ufaysa qaala mala yeletides.
hayti naam7u macashati nam7u caqota besiza gish haysi lemusos imetides. Koyro caqoya sina zuma bolla gidashe ayletethas gidiza nayti yeliizaro izaka agaro guussa.
Hesa gish agara arvbe biitan diza sino zuma giish gidada hai diza Yerusaleme milataysu iza ba nazara ayletethan daysu.
Pude bolla bagara diza Yerussalamey gidiko goqqa Goda daysu izaka nu ayiyo
“Neni yelonta makaraye ufa7ista Hane miixata erontare Illil ga wassa Azinay dizarape balara Berka dizari nayti darida” geteti kasse xafetides.
Hesa gish ta ishato inteka Ysaqamala ufaysa qaala naytako.
Asho shenemala kaseti yelettidaysi guyepe ayna woliqan yelettidaysa yedethides (godides) haiika godethan des.
Gido attiin maxxafay qasse ay gize? “Ayleyo izi nazaragathi diiga ayley nay goqaynara latina” ges.
Hesa gish ta ishato nuni goqay nayti attiin ayley nayta gikoka.
Nuna Kiristossay geshiday nuni geshatethan danas. Hessa gish miini eqite nam7antho ayletetha qanbaran ge
Ta insa gizaysa wozina wothite inte qaxaristanakoyko Kistossay intes kiyontasa ta isas isas qoncen yotays.
Qaxaristanakoyzayti wuri Muse woga wursi polanaysi dosa gidenaysa ta intes isas isas qonccen yotays.
Inteno Muse wogan geyana (Xilana) waytizayto inte Kiristossape shaketidista iza kiyatethafeka hakidista.
Nu qase ufaysan nagetiza xiilotetha ayana bagara amanon lamotethan nagon dosu.
Asi Yesuss Kirstossan diko qaxaretin woykko qaxaretonta agin ayne go7ene go7ay dizay siqqon qoncciza amano xala.
Kase loo7o wothu woxista shin haii intes xuphe gididi tumasi inte azazetonta mala intena digiday oone?
Hessa mala balethoy intena xeygidadefe yibeyna.
Gutha irshoy (calay) lixxe wuris callises.
Intes hara qofay dena gada tani Godan amanistaysi intes taki gizaz oothozay ona gidikone izi ba piirda ekana.
Ta ishato hachi gakanas tani qaxara gish sabakiizako oone tana godanay? Hesamala gididako masqalas shuphe gidenako shin.
Intes tii gizaz oothizaz oothiza asati co wogara qaxareteth agidi untafe dutheto.
Ta ishato inte goqateth kezanas xeygetidista. Inteni inte goqateth zaridi untafe dutheto sho amo polanas go7etopite. Hessafe inte inte garisan siqqon isay isa madite.
Muse wogay wuri shiqetidi isi qalan qachetes hesika “Neni ne lage ne mala xeela gizaysa.
Gido attiin inte isay isara saxxetizayta gidiko inte inte garisan wurontamala nagetite.
Hessa gish ta intena ayanan simeretite gays asho amoka polopite.
Ashoy ayanay koyontazi amotes ayanayka ashoy koyontaz amotes. Heyti isay isara ba garisan shocetiza (Ayetiza) gish inte inte koyda mala othekista. (hanekista)
Inte ayanan diza gidiko Muse woga garisan dekista.
Asho oothoy qonccen eretes hesika laymateth tunateth layma kasse (ziita)
Eqas goyno biita pola (adheteth) ooshu miqaneteth hanqo bena xala doso shaketeth zufeteth.
Qanateteth mathoteth 7lame yeth yexxethane heytanta milatizayta. Tani intes kaase yotida mala ha7ka inte nagistanamala qofisays. Hesamala dusu dizayti wurikka Xoossa kawotethi latetena.
Ayana ayfey gidiko siiqo, ufays saroteth, danda7a, kiyateth, loo7oteth, amaneteth
Ashoketetha berka bena haro. Haytantamala digizay Muse wogga garisan dena.
Yesuss Kiristossas gididayti asho iza ita qofarane iza ita amotethara gathi kaqqida.
Nu ayanan dana koyko ane ayanan simeretosu.
Ane nuni nu garisan isay isara mindi letizaysane qanatetishe mela hada ceeqetoko.
Ta ishato isi uray nagara oothi betiko inte qase ayanan loo7o dizayti iza ashaketethara zaranas beses gido attiin nekka izademala paccetonta mala ne hu7es nagista.
Isay isa dexxo toho toko hessamalan oothon Kirstossa wogga pollista.
Isadey ayne hanonta dishe ayko giitaso gakida milatiko he uray berika bena balethes.
Isi isi uray ba ootho berika pacci xelo. Hesafe guye hara urara bena ginasonta diisheizi bena ceqisizaz demana.
Isi isi uray berka ba toho tokanas beses.
Qala tamarizay onika ba tamarida loo7o misha ba astamarera gishetes.
Baletofite Xoosi qlicca erena. Assi ba zeridaro iza zera buccana.
Be asho amo kunthanas zerizadey ashope dhaysi buccana. Ayana ufaysanas zeridadey gidiko ayanape medhina deyo buccana.
Ane nu loo7o ootho oothanas azaloko nu ufaysi qanxonta agiko wodey gakishin nu gakida kaatha maxana.
Hesa gish loo7o ootho oothanas azaloko nu ufaysi qanxxonta agiko wodey gakiishin nu gakiida kaatha maxana.
Tani ta kushera intes aymala gita piidalen xafidakone ane xeliite.
Co kare bagara bistana koyza asati inte qaxaristanamala gidesana koyetes. Isti hessa oothzay Kirstossa masqale gish gidi godetonta malako.
Isti inte qaxaristanamala koyzay inte ashon ceeqistanas koyza gish attiin qaxaretidayti Muse wogga nagizayta gidetena.
Qase 7alamey tas taka 7alames kaqetida Goda Yesuss Kiristossa masqalepe attiin hara ceqoy tape hakko.
Qaxaretin woykko qaxaretonta agin izas go7ay bawa. Go7ay medheteth.
Haysa ha azazoza kaalliza wurisosine Xoossa dere gidida Isra7elistas saroyne marotethi gido.
Tani Yesussa malata ta asatethan tokadis hessa gish hi7a tana oonikka waysena.
Ta ishato Goda Yesus Kiristossa adho kiyatethi intenara godo. Amiini
Xoossa shene mala Yesus Kiristossa Haware gidida Phawulossape. Yesus Kirstosan diza amanetizaytas Efesonen amaniza asas.
Nu aawa Xoossafe Goda Yesus Kiristossape kiyatethine sarotethi intes gido.
Nu Goda Yesuss Kiristossa bagara sallon ayana anjjo wurison nuna anjjuda Goda Yesuss Kirisitossa aaway Xoossi anijjeto.
Nu iza sinthan geshatana wothoy bayndayta gidana mala buro alamey medhetanape kasse ba siqon Kirstosa bagara nuna dorides.
Yesus Kiristossa bagara nu iza na gidana mala ba loo7o qofan koyro wursi wothides.
Hesika ba dosizade bagara coo mela nusu imetida boncho kiiyatethay galatistan malakko.
Xoossa adho kiyatethan Yesuss sunthan nagarape nu maretidos.
Izi ba kiyatethane cincateth nu bolla kezi darsides.
Kiristossa bagara Xoossi nuus qopida xuura qofa Kirstosa bagara nuna erisides.
Burope wode wurisethan hanana diza iza qofay sallo bolane biita bolla dizaytas wurisos hu7e gidida Yesuss Kiristossape wursi garse oothanaskko.
Wurisikka ba shene mala oothiza iza shenemala nuka iza koyroka izi dorida gish nuni izan doretidosu.
Nuni kasetidi Kiristossa bagara ekana gidi ufaysan nagizayti Xoossa boncho galatan qoncisansikko.
Inteka qase tuma qaala hesika intena ashiza mishiracho qaala siydi Kiristosan amanidista. Iza amanidi kase imistana getetida xiilo ayanan atametidista.
He ayanazikka iza boncho galatan qoncisana mala Xoossi bees gididayta worsota wozana gakanas nu latas ooythoko.
Hesa gish inte Goda Yesussa amannida gishine amaniza asa inte siqizaysa ta siyosope ha simin intena qopa qopa ekada tani ta wosan inte gish Xoossas galata shisho agabeyke.
<range>
Boncho aawa gidida nu Goda Yesuss Kiristossa awa Xoossi inte loo7ethi eranamala qonccisiza ayanayinne eratetha ayanay intes imistana mala ta intes paccey baynda wosays.
Hessathokka inte izan xeygetida ufaysay hessikka amanizayta achan diza iza latisiza duretethay azakone inte erana mala inte wozina ayfey po7ana mala wosays.
Amaniza nunan oothiza wursofe bolla gidida gitta Xoossa wolqa inte erana mala ta wosays. He wolqaykka oonikka teqontayssanne mulekka daburontaysakko.
Kirstosa hayqoppe denthidi salon Xoossa ushachan utisiday he wolqakko.
Aysizaytape godatethape woliqafene kawotethappe qaseka ha7i xala gidonta burope yana wodeka gidin sunthu wurisofe izi bollakko.
Xoossi hara wursi iza tope garissan harisides. Wossa keeththanka wuriso bolla hu7e histides.
Wossa keethiya kirstossa asatethikko. Kirstosaykka wossa keethaynine awanka wuriso miishi kunthes.
Intene inte qohida qoho gishine inte nagara gason hayqodaytakkko shin,
Hessa inte hayssa alameza ita ooge kalidista. Bolla cariko bolla diza woliqama harizaysas ha7ika Xoossas azazetonta asa bolla oothiza ita ayanas inte azazetishe deista.
Haysafe kasse nuni nu asho amoteth polishe ashoy koyiza oge kallishe istara doos. Nuunikka hankko asa mala nu medhetethappe Xoossa hanqo garsan dookko shin,
Gido attiin Xoossi keehi siqida gish ba marotetha daron nuni nu qoho dartethan hayqidayta gidi diishin Kirstosa bagara nuna ashides. Inte paxxiday iza kiiyatethankko.
<range>
Xoossi nuna Kiristossara gathi denthides. Yesuss Kiristossa bagara nuna sallon benara utisides.
Hesika hayssafe guye yana wodezan Yesuss Kirisossay nuus ba kiiyatethan qonccisida zaway baynda ba kiiyatetha duretetha nuna besanas.
Inte Xoossa kiyatethan amanon atidista. Hesikka Xoosi intes mela coo imidazape attiin inte oothoppe gidena.
Onika ceqetonta mala oothope gidena.
Hesika Xoossi kasse koyro nus gigisi wothida loo7o ootho nuni oothanamala Yesuss Kiristossa bagara nuni nam7antho medhetidaytane Xoossi medhetethatakko.
Hesa gish inte kase inte yeletethan amanonta dere asati inte asatetha bolla asa kushe ootho geedon nuni qaxaretidosu giza asati intena “qaxaretontayta” gizayto inte hessa ane wozinan wothiite.
Inte he wode Kiristossape shaketidi Isra7ele naytape hakiidi caqqo qalaska alaga gididi hayssa alameza bolla ufaysine Xoosi baynda inte kasse dizaysa yushi qopiite.
Ha7i qase inte kasse hanon dizayti Yesus Kiristossan gididi iza sutha bagara shiqidista.
Nam7ata isi bolla gathidi gidon shakiiza oosha goda lallida nu saroy izako.
Wogga iza azazora gathi isife ba ashon sharides. Hessa izi oothida gasoy izas wana qofay nam7atape isi ooratha asa ba bagara medhidi sarotethi ehanasa.
Izi masqale bolla hayqidi morketeth digides. Nam7atakka isi asho histidi Xoossara maqanthidees.
Izi yidi intena haki dizaytasne matan dizaytas gathii sarotethi sabakiides.
Nu wurikka iza bagara isi ayanan awwa ach shiqqana danda7os.
Hesa gish inte amanizaytara isife isi dere asanne Xoossas so asa attiin heysafe gyue betistane alaga gidekista.
Inte Hawaristane nabeta baasan kexetidista, kethas worsetha qustey Yesus Kiristossakko.
Kethzi wurikka isipe oyketidi Godas duma keth gidanas dicces.
Intenika Xoosi ba ayanan danas izas dusaso gidanamala isipe kexxetishe dista.
Hesa gedon ta Phawulossay intes amanontayta gish Yesuss Kiristossay qachidade gidadis.
Ta intena go7ana mala Xoossi kiytethan taas oothos exxa imidaysa inte tumape siydista.
Haysafe kasse ta intes qanthara xafida mala tas qonccin ta eranas danda7ida xura hayssako.
Hesa gish inte hessa nababishe Kirstossa xura ta ay mala eridakone inteka eranas danda7ista
He xurayka ha7i amaniza Hawaristasine nabetas qonccidaysa mala kasse beni adhida wode diza asataska qonccibeyna.
Hesi he xuray hanko amanonta asay mishiracho qaala bagara Isra7eele naytara isipe latizayta isipe isade asatetha mala gididi Yesuss Kiristossa bagara betida ufaysa ispe gisheti latizayta gidanskko.
Taka iza woliqa ootho mala tas imetida Xoossa kiiyatetha imota mala hayssa mishiracho qaala oothancha gidadis.
Ta qass hanko amaniza asape lafa gidikkoka oonikka zaway baynda Kiristossa dureteth hanko derezas sabakana mala Xoossa kiyatethan haysi tas imetides.
Hesathoka wursikka medhida Xossan beni wode qoteti diza xuuray Xooossa qofay azakonne wurisos ta qonccisana mala tas Xoossa kiyatethi imetides.
Iza cincatrthi ha7i wode wossa keeththa baggara duma duma medhay diza Xoossa hilatethi sallon diza halaqatasine godatas eretana mala hanides.
Xoossi nu Goda Yesuss Kiristossa bagara hayssa poliday medhina ba qohaaththaa malakko.
Nuuni izayta gidida gishinne izan amanida gish xalatetharane hirgay baynda nuni Xoossako shiqana danda7os.
Hessa gish inte bonchetana mala tani inte gish ta bolla gakida wayezan inte ufaysi qanxonta mala ta intena hadara gays.
Hesa gish tani Xoossa sinthan gulibatays.
Sallon dizayne biita bolla dizay izaso asay wurikka izi sunthin suumes.
Intes garisa bagara miinana mala ayana bagara iza boncho duretethay intes imistana mala ta woosays.
Hesikka Kiristossay inte wozinan amanon dana malanne qaseka inte izan xaphidi siqon minana malakko.
Kiristossa siiqos ahotethay adusatethay dhoqatethayine ciimatethay ay ginakko inte amaniza asa wurisora isipf shakii erana malakko.
Inte Xoossa kumethara shaaki eridi izan kumeth gidana mala asa erape bollara gidiida Kiristoosa siiqo inte erana mala wossays.
Hessa gish nu gidon oothiza ba wolliqa gina nu wosiizaysafene woykko nu qopiizaysafe wurisofe bollara kezi darsi oothanas danda7iza Xoossas,
Wossa keeththan qaseka Yesuss Kiristossa bagara wode wurson medhiinape medhina gakanas izas bonchoy gido. Amin7i
Hessa gish Goda sunthan qachetida tani inte xeygetida xeysas besiza dusu dana mala intena wosays.
Muleka ashikistane shugista gidite. Issay isara siiqon diitene isay isa danda7ite.
Sarotethi immiza ayana isipeteth naganas miinite.
Inte xeygetida galas isi ufaysako xeygetidaysa mala isi asatethine isi ayanay dees.
Isi Goday isi amanoyne isi xiinqatay dees.
Wurisofe bollara gididay, wuriso bolla oothizay, wursoson dizay, wursos awwa gidida isi Xoossi des.
Gidikoka Kiristossay imana gi qachida mala nusu isas issas duma duma imotethi imetides.
Hessa gish “Izi pude kezida wode dii7o di7ides. Assas kiiyateth imota imides.” geteti geisha maxafan xafetidees.
Histin “Iza pude kezides” gusi qaseka duge biita garisa wodhides gusu giodonta agiko hessi ay guse?
Duge garise wodhidaysi kumeth alame medheteth kumana mala sallopekka bolla keziday izako.
Isi isi asati hawarista bagati nabeta harati mishracho qaala sabake bagayti qasse hemizaytane tamarisizayta gidana mala izi imota immidees.
Hesika Kiristossa asateth gidida wossa kethiya keexistana mala amanizayta amano oothos giigsinaskko.
Hesika hananay nu wurikka Xoossa na amanonine iza eron betiza isipetethiko gakidi kumetha asi gidanas Kiristossan nuni kirstosatho kumethinne polo gidana malakko.
Hesa gish aba bolla dendiiza gote caarkoy hene ha shocechiza mala dumma dumma timirte carkon asa geneninne balethon anne nuni hene ha phonqitise qeeri gutha nayta mala hanoko.
Hesatho hano agidi ane tuma siiqon hasaishe ispetethan hu7e gididaysako hanizazan wurison ane diccos. He hu7ezikka Kiristosako.
Iza gedon asatethi wurii xaphon ooyketidi isi isi asatethi ba ootho othishe wurikka siiqon diiceesine benaka miinthes.
Hanko amanonta asamala coo mela qohaaththaan mela siimeristanas intes besena gada ta intena zorays.
Ista wozinay mumida gishane yushi qoponta gish issta wozina ayfey qoqides. Isiti Xoossa de7ope shaketida.
Ista wozinay doccida gish kalloy baynda ba koydamala bena kallisonta amonine tunatethan danas wogay baynda iita oothos bena aathi immida.
Inte qasse Kirstossa hessa malan eribeykista.
Ee tumukka inte iza gish siiydistane Yesussan diza tuma izape tamaridista.
Inte kasse diza dussay balethiza amon qitida gise kase ceega asatetha intefe intefe qariyogana tamaridista.
Qasseka inte qofay ayanan oraxo.
Tumu xillotethaninne geshatethan Xoosu milatana medhetida ooratha asateth mayte.
Nu wurikka issi asho gidida gish wordotethi digidi nuni nu garasan issay issara anne tumma hasa7os.
Hanqetite shin nagara oothofite, iinte hanqon diishin awwa arshey wulofo.
Xala7es so imofiite.
Kasse kaysotizadey hayssafe guye kaysotpo. Gido atiin metotetidi iza wosizaytas imizay iza kushen deyana mala loo7o miish ba kushera oothi demanas daburo.
Koshiza mala hanko siyzayta go7izazine madiza qalape attiin go7oy baynda qalay inte dunape kezopo.
Inte atana galasas atametida Xoossa Xillo ayana michisopite.
Camo yo wuriisi hanqoka, yilo, ooshu, cashe, qassekka hanko hara itateth wursi intefe digiite.
Intena Xoossi Kiristossa bagara ato gida mala intekka inte garisan atto atto getetite, issay isara kiiyatane isay isas qadheetizayta gidite.
Hessa gish inte dosetiza nayta mala Xoosu millaatite.
Kirstossay nuna siqidaysa mala qasseka nu gish bena sawiiza yarsho mala Xoossas aathii imida mala inteka siiqon simiiretite.
Laymay woykko tunatethi woykko uzetethi mulekka inte gidon betoy attin zigirsikka siyetofo. Hesamala gesha Xoossa asas besena.
Inte galata galatizayta gidite attin asse yelachiza lafa hasa7ay co eyatetha yoy intes besontaa gish hessamalay inte garisan doppo.
Qasseka inte laymatizaytas woykko tuanatas woykko uzetizaytas Kiristossa kawotethanine Xoossa kawotethan istas latasoy bayndaysa inte eriite. Uzetethi eqqas goyno malakko.
Intena oonikka worido hasa7on balethofo. Gasoyka Xoossa hanqoy izas azazetonta nayta bolla yanay haytanta malana.
Hessa gish hessanta malara isipetopitte.
Kasse inte dhuuma shin Godan ha77i inte poo7o. Inte poo7o nayta mala diite.
Poo7os ayfey loo7otethan xiilotethanine tumatethan wurison des.
Hesathoka Goda ufaysiza miish koyite.
Ayfey baynda dhuma oothora intes ayko gagotethi dopo. Hessafe iita ootho qoncce kesite.
Dhuman diza asati geman oothiza misha gish hasa7aykka yelaches.
Po7oy po7iidazi wuri qonceen betes.
Gasoyka wursi besiizay poo7o. Hessa gish “Neno dhiskizayso beega, hayqope denda, Kiristosay nes po7isana” getetides.
Hesa gish eratethi bayndayta mala gidonta inte wanidi erata mala danakone nagetite.
Haysi wodezi iita gidida gish hessa lo7ethi eritte.
Hesa gish eyata gidopiite Goda sheney azakone yushi qopiite.
Ayanay kumidayta gidite atiin mathosiza ushan mathotofiite. Hessi meela miishe lallethikko.
Ayana yethan galatara gathi yexishe inte garsan isay isara hasa7etite. Inte sabaninne yethan kumetha wozinape Goda galatite.
Hesan Xoossa aawwa Goda Yesuss Kiristossa suntha wuriso mishas wuriso wode galatite.
Inte Kiristossas imiiza boncho yashara issay issas azazetite.
Macheeto inte Godas haretizamala inte azinatas haretite.
Kirstossay ba asho gidida wossa kethaysi hu7e gidida mala azinayka ba machcheysi hu7ekko.
Hesa gish wossa kethiiya Kirstosas azazetiza mala machchetika ba azinatas ay hanonka azazistanas beses.
Azinato, Kirstossay wossa keethayo siiqida malane bena izi gish athi imida mala inteka inte machcheta siiqite.
Be qaala bagara haathan meecci geshiidi bes dumasida mala.
Hesathoka qitay woykko ayfeso xiirphotethi woykko isi iitay izi bolla betonta geshiine balay izi bolla bayndaro boncho wossa keeth histidi bes shishanaskko.
Azinatika hessaththo ba machcho ba ashsho mala siiqanas beses. Be machcho siiqizadey bena siiqes.
Berika bena ixxiizadey oonikka ba. Be ashshos mesine bena nages. Kirstossayka wossa keethas hinithokka oothiides.
Nuni Kiristossa asatetha bollatakko.
Hessa gish “assi ayone aawa agidi ba machcheyra isino gidens, nam7aykka isi ashsho gidetes” Geteti gesha maxafan xafetides.
Haysi daro xuura yo, taka hayssa Kirstossa gishine wossa keeththa gish yotays.
Gidikkoka intefe isi issadey ba machcho bena siqqiza mala siqqo machchaka ba azina bonchu.
Nayto inte intena yellidaytas Godan azazetite. Hessi intes beses.
“Ne aawane ne ayiyo boncha” giza azazo gidon diza ufayssay koyro azazokko.
Ne hessaththo oothikko nees loo7anane nes laythay biita bolla aduqana.
yelidayto inteka inte nayta hanqeetisopite giido attin inte nayta Goda zoreen suran diichite.
Othanchato inte Kiristossa azazetizamala biitta bolla intena oothisizaytasyashatethan bonchon sure wozinape azazetite.
Co asa ayfen bistanamalane oothisizaytappe duna anjjo ekanas gidonita inte Kiristossa aylleista mala Xoossa shene kumetha wozinape polanamala wozinape azazetite.
Assas oothiizamala gidonta Godas oothiizamala inte kumethi wozinape oothiite.
Gasoykka aylle gidin woykko goda gidin ba oothiiza loo7o oothos wurisos woyto ekanaysa inte ereta.
Inteno Godato inteka inte oothisizaytas hessaththo oothite. Istasie intes Goda gididay bolla sallon dizaysa izikka as ayeso xeeli madontayssakka intekka eriiza gish oothanchata babiso agidi loo7o oothite.
Hara bagara miino Godaninne iza gita woliqana minite.
Dabullosa gene ootho inte eqistanasa danda7anamala Xoossa olla mayota mayte.
Gasoyka nu olistanay ashorane suthara gidonta hayssa dhuma alameza hariiza Godatarane wolliqamatara qasekka sallo bolla diza tuna ayanata oolanchatarako. Nu olleetizay.
Ita galasay gakiishin inte morikke wolqara eqistanas danda7anamala Xoossa oola mayota kumeth mayte. Inte wursikka pollidape guye mini eqanas danda7ista.
Hesagishi inte daban tumu zinare dancetidi xiilotehta biirista mala tiran maydi.
Sarotetha mishiracho qaala toon cama mala oothid gigeti eqiite.
Heytantafekka bolara tamamala pofol7u giizza ita ayana wondafista inte wursi toysana danda7anamala amano gondale mala denthite.
Intes birata qobe mala hu7en wothite. Ayana giththa masha ooykite heesikka Xoossa qalakko.
Wossan ay hanonka ayanan wosite. Hesa qopiidi begiite amanizayta wuriso gish qanxxonta wosiite.
Tani mishiracho qaala xuura asas konccisanas duna doyza wuriso wode yashii baynda ta xalatethan yotana qalay tas imistanamala wosiite.
Tani mishiracho qaala gish sanbalatan qachistada kiitetidade gididay hessasako. Hessa gish ta yotanas besizaysa babonta yotanamala tas wosiite.
Ta aymala dizakone ay oothiizako inte eranamala dosetida ta ishay Godas amanetida oothanchay Tikiqosay intes hanidaysa wursikka yotana.
Inte nu hanoteth eranamalane inte wozina izi minthethanamala ta iza inteko yedadiis.
Aawa Xoossafe Goda Yesuss kiristossape sarotethine siiqoy amanora intes ta ishataso gido.
Goda Yesussa Kirstossa pacey baynda siiqiza wursos sarotethi giido. Amin7i.
Yesus kiristoosa oothancha gidida Phawulosapene Xintoosape woossa keeththa cimatarane daqonistara issife Pilipisiyosa deren diza ammanizaytas Yesus kiristoosas dummatidaytas wursios,
Nu Aawa Xoossafe Goda Yesus kiristoosape kiyatethine saroteth intes gido.
Intena qopiza wursio galas tani ta Xoossa galatays.
Wurisio gallas inte gishshi ta woossiza wode ufayssan woossays.
Koyro gallasafe ha simmin ha7i gakanas mishiracho qaala oothon inte tanara deista.
Intenan lo7o ootho doommmidayssi izi Yesus kiristoosay wursietha piridas yaana gakanas intena danda7issanayssa ta ammanays.
Ta ha7i qasho keeththan dishinine ta qachistanapeka kase mishiracho qaala tuma naaganasine minithanas Xoossi taas ba kiyatethan immida maadon inte wurikka tanara issife oothidayta gidida gishshi inte wursio galas ta wozinape dhayekkista. Hessa gishshi ta inte gishshi qopanas taas besses.
T ainttena Yesus kiristoosa siiqon wossita amotizakkone Xooss taas marikako.
Inte siiqoy eratethaninne akkekan keehi darana mala ta woossays.
Hessika inte wursiofe adhdhizayssa shaaki erana malane Yesus kiristoosa yuusa galas gakanas inte geeshatane wothoy bayndayta gidana mala koyayiss.
Xoossa bonchisizayssane galatissizayssa inte oothana mala Yesus kiristoosan beettiza geeshatetha ayfen inte wozinay kumo.
Ha7ika ta ishato ta bolla gakida metoy mishiracho qaalay kasepe dari aakanas gididayssa inte erana mala ta koyays.
Hessa gishshi ta qachetethay kiristoosa gishshi gididayssi kawo keeththa zabaynatasine hartasika eretides.
Ta qachetidayssa geedon ammanizayti Xoossa qaala babbontta xalatethan asas marikatanas minoteth demmida.
Issi issi asati coo nu izape waanidoni geethanine hollotethan sabakettes. Baggayti qasse lo7o qofara Kiristoosa gishshi sabaketes.
Baggayti ta mishiracho qaala gishshi mootistana haan dizayssa eriza gishshi siiqon sabaketes.
Hankoyti qasse lo7o qofan gidontta tana gakida qashoza bolla hara waaye gathanasine ba iitta qofa polanas Kiristoosa sabaketes.
Heessa gidikone aya meto dizay! Waana ayfe yooy suuretethan gidin woykko milatoson gidinka awaraka kiristoosa sabakiza gishshi ta ufa7istayss. Qassekka ta ufa7istana.
Ta birshista atany inte woossanine Yesus kiristoosa ayana maadon gididayssa ta erayss.
Ta ay ogeraka yeellatontta mala mino ufayssine laamotay taas dees. Gido attin kaseka hachchika, ta hayqqinka paxa diin kiristoosay ta ashon bonchetanayssa ta xalatethan hasa7ayss.
Taas duusu guusi kiristoosako. Hayqoyka taas go7ako.
Gido attin hayssa tanni hayssa asho dusan guja dizakko ayfe immiza ootho othays gusukko. Ta awayssa dooranakone taas erettena.
Ha nam77u Hanotan metotistadis. Ta baada kiristoosara daanas laamotayss. Hessi hara wursiofe keehi lo7oko.
Gido attin taas ashon duusi intes keehi koshees.
Hessan amanistada ta hayqoppe atada intenara deyin ntte diccanaysanne inte amanon ufa7istanaysa ta ammanetayss.
Ta he bada inte achan deyikko ta gedon intes Kirstosan diza ceqetethi darana.
Kiristoosa mishiracho qaalas bessiza mala diite. Hessatho hanika ta intena hee baada be7idako woykko hahon daada inte gishshi ta siyizako inte mishiracho qaala ammanos issino oletishe issi ayanan inte minni eqnayssa ta erayss.
Ay ogeraka intenara eqetizaytas hirigopite. Hessi istti dhayanasine inte atanayssas Xoossafe imettida malatako.
Inte kiristoosa ammanizayta xalala gidontta iza gishshi waaye ekizayta gidana mala hayssi Xoossa kiyatethi intes imettides.
Inte kase beyida mala ha7ika ta bolla dizayssa inte siyizayssa mala hessaththo intenaka waayison dees.
Intes kiristoosa baggara bettida issifetetha gaason issay issa minithethiyssa siiqo gidinka woykko ayana issifeteth woykko maaroyne asa micheteth inte garisan diiko inte asi siiqon issi ayanannine issi qofan gididi ta ufayssi polite.

Taka inteko mata wode baanaysa Godan ammanetayss.

Ta ishato hayssafe hara ta intena gizay Godan ufa7etite. Ha7ika zaarada izo ta intes xaafiko tana salethena. Intenaka go7ana.

Ta ceeqana koyko asho baggara ceeqana miishi taasika dees. Oonasika ashon ceeqiza miishi diza milatiko ta izape aadhayssi.
Tani yelletida ossipuntha galas qaxxaristadis. Ta Isiraa7eele zerethine Biniyame kochafe yeletadis. Ibirawista gidon taka adda Ibiraweko. Woga baggara oychizadey diiko ta kase Perisawe.

Gido attin taas go7a gididayssa wursia kirisoosa gishshi gaada go7ay baynda miisha mala qoodadis.

Tani hessaththo oothiza gaasoy kase Muse wogan taas diza xiillotetha aggada ammanon beettiza Xoossa xiilloteth kiristoosan ammanada demmanasine ta izara issife deyansiko.

T a ishato ta ha7i ta koyzayssaka oyikida mala qoodike. Gido attin ta issi miishi oothana. Tape guyera dizayssa agga aggada tape sinthan dizayssa oykanas zaradhayss.

Asa qofape bollara diza Xoossa sarotethi inte wozinane inte qofa wursii Yesus kiristoosan naagees.
Wurisietha bolla ta ishato tumu gidida yoo wursi, boncho gidida yoo wursi, adda gidida yoo wursi, geeshi gidida yoo wursi, dosetida miishi wursi, lo7o gidida yoo wursi, lo7otethi gidinika galataka haytantta milatiza wursi qopite.
Inte taape tamaridayssa woykko inte taape ekkidayssane siyidayssa woykko beyidayssa ay gidiko wursi oothite. Goday intenara gidana.

Medheteth wuri izan medhettides. Salonine sa7an dizayti, ayfen beetizaytine beetonttayti gidinkka woliqamata gidinka haarizayta gidinka woykko godatethi dizayti haniday wurikka izan izas medhetides.
Izi wursofe kase dees. Wurika issi bolla oyketi minniday izaniko.

Xoossa qaala ta intes pacey baynida gaththana mala taas Xoossafe imettida hadara mala ta woossa keeththa oothancha gidadis.
Ha qaalay beni wodepene kase yeletethafe geemmid xuura gidi gammi7des. Ha7i gidiko ammanizaytas wursos qonccides.
Xoossi ba asas qonccisanas koyida xuuray iza boncho duretethay dere asa gidida inte giddon ay mala gitakone bessanaskko. Izika iza boncho ufayssi gidida inte gidon diza kiristoosako.

Hessa wurso bolla wursi kumetha issifetethan shiishi qachchiza siiqo mayite.
Inte wurikka issi asho gididi sarotethas xeeygetida kiristoosa saroteth inte wozinan kawoto. Inte galatizayta gidite.
Kiristoosa qaalay intenan kumeth gido. Inte inte garisan cinccatethara tamarttene zoretote. Mazumurenine saban ayana yethan galatara gathi inte wozinara Xoossas yexxite.
Iza baggara Xoossa Aawas galata shiishishe qaalan gidin woykko oothon inte oothizayssa wurs Goda Yesusa sunththan oothite.
Macheto Goda achchan intes bessiza miishi gidida gishshi inte azinatas azazetite.
Azinato inte inte machcheta siiqitene isttas menxxe (meqeth) iittopite.
Nayto, inte Goda ufayssana mala inte intena yelidaytas wurso miishan azazetite.
Aawato, nayti ufayss qaxxontta mala inte nayta hanqethopite.
Aylleto, ase ufayssanasine coo ayfeson beistanas gidontta suure wozinape inte Godas babbite. Hayssa biittan haariza godataskka hano wurson azazetite.
Inte oothiza miishi wurs asas gidontta Godas oothiza mala taybidi kumetha wozinape oothite.
Inte Goda achchafe inte ootho mala ekkanas laatay dizaysa inte ereta. Inte oothizay Goda Yesus kiristoosaskko.
Qoho oothidadey ba oothidari kushe ekkana. Iza achchan dumma maadoy deena.
Godato, intes salon Goday dizayssa inte eriza gishshi intes oothizaytas tumanine suuretethan oothite.
Beegidi galatara gathi pacey bayinda Xoossa woossite.
Ta iza gishshi qachchetida kiristoosa xuura awajanas danda7ana mala Xoossi nuus qaala yootanas oge doyana mala nu gishshika woossite.
Qasseka hasa7anas bessiza qaala qonccen ta hasa7ana mala taas woossite.
Ammanontta asatara intes diza hanotethan cinccatethan Simeretite. Intes beettida lo7o qaadan go7etite.
Issi issi uras inte malithe wositi immanakone inte erana mala inte hasa7ay maxxinera kaxxida kaththa mala mali7o gido.
Tiqiqosay ta duusa gishshi wurs intes yootana. Izi daro dosotida ishane Godas tanara issife oothiza ammanetida oothanchako.
Nu duussa gishshi inte erana malane inte wozina minithana malata iza inteko kiittadis.
Izi inte bagga gididi ammanetidadene dosetidade gidida nu isha Anasimosara inteko bees. Isttika haani diza hanoza wurs intes yootana.
Barinabasa Aawa michchey naa Mariqosayine tanara issife qachchetida Arixirokosay intena saro geetes. Mariqosa gishshi inte ay oothanakone kase intena ta qofisa wothida mala izi inteko gakkishin mokki ekite.
Iyosixosa geetettiza Yesusayka intena saro gees. Ayhuda asa gidofe Xoossa kawotethas tanara oothizayti haytantta xalalako. Istti tana minththethida.
Inte baggafe gidida Yesus kiristoosa oothanchay Ephafiray intena saro gees. Izika intena ayana duusan lo7eth minnidine mulera wopu giidi Xoossa shenen minni eqqana mala wurso wode inte gishshi woossan baaxetes.
Qasseka inte gishshi hessathoka Lodoqiyanine Iyara kataman dizaytas izi pacey baynda oothizayssa ta izas marikatayss.
Daro dosetida aakime Luqasayne Deemasay intena saro geetes.
Lodoqiyan diza nu ishatas, Nimifussisine izi keeththan shiiqiza ammaniza asatas ta saroka yootite.
Hana ta kiittaya intes nababettida mala qasseka Lodoqiyan diza woossa keethayin nababistana mala oothite. Inteka qasse Lodoqiyape intes kiitetida kiitta nababite.
Akiriphas “Neni Godape ekkida oothoza wurseth gathanas minna” giite.
Hayssa saroka tani Phawulosay ta kushera xaafadis. Ta qachista dizayssa dogopite. Xoossa kiyateth intenara gido.
Phawuloossape, Sillasepenne Ximitossape; Intes Xoossa Aawa Goda Yesuss Kiristtosayta gidida Taselonqqen diza ammaniza asas nu Aawa Xoossafene Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa kiyatethinne sarotethi intes gido.
Nu intena nu woosan qoppishe wursso wode Xoossa inte gish galatoos.
Ammanoninne mino siqqotethane inte oothida ootho qasseka Goda Yesussa Kiristtoossa bolla diza inte mino ufayssan beettida inte minotetha gish nu Godaa Xoossa, nu Aawa sinththan wursso gaalas inte gish qopoos.
Xoossan dosettida nu ishato izi intena doordayssa nu eroosu.
Gasooykka mishirachcho qaalay inteko yiday wolqara xillo ayananine loeththi shaaki erin attin coo qaala xalla gidena; Qasseka nu inte gish giidi nu waani deydakkone inte ereta.
Ha7i inte nunane Goda milatidista. Inte bolla ay metoy gakkida gidikokka Xillo Ayana ufayssan qaala ekkidista.
Hessafe denddidayssan inte Maqidoniyanine Akayan ammaniza asa wursos lo7o leemisota gididista.
Goda qaalay intefe kezidi Maqidoniyanine Akayan siyeteth xalla gidontta intes Xoossa bolla diza ammanoy wurssoson erretides; hessa gish nu intes yootanas aykkoka koshshena.
Inte nuna wostt mooki ekkidaakone deyon diza tumu Xoossas oothanas inte eeqatape Xoossakko inte waani simmidako asay inte gish hasa7es.
Qasseka Xoossi hayqope denththidayssa buro yaana hanqqofe nuna ashshana salope yaana Xoossa na yesusa yuusa inte wosti nagizakkone asay hasa7es.
Nu ishato nu intekon gammida gammioy coo mela gidonttayssa inteka errista.
Inteka errizayssa mala hayssafe kase Pilphphisiyosan nu waayene meto beyidossine cayetidosu; gido attin aynne mino waayey nuna gakkikokka Xoossa mishirachcho qaala intes yootanas nu Godape xalateth demmidos.
Nu intena zorida zorey iita qofara woykko intena baalethanas koydi gidena.
Gido attin nu mishirachchoqaala hadara ekkanas danidaiza asata mala xoossay nuna qoodida gish nu haasaos; hessaka nu oothizay nu wozina paacci erriza Xoossa ufayssanas attin ass ufayssanass giidi gidena.
Nu mulekka baleththo aala yootibeyko woykko nu uzeeteth kammanas giidi baaletho hano nu hanotayssa inte errista. Hayssaskka nu markkayXoossa.
Intefe gidin woykko haratape oonapekka asape immettiza boncho nu koybeykko.
nu Kiristtosay kiittidayta gidida gish intes tooho gidanas danddaoskko shin; Gido attin Aaya ba nayta dichchiza nukka inte giidon ashikeetethan simeretidos.
Xoossa qaala gidontta dishin nu shemppoka inte gish ufayssan immana gakkanaas intena siiqqidosu. Gasooykka nu intena daro siiqida gishaskko.
Nu ishato nu dafetethane nu daabura inte ereta; oonaskka tooho gidontta mala qamane gallas nuus oothishe miishirachcho qaala intes yootidos.
Nu intenara ammanizaytara diza wode xillotethanine geeshatethan qassekka wothoy bayindda nu waani deyidakkone inteka Xoossika nuus markka.
Aaway ba naytas haniza mala nukka intes issas issas ayy hanidakone inte errista.
Inte intena ba kawootethassine ba bonchos xeyigida Xoossas bessiza mala inte daana mala nu intena minisidos, loo7ethi zoridosinne hadara gidos.
Inte nuuppe siyida Xoossa qaala ekkida wode ammaniza inte achchan tumu oothiza Xoossa qaala mala ekkidista attin coo asa qaala mala inte ekkontta aggida gish nu Xoossa qanxxoy bayindda galatoos.
Nu ishato! yuuda biittan yesus kiristtosa ammaniza xoossa woosa keethata millatidista; istti Ayhuddatape matone waaye ekkida mala inteka inte asape waaye ekkidista.
Istti Goda Yesussane kase nibistakka wodhdhida; nunakka goodida; Xoossuka ufayssibeytena; Asa wursora eqetizade gidida.
Hessika xoossu errontta deret siyidi attana malako. Nu qaala yootontta mala diganaskko. Hessa mala oothon ba nagara wursso wode ba bolla wurththeth gakkanaas gujji gujji beetes; Xoossa hanqqooyka istta bolla wodhdhides.
Gidikkoka nu ishato nu guutha wodes intefe ayyanan gidontta ashon shaakeetikokka inte laamotay nuna wodhdhiza gish inte ayfeso beyanas daro dafeetethan doos.
Nu intekko baanas daro laamotidos shin harrapeka ta Phawuloosay daro wode dafistadis shin xalaey nuna digides.
Goda Yesussay ha yiza wode iza sinththan nu amoy woykko nu ufayssi woykko nu zuwudeey nuus intefe haray oone?
Tumapekka nu ufayssine nu bonchoy intena.
Hessa gish nuus danda7etontta ixxin he wode Atenan nurkka nu attanayss nuus loo7o gidi beettides.
Intena ammanon minththana mala nunara asas Kiristtossa miishshirachcho qaala yootiza Xoossa ashikara gidida ximotoosa inteko yeddidos.
Hessika hayssa paccezan oonkka ammanope qanxxontta malako; nukka hayssas dooretidayssa inteka errista.
Nu qasse intenara diza wode waayey nu bolla gakkanayssa kasetidi intes yootidos; Inte erriza malakka hanides.
Hessa gish ayikkoka ta genccecin taas danddaetoontta ixxida gish inte ammano gish erranas gaada ximotoosa kiitadis. Ta hessa oothiday ooni errize paaccizadey istta paaccin haanni wode nu daaburay wurkka mela gidontta aggena ga babbida gishaskko.
Hai qasse Ximotoossay inte achchafe nukko yidi inte ammano gishshine inte siiqotetha gish loo7o wore nuna sissidees. Qasseka inte wursso wode nuna looethi qooppizayssane nukka intena beyanas laamotiza mala inteka nuna beyanas laamotizayssa nuus yootides.
Hessa gish nu ishato nu dizay waayenine meto garththan gidikkoka inte ammano gaason intenan hai nu minetoos.
Inte Godan minni eqqida gish tumape hai nu paxa daana.
Inte geedon nu Xoossa sinththan nu demmida ufayssa wursso gish Xoossa aymala galatanas danddaizon?
Qasseka nu intena beyanasine inte ammanope paccidayssa kunththanas omarththine gallas keehi woossos.
haikka nu intekko baana mala nu Aaway Xoossi Goda Yesuss Kiristtossay ogeza izi nuusu suuriso.
Nu intena siiqqiza mala intes inte garththan diza siiqqone inte harata siiqqiza siiqqoza Goday darththone keezi gujjo.
Nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtossay geeshshata wurssotara yiza wode nu Aawa Godaa Xoossa sinththan inte wothoy baynddaytane geeshshata gididi beettana mala inte wozina izi minsso.
Ha7i wurththethan ta ishato inte Xoossa ufayssanas inte waani waani daana bessizakone nu intena tamarsidos. Tumapekka nu tamarsida mala deista; hessa gish Goda Yesuss Kiristtossan nu intena woossizayne zorizay hayssafeka adhdhida hanora inte sinththe gujjana malako.
Goda Yesuss Kiristtossa wolqan nu intes ay azazo immidakkone inte errista.
Xoossa sheney inte laymmafe hakkidi dummatanaskko.
Qasse issi issi asay ba machcho geeshshatethanine bonchon ayso bessizayssa shaaki erro.
Hessika Xoossu ammanontta dere asa mala laymma qaqetethan gidoopo.
Hessa malan oonikka balettidi ba isha balethofo; Gasooykka hayssafe kase nu intes yootida malane nagistana mala akekissida mala Goday heyitantta mala nagara oothiza wurssota bolla ba hanqqo ehana.
Xoossi nuna geshatethas xeeyigides attin tunatethas xeyigibeyna.
Hessa gish hayssa ha zoreza kadhdhidi ekkonttadey xiillo ayana izas immida Xoossa kadhdhes attin asi kadhdhizade gideena.
Ishata siiqootetha gish intes oonkka xaafanas kooshshena; Gasooykka inte inte garssan siiqeistana mala inte inte baggara Xoossafe tamardista.
Kumeetha maqidonyyan diza ammaniza asa wurss inte siiqizayss erretidayssa. Gido attin nu ishato inte hayssafe aathi sinththe bagga siiqistana mala nu intena zoroosu.
Nu hayssafe kase intena azazida mala inte inte kushera oothite; woopu gi diite; intes gidizayssa loo7ath xeellite.
Hessika gallas gallas inte duussay hankko ammanontta asa achchan intena bonchisana malane inte ayy asaskka tooho gidontta malakko.
Ta ishato inte shempidayta gish erontta attana mala nu koyokko. Qasseka ufayss bayindda hinkko hara asata mala inte muuzootana mala nu koyokko.
Yesussay hayqqidi denddidayssa nu ammaniza gidiiko Yesussa ammanidayta Xoossi yesussara hessathoka zaari ha yeedana.
Nu Goda qaalan intes gizay hayssa. Nuni hayqqontta paxxa dizaytine Goday yaana gakkanaas gam77anayti kase hayqqidaytape sinththetoko.
Goday ba hu7era gita azazoni kitanchata halaqa giireththara Xoossa xurummiba giireththan salope wodhdhana. Kase Kiristtossa ammanidi hayqqidayti istti kaseti denddana.
Hessafe guye nu qasse paxxa dizayti Goda carkko bolla gaaganas isttara isife shaarara denddana; hessathoka nu medhdhinas Godara deyana.
Hessa gish hayssa qaalan issay issara minettite.
Ta ishato hesi hanana wode gish nu intes xaafanas kooshshena.
Kaysoy qaman yiza mala Goda gaallasayka hessa mala yaanayssa inte inte baggara looethi ereista.
Asay “gadey sarone loo7oko” gishin miixay qanththara diza maccash oyyikiza mala hessathoka asi dhayssizay qoopontta asa bolla gakkana. Oonikka kessi ekkena.
Inteno ishato, he gaallasay kayso mala intena daganththanas inte dhuman deekkista.
Inte wurkka poo7o nayta; nuni dhuma woykko qama bagga gidokko.
Histtiko ane beegos; ane nurkka nuna haaros attin hankko dhiskkiza asa mala nukka dhiskkoko.
Dhiskkizayti qamara dhiskketes; maththotizaytikka qamara maththottettes.
Nu qass gaallasa asata gidida gish ammanone siiqo tiran mayiza asa mayo mala mayidi atotetha ufayss hu7en woththiza asa qoobe mala nu hu7en woththidi ane nunatetha haaridi deyoos.
Xoossi nu atoteth Goda Yesuss Kiristtossa baggara demmana mala attin nuna hanqqos xeygibeytena.
Nu hayqqikkoka woykko paxxa dikkoka izara isife daana mala izi nu gish hayqqides.
Hessa gish tumape inte hai oothizayisa malakka issay issara minettite; issay issa minsso.
Histtiko ta ishato inte garssan miinni oothizayta Godan intefe bollara diza halaqatane intena zorizayta inte bonchana mala nu intena woosos.
Istta ootho gishakka istta siiqora looathi bonchite; inte inte garssan saroni diite.
Ta ishato nu intena “ootho oothontta asata hanqqetite; babbizayta minssite; daaburanchata maadite; asi wurthth danddaite” gi zorosu.
Oonasikka iita gish iita zaarontta mala naagettite; Gido attin inte inte garssan gidin hara asara gidin wursso wode loo7o gidizayssa oothanas baaxetite.
Wuri wode ufaettite.
Qanxxontta woosite.
Ayi hanonkka galatite Xoossa sheney intes Yesuss Kiristtosa baggara hessako.
Xiillo ayana tama toyssofite.
Buro hananas immetida qaala kadhopite.
Wurththika paacci xeellite, loo7o gidida oykkite.
Iita milatiza ay miishapekka hakite.
Sarotetha Goday izi intenatetha bees duummaso; inte ayanay, inte shemppoyne inte ashoy Goda Yesuss Kiristtossay yiza wode wothoyi bayindda naagetto.
Intena xeyigidayssi ammanetidade gidida gish izi hessa oothana.
Nu ishato nu gishakka woosite.
Ammanizayita wurssi geeshshata yeeretethan saroththite.
Ha kiitay ammanizaytas wurssos nabbabistana mala Goda sunththan hadara gayis.
Nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtossa aadho kiyatethi intista gido.
Phawuloossape, Sillasenepene Ximotoossape; Nu Aawa Xoossan Goda Yesuss Kiristtossan gidida tesolonqqen ammaniza asas.
Xoossa Aawa Goda Yesussa kiyateththine sarooteth intes gido.
Ta ishato inte ammanoy wodepe woden diicci diicci biza giishshine inte siiqqoyka inte garsan gujjeti gujjeti biza gish nu inte gish Xoossa lo7ethi galatanas beeses.
Hessa gish inte bolla gakkida goodetethanine meto wursson inte miinnida gish nu nu baggara inte danddao giishshane inte ammano gish ammaniza asa wursso achchan ceeqetoos.
Hesi wurkka Xoossa piriday suure gididayssa beeses. Hessa geedon waaye beeyiza inte Xoossa kawootethas bessizayta gidi beettidista.
Xoossi xiillo gidida gish intena waayisizayta izi waaysana.
Waaye ekkida intesine nuus shemppo immana. Hessikka Goda Yesus Kiristtoossay wolliqama Salo Xoossa kiitanchatara salo bolla qoncciza wode hanana.
He wode Xoossu erontta asatane Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa mishshirachcho qaalas azazetontta asata bolla izi ba halo eexxiza lacco taman kessana.
Isttika Goda sinththafene iza boncho wolliqqa achchafe kichchidi medhdhinas dhayson qaaxxayistana.
Istti qaaxxayistanay izi geeshshata achchan bonchetanasine ammanizayti wuri izan malalistana mala izi yiza gaallasan hanana. Inteka he ammaniza asara deyana; Gasooykka nu intes markkatidayssa inte ammanida gishasiko.
Nu hessa qooppishe nu Xoossi intena ba xeeyissas gidizayita histti qoodana mala inte loo7o oothanas amotiza amozane ammanoni inte oothida oothoza wurssi izi intes ba wolliqqan polana mala nu intes wursso wode woosos.
Qassekka nu Godaa Xoossane nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa kiyatetha mala Yesuss Kiristtoossa sunththi inte achchan bonchetana malane inteka izan bonchetana mala nu intes woosos.
Ta ishato Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa yuussa gishshane nu izaakko baana buussa gish nu intena qoopisos.
Ayanay qonccisides woykko qaala gees giidi woykko nuupe intes kiitetida kiita mala Goda yuusa gallas gakkides giidi inte qofan yarkkiyarkkofitene dagammopite.
Oonikka ay hanonkka intena baleththofo. Daro asay amano kadanappe sinththe dhayanas besiza issi makka7ay as qonchontta dishin he gaallasay gakkena.
Izikka Xoossu geeteti gooyinetiza eeqa xoossata wurssofe bollara bena dhooqu dhooqu histtizadene Xoossara eqetizade. Izikka xoossa keeththan uttidi bena “tani xoossa” giidi awajje awajjisana.
Ta intenara diza wode hayta ha yoota intes ta yootidayssi intes qofetizesha?
Izi ba woden qonccana gakkanaas ha7i iza qonccontta mala aazi diggizakkone inte ereta.
Makkalancha xuura haray attoshin ha7ikka ootho bolla dees. gido attin hayssi hananay izi hai oothontta mala iza diggizadey iza ogepe kichchana gakkanaas xaalla.
Hessafekka kaallidi Goda Yesussay ba duuna peenonine ba boncho yuussan dhayssana; makkalanchay qonccana.
He makkalancha yuusi xalae oothon hessikka asi balethiza malatatanine malalisiza miishshatan hanana.
Hessathokka ekkidi attontta mala tuma ixxidi dhayza asata balethanas dumma dumma iita oothoy yaana.
Hessa geedon istti wordo yoo ammanana mala Xoossi istta bolla balla ootho kiittana.
Hessi hananay tuma ammanontta ixxidine wordo yoon ufa7etizayti wuri pirdistanasiko.
Godan dosetida ta ishato nu gidiko wursso wode inte gish Xoossu galatanas nuus beeses. Gasooykka Xoossi intena koyrope oykkidi inte xiillo ayanan dummatidaytane tumu ammanidi inte attana mala intena doordes.
Nu Goda Yesuss kiristtooss boncho gishetizayta inte gidana mala nu yootida mishshirachcho qaala baggara intena xeeyigides.
Hessa gish ta ishato inte minni eqqite, nu nu duunan gidin woykko kiittan woykko nu intes aathi yeddida timirtteza looethi oykkite.
Izi nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossay qasse nuna siiqqidayne ba kiyateththan medhdhina minththethone loo7o ufayss izi nuus immida Xoossa nu Aaway
Izi inte wozina loo7o oothonine qaalan minsso.
Wurththethan ta ishato qassekka Goda qaalay inte achchan hanoyssathoka eleeli wurssoso gakkana malane bonchetana mala nuus woosite.
Qasseka asi wuri ammanizayssa gidontta gish makkalanchatapene iita asatape nu attana mala nuus woosite.
Goday gidiko ammanetidayssa. Izikka intena minnisana; xalaepaka intena naagana.
Nu intena azazidayssa inte hai oothidista shin sinththefekka inte oothanayssa nuni Godan ammanetosu.
Goday inte wozina Xoossa siiqqookone Kiristtoossa dandda7ako kaaletho.
Ta ishato ootho othantta asapene inte nuupe ekkida timirtteza mala doontta ammanizaytape inte haakkana mala Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa sunththan intena nu azazoos.
Inte nu lemuso wostti kaalanakone inte inte baggara ereista. nu intenara diza wode ootho oothontta coo deybeykko.
Qassekka oona soopekka kaththi coo mela mibeykko. Gido attin intefe oonaskka nu tooho gidontta mala qamane gallas daaburan oothi midos.
Nu hessa oothiday inte nuna kaalana mala intes loo7o lemuso gidana giidipe attin nuus kooshshizayssa intefe ekkana nuns woqay dhayin gidena.
Nu intenara diza wode “ootho oothanas dosontta asi kaathth moopo giza azazo intes immidos.
Inte garssan issi issi asati ootho oothonttayssa nu siydosu. Heytantti ootho oothontta mela bena gaathontta asa yooni gelizaytako.
Heyta mala asati ba ootho co7u gi oothana malane ba kath maana mala Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa sunththan nu istta azazoosine zoroos.
Inte gidikko ta ishato loo7o ootho oothanape mulekka azaallofite.
Hayssa nu kiittida qaalas azazetoonttay oonkka diikko hessa milatizade lo7ethi kaalitene izi ba oothon yeelatana mala izara gaggofite.
Gido attin iza inte isha mala hanqqite attin morkke mala xeellofite.
Sarotetha Goday izi ba baggara yoo wursson intes saroteth immo. Goday intenara wurssara gido.
Hayssa sarota ta ta kushera intes xaafiday tana phawuloossa. Ta kiittas dumma malatay hayssa ta xaafiza xaafoy hayssa milates.
Nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa aadho kiyateththi intenara wuryyssara gido.
Nuus ufayss gidida yesus kiristtoossaninne nuna ashshida Xoossa azazon, Yesuss kiristtoossay kiittida Phawuloossape.
Ammanon taas tumu naa gidida Ximttoossas Xoossa nu Aawape nu Goda Yesus kiristtoossape kiyateth, maarotethine saroy nees gido.
Tani Maqqidonyya bashe nena hadara gida mala hayssafe sinththan issi issi asati wordo timirtte tamarssontta mala ne azazana mala Efesoonen daasha.
Qassekka asay yootin wurontta beni wode hayssu7en ba wode wurssontta mala azaza. Heyta mala yooy palama denthethes atin ammanon oothetiza xoossa oothos aykkoka go7ena.
Ha azazoozas waana ayfe yooy gidikko geeshsha wozinape loo7o qofara hessathoka tumu ammanope beettiza siiqo.
Issi issi asay haytape pooqqeti eqqidi go7ay bayndda yootakko simmides.
Woga tamarssizayta gidana mala koyetes. Gidikkoka istti ba yootizayssa woykko keehi moottetiza yooza lo7ethi ereetena.

Ha biitta loo7o duussu xaalla koyiza amm7eya gidikko iza paxa dashe hayiqqidarokko.

Ta ishato intefe oonikka deyo Xoossafe haraso intena haasiza iittane ammanontta wozinay dontta mala naagetite.
Harapeka inte garisafe oonikka nagaran baletidi ba wozina muumisontta mala “Hachchi” geetetishin hachchi hachchi inte inte garisan minetite.

Xoossi istta bolla oyddu tammu laytha hanqettidayti istti oonanitee? Nagara oothin istta ahay bazzo biittan kundi attidayta gidetenee?
Izas azazetontta ixxidaytape attin iza shemposo gelontta mala izi caaqi digiday haray oonanitee?
Hessa gishshi istti gelontta attiday ammanoy baynda gishshi gididayssa nu erosu.
Gede shemposo gelanas immetida ufaysay ha7ika naageti diza gishshi inte gidofe oonikka hessas besonttade gidontta mala ane naagetos.

Nu qasse ammanizayti he shempo sooza gelana. Xoossi “Hessa gishshi tani ta hanqon <Istti ta shemposo muleka geletena> gaada ta caaqadis” gides. Gido attin hayssi alamey medhetosope ha simmin iza oothoy poletides.
Issi son lapunththo gallas agishshi “Lapunththo galasi Xoossi ootho wurisofe shempides” geeteti geisha maxaafan xaafetides.
Qasseka he sozan “tumappe istti ta shemposo muleka geletena” gees.
Iza shemposo buro gelana issi issi asati deetes. Kase isttas mishshiracho qaalay sabaketidayti azazetontta ixxida gishshi iza shemposo istti gelibeytena.
Hessa gishshi Xoossi “Hachchi” giidi qasseka hara gallas wothides. Hessika aro laythatape guye Dawite baggara “Hachchi inte iza qaala siyiko inte wozina muumisopite” geeteti kase yootetida mala hanides.
Iyaasoy isttas shempo immidako Xoossi hara gallas giidi yootenakoshin.
Hessa gishshi sambata gallas shempoy Xoossa deres ha7ika dees.
Gaasoyka Xoossa shemposo gelizay wuri Xoossi oothi shempida mala izika ba oothope shempana.
Hessa gishshi oonikka heytantta mala azazetontta ixxidayssa lemuso kaallidi kundontta mala he shemposoyo gelanas ane minos.
Xoossa qaalay paxxa dizayssane oothiza qaalako. Nam77u bagga qara mashafeka adhdhi qara; Shempone ayana; shayane qinccifileka shaakana gakanas caades. Wozina qofane amotethaka paaci xeeles.
Xoossa ayfefe geemetida medhetay muleka deena. Nu izas nu gishshi malithe immanas bessiza iza sinthan hanoy wurikka qonccen kallo dees.
Hessa gishshi pude salo bida qessista halaqa Xoossa na Yesusay nuus diza gishshi ane nuni nu ammano minthi oykosu.
Nu daburishin nuus qadhetana danda7iza qessista halaqay nuusu dees. Izi nu mala wuriso mishshan paaacetides. Gidikoka izi ayko nagaraka oothibena.
Hessa gishshi nuni maarotethi ekanasine nuna koshiza wode nuna maadiza iza kiyateth nu demmana mala gede iza maarotetha aliggako ane ammanon shiiqos.
Qessata halaqa gidi shuumetiza uray daro asa gidofe dooretesine asa gishshi gididi imotanne nagara gishshi yarsho shiishanas dooretes.
Izika ba baggara daburachcha gidida gishshi erontta asatasine oge balidaytas qadhetana danda7es.
Izi ba nagara gissine hara asata nagara gishshi yarsho shiishanas izas bessizay hessa gishshiko.
Aroney xeyigetidayssatho izi Xoossi xeyigidade gidanas besses attin hessa he bonchoza berika bess ekiza uray deena.
Hessaththoka kiristoosay qessista halaqa gidana boncho berika bees ekibeyna. Gido attin “Ne ta naako; Ta nees hachchi Aawa gidadis” gida Xoossafe ekides.
Hessaththoka haraso “Malke-xedeqe shuumista mala neni medhinas qessista halaqako” gees.
Yesusay hayssa biitta bolla diza wode iza hayqope ashana danda7izayssako ayfunxishe gita qaalara woossa woossides. Addafe ashiketethara izi azazetida gishshi iza woossay izas siyettides.
Izi Xoossa na gidikkoka ba ekida waayezape azazeteth tamarides.
Hessa baggara pacey bayndade gidi beetidayssafe guye bena azazetizaytas wurisos medhina atotethas gaaso gidides.
Malke-xadiqe shuumetetha mala qessista halaqa geeteti Xoossan shuumetides.
Hessa gishshi nu hasa7ana miishey buro daroy dees. Gido attin inte dota7ata gidida gishshi intena erisoy metoko.
Inte hanni wode asitamare gidanas bessishin Xoossa qaala buro koyrope denthi intena tamarisiza asi intes koshshena. Intes koshizay mino kathi gidontta maathiko.
Maathi pahetizay qii guutha na gidiza gishshi lo7one iitta shaakiza timirtte shaaki erena.
Mino kathi gidiko lo7one iitta shaakanas benatetha dosisida wozina kunththida asatasiko
Hessa gishshi koyrope kiristoosa gishshi immetida timirtteza aggidi ane gede mino timirtteko boosu. Hayqida oothope maarotethan gelo gishshine Xoossan ammano gishshi buro ane izan wodhdhi maadhokko.
Hessaththoka xinqqate gishshine kushe asa bolla wotho gishshi qasseka hayqidayata dentha gishshine medhina pirida gishshi buro wothi demoko.
Xoossa shene gidiko nu hessaththo oothana.
Be ammano kaddida asata istta maarotethan wositti zoranee? Po7oy isttas issi to po7idayta salo imotetha ekki be7idayta xiillo ayana ekki be7idayta;
Lo7o Xoossa qaalane buro yaana alameza woliqa ekki be7idayta;
Zaaridi kadidayti istta nam77antho zaaridi maarotethin ekoy danda7etena. Gaasoy istti ba mooros Xoossa na zaari kaqetesine kawushetes.
Wuriso wode ba bolla ira uyza biittay qesseka iza goyzadey ayfe immiza biittayaka Xoossa achchan anjjistadus.
Gido attin agunthune caca mokisiza biittay go7ay baydaro gidana. He biittays qangetethi matan dees. Izi wurisethi taman xuugeteth gidana.
Ta ishato nuni hessaththo hassa7ikoka intes inte atotethara oyketida lo7o miishey dizayssa nu sidhoko.
Kase gidin woykko ha7i gidinka inte ammanizayta maadidayssane iza suntha gishshi inte bessida siiqotetha balanas Xoossi makal7ancha gidena.
Immetida ufayssay polistana gakanas intefe issi issi uray hessa mala ootho wuriseth gakanas genccidi oothana mala nu amotoos.
Ammanonine danda7an inte iza ufayssa qaala laatizayta milatanape attin dota7ata gidanayssa nu koyoko.
Xoossi Abirames ufayssi immida wode caaqishe hara izape adhiza uray baynda gishshi berika benan hizgiza caaqides. “Ta nena tumape anjjana; tan e zeres darisana.”
