Abirameyka gencci naagidape kaalidi izas immetida ufayssa demmides.
Asay caaqo caaqishe beepe dhoqan caaqees. Caaqozika geetetidayssi poletena mala minthiza gishshi caaqidayta gidon palamay dendiko kase caaqo qaalay digees.
Xoossi laametontta ba qofa ufayssa qaala laatanaytas qonccisana mala koyda gishshi caaqo qaalan minthides.
Xoossi ay wodeka woridotena; danda7ena. Izi laametontta nam77u miishatan nu sinththan diza ufayssa oykanas izako shiiqida nuusu gita minoteth nu demmana mala oothides.
Nuka shempo teqe gidida minone ammanithiza ufayss demmides. He ufayssayka magalashazape guye baggara gede Xoossa keeththa gido gelees.
He sozika nu gishshi Yesusay kaseti gelida sooko. Izika Malke-xedeqe shuumetetha mala medhinas qessista halaqa gidides.
Hessi malke-xedeqey saleme kawone Xoossa qesseko; Izika Abiramey kawota oli xoonidi simmishin demmidi Abirame anjjides.
Abirameykabess diza wurisofe tammu kushepe issi kushe izas immides. Koyro iza sunthas birshechi “Xiillo kawo” guusako. Kaallidi qasse “Saleme kawo” guusi “sarotetha kawo” guusuko.
Izas Ayaka Aawayka woykko iza yeletethas zarikeyka baawa. Izi ayde yeletidi, ayde hayqidakone eretibynna. Izas doomethine wurisethi baawa. Gido attin Xoossa na mala medhinas izi qesse gididi dess.
Ane inte izi aymala gitakone qopite. Haray attoshin Aawatas wurisos koyroy Abiramey ba di7i ekkidayssa wurisofe tammafe issa kessi immides.
Isttas qessetethi immetida Lewe nayti istta ishati Abirame zerethata gidikkoka derape hessika ba ishatape tammafe issa ekkana mala isttas wogan azazetides.
Hayssa ha addeza zerethi Lewe zereth gidena. Gido attin izi Abiramepe tammafe issa ekkides. Kase izas ufayssa qaalay immetida Abirame anjjides.
Bayray kaallo anjjizayss wogako.
Issi baggara tammafe issa ekkizayti hayqizaytako. Hara baggara qasse tammafe issa ekkizadey hayqontta paxa diza mala izas marikatidadey malke-xedeqeko.
Haray attoshin Leweyka Abirame baggara tammafe issa kessides gaanas danda7etes.
Gaasoyka malke-xedeqey Abirame gaagiza wode Lewey buro ba Aawa Abiramepe yeletibeyna.
Paacey baynda poloy bettidayne wogay derezas immetiday Lewe qesetetha mala gididako Aaroone mala gidontta Malke-xedeqe shuumetetha malay hara qessey yaanas aazas koshidee?
Qessetetha zarikey laametiza wode wogayka laamistanasi attontta miisheko.
Hessi wurikka izas yootetida qessey izi hara zerethiko. Iza zereththafe ooinka yarshoson oothi erizadey baawa.
Ne Goday Yuda baggafe yidayssi tumoko. Musey qessista gishshi yootishe ha zeretha gishshi yootidayssi issi mishshika baawa.
Malke-xedeqe malay hara qessey dendiko nu kase yootida yoy daro qoncce gidena.
Izi qesse gididay dhayontta deyo wolqan attin zereththafe yida wogafe gidena.
Izas hizgi markatides “Ne Malke-xedeqe shuumetetha mala medhinas qesseko”
Kase azazoy laafane go7ontayssa gidida gishshi attides.
Wogay oonaka geeshanas danda7ontta gishshi nu Xoossa achchi shiiqanas izape adhdhiza hara ufayssi nuusu yides.
Hessika caaqoy baynda hanbeyna. Hanko Qesse gididayti caaqoy bayndaytako.
Izi gidiko qessetetha caaqon ekkides. Gaasoyka Xoossi iza gishshi hizigides “Goday caaqides, ba qofa izi laamena, <Ne medhinas qesse.”>
Hessa mala caaqope dendidayssan Yesusay hessafe adhdhiza caaqo qaalas waase giddies.
Kase qesseti ba oothon sinthe gujjontta mala hayqoy istta digida gishshi qooday isttas darooko.
Yesusay gidiko medhinas dizade gidida gishshi iza qessetethi shaaretontta qessetethiko.
Hessa gishshi izi istta gigissana cimatishe wuriso wode hayqontta paxa eqqi diza gishshi iza baggara Xoossako yizayta wursi ashanas danda7es.
Hessa gishshi nuusi koshshsiza qeessista halaqay hessa mala geeshine wothoy iza bolla baynda xiillone nagaranchatape shaaketidi salotape bollara bonchetida qessata halaqako.
Izi hanko qessata halaqata mala koyro ba nagara gishshi qasseka kaalethidi hanko dereza nagara gishshi gallas gallas yarsho shiishanas iza koshshena. Izi bena aathi immida wode asa nagara gishshi issi too sinththa baggassara yarsho wu wursi polides.
Wogay daburancha asata qessatas waana halaqa hisiti shuumes. Wogape kaallidi yida caaqo qaalay gidiko medhinas iza bolla wothoy baynda naaza shuumides.
Hessa gishshi nu ha7i oothana waana yoy hayssako. Hayssa mala salo bolla Xoossa boncho aliga oshachan uttida qessista halaqay nuus dess.
Izi asi tokkida dunkkane gidon oothizade gidontta Godaa Xoossay tokkida tumu dunkanen geeshason oothizadeko.
Qessista halaqay shuumetizay asay Xoossas immizayssasa Xoossas shiishanasine yarsho yarshanasko. Hessa gishshi hayssi ha qessata halaqayka Xoossas shiishanas issi shiishiza miishi izas koshees.
Izi biitta bolla dizako qesse gidena. Aazas giiko wogay giza mala yarsho shiishiza hara qesseti dettes.
Istti kase salon diza Xoossa keethays lemusone eeshoko. Musey Dunkaaneza oothana gishshin “Nees zuma bolla qonccidayssatho wursa oothanas naagista” giza azazoy hessa gishshi izas immetides.
Gido attin Yesusay gido geli cimatiza caaqo qaalay kaseyssafe adhizayssa mala izi ekkida oothoyka kaseyta oothope aadhes. Hesssika kaseyssafe lo7iza ufayssa qaalanko.
Kase caaqo qaalan paacey bayndako nam77anththo hara caaqanas koshenashin.
Gido atin Xoossi dereza bolla paacey dizayssa demmida gishshi hizges “Isiraa7eele asarane Yuda asara tani oratha caaqo caaqetana wodey yaana” gees Goday.
“Hessika ta istta Gibixepe kesanas istta kushe oykkada kase istta Aawatara paaceti qaala mala gidena. Gaasoyka istti kase ta caaqo qaalan eqqibeytena. Taka istta yeda bessadis” gees Goday.
“Hessafe guye Isiraa7eele asara ta caaqetana qaaalay hayssa malako gees Goday. tani ta woga istta wozinan wothana. Istta wozina bollaka xaafana. Ta istta Xoossu gidana. Isttika tad ere gidana.
Hayssafe guye asi ba guta asa woykko ba isha <Ne Goda era> gi tamarsena. Gaasoyka asi guuthatethafe gitata gakanas wurikka tana erana.
Istta qohoza ta maarana. Hayssafe sinththan ta asa nagara nam77antho zaara qopike.”
Hayssa ha caaqoza izi “Orath” giidi kase caaqoza gali7a kessides. Hessa gishshi gali7idi wuridayssi dhayana wodey matides.
Koyro caaqo qaalazan Xoossas goyniza wogayne biitta bolla diza Xoossa keethey dees.
Kse nam77u kifilera diza dunikaney giigeti dees. Koyro kifilezan xomippe wothosoyne xaraphezay qasse ukethi dees. Hessa he kifilezi dumma kifile geetets.
Nam77antho kifiley nam77antho magalashape guye baggara diza kifiley wurisofe dumma geetetes.
Hessa gidon worqqafe oothetida exane cu7asiza pili7o malayne worqqan meeshettida caaqo Taabootay dees. He tabotayka iza gidon man7ay diza worqqa leematey, cililida Aaroone gufeyne caaqo qaalati iza bolla xaafetida shuchcha masethi dees.
He tabotaza bolla diza nagarape maarotetha kamaza bolla ba qefera kammiza boncho Kurubeti detes. Ha7i qasse nu heytantta issa issa gishshi shaaki shaaki hasa7anas danda7oko.
Wurika hessaththo giigetidape guye qesseti ba ootho polanas dunkanas koyro kifile geletes.
Gidikoka wurisofe gidotiza kifile qessista halaqay xalala gelees. Hessika layththan issi to xalala gidishin izi ba nagara gishine derey erontta oothida nagara gishshi shiishiza yarsho suuthu oykontta muleka galena.
Koyro dunkanezi kase diza wode gede wurisofe dumma geetettizaso efiza ogey he wode qoncce gidonttayssa xiillo ayanay besses.
Hessika hayssa ha wodezas lemuso gidishin kase shiqiza yarshotine coo immetiza imotati immizayta wozina shempisanasine mule geeshanas danda7ibeytena.
Heytanti wurikka oratha wogay yaana gakanas coo mela duuna hasa7a malako. Qasseka istti muusa gishshine usha gishshi qasseka dumma dumma geesho wogata xalalako.
Gidikoka Kiristoosay burope yaanas diza lo7o miishshatas qessista halaqa gididi qonccides. Izi izan gelida dunikanazi gitane geeshiko. He dunkanazi asa kushen oothetonttayssane hayssa ha medhetethafe gidena.
Izi he dunikanezan gelishe deyshata suuthune mirgo boorata suuthu ekki gelibeyna. Gido attin ase ashanas medhinas ba suuthu ekkidi wurisofe dumma geetettiza kifile hara wode nam77antho elontta mala wurisetha gelo gelides.
Isttas kare bagga asatethay tunida asata bolla araciza deysha suuthune mirgo boorata suuthu hessathoka yarshos xugettida ussa bidinththi istta geeshizayssa gidiko
Medhina ayanan bena wothoy baynda yarsho oothi Xoossas shiishida kiristoosa suuthi nuni deyo Xoossas goynanas hayqetha oothope nuna ay mala aaththi geeshandee?
Hessa gishshi xeygetidayti isttas immana geetetida medhina biitta ekkana mala kiristoosay oratha caaqo cimattizade gidides. Koyro caaqoza garisan diza wode istti oothida nagarape geeyana mala istta gishshi izi hayqides.
Bazay bazetizayssa gidiko bazidade hayqo shaaki eranas besses.
Gaasoyka bazay minnizay bazidadey haqinko. Bazidadey paxa dishin bazay aykoka oothena.
Hessa gishshi koyro caaqo qaalay suuthi baynda minnibeyna.
Musey ba azazo woga deras yooti simmidi deyshata suuthu mirgo boorata suuthu haathara ekkidi zo7o ithiken ecere wurice mala hesophe geetettiza miththara ekkidi ba xaafida woga maxaafa bollane dereza bolla wuuxides.
“Inte naagana mala inten Xoossi azazida caaqo qaala suuthay hayssako” gides.
Hessaththoka dunikanezane iza gidon diza ootho miisha wursi suuthu iza bolla wuuxides.
Addafeka guutha mishshati attishin hankko daro miishay suuthan geeyanas bessizayssa wogay azazes. Suuthi gukontte dishin maaroy baawa.
Hessa gishshi salo miishshatas lemuso gididayti haytanttan geeyanays attenashin. Salon diza mishshati gidiko hayssafeka adhiza yarshon geeyanas besse.
Kiristoosay tumu dunikaneyss lemusone asa kushen oothetida Xoossa keeth gelibeyna. Gido attin ha7i nu gishshi Xoossa sinththan bettanas pude salo gelides.
Qessista halaqay ba suuthu gidontta suuthu ekkidi laythan laythan wurisofe dumma kifile gelizayssatho kiristoosay bena yarshanas pude salo shiretti shiretti gelibeyna.
Hessa mala gidizako kiristoosay alamey medhetosope haa simmin daro wode meto ekkanas besses. Ha7 qasse wode wurisethan bena yarshidi nagara diganas wurisethas issi to qonccides.
Hessathokka asi issi to hayqees. Hessafe kaallidi pirida sinththan eqanas giigi uttides.
Kiristoosay daro asa nagara diganas issi to yarshetides. Nam77anthoka izi qonccana. Hessi iza naagizaytas atotethi ekki yaanas attin nam77antho zaari nagara tookanas gidena.
Muse wogay buro sinththara yaana lo7o hanotas Eshoope attin tumu adda medhay izas deena. Hessa gishshi laythan laythan paacey baynda shiri shiri shiishiza yarshoy Xoossu goynanas shiqiza asa geeshanas muleka danda7ibeyna
Asa mulera geeshana danda7izayssa gididako istti yarsho yarshanayssa aggagetenee? Qasseka Xoossu goynana shiiqiza asay issito geyizako ba wozinara nagarancha gididayssa sidhanakoshin.
Gido attin heyti yarshoti layhtan laythan nagara zaari zaari qofisitees.
Gaasoyka mirgotane deyshata suuthu asape nagara diganas danda7ena.
Hessa gishshi kiristoosay hayssa ha alameza yidi hizgides “Neni imotane yarsho koyabeyke shin ne taas nena giigisadasa.
Taman xuugettiza yarshone nagara gishshi shiiqiza yarshon ufa7istabeyka.
He wode tani hizgadis “Ta gishshi geisha maxaafan xaafetida mala <Xoosso hekko ta ne shene oothanas yadis” > gadis.
Muse wogay hessi hessaththo hanana mala azazikoka izi qasse koyro “Yarsho, imota, xuugettiza yarshone nagara gishshi shiiqiza yarsho ne koyabeykane izan ufa7istabeyka” gees.
Kaallethidika “Hekko ta ne shene oothana yadis” gides. Nam77anthoza esanas koyroyssa diggides.
Hayssa ha “iza shene” giza qaala mala hara yarsho zaarethi shiishanas koshontta mala Yesus kiristoosa baggara issi to shiiqida yarshon geeydosu.
Qessey hachchi hachchi eqqidi ba ootho polees. Ase nagarape geeshanas danda7onttayata wonttin wonttin shiishes.
Kiristoosay gidiko yarsho issito medhinas gidanayssa shiishidi Aawa oshachan uttides.
He gallasafe simmin iza morketi iza to garisan yedhistana gakanas naagon dees.
Gaasoyka issi to shiishida yarshon geyana asata medhinas geeshides.
Hessa he hanoza gishshi xiillo ayanayka nuusi marikatees. Koyro hizgees
“Hessafe guye ta isttara gelana caaqo qaalay hayssako gees Goday Ta woga ta istta wozinan wothana. Istta Wozinan ta xaafana.
Qasseka “Ta istta nagarane makal7a nam77antho qopike” gees Goday.
Heytantti wurikka atto geetetidape guye nam77antho nagara nagara hara shiiqana yarshoy deena.
Hessa gishshi ta ishato nuni Yesus kiristoosa suutha baggara gede wurisofe dumma geeshi geetettizasoyo gelanas xalateth demmidosu.
Hessika magalasha baggara; hessika izi ba asho baggara nuusu doyida orathine deyo gidida ogenkko.
Xoossa keeththa bolla shuumetida qessista halaqay nuusu diza gishshi
nuni nu iitta qofape geeyanas nu wozina aracetidi nu asatethaka xiillo haathan meecetidi tumu wozinapene kumetha ammanon Xoossako ane shiiqo
Nuusu ufayssa qaala immidadey ammanetizade gidida gishshi nuni ammanidi iza gishshi marikatiza ufayssafe hee haa goontta ane lo7ethi oykkos.
Siiqonine lo7o oothon nu minni daana mala ane issay issa qofisos.
Ane nu wuriso gallas issay issara gakki gakki issay issa minthethos attin issi issi asati shiiqo aggida mala ane nuni shiiqoza aggokko. Harapeka Goda Yussay matatidaysa qopishe kasep minni shiqite.
Nuni tuma shaaki eridi ekkidayssafe erishe nagara oothiko hayssafe guye nagaras shiiqanas hara yarshoy deena.
Hara buro hananay daro babisiza piriday Xoossa morketa xuugana naagiza mino tamay xalala dees.
Muse woga kadhida uray nam77u woykko hedzdzu markkati markkatiko maaroy baynda hayqon qaxxayetes.
Histin Xoossa na kadhida uray izan geeyida caaqo suutha hiraysso miisha mala qoodidadesine iza kiyatetha ayana isethidades ay mala hessafe adhiza piriday izas ba ssiza intes milatizee?
Tani izas halo kessan. Izade ootho mala izades ta zaarana” gidayssa nu erosu. Qasseka “Goday ba dereza bolla piridana” gees Goday.
Deyo Xoossa kushen kundethi daro babises.
Intes issi to po7oy po7idape guye meto wode daro baxen inte kase minni eqqida beni wodeza yuushi qopite.
Issi issi wode inte duulata dere sinththan cashasine goodetethas aadhi imettidista. Qasse hara wodeka hessa mala waayey istta bolla gakida asatara inteka issife waaye beyidista.
Inte intes harape aadhiza medhinas daana haaroy dizayssa eriza gishshi qachchetidaytas michetidistane inte haaroy bonqetishin ufayssan danda7idista.
Hessagishshi gita waggay diza kase inte ammanotethiyo agopite.
Inte Xoossa dhene polidi izi intes immida ufayssa qaala ekanas minni eqanas intena koshes.
Gaasoyka guutha wodepe kaallidi “Yanadey izi yana; gammi7ena”
Xiillo uray gidiko ammanon deyo demmana. Guye shiriqaqizadey diiko ta shempoy izade. bolla ufa7etuku
Nuni gidiko ammanidi attidayta baggako attin gede guye unddudi dhayzayta bagga gidoko.
Ammano geethi issi miishe hanana giidi nu sidhontta dishe beyontta miisheka beyida mal aero gi ekkoko.
Kase Aawati galatetiday hessa mala ammanonkko.
Hayssi ha alamey Xoossa qaalan medhetidayssa nu ammanon erosu. Hessaththoka ayfen beettizayssi medhettiday beetiza miishafe gidonttayssa nuni erosu.
Abeeley Xoossas, Qayele yarshofe adhiza yarsho ammanon shiishides. Xoossi iza yarshoza gishshi hasa7ishe izi ammanon geeshi gididayssa marikattides. Izi hayqqinkka iza ammanoy ha7i gakanas hasa7etes.
Henokey hayqo beyontta mala hayssa alamezape ammanon eketides. Xoossi iza ekkida gishshi izi bettibeyna. Ekistanape kasettidi izi Xoossa ufayssidaysi yootetida gishshi izi eketides.
Qasseka ammanoy bayndda dishin Xoossa ufayssanas muleka danda7etena. Gaasoyka Xoossako shiiqiza uray wurikka Xoossi gizayssane wozinape iza koyzaytas izi waaga immanayssa ammananas besses.
Nohes Xoossi buro Nohey ba ayfen beyontta miisha gishshi naagettana mala yootin Nohey Xoossa babbidi ba so asa ashanas ammanon marikabe kexxidi alame asa piridisides. Ammanon bettiza xiillotethi laatizade giddies.
Abiramey bees laata biitta ekkanas xeyigettida wode ammanon azazetides. Awa bizakone erontta aggikoka ero gi bides.
Alaga biittan bete asa mala buro nees immistana geetetida biittan ammanon uttides. Izas immetida ufayssa qaala izara issife laatana Yisaqa malane Yaqobem mala dunikanen deyides.
Gaasoyka minna dizaaro Xoossi izo qopi medhida katamayo ekkana naagides.
Abirames wode gede bidade gidikkoka Saarayka yelontta makara gidikkoka ufayss isttas immidadey ammanettidade hisiti xellida ammanon na Aawa gidanas gakides.
Hessa gishshi hayssa hayqqida asa mala qoodetida issi Abiramepe salo xoolintte malane abba ace mala qooday bayndda daro zerethay beettides.
Heyti wurikka isttas immetida ufayssa qaala demmontta ba ammanon naagida mala hayqida. Gidikoka istti hayssa biitta bolla immathene bete asi gididayssa erida gishshi haahon dishe beyidi kushen aathida mala ufayssan ekkida.
Hessa mala giza asati istta derey awakone ba dere naagizayssa qonccen bessetes.
Istti ba yeggi kezida dere zaari qopizako guye simmi baana danda7etesshin.
Ha7i hessafe aadhiza pude salon diza dere laamotetes. Hessa gishshi Xoossi isttas salon katama giigisida gishshi istta xalala Xoossa geeteti xeygistanas yelatibeyna.
Xoossi Abiramey ba naaza Yisaqa shukana mala paacin Abiramey Yisaqa yarshana ammanon shiishides. Xoossi izas immana gidayssa izika ba na issineza shukanas giigetides.
Hessika Xoossi izas “Ne zerethi Yisaqa baggara xeyigistana” gidaysa malakko.
Xoossi hayqidade denthanas danda7izaysssa Abiramey ammanida gishshi Yisaqaka hayqope denidida asa mala nam77antho demmides.
Yisaqay burope hananayssa qopi ekkidi Yayiqobene eesa mamanon anjjides.
Yaqobey hayqana gishshi Yosefo nayta issa issa ammanon anjjidayne ba guufe bolla dariti eqidi goyniday ammanoniko.
Yosefoy hayqana gishshi Isiraa7eele asay Gibixepe kezanayssa izi yootidayne ba meqetha gishshi istti ay oothanakone izi istta azaziday ammanonkko.
Musey yelettin izas malay lo7o gididayssa beyidi iza yelidayti iza hedzdzu agina gakanas kawoza azazzo babbontta qottiday ammanonkko.
Musey dicci gakida parinose nay na geetistanas ammanon ixxides.
Guutha wodes nagaran bettiza ufayssafe aathidi Xoossa asara meto beyanas doorides.
Gibixe deren diza haarope bollara kiristoosa gishshi waaye ekoy daro aadhiza haaro gididayssa yuushi qopides. Gaasoyka izi sinththafe ekanayssa buro haahon beyida gishshiko.
Kawo hanqqos babbontta ammanon Gibixe yeggi kezides. Buro betonttayssa beyza mala qopidi he qofan minni eqqides.
Bayrata urisi wodhizayssi Isiraa7eelista bayra nayta wodhontta mala ammanon paazigane suutha wuxxesa woga wothides.
Isiraa7eele asay mela biitta bolla hamuttiza mala Eritera abba gidora ammanon pinides. Gibixe asay qasse issitatho hanana gishshi abban mitettides.
Isiraa7eele asay Eyariko gimbeza laapun qamma yuuy yuuy aadhidape guye gimbeza ammanon laalides.
Layiman aqiza Raba7a dere xomosana yidayta saron mokki ekkida gishshi hanko azazetontta asara dhayontta ammanon attadus.
Hayssafe aadhethi ay gaanee? Geedne gishshi, Baaraqe gishshi, Somsone gishshi, Yofitahe gishshi, Dawite gishshi, Samela gishshi qasse nabeta gishshi ta yootontta mala taas wodey deena.
Heytantti ammanon kawota xonnida suure pirida piridida bees imettida ufayssa qaala ekida gaamota duuna goridida.
Tama woliqa toyssida qaara maccashafe kessi ekki attida. Daaburape minnida. Olason goobata gidida allaga asa ola goodida.
Macashatas hayqidayti paxida baggayti qasse hessafe aadhiza hayqope denthi demmanas giidi hayqope atethi leqidi hayqos bena aathi immida waayepe atanas koybeyttena.
Issi issi asati asan kaa7ettida. Garafettida. Bagayti qasse qachcho keethi gelida.
Shuchan cadettida magazenka nam77u kezi phaliqetida. Mashan shuketi hayqida waayetishe, Goodetishene daaburshe dorisa ittene deyshe itte mayidi waayetida.
Ha alamey isttas besontta gidida gishshi bazzonine gezen gongolon ne holla gidon waayetida.
Heytantta wurisota ammano gishshi marikatikoka isttafe oonikka imistana geetetida ufayssa qaala gakkidi ekkidadey deena.
Xoossi nuusu hessafe aadhzazi giigisida gishshi nu baynda istti xalala kumethi gidana danda7ibeyttena.
Hessa gishshi shaara mala nuni yuuy aadhida daro marikati nuusi dishin nuna deexiza toohone qasse nuni qachchi oykiza nagara wursi nuupe wora yeggidi nu sinththan diza wotha genccanine dandan7an ane wothos.
Nu ammaniza ammanozas koyrone polo gidida Yesusa ane xeellos. Izi ba sinththan diza ufayssa gishshi masiqale bolla hayqo danda7idi masiqale bolla bena gakana kawushatetha leqqidi Xoossa aligas oshachchan uttides.
Histinko inte daaburidi ufayssi qanxxontta mala hessathoka nagaranchatape kase iza bolla gakida hessa mala eqetethi danda7ida Yesusa qopite.
Suuthu gukana gakanas nagarara inte buro eqettibeykista.
Inte Xoossa nayta gidi uttidi qaalay gizayssa balidista. “Ta naazo Xoossa seera kawushan xeelofa, Nena izi seeriza wode ufayssi qanxxofa.
Gaasoyka Goday ba dosizade hanqees. Izi ba dosizade seeres. Izi ba na mala xeellizade qaxayees.
Xoossi intena ba na mala qoodiza gishshi hanqo danda7ite. Aaway hanqontta nay oonee?
Nay wuri seeran diccizatho inte diccontta aggiko inte Karen yelettida na attin so na gidekista.
Hessa wurisofe bollara hayssa biitta nuna hanqqi dichchida asho Aawati deetes. Nuka istta bonchos. Histin deyon deyanas nuus ayana Aawa gididayssatho aazas hessafe aathi azazetokonii?
Nu Aawati nuna bees lo7o milati bettida mala guutha wodes qaxayeetes. Xoossi gidiko nuni izan geeshatetha izape demmana mala nuna go7anas qaxayees.
Qixatey wurikka ha7is ufayssontta iitta milatees shin guyepe qase dosi ekkida asatas sarotethi izan kumida xiillotetha ayfen gaathes.
Hessa gishshsi daaburida inte qesene inte gulibate minisite.
Wobey paxana attin kasepe aathi wobontta mala “Inte toos lo7o oge giigisite”
Asi wurisora saro daana mala intes danda7etizayssa wursi oothite. Geeyena mala koyite. Geeshatethi baynda Goda beyanas danda7etena.
Intefe issadeskka Xoossa kiyatethi paccontta mala qasseka camo ayfe ayfiza mithi mokkidi meto medhontta malane darota moorontta mala naagetite.
Issito maana kaathas ba bayrateth bayzida Eesa mala intefe oonikka laaymattizade woykko Xoossu bonchontade gidi beetontta mala naagetite.
Eesay guyepe kase ba anjjoza laatanas zaari koyin izas imetontta digettidayssa inte ereista. Izi bena gakiza anjjozaskka daro yekkishe koyidika zaari demmanas danda7ibeyna.
Kushen bochchiko bochchetiza tamay iza bolla exxiza Siina zumako he dhumako, he tulalezaakone he gote carikozako inte gakibeykista.
Inte zaye giirethako woykko haythan siyetiza qaala giirethako gakkibeykista. Hessa siyida asatika hara qaala gujjontta mala woosssida.
Hessas gaaasoyka “Haray attoshin meheyka zuma bochchiza gidiko shuchan cadeti hayqo” giza azazoza asay naaganas danda7ibeyna.
He wode heeni hanizayssi wurikka daro babisizayssa gidida gishshsi Museykka “Ta babbada kokoradis” gides.
Inte qasse ha Xiyone zuma bolla pude salo Yerusalame ha deyo Xoossa kataman ufayssan shiiqida qooday baynda kiitanchatako yidista.
Istta suunthi salon xaafetida bayrata maabarako wurisos daana gidida Xoossako istta bolla wothoy baynda xiillo asata shempoy dizaso matidista.
Oaratha caaqon iginththiza Yesusako hessathoka Aabeley shiishida suuthafe aadhiza caaqo qaala yootiza aracetida suuthako gakidista.
Intes yootizayssa inte akkaye goontta mala naagetite. Heytantti Xoossi biitta bolla diza asa baggara isttas yootizayssa ekontta ixxidi izape attanas danda7ontta aggiko nuni salzope yidayssi nuusi yootishin nu ekkontta ixxiko izape waanidi attanee?
He wode qaala giirethan biitta qaathides. Ha7i qasse biitta xalala gidontta ta saloka qasseka ta zaarada issito qaathana” giza qaala yooti wothides.
Hayssi “Qasseka ta zaarada issito” giza qaalay nuna bessizay qaxxonttayti minni daana malane qaxxizayti heytika medhetidayti kichchanas besses.
Hessa gishshi nuni muleka qanxxonttayta kawoteth laatanayssa gishshi ane Xoossu galatosu. Qasseka iza ufayssiza ogera bonchosine yashatethan ane izas goynoos.
Nu Xoossi xuugiza tama malako
Inte inte gidon ishata mala dosetite.
Imatha mokko balopite; Issi issi asati hessaththo oothishe erontta kiitanchata imathateth mokki ekkida.
Qachcho keeththan dizaytara inteka qachettida mala isttas qopite. Hessaththoka asa kushen waayetizaytara inteka waayetiza mala isttas qopite.
Ekoy geloy wuriso asa achchan boncheto. Inte hithey geesh gido. Gaasoyka layma amoy dizaytane laymatizayta bolla Xoossi piridana.
Miisha siiqope naagetite. Intes dizaysi gidana. Hessas gaasoy Xoossi “Ta intena muleka aggikene yegike” gides.
Hessa gishshi kumetha wozinape nuni “Goday taas maado; ta babbike. Tana asi ay oothana danda7izee? goosu.
Intes Xoossa qaala koyrope yooti kaallethizayta balopite. Istta duusan beettiza lo7o ayfey dizayssa yuushi qopite. Inteka ammanon istta milatite.
Yesus kiristoosay hachchika wonttoka medhinaskka izi izako.
Dumma dumma imatha timirtte ekopite. Nu wozinay minni eqqizay Xoossa kiyatesan attin kaththa woga naagon gidena. Hessa he woga naagizaytaka izan go7etbeytena.
Nuusi yarsho soy dees. Gidikoka Dunkaaneza gidon oothiza qesseti he yarsho sooza bolla diza kaththafe ekki montta mala digetida.
Qessista halaqay nagara teqqiza mehe suuthu ekkidi wurisofe dumma geetettiza kifile geeles. Mehista ashoy gidiko katamape Karen xuugetes.
Hessaththoka Yesusay ba suutha baggara asa geeshanas katama pengefe Karen meto be7ides.
Hessa gishshi nuka izi tokkida kawushatetha tokkida nu dizasope gede izako kare ane kezoosu.
Gaasoyka hayssan eqqi daana. Katamay nuusi deena. Gido attin buro sinthafe yaana katamayo naagosu.
Hessa gishshi wuriso wode galata yarsho hessika iza sunthas marikatiza nu dunape bettiza ayfe gididazi Yesusa baggara Xoossas ane shiishos.
Qasseka lo7o oothone intes dizayssafe haratas imo balopite. Xoossi heytantta mala yarshon ufa7etes.
Intena kaallethizaytas azazetitene haaretite. Hessas gaasoyka inte gishshi istta alafetethan daro oychiza guday diza gishshi inte shempo gishshi daro baxetetes. Hessa gishshi istti ba oothiza oothoza lanccetishe gidontta ufayssan oothana mala inte isttas azazetite. Inte hessaththo hisitontta aggiko intes lo7ena.
Nuusika woossite. Wuriso sooraka lo7o duusu daanas laamotiza lo7o qofay nuusi dizayssa nu sidhoko.
Harapeka ta inteko ellen simma baana mala ta as inte woossan mala hadara gayssi.
Dorthata hethanchay wogga Goda Yesus kiristoosa ba medhina caaqo qaala suuthan iza hayqope denthida sarotetha Xoossi,
Inte iza shene polana mala lo7etethan intena gixiso. Xoossa ufayssizayssa Yesus kiristoosa baggara nunan ootho. Izas medhinape medhinas bonchoy gido. Amin7i.
Ta ishato, intes xaafida zore qaalay guuthu gidida gishshi inte hanqetontta mala ta intena hadara gayss.
Nu isha Ximotosay irishetidayssa inte erana mala ta koyayss. izi eeson taako yiiko ta izara hee baada intena heen beyana.
Inttena kaalethizayta wurisosine ammaniza asa wurisos ta saroka yootite. Xaalanen diza ammaniza asayka intena saro gees.
Xoossa kiyatethi intenara gido. Amin7i.
Xoossa Goda Yesusi Kiristossa oothancha gidida Yaqobeppe biitta bolla laletida tammane nam77u kochatas sarotethi intes gido.
Ta ishato inte bolla duma duma wayey gakkiiko hessa wursi ufaysan qoodite.
Gaasoykka inte amano paccetithi intes danda7a immizayssa inte ereetta.
Inte danda7an mini eqanaysi intes issi miishshikka pacconta kumetha assine wothoy bayndayta gidana mala ootho.
Inte garssafe oonasikka eratethi pacciko oonakka kadhontta ba kiiyatethara wurisos immiza Xoossa wosso; izadeskka imettana.
Gido attin sidhey baynda amanon wosso. Gaasoykka sidhiiza uray abba qathiza bullahe cariko malakko.
Hessadey Godape aykokk demana giidi issinokka qoppofo.
He uray nam77u qohaaththaan ooyketidi ba bizza oge bolla hene haane giza asa malakko.
Kase ziiqan diza ura Xoossi dhoqqu histiza gish ufa7etto.
Asa haroy maata cisha mala qoqofettiza gish dure ura Xoossi ziq histikko ufa7etto.
Away xugidi maata shullisees; maata ciishayka shullees; iza loo7etethikka dhayees; hessathokka durey hachchi hachchi dabursan diishin iza duretethi dhayees.
Paccen miinni eqidadey izi anjjetidade. Gaasoyka izi paccera eqitishin Xoossi bena dosizaytas immida ufaysa deyo zawude izi ekkana.
Oonikka paccetiza gidikko tana Xoossi paccees goppo, gaasoykka Xoossi ase iittan paccena, izi oonakka pacci erena.
Gido attin issi issi uray paccetizay berika ba iitta amo kalishene baletishekko.
Amoy qanthetetidape guye nagara yellees. Nagaraykka dicciidape guye hayqo yellees.
Ta siiqo ishato inte ballettopite.
Loo7o imotethine kumetha anjjoy wuri bolla Salo poo7ota Aawape wodhetes. Iza achan gede ha yuyiza kuwayka (eshoykka) dena.
Nu iza medhetethas koyro bayrata gidana mala ba sheninne ba tuma qaalan nuna yellides.
Dosetida ta ishato hayssa yuushi qoppite. Asi wurikka siyanas esoto, hasa7asinne hanqqos esotopo.
Asa hanqqoy Xoossa xiiloteth oothena.
Hessa gish tunatethinne dalggida iittatethi intefe kessi yegidi inte shemppo ashanaas danda7iza inte gidon toketida qaala ashketethara ekkite.
Qaalay gizayssa oothite; attin mela siisi xalala siyzadista gididi interkka intena balethofite.
Qaala siyishe siyida qaalay gizayssa oothontadey ba ayfeso mastotera xelliza asa malakko.
Bena xeelli beydi bees; izi ay milatizakone heraka baletti gides.
Gido attin bena geshiza loo7o woga xeelli beydi izan minizadey ba siydayssa oothizadeynne balonttadey izi ba oothon anjjetidade gidana.
Be duuna nagontta berikka ba wozina baleththishe ta ammanayss gizadey berikka bena baleththees. Iza ammanoykka mella hada ammanokko.
Xoossa Aawa sinthan iittatethi baynda loo7o ammanoy; “Aayanne Aaway hayqqida nayta, istta azinati hayqqida maccashata metotetishin maadonne hayssa alameza tunatethafe bena nagokko.
Ta ishato inte bonchettida Goda Yesussa Kiristosa ammanizayta gidida mala asse besontta ogera maadofiite.
Worqqa yiich biradhen aaththdi loo7o mayo mayida asi inte shiqqizaso yiikko hessathokka qiita mayo mayidadey he shiqqizaso yiko qaseka hara qiita mayo mayda manqqo uray gelliko loo7o maydaysa duma boncho bonchidi “nees besiiza loo7o utizaso hessa beya” giidi hayinko manqqoza qasse “Ne hen hessan eqa, woykko haa ya ta garisan hugen uta” inte gikko;

Inte inte garsan besontta maado oothista gideketi? Qasseka inte iitta qofan ooykittida iitta pirda piirdizayta gideketi?
Ta siiqo ishato ane siyte; isti ammanon durista gidana mala Xoossi bena dosizaytas ufayssan isttas immida kawotetha istti laattana mala hayssa ha alamezan diza manqota dooribeynee?
Inte qase manqota kawusheista. Intena waysiza durista gidetene? Intena piirdeso gochizay istta gidetenee?
Intenan xeygetida boncho Xoossa sunththa zigirizayti ista gidetenee?
Maxaafan “Ne lagge ne hu7e mala siiqa” geeteti xaafettida kawo woga inte polikko loo7o oothista.
Inte besonta maado madikko nagara oothista. woga sinthanka inte woga yedhidade gidi qodistana.
Gaasoykka woga wursi pollizadey qasekka wogape issineyin dhuphetiza uray wursikka moridade mala qoodettees.
“Laymatopa” gidadey izikka zaaridi “wodhopa” gides. Ne laymatontta agikokka ne asa wodhikko wogape adhiidade gidaassa.
Inte hasa7a hasa7ishe woykko issi miishshi oothishe intena xiillisiza asa mala gidite.
Gaasoykka marontay wurikka maroy baynda pirdistana. Maroy pirda Xoonees.
Ta ishato issi uray taas ammanoy dees gikko qasse oothon besontade gidikko iza ay maadanee? Hesamala amanoy iza ashane?
Ane qoppite, issi ishay woykko issi michiya mayoy woykko mizayssi baynda aggiko intefe isadey “Inte saron biite, intena megopo, kallite” giiko istta ashos koshizayssa immontta aggikko ay maadanee?

Hesathokka oothoy baynda ammanoykka bees hayidayssa.
Gido attin isadey “Taas oothoy dees nees ammanoy dees. Neni ne ammano oothope shaakada tana bessa, ta qasse ta ammano oothon nena bessana gikko;
Ne “issi Xoossi dizaysa ammanayss” loo7oko; daydanthatikka hessa mala ammanettesinne kehi kokoreetes.
Neno eeyazo! oothoy baynda ammanos go7ay bayndayssa eranas marikka koyazii?
Nu Aawa Abramey ba na Yisaqa yarshizasoza bolla shiishshida wode oothon xilli beynee?
Hessan ammanoy iza oothora isife dizaysanne amanoy ooothon poletidayssa beyazii?
“Abramey Xoossu ammanides; He amanoy izas xiillotethan qoodetides” giza maxaafa qaalay poletides; izikka Xoossi dosidade geetettides.
Hessa gish asi ammanon xalala gidontta oothonkka xiillizaysa inte beyeista.
Hesathokka laymman diza Era7aba kiiteti bida asata mokka ekada hara ogera moyza yedida gish ba oothon xiillabeykee?
Shemppofe shaakettida ashoy hayqeeth gidida mala oothopekka shaakettida ammanoy hayqethikko.
Ta ishato intefe daroti astamarista gidopeto, gaasoykka nu astamare gididayti aadhetha pirda ekanaysa inte ereista.
Nu wurikka daro miishan dhuphetoos. Hasa7an dhuphetontadey dikko izi ba asateth loo7athi naganaas danda7iza kumetha asakko.
Nuni parazota azazanaas bixxala barsidi nu koyda mala istta azazoos.
Woykko ane markabista xeelite. Ay gitatanne carikon lagetizayta gidikokka marikabe lagiizadey qeeri laafa laagiza misheyira ba koyizaso efees.
Hessathokka asatetha garisan inxxarisi guuthu gida utada giita wollqama oothoro oothoristaysu, qeeri tamay gita wora wostti xuuggi dhaysiizakonne ane yuushi qoppiite.
Inxxarasikka ba bagara tama malakko. Nu asatetha gidon diza iitta alamekko. Asatetha wursa tuniisaysunne asatetha bolla tama gujawusu, besiika gaaname taman xugistana.
Mehey do7ayka kafoti hayssathokka biita bolla gochetizaytinne abba gidon diza medhetethata wursi asi harana danda7esinne istikka haraettida.
Gido attin inxxars haranaas danda7ida uray oonikka dena. Wodhiiza maridzdzey izin kumidaronne iza shemppa ekontta iitta mishshikko.
Nuni nu inxxarasayra Godanne Aawa anjjoos. Izinkka Xoossa lemison medhetida asa nayta zaaridi qangoos.
Anjjoynne qangethi issi duunara keezes. Ta ishato hessi hessaththo hananaas bessena.
Issi pullto ollafe mal7o haththinne camo haththi pullti erizee?
Ta ishato Balase geetettiza miiththi woyra ayfe woykko woyine miiththi Balase miiththa ayfe ayfanaas danda7ize? Hesathokka camiza hathefe mall7iza haththi bistana danda7ena.

qanateyinne berika bena siqqoy dizason wasoynne iitta oothoy wuri dees.
Sallope gidida eratethiya gidikko koyro geshshikko, guyepekka saroteth dosizaro, danda7izaaro, ero gizaro, marotethinne loo7o ayfey kumidarokko. Qasse worodo madontaronne ulon geney bayndaro.
Saroteth dosiza asati sarotethan zeridi xillotetha ayfe maxeettes.
Inte garsan diza oolaynne ooshay awape yidee? Inte wozinan diza amotethafe dendida oola gidenee?
Inte amottista shin demekista. Inte asi wodhistanne kehi amotista shin demana danda7ekista. Inte inte garisan ooyetiza gishanne ooletiza gish qasse wosontta gish intes imettena.
Inte inte asho ufaysanaas iitta qofan wosiza gish wosidaysa inte ekekista.
Inteno laymatizayto alamera siiqetethi Xoossara morketeth gididaysa ereketii? Hessa gish hayssa alamezara siiqitethi koyzay wurikka Xoossas morke.
Woykko gesha maxaafa gidon “nunan izi ayssiida ayanay nu ziaysa gidana mala daro amottees” gizaysi intes coo mela gidayssa milatize?
Gido attin izi ba kiiyateth nuus gujji immees. Maxafaykka “Xoossi ootoranchatara eqettees, ashikistas qase ba kiiyateth immees” giday hessasikko.
Hessa gish intena Xoossas harisiite. Dabuloosara eqitite, izi intefe baqatana.
Xoossako shiiqqite izikka intekko shiiqqana. Inteno nagaranchato! inte inte kushe geeshshite, inte nam77u qofan qaxiizayto, inte inte wozina geeshshite.
Darsi qoppite; muyagiite; yekiite. Inte michay yehon; ufaysay qasse qadhetethan siimo.
Goda sinththan inte intena kawushite qasse izi intena dhooqu dhooqu histtana.
Ta ishato inte inte garisan issay issay motoopite ba isha motizadeynne ba isha bolla piridizadey woga bolla iitta hasa7esinne woga bolla piridees. Ne woga bolla pirdizade attin woga naagizade gidakka.
Woga wothidadeynne pirdizadey issade xalalakko. Izikka dhaysanaasinne ashanaas danda7izadekko. Gido attin neni ne lagge bolla pirdizadey oone?
Inte hachchchi woykko wontto hano ha katamayo woykko hiino he katamayo nu baana, biidi hen izin issi laythth utananne zal77i wodhisana gizayto ane haa siyte.
Wonto hananayssa inte erekista. Inte shemppoy iza azee? Inteni guutha wode ayfes bettidi dhayiza haththa penta malakko.
Hassa gaanappe “Goda shene gidikonne nu paxxa dikko, hessakka hayssaka oothana” gaanas intes bessees.
Ha7i gidiko inte otoretethan ceqetista. Hessa mala oothoretethi wurikka iitta.
Hessa gish loo7o gidizayssa oothanas besizaysa erishe oothonttades nagara gidana.
Histikko inteno dure asato, ane siiyte. Buro inte bolla gakkana metoza gish yekiite, wu! wu! gi wasiite.
Inte haaroy buqqides, inte mayoykka bil7ay/baday/ mides.
Inte worqayinne inte biiray shiyides. He shiydaysikka inte bolla marikatesinne inte ashoy tama mala xuugees. Inte wode wurisethas miishshe shiishshidista.
Inte inte wozinan wothite inte kaththi maxishe pe7idaytas istta wollqa waaga inte qanxxontta aggida gish inte bolla wasishe inte achchan deettes. Kaththi maxizayta wassoy wursi danda7iza Goda haythan gakides.
Inte biitta bolla ishallonne aloo7etethan deyidista, inte wozina shuka galasas dhiikki handadhathidista.
Inte intenara eqetontta xiillo asata bolla worido wothidi wodhiidista.
Hessa gish ta ishato Goday ha yaana gakanas danda7ite. Goshshe goyizadey biittay loo7o kathth kaxxana gakanaas wani danda7izakone balgo/asura/ irane ofintha ira izi wostti naagizako ane akekkite.
Inteka hessaththo danda7ite. Inte wozina miinthite. Gaasoykka Goda yussa gallas matides.
Ta ishato inte inte garsan zigretopite, inte zigretiko inte bolla piridistana. Piridanadey heko inte penge bolla eqqides.
Ta ishato Goda sunththan intes yootida nabeta wayetethinne istta danda7a intes lemuso histti xeellite.
Danda7an genccida asata nu istta “IstTi anjjetidayta” gi qoodizayssa inte ereista. Iyobey wanii danda7idakonne inte iza gish siyidista. Goday iza wurisethan ay oothidakone inte beyidista. Goday asas keehi michetizadenne marizadekko.
Harapeka ta ishato sallon gidin woykko biitta bolla gidin woykko ay mishanka caqqofite; “Ee” gaanas bessiza miishsha gidikko “Ee” giite; “Akaye” gaanas gidiko “Akaye” giite hessafe hara giiko inte bolla pirdistana.
Inte garisan metotiza uray dizee? Diza gidiko izi wosso. Ufa7etizadey dizee? diza gidiko ufayssa yeethi yeexxo.
Inte gidon saketiza assi dizee? diiko wossa keeththa ciimata xeyigo. Isttikka Goda sunththan zayte iza bolla tiyidi izas wosseto.
Ammanon wossida wossay hargidade pathana. Godaykka iza denthana. Izi nagara oothidade gidikokka Xoossi iza maarana.
Hessa gish intekka inte garisan issay issara inte nagara paxxetite; paxana mala issay issas wossite. Xiillo asa wossay wolliqara dees. Wollqama oothokka ooththees.
Elasay nu malaka asekko. Izi iray bukontta mala minthi wossin biitta bolla hezdzdu laythanne bagga gakanaas iray bukiibeyna.
Qasseka zaari wossin iray sallope biitta bolla bukides. Biittayka kaath immides.
Ta ishato intefe issadey tumape baletin hara uray iza zaariko hessa wozinan wothiite. Nagarancha izi balletida ogepe iza zaaridadey he uray shempo hayqope ashesinne izaade nagara darozaka kammees.
